## 10TH-01 序·致新年 / Annum Novum Faustum et Beatum

我是一句测试文本。\
A sealed office, with a screen emitting white light.

密闭的办公室内，唯有暗处一面显示屏的白光，在这个阴暗沉寂的空间中显得十分抢眼。\
A dial tone echoes through the quiet space before the call is answered.

密闭的办公室，一面闪烁着白光的显示屏。

拨号声在安静的室内回荡，很快，通讯的另一头出现了回应。

**？？？**：联络员刻雷乌斯，请查收，鸽子屋调令：Annum Novum Faustum et Beatum\
**???**: Liaison Creius, here's the order signed by the Pax House: Annum Novum Faustum et Beatum.

通讯那头响起按键声，不久传真机开始运作。\
Beeping sounds come from the other end of the line, and soon the fax machine whirs to life.

**？？？**：军事委员会裁定的最终结论——即刻联系芝诺的索姆将军，整顿队伍，带兵前往这个坐标区域。\
**???**: This is the Military Commission's conclusion: Contact Admiral Somme of Zeno and lead the troops to these coordinates immediately.

**？？？**：做好背水一战的准备。\
**???**: Be prepared for an all-out battle.

**刻雷乌斯**：……\
**Creius**: ...

通讯那头沉默了半秒。\
The other end falls silent for half a second.

**刻雷乌斯**：……我还从未见过这样的调令。\
**Creius**: Hmm. I've never received an order like this.

霜雪凝结在玻璃窗外，站在半光半影的房间中，副会长抬起手在玻璃的冷雾上画了一个圈。\
Standing in the half-lit room, the vice president draws a circle on the frosty window.

**康斯坦丁**：出兵坐标指向南极。\
**Constantine**: Note that the designated coordinates lie in Antarctica.

**康斯坦丁**：那里是重塑之手最大的据点，也是仪式的中心。\
**Constantine**: There, you'll find Manus Vindictae's largest stronghold and the site of their ritual.

**刻雷乌斯**：仪式？\
**Creius**: Ritual?

**康斯坦丁**：一场关乎所有时代的仪式，重塑之手避人耳目地准备了许久，就是为了这一刻。\
**Constantine**: Yes, the ritual of both past and future. It seems Manus Vindictae has been preparing it in secret for quite some time.

副会长的语气中略有些冷意。\
Her tone is as cold as the weather beyond.

**刻雷乌斯**：仪式的目的是？\
**Creius**: What's this ritual for, exactly?

**康斯坦丁**：你很快就会知道的。\
**Constantine**: You'll find out soon enough.

**刻雷乌斯**：……我们从未进行过如此大规模、却又如此突然的作战。\
**Creius**: We haven't fought a battle of such scale and so suddenly since ...

**刻雷乌斯**：除了1999年的那场“战役”。\
**Creius**: The battle of 1999.

**康斯坦丁**：……\
**Constantine**: ...

副会长的目光始终落在窗外。\
Her eyes remain fixed outside the window.

雪霜挂在合金窗栏外的蛛网上，一根细细的网丝难以承受其重量，断在咆哮的寒风里。\
Frost clings to spiderwebs outside the alloy window frame.

网丝飞扬千里，绕雪旋转下降。\
A thin strand flies off on a long journey down into the piling snow.

**刻雷乌斯**：历史正在重演，对吗？\
**Creius**: History is repeating itself, isn't it?

**康斯坦丁**：刻雷乌斯联络员。\
**Constantine**: Liaison Creius.

副会长打断了接下来的询问。\
She doesn't give him the chance to continue.

**康斯坦丁**：我们期待你这次的表现。\
**Constantine**: We look forward to your performance on the field.

**康斯坦丁**：你清楚，手握成功履历的人能得到更多信息的知情权。\
**Constantine**: As you know, officers with successful track records are often given greater access to information.

**刻雷乌斯**：……\
**Creius**: ...

**刻雷乌斯**：是。\
**Creius**: Yes, madam.

压抑着尾音，通讯那头最终挂断了信号。\
Suppressing any betrayal of tone or emotion, he ends the call.

雪花屏的白光始终映照在窗户上。副会长的目光被其吸引。\
The screen's white glow illuminates the window again.

雪花屏的白光始终映照在窗户上。\
Labeled videotapes organized by time and date are slotted neatly on the shelves.

书架上，刻录着时间的录像井井有条。\
A tape is pulled down and inserted into the projector.

最终，其中一盘录像带被挑拣，推入放映机中。

**康斯坦丁**：历史正在重演……\
**Constantine**: History is repeating itself.

**康斯坦丁**：但“希望”依旧在我们手上。\
**Constantine**: But we still have "hope" on our side.

显示屏里发出老旧的电流声，噼啪作响。\
The screen crackles with static.

隔着时间钻过老化的电流，年幼的声音从显示屏内传出。\
A child's voice comes garbled by aged electronics.

**？？？**：这是什么？\
**???**: What's this?

**Z女士**：这是给你的礼物。\
**Z**: It's a gift for you.

**维尔汀**：礼物？一个……箱子？\
**Vertin**: A gift? A ... suitcase?

**Z女士**：是的，为了庆祝你正式成为基金会的司辰。\
**Z**: That's right. To celebrate your appointment as the Foundation's Timekeeper.

**Z女士**：这是一个值得纪念的时刻。\
**Z**: This is a moment to remember, Vertin.

孩子似乎并不能理解箱子作为礼物的含义。\
The child doesn't seem to understand the suitcase's significance.

而与此同时，她仍有更多的疑问。\
And yet she has more questions.

**维尔汀**：那——它是谁送的呢？\
**Vertin**: Who's it from?

**维尔汀**：那个人为什么不自己送给我？\
**Vertin**: Why didn't they give it to me themselves?

**Z女士**：它来自一位故人。\
**Z**: It's from an old friend.

**维尔汀**：一位……故人？\
**Vertin**: An old friend?

**Z女士**：她还为你留下了一句话。\
**Z**: She left you a message, too.

她说……\
She said ...

P a r a d i s e R e g a i n e d 复 乐 园\
P a r a d i s e R e g a i n e d

P a r a d i s e R e g a i n e d 复 乐 园

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**十四行诗**：怎么了？司辰。\
**Sonetto**: Is everything alright, Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：……没事。\
**Vertin**: I'm fine.

思绪恍然抽回。\
Thoughts return to the present.

**维尔汀**：只是想起了过去的一些事。\
**Vertin**: A memory just came to me.

**维尔汀**：感觉船越往南、越寒冷，就越是熟悉……\
**Vertin**: The further south we go and the colder the weather gets, the harder it is to shake this feeling of déjà vu.

**维尔汀**：就仿佛……\
**Vertin**: It's like ...

酥麻、疼痛、愉悦，称之为情绪，抑或称之为某种杏仁体生理机制。\
That titillation, pain, and pleasure—call it emotion or some physiological mechanism of the amygdala.

**维尔汀**：就仿佛我曾到过这里……\
**Vertin**: Like I've been here before.

同伴担忧的目光透过玻璃窗反射而来。\
Her companion's concern reflects back to her from the window.

深吸一口气，脉搏的跳动被强行压抑回平静。\
A deep breath suppresses her heartbeat.

**维尔汀**：……我们、我们快到了吗？\
**Vertin**: Will—Will we be there soon?

话音被船体靠岸的碰撞打断。\
Words are cut off by bustle of the ship's docking.

**十四行诗**：呃——！\
**Sonetto**: Ugh!

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

呵出的热气化作白雾飘远，船只由晃动渐渐变得稳定。\
Her breath crystallizes into mist as the vessel stabilizes.

**维尔汀**：看样子，我们已经到了。\
**Vertin**: Looks like we've arrived.

二人从船舱中走出。\
The two emerge from the cabin.

经过多日隐秘的绕行，最终她们站在明媚的甲板上，向远方眺望。\
After days of covert detours, at last they stand on the sunlit deck, looking into the distance.

**十四行诗**：这里是罗斯冰架西北部边缘的麦克默多湾，南极探险的中心与起点。\
**Sonetto**: This is McMurdo Sound, the starting point of our Antarctic expedition.

举目之下，白色的冰原漠然耸立着。\
Before them stretches a white field of ice.

它永恒冰冷坚硬，耀眼又死寂。\
Dazzling yet lifeless.

它对发生在自己身上的一切都保持沉默、不予置评。\
A droning silence that gives up no hint of what may once have been.

但同时，它又以人们所无法辨识的分贝怒吼着，震慑所有企图踏上这片土地的人。\
Yet beneath the silence roars an imperceptible foreboding.

Hic iacet revelatio; hic iacet finis. “这里将是启示之地，亦将是终结之地。”\
"Hic iacet revelatio; hic iacet finis." "This will be the place of revelation, and it will also be the place of conclusion."

## 10TH-02 古舟子咏 / The Rime of the Ancient Mariner

不要探求真相\
不要深入南极\
不要前进

**队友Ⅰ**：已经进入冰区了！拿上望远镜，探险家们！\
**Team Member I**: Entering the ice zone. Grab your telescopes, explorers.

**队友Ⅱ**：报告你所看见的每块浮冰的位置，咱们的船可不是泰坦尼克号——\
**Team Member II**: That's right. We need your eyes on every ice floe. Let's not make a second Titanic.

**队友Ⅰ**：现在不是开这种玩笑的场合，考特！\
**Team Member I**: This isn't the time for jokes, Koht.

……怀着极度兴奋的心情，我们出发了。在接下来的一段时间内，我们以无可估量的勇气和缜密充足的准备横跨了德雷克海峡。\
Hearts thumping with excitement, our team set off. Thanks to our courage and careful preparation, it wasn't long until we crossed the Drake Passage.

再猛烈的下降风都无法摧残前进的意志。事实上，我们所遭遇的暴风与实验室模拟过的相差无几，船长很快就找到了抗衡自然的办法。\
No matter how fierce the katabatic winds were, our will stood firm. In fact, the windstorm we met was very similar to the lab-simulated ones. It didn't take long for the captain to find a way to deal with it.

我们驶入了南设得兰群岛，这里除了黑色的冰碛外，只看得见成群的阿德利企鹅。\
Soon, we were sailing through the South Shetland Islands. There wasn't much there but black moraine and a few groups of Adélie penguins.

很显然，要抵达我们预定展开探索的地方，需要更多跋涉。但我们信心满满，队伍所有人都相信最深远艰险之地是所有古老秘密的渊薮。\
It was clear to us that there was more trudging to be done before we reached our destination. But every one of us was confident that a journey of this magnitude would pay off with very many ancient secrets.

当天光再次亮起，我们看到地衣铺满埃特绍群岛，赤红色、藻绿色、赭石色，流动的颜色使远方的“陆映光”失语。\
When the sun dawned, we saw the lichen that grows all over the Aitcho Islands. Crimson, green, ocher ... Even the landblink couldn't pale those colors.

在那一刻，我们发出感叹，岩石是会流动的。\
That was when we realized that rocks can move too.

我不禁联想起著名的“戈文伦号”满载而归时，人们沐浴在整桶整桶的收获所带来的欢欣之下。\
I can't help but recall when the famous Guvernøren returned with a full and bountiful load. We celebrated the harvest very amazingly.

我们开了一桶啤酒，在霞光掩映下唱响故乡的歌谣。\
We opened a keg of beer and sang the songs of home under the rosy sky.

“富足的收成是人类的福音，盲童亦要被指引迷津。”\
"The harvest's bounty mankind's blessing be. We children, blind, from mazes must be free."

“地母古迹的光芒，引导我辈臣服于自然的律法。”\
"The Mother Spirit's light, with ancient glow, guides us to the great current—nature's flow."

是的，我们是极地探险家，我们理应挑战最不为人知的伟大。\
Yes, we are the polar explorers. We are meant to be the challengers of the most unknown greatness.

于是怀着这样的心情，我们向着更深的腹地进发。\
So, with this feeling in our hearts, we will continue our march into the depths of Antarctica.

今宵苦短，我感到我的人生中没有一刻比此时更欢愉，更充实，更有价值。\
Carpe diem, as the saying goes. I've never felt more joyful and fulfilled and worthy in my entire life.

二冲程柴油机突突作响。\
A two-stroke diesel engine sputters.

嗞——嗞嗞——噗……\
Bzz—bzzt— *thud* ...

随着电火花的飞溅，无线电发报机发出一声呻吟。\
Sparks fly as the radio transmitter groans.

**诺谛卡**：一定要……一定要将这份电报发送出去……\
**Nautika**: I, I must ... I must send it out.

破烂颤抖、几近疯癫的声音从科考站最里端的黑暗角落中传出。\
A ragged, maddened voice comes from the research station's darkest corner,

她正对着一台报废的设备颤抖，徒劳地发送着不再可能被送出的电报。\
speaking into broken equipment with undeliverable messages.

**诺谛卡**：噢……呼……放轻松，诺谛卡，放轻松……\
**Nautika**: *panting* Calm down, Nautika. Calm down.

**诺谛卡**：这里是你的科考站，你和大家一起建立起来的科考站。\
**Nautika**: This is your research station. You built it together with the team.

**诺谛卡**：你现在很安全。没错，“地母”会保护好你……你、你现在……很安全。\
**Nautika**: You're safe now. Yes, the Mother Spirit will protect you. You're ... You're safe now.

**诺谛卡**：呼……呼……你只需要再试一次，再试一次……\
**Nautika**: Just-Just try it one more time, just one more.

手指反复用力按下已然报废的发报机电键，她的全身却在不自控地颤抖。\
Her fingers keep pressing the broken transmitter key while her body shakes uncontrollably.

**诺谛卡**：来吧，加油，它们不难，你没有疯，你完全正常，你知道所有字母对应的摩尔斯电码。\
**Nautika**: Come on, come on. You can do it. It's simple. You didn't go crazy. You have all your brains in here in your head. It knows all the letters of Morse code and how to send them.

**诺谛卡**：A、D、E、F、C，拼出警告讯息，然后发布给世人，任何人……这不难，就像玩萨米板棋一样，一点儿都不难……\
**Nautika**: See? There's A, and D, and E, F, C. You know them all. Just use them to spell out the warning message and send it out across the whole world ... everyone. It, it's easy, like playing a game of "tablut." Yes, so easy.

**诺谛卡**：——来吧！\
**Nautika**: I can do this.

她发狠般地猛嚼了一口嘴里的黑色胶质流体。\
She munches down on a black gelatinous fluid in her mouth.

不要探求真相\
不……

**诺谛卡**：寒冷……发霉的酸橙汁和难吃的冰藻……该死的冻疮——以及，闻着血腥味等死！\
**Nautika**: Cold. This moldy lime juice and disgusting ice algae, this damn frostbite ... Nothing left to do but sit here, stinking of blood, and wait for death to take me.

**诺谛卡**：必须警告所有人，这里不是人类最后的绿洲，也根本没有什么地心世界……\
**Nautika**: I have to warn the world. This place isn't the last oasis, and there's no such thing as the Hollow Earth.

**诺谛卡**：可、可如果没有亲眼见证，不会有人相信我在说什么的……没有人会相信！\
**Nautika**: But-But no one will believe me if they don't see it with their own eyes. Nobody!

**诺谛卡**：就像……\
**Nautika**: Because ...

**诺谛卡**：我自己曾经那样……\
**Nautika**: Because I used to be the same way.

**耳朵虫**：“巨人人母之骨是必经之路，血染的苦痛使子民永生顿悟。”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "Through Giant Mother's bones the path is laid. In bloody pain, eternal life is made."

**耳朵虫**：“地母古迹的光芒，引导我辈臣服于自然的律法”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "The Mother Spirit's light, with ancient glow, guides us to the great current—nature's flow."

**诺谛卡**：又开始闹了……我的小耳朵虫……\
**Nautika**: Not now, little Máhtu.

**诺谛卡**：地母保佑……求地母降下她的福祉与荣光保佑我这个弱小的人类能够捱过去……\
**Nautika**: Mother Spirit, bless me. Lend me your glorious strength and grant me your protection. L-Let me live through this.

“轰隆——”科考站外传来如雷般的声响。\
"Boom—" A thunderous noise comes from outside.

**诺谛卡**：——！！！\
**Nautika**: !!!

这小团蠕动的黑影被吓了一跳。\
The small figure startles.

她侧身移动到窗户旁，透过隔热锡垫的边缘看向外面。\
She sidles to the window, peeking through the insulation's edge.

**诺谛卡**：——是疯、“疯雪怪”的船！\
**Nautika**: A Snow Monster ship?

**？？？**：打扰了……我们……\
**???**: Excuse me, is anybody ...

**诺谛卡**：——！！！\
**Nautika**: !!!

**诺谛卡**：别过来，别过来，别过来……\
**Nautika**: Please don't come over here, please, please, please.

亮色头发的“疯雪怪”闯入了探险家最后的栖息地。\
A bright-haired "Snow Monster" has invaded the explorer's last refuge.

**？？？**：不好意思，我们注意到这里是附近唯一的建筑，想要寻求一些帮助……请问有人在吗？\
**???**: Excuse me, is there anyone here? We just landed, and this is the only building around. We were hoping to ask for some help.

**诺谛卡**：我、我已经是一具冰冻的破烂皮囊，你们休想打碎我的颅骨吸食我的血！\
**Nautika**: I-I'm already half frozen to death. Don't you dare crack my skull and suck my blood. I won't taste any good.

**？？？**：请稍等一下，我想我们之间存在一些误会……\
**???**: My apologies. There must have been some kind of misunderstanding.

**诺谛卡**：冰川里的黑色疫病、地母脚下的蠕虫、令人反胃的面具暴君！\
**Nautika**: Plague in the glacier, the worms beneath the feet of the Mother Spirit, and those sickening masked tyrants.

**诺谛卡**：疯雪怪！！我跟你们、跟你们拼了——！！！\
**Nautika**: Bring it on, Snow Monster. If I can wrestle a reindeer, then I can take on you.

**？？？**：等、等一下——\
**???**: W-Wait!

**诺谛卡**：……不是“疯雪怪”？\
**Nautika**: You're not a Snow Monster?

**诺谛卡**：正常的言行举止，没有戴面具，会使用神神叨叨的“魔术”……对，暖和的魔术，我的手指不像之前冻得那样僵了。\
**Nautika**: N-Normal behavior, no mask, uses magic, yes, warm magic. I can move my fingers again.

**诺谛卡**：对，小耳朵虫，他们确实……看上去不是坏人……\
至少不像“疯雪怪”那么坏。\
**Nautika**: You're right, Máhtu. They don't seem like bad people.\
At least, not as bad as the Snow Monsters.

癫狂的黑影瑟缩了一下，终于又退回角落。但警惕的目光始终没有从闯入者身上移开。\
Crazed but still wary, she shrinks back to keep an eye on the intruders.

两位闯入者正小心翼翼地把桌椅推回原位，表现得正常而礼貌。\
The two newcomers seem without concern. They straighten the furniture and examine the scene as if looking at a puzzle.

**十四行诗**：根据阿莱夫先生提供的信息，德洛丝女士应该就是在这一带的海岸登陆的。\
**Sonetto**: Hm. According to Mr. Aleph, this should be the coast that Dr. Dores landed on.

**十四行诗**：这处平原是通往腹地的必经之路，如果我们加快脚步，说不定还能追上她。\
**Sonetto**: This plain is the way to the heart of Antarctica. We may still catch up with her if we pick up our pace.

**维尔汀**：不过我没想到，路上居然有一座科考站。\
**Vertin**: I see. But I didn't expect there to be a research station all the way out here.

**十四行诗**：这里确实不在任何我们能找到的南极地图上，应当是最近半年才搭建起来的。\
**Sonetto**: This place isn't on any map of Antarctica I've ever seen. It must have been built less than half a year ago.

**十四行诗**：设施相当完备。柴油发电机、雪地摩托、无线电发报机……\
**Sonetto**: The facilities are quite complete. Diesel generators, snowmobiles, radio transmitters ...

第一助手向前靠近了一步，一个空罐头滚落在她的脚边，罐底已经空无余渍。\
Sonetto steps forward. An empty can rolls to her feet.

**十四行诗**：不过，食物储备已经告罄了。\
**Sonetto**: However, they seem to have run out of food.

视线投向了暗处角落瑟缩的人影。\
Her eyes turn to the cowering figure.

**维尔汀**：我们只是过路的旅人，希望得到来自科考站的一些帮助，无意伤害大家。\
**Vertin**: We're just passing by. We mean no harm. Is there anyone else at this station that can help us?

被困百日的探险家站在角落里，搓了搓鼻子。\
A hundred days of solitude ends with a simple question. Nautika stands half-hobbled in the corner, rubbing her nose.

**诺谛卡**：这、这里没有“我们”——\
**Nautika**: N-No. There's no one else.

**诺谛卡**：只有我了。\
**Nautika**: Only me.

**十四行诗**：请恕我直言，你看起来很糟糕……请允许我为你进行一次健康诊断。\
**Sonetto**: I don't mean to offend, miss, but you don't look very well. May I give you a health evaluation?

**诺谛卡**：不——不必了！我很好，我是探险家，我对自己的身体状况了如指掌……\
**Nautika**: No, no need. I'm fine. I'm an explorer. I-I know my body. I'm fine.

探险家拒绝之余，更加防备地往墙角退了半步。\
She retreats back from the newcomer's offered hand.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

**十四行诗**：你……在吃什么？\
**Sonetto**: What are you eating?

年轻的探险家捧着一把滑溜溜的黑色物质，它像一团由纤维及黏液组成的非牛顿流体，正沿着手指的缝隙往下流——\
Nautika clutches black slime—a fibrous, mucus-like fluid oozing between her fingers.

探险家舔了舔嘴唇，猛地把它吞进了肚子里。\
She licks her lips and swallows it whole.

**诺谛卡**：这里唯一能吃的。\
**Nautika**: The only thing there is to eat here.

发色明亮的基金会职员摇了摇头。\
Sonetto shakes her head.

皮箱的金属卡扣被打开，发出两声清脆的细响。\
And the suitcase's metal clasps are opened with two clicks.

**十四行诗**：配方是牛肉高汤、芜菁与土豆块，希望能合你的胃口。\
**Sonetto**: Please, take this. It's turnip and potato soup with beef. I hope it suits your tastes.

食物。\
Food.

新鲜的食物。\
Fresh food.

受困者颤抖地向前伸出手。\
The long-suffering explorer reaches out as tenderly as a fawn.

**诺谛卡**：那、那是魔术箱？\
**Nautika**: I-Is that a magic suitcase?

她指了指神奇地变出食物来的手提箱。\
She points at the suitcase that conjured food out of thin air.

**维尔汀**：噢，一个神秘学箱子。里边比看起来更大，能装下很多东西，食物、房间，甚至是神秘学家本身。\
**Vertin**: Yes. It's an arcane suitcase. It's bigger on the inside. It can hold food, rooms, even arcanists themselves.

**诺谛卡**：所、所以你们是神秘学家！\
**Nautika**: So you're arcanists!

探险家苍白的脸恢复了一点血色，她兴奋地上下打量着两位访客。\
Color finally returns to her pale face as she begins to examine her visitors with fresh eyes.

**维尔汀**：是的，我们是神秘学家。\
**Vertin**: That's right.

蛋白质馥郁的香气从锡罐中飘出。\
A protein-rich aroma wafts up from the tin.

**维尔汀**：我们打算深入南极腹地。或许，你愿意为我们提供一些忠告吗？\
**Vertin**: Actually, we're heading to the heart of Antarctica. Perhaps you'd be willing to offer us some advice?

**诺谛卡**：——！\
**Nautika**: ...!

罐头在惊慌中被打翻，洒了一地汤汁。\
She knocks over the tin in panic. The soup inside splatters out across the floor.

探险家疯狂地颤抖。她下意识地不断喃喃着，像是已经在脑海中重复过无数遍相似的话语。\
Her body shakes erratically, and she returns to a mantra of bizarre muttered half-phrases rehearsed in her mind over and over again.

**诺谛卡**：不要深入……不要深入南极……\
**Nautika**: No. You mustn't. Do not go into Antarctica.

**诺谛卡**：不要前进！！\
**Nautika**: You mustn't go any further!

## 10TH-03 冰中苦旅 / An Icy Road

真正的恐怖发生在进入腹地的第三天，那一天，我们在白日看到了极光。\
The true horror happened on the third day, when we reached the hinterland. An aurora australis appeared in the sky in the broad daylight.

太阳耀斑伴随着日冕物质抛射，即便是在朗朗白日中，极光都闪耀得几乎能烧瞎人眼。\
Solar flares and the coronal mass ejections that came with them caused the aurora to appear so bright that it was almost blinding.

弗里莱提出渎神假设，她认为这次不正常的太阳运动是造物主发出的告诫，禁止我们继续深入。\
Friele saw it as a warning. She said that exploring the hinterland was a profanation of the Creator.

但考特却并没有放弃。他认为我们辛苦多日，用厚雪砖垒起的防风墙就是为了抵御所有未知的苦难。\
Koht, however, stood against her. He said that the snow brick windbreak we made would protect us and we couldn't let all those days of hard work be in vain.

可没有人意识到，真正的恐怖，来自脚下的深渊。\
No one knew that the real terror was beneath the snow, deep below our feet.

**队友Ⅰ**：六分仪的测算准确无误，只要我们一直沿着这个方向进发……\
**Team Member I**: The sextant was right. As long as we stick to this direction ...

**队友Ⅰ**：——唔、呜呜呜、唔！唔啊啊啊啊啊啊啊啊啊——！！！！！\
**Team Member I**: AAAAAGGGHHHH!!!!

第五天，埃德掉队了。\
Day 5. Eide has been left behind.

**队友Ⅱ**：现在情况紧急，一部分人的工作重点需要转移到重筑防风墙上。\
**Team Member II**: This is an emergency situation. We need some people to shift focus to rebuilding the windbreak.

**队友Ⅱ**：其他人专注修理通讯设备，尽早摆脱电磁干扰——把那些研究计划先放下！\
**Team Member II**: Those of you who're fixing the communication devices and getting rid of the EMI—drop it for now!

**队友Ⅱ**：……恶、恶魔……魔鬼……哈哈、哈哈哈！啊啊啊啊——！\
**Team Member II**: Devil! D-Demon! Hahahahahaha! AAAHHHHHHH!

第七天，出现了第二名牺牲者。考特的离开让我们陷入了更糟糕的处境……\
Day 7. Koht is gone. The situation is getting worse.

**队友Ⅲ**：这鬼地方终于向我们露出了它的爪牙，我从一开始就反对这么深入腹地，我们没有足够的经验——\
**Team Member III**: Finally, this damned place has shown its claws. I told you we shouldn't have headed so far into the hinterland! We're in way over our heads.

**队友Ⅲ**：再见了各位，我脑中的声音已经无法割舍，与我融为了一体……我会带走它……哈哈，我会亲自带走它！\
**Team Member III**: Farewell, everyone. There's no escaping it now. The voice in my head has become one with me, so, so let it end with me. Hahaha. Once I'm gone, it will be gone forever too.

**诺谛卡的日记**：第十天。\
**Nautika's Diary**: Day 10.

**诺谛卡的日记**：第十五天。\
**Nautika's Diary**: Day 15.

**诺谛卡的日记**：第二十三天。\
**Nautika's Diary**: Day 23.

第三十天，只剩我和弗里莱。\
Day 30. Everyone is gone. Only Friele and I have survived.

**队友Ⅳ**：没关系，不用担心，任何一条渔船都可以看到我们的求救信号，你只需要往回走，不要管我……\
**Team Member IV**: It's okay. Don't worry about me. Any passing fishing boat will be able to see our distress signal. You just need to go back and wait.

**队友Ⅳ**：给，这是我最爱的奈普顿巧克力，它能让你多暖一阵子。\
**Team Member IV**: Here. It's a Neptune bar—my favorite. It'll keep you warm a little longer.

探险家合上她的日记本。\
Nautika closes her diary.

**诺谛卡**：这就是为什么我不想让你们进入南极腹地……\
**Nautika**: That's why you cannot go to the hinterlands.

**诺谛卡**：我甚至、甚至希望你们最好尽快离开。\
**Nautika**: In fact, you-you should leave as soon as possible.

**十四行诗**：我了解了……原来这就是你的恐惧和顾虑……\
**Sonetto**: I see. So this is your concern.

**十四行诗**：但相信我，我们会留心自身的安全。所以哪怕是一份大概的地图，对于我们来说也是至关……\
**Sonetto**: But rest assured. We are taking every measure to ensure our safety. That said, even a draft map would be extremely helpful to us.

**维尔汀**：好，我们明白了。\
**Vertin**: Ah, I get it.

**十四行诗**：——司辰？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：请收下这台卫星定位系统，不需多时救援就会抵达。\
**Vertin**: Please take this GPS device. I've pinged its location. Help will arrive soon.

**维尔汀**：但由于时间紧迫，我们必须先行离开。请恕我们失陪。\
**Vertin**: My apologies that we can't stay with you until they arrive. I'm afraid we're on a time limit. Excuse us.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

**诺谛卡**：……为什么？\
**Nautika**: Why?

**诺谛卡**：为什么即使我已经这么警告过了，你们仍然要去南极腹地？\
**Nautika**: W-Why don't you give up, even after all my warnings?

**维尔汀**：我们有必须这么做的理由。\
**Vertin**: We have our reasons.

抬腿跨过门槛，呼啸的风雪砸在外衣衣角。\
Wind and snow batter their coats as the two step outside.

**诺谛卡**：等……等一下！\
**Nautika**: W-Wait!

幸存的探险家对着来访者的背影大喊，发泄一般倾泻着长久积累的惊慌与恐惧。\
Nautika, finding some hidden reserve of sanity and strength, shouts to her visitors.

**诺谛卡**：这片冰洲是活的！是有生命的，它会吃人——！这不是危言耸听！你们根本无法想象腹地的恐怖！\
**Nautika**: This land of ice is alive! It's alive, and it eats people! I'm not lying! You have no idea what horrors lie in the hinterland!

**诺谛卡**：即便成功逃脱也会精神崩溃，就像、就像……我的祖父罗夫一样——！！\
**Nautika**: Even if you somehow escape, you'll go insane! Just like—like Rolf, my grandfather!

向雪原离去的背影似乎放缓了些许步伐。\
The footsteps of those walking toward the snowfields slow.

**诺谛卡**：总、总而言之，你们不能走……\
**Nautika**: S-So, you have to stop! You have to! You have to ...

**诺谛卡**：至少为了你们自己的安全着想，不能再前进了——\
**Nautika**: For your own safety.

沉默中，喘息在天地间显得异常明晰。\
Breaths hang in the silence.

片刻的思索后，来访者的脚步缓缓调转而来。\
After a pause, they turn back.

**维尔汀**：罗夫·阿蒙森……？\
**Vertin**: Rolf Amundsen?

**维尔汀**：我听过这个名字。\
**Vertin**: I know that name.

**诺谛卡**：——什么？\
**Nautika**: What?

**维尔汀**：伟大的人类探险家。他的研究帮助发展了许多神秘学的应用技巧，无数神秘学家受益于此。\
**Vertin**: The outstanding human explorer. His research has formed the basis for understanding many applications of arcanum. Countless arcanists have benefited from his work.

**维尔汀**：你的家族相信造物主留下的古老未知，热爱一切神秘学相关的事物。\
**Vertin**: It's said that your family holds a particular set of beliefs about the unsolved mysteries of the world, and that every one of you holds a passion for arcanum.

诺谛卡低下头。\
Nautika looks down.

**诺谛卡**：我们、我们真的这么有名气吗？\
**Nautika**: Are-Are we that famous?

**维尔汀**：阿蒙森家族走出了许多探险家，这种纯粹而简单的热忱甚至被写进了神秘学家学校的教科书里。\
**Vertin**: Indeed. It's widely known that many members of the Amundsen family became explorers. Their passion was so strong that it's been recorded in arcanist textbooks.

诺谛卡惊讶地瞪大了眼睛，脸颊也因寒冷与激动而变得更红。\
Nautika's eyes widen, cheeks red from coldness and excitement.

**维尔汀**：你会出现在南极，一定也是和你的家人们一样，有着想要追寻的东西吧？\
**Vertin**: I assume you're here in pursuit of something, just like the rest of your family.

**维尔汀**：我猜，这就是即使在南极经历了诸多不幸，你也依然不愿离开的理由。\
**Vertin**: And that's why you're reluctant to leave, even after all the misfortune you've encountered. Is that right?

**诺谛卡**：我、我没有不愿意离开！我每天都祈祷着地母带我离开这个鬼地方……\
**Nautika**: Reluctant to leave? I pray to the Mother Spirit to take me away every single day.

**维尔汀**：这个科考站离海岸很近，你有无数种方式引起来往船只的注意。\
**Vertin**: This station is close to the shore. There are many ways you could've got the attention of passing ships if you'd wanted to.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

**维尔汀**：我们也是一样的。\
**Vertin**: We're also here in pursuit of something.

**维尔汀**：——我们要找一个人。\
**Vertin**: A person, to be specific.

探险家不解地瞪大了眼睛。\
Nautika's eyes widen again, this time with confusion.

**诺谛卡**：什么……？\
**Nautika**: A-A person?

一声叹息，回荡在小小的科考站内。\
A sigh echoes through the small station.

……你知道重塑之手吗？\
Are you familiar with Manus Vindictae?

黑暗的窟窖内，一个巨型法阵被鲜血与莎草燃尽后的粉尘刻印在地上。\
In a dark cavern, ritual symbols have been carved in a massive array drawn in blood and papyrus ash.

吼狮之尾，置于法阵的顶部。\
The Roar Lion's Tail is placed at the top.

千百万潮水，皆遵循潮汐奔流\
Tides run in blind by their ever-be routine,

圣甲虫双翼，置于法阵最左端。\
Sacred Scarab Wings at the left.

以亵渎不洁的姿态，玷污天幕\
Staining that Heaven with obscene calamity.

承载着魂声的心灵贝壳，镶嵌在头颅遗骨上，置于法阵最右端。\
A seashell holding a spirit is embedded in a skull at the right.

破除枷锁者，主宰一切的复苏之母\
The breaker of death's shackles shall rule us all,

从叛军者手中获得的黑色焦土，放置在圣像之上。\
Black soil from the rebels is placed above the idol.

以受反噬的炼金术士所炼制的不老泉浇祭。\
The Fountain of Youth elixir from a cursed alchemist completes the offering.

于今降下，至高福祉\
From this day forth, and evermore.

年轻的传道者站在祭坛边缘，遥望向远方的阴影。\
The young Preacher stands at the altar's edge, watching distant shadows.

她所期盼的身影穿过了狭长的甬道，踏入祭坛窖室内。\
The figure she awaits traverses the narrow passageway, entering the altar cavern at last.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：一如谕中，你抵达了这里。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: You've arrived, as the prophecy foretold.

目盲的女士，一手端着一杯豪麻汁，一手执着一束把森，赤足走来。\
A blind woman approaches barefoot—in one hand a cup of Hauma, in the other a bundle of Barsom.

最终，她停在了法阵空缺的唯一一角上，补全了最后的图形。\
Finally, she stops at the ritual's sole vacant corner, completing its shape.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：仪式的准备已经来到了最后的阶段。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The preparation of the ritual is about to enter its final stages.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：阿尔卡纳女士，我们的秘之教诲者已通过六音步诗向我传递祂最终的启示和神谕——\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The Inculcator of Arcanum, Lady Arcana, has revealed to me the final revelation and oracle. Hear ye:

**传道者·苏菲亚**：目盲的来客，将代为开启这一伟大的仪式。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The blind visitor shall start the great ritual on our behalf.

黑袍的信徒们向着目盲者屈膝，匍匐，持续吟诵着。\
The black-clad believers kneel and prostrate themselves before the blind woman, their chanting synchronized and unceasing.

目盲者虚空的目光仿佛穿越无尽时间，最终落在法阵的中央。\
Her sightless eyes seem to pierce through eternity before finally settling on the ritual's center.

一架金色的纺车静立于此，同她无声对望。\
There stands a golden Spinning Wheel, locked in silent communion with her.

## 10TH-04 引路人 / My Travel Companions

**十四行诗**：作为一个极端的纯血神秘主义组织，重塑之手行动隐秘，他们惯于在暗中搅乱世界秩序，以达成自己复兴神秘学的目的。\
**Sonetto**: Manus Vindictae is an extremist pure-blood arcanist organization. They used to act covertly to disrupt the world order in hopes of reviving arcanum.

**十四行诗**：但近一年中，他们变得活跃而高调，甚至不惜让普通人也戴上试炼的面具，疑似是为了快速吸纳更多信徒。\
**Sonetto**: However, in the last year, they've become much more active, even encouraging ordinary people to wear their masks and endure their trial. It's suspected that they went high-profile in order to quickly attract more believers.

**十四行诗**：结合我们的情报，基金会得出了重塑之手即将在南极举行一场重要仪式的结论。\
**Sonetto**: According to our intel, they'll hold an important ritual in Antarctica soon.

**维尔汀**：而我们要找的，也许是一位对于仪式来说至关重要的人物。\
**Vertin**: And we're searching for someone who may play a vital role in this ritual.

**诺谛卡**：神秘学家，面具……难道说，那些“疯雪怪”就是你们所说的重塑之手？\
**Nautika**: Arcanists, masks ... Are the Snow Monsters what you call Manus Vindictae?

探险家脸上出现不正常的激动。\
Nautika's words are marked with a strange excitement.

**诺谛卡**：——那、那你们说的仪式是什么意思？\
**Nautika**: W-What exactly is this ritual they're holding?

**十四行诗**：很遗憾，我们也尚未获取到更具体的细节情报，这也是这次任务的难点之一。\
**Sonetto**: Sadly, we don't have much information in that regard. We're hoping to figure it out on this mission.

**诺谛卡**：仪式……神秘学仪式……\
**Nautika**: Ritual ... Arcane ritual ...

**诺谛卡**：——等一下，这不就是我的研究课题之一吗！\
**Nautika**: Wait, wasn't that one of my research topics?

**诺谛卡**：画阵，摆饰祭品，通过一系列非功能性的行为召唤或降神……与“地母”沟通！\
**Nautika**: Draw the formation, place the offerings, and summon or invoke Her spirit through a series of actions to communicate with the Mother Spirit!

探险家激动地抬起头。\
She looks up with pure eagerness.

**诺谛卡**：或、或许你们听说过“地母”吗！！\
**Nautika**: D-Do you know of Her? Do you know the Mother Spirit?

**十四行诗**：……？\
**Sonetto**: ...?

**十四行诗**：我们……我们没有听说过。\
**Sonetto**: Um, sorry, no.

**诺谛卡**：——？没听说过……？\
**Nautika**: N-No?

**十四行诗**：……我想，事不宜迟，我们必须立刻动身了。\
**Sonetto**: Please excuse us, miss. We have to leave now.

**维尔汀**：对了，鉴于站点里的通讯设备已经无法使用……\
**Vertin**: Oh, and given that the communication equipment at this station isn't working ...

箱子的金属卡扣被再次打开，这次从里面钻出来的是一台头顶小花的方形无线电。\
The suitcase opens again, this time revealing a radio decorated with a flower.

**无线电小姐**：……阿、阿嚏--!\
**Ms. Radio**: Ah-Atishoo!

对南极气候还不足够适应的无线电小姐，颤悠悠地落在诺谛卡的手上。\
Ms. Radio shakes in Nautika's palm, struggling with the harsh shifts in the Antarctic temperature.

**维尔汀**：这是无线电小姐。她能够接收到救援队伍的通信频率。\
**Vertin**: May I introduce you to Ms. Radio? She'll receive the signal from the rescue team for you.

**十四行诗**：你可以暂时在这里等待救援。之前对你施展的温暖咒会一直生效。\
**Sonetto**: In the meantime, you may await their arrival here. The incantation keeping you warm will remain effective until then.

**十四行诗**：谢谢你的忠告，我们会更加小心的。\
**Sonetto**: And thank you for your advice. We will proceed with caution.

科考站摇摇欲坠的门被再度打开。\
The station's creaking door reopens.

……\
...

**无线电小姐**：你好，小探险家。你可以像司辰那样，直接称呼我为“无线电小姐”。\
**Ms. Radio**: Hello, little explorer. You can call me Ms. Radio, as the Timekeeper said.

**诺谛卡**：南极腹地，神秘学仪式，一个关键性的祭祀角色……\
**Nautika**: The heart of Antarctica, an arcane ritual, a vital role ...

**耳朵虫**：“引路人的出现转瞬即逝，虔诚者若已在路上，请吹响同路的歌谣。”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "The guide appears, then fades from human sight; If the devoted journey, let their songs unite."

**诺谛卡**：……该死，诺谛卡。\
**Nautika**: Damn it, Nautika.

**诺谛卡**：耳朵虫在给你传来“地母”的讯息，你可要好好听着。\
**Nautika**: Little Máhtu is reciting a message from the Mother Spirit Herself. Focus!

**耳朵虫**：“引路人的出现转瞬即逝，虔诚者若已在路上，请吹响同路的歌谣。”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "The guide appears, then fades from human sight; If the devoted journey, let their songs unite."

**无线电小姐**：呃……你好？你能听见我的声音吗？\
**Ms. Radio**: Um, hello? Can you hear me?

**诺谛卡**：你的课题、你的研究……\
**Nautika**: Your topic ... Your research ...

**维尔汀**：“你一定也是和你的家人们一样，有着想要追寻的东西吧？”\
**Vertin**: "I assume you're here in pursuit of something, just like the rest of your family."

**诺谛卡**：他们的梦想……你的梦想。\
**Nautika**: Their dream ... Your dream.

耳朵虫的声音戛然而止，探险家猛地站了起来。\
Máhtu's voice is snapped off as Nautika bolts to her feet.

**诺谛卡**：——这是你此生绝无仅有的机会！\
**Nautika**: This is the chance of a lifetime.

外来者的雪地靴在科考站外的雪地上踩下脚印。\
The visitors' boots are already cleaving a deep path through the snow outside the station.

门缓缓合上。\
The door closes heavily and slowly behind them.

**诺谛卡**：等等！\
**Nautika**: Wait!

门又被急躁地推开，探险家捧着无线电小姐冲出了科考站。\
The door swings open again as Nautika rushes out holding Ms. Radio.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

她有些战战兢兢地从口袋里掏出一张地图，迎风招展。\
Her hands tremble with excitement as she pulls a map from her pocket and struggles to unfold it in the wind.

一张皱巴巴的防水合成纸，红色的圆珠笔迹深深地刻印其上。\
A crumpled sheet of waterproof synthetic paper, bearing deep grooves with red ballpoint ink.

**诺谛卡**：这是我自己手绘的地图，虽然看起来很简陋……但现在它毋庸置疑是南极神话考古学的权威指南！\
**Nautika**: I-I drew this map myself. It's a draft, yes, but, well, in this situation, it is the authoritative guide on Antarctic mythological archaeology.

**诺谛卡**：它记录了我在南极遇见的一切，如何从站点抵达腹地、在途中会经过什么地标……以及腹地核心里那片类遗址建筑群周边的大致地貌。\
**Nautika**: I recorded everything I saw in Antarctica on it, see? Here's the route from the station to the hinterland. A-And here, the landmarks along the way. And this—I charted the topography around the ruins at the heart of Antarctica. Right here.

**十四行诗**：建筑群？你的意思是在南极大陆存在一处未被发掘的遗址？\
**Sonetto**: Ruins? You mean there's an undiscovered site in the heart of Antarctica?

**诺谛卡**：是的。它甚至从未在任何学术报告中出现过，这是我们队伍的全新发现！\
**Nautika**: Yes, exactly. It's never been recorded in any reports. It's a brand new discovery of our team.

结伴的两人对视了一眼。\
The two exchange glances.

**维尔汀**：“重塑之手”的藏身之处。\
**Vertin**: And Manus Vindictae's hiding place.

十四行诗点点头。\
Sonetto nods.

**维尔汀**：仪式很有可能会在那里举行。\
**Vertin**: It's highly possible that the ritual will be held there.

**诺谛卡**：不过……我们其实还没有真正对遗址展开过科考活动。队伍最深入的一次只抵达了外围，就因为恶劣天气而不得不中断了调查。\
**Nautika**: But, hmm, we've never entered the ruins. The closest we came was in its periphery, but the weather was too severe. We had to turn back.

**诺谛卡**：但、但如果耳朵虫说得没错，这次我们一定能顺利抵达！\
**Nautika**: But-But if Máhtu is right, we'll make it this time.

**十四行诗**：如果我没理解错的话，“我们”意味着……？\
**Sonetto**: And by "we," you mean ...?

**诺谛卡**：没错，如果不麻烦的话……可以带上我吗？\
**Nautika**: Well, if it's possible, would you mind taking me with you?

探险家颤抖地迈出阿德利企鹅的细碎步伐。\
Nautika takes a timid step, shuffling forward like a penguin.

**诺谛卡**：对啊，你、你们看，我一个人在这里等救援，还不如跟着你们一起……\
**Nautika**: You-You see, I could be in danger waiting here by myself. Why not just follow you and ...

探险家猛地吸了一口干冷的空气，声音再度战栗起来。\
She gulps a sharp breath of dry, cold air, and her voice quivers again.

**诺谛卡**：等一下，说起来……真的有后援在赶来的路上吗？\
**Nautika**: And, wait a minute. Is there really a rescue team on the way?

……与此同时\
Meanwhile ...

一艘小型纵帆船驶入冰海。\
A small schooner enters icy waters.

磁流体不稳定地抖动着，它一手持通讯器，一手不耐烦地敲着舷窗。\
Ulrich's ferrofluid moves erratically. He grips a communicator in one hand while impatiently tapping the porthole with the other.

**乌尔里希**：没错，我们曾非常艰难地验证过“星锑”在“暴雨”中的稳定性，但我们还没有完成所有实验，这就是问题所在。\
**Ulrich**: Yes, we've tested the stability of the "Regulus" record in the "Storm" the hard way. But there are still some experiments to be completed, and that is a problem.

**乌尔里希**：它就像是一个巨型婴儿，刚刚学会爬行，但如果要一跃成为马拉松冠军，那还差着相当大的距离！\
**Ulrich**: Our study is like a baby who's just started to crawl. It's making moves, yes, but isn't exactly going to win a marathon anytime soon.

**乌尔里希**：这就是为什么需要你留在实验室，你最了解“人工暴雨”实验，你有足够的能力保证我们的工作继续进行下去。\
**Ulrich**: That's why we need you to stay in the lab. You have the greatest knowledge of the "Artificial Storm." You're more than capable of continuing the work on your own.

……

**乌尔里希**：……是的，是的，我知道你想要见到司辰，想要和她一起进行你们的跨世纪摇滚探险。\
**Ulrich**: Yes, yes, I know how much you wanna see the Timekeeper and embark on your "cross-century rock expedition."

**乌尔里希**：但南极实验并不是任何一场表演，它是一次豪赌，赌的就是我们此前的所有假设是否真的成立。\
**Ulrich**: But the experiment in Antarctica isn't one of your concerts. It's a gamble, and we're betting every hypothesis on it.

**乌尔里希**：如果“星锑”，也就是你的唱片，确实如我们所预想的，是人为控制“暴雨”及暴雨症候群的关键。\
**Ulrich**: If "Regulus," that is, your record, is in fact the key to artificially controlling the "Storm" and its Syndrome as we suspect ...

**乌尔里希**：那么它至少能在此次南极行动中成为司辰的后援，预防最差的情况发生。\
**Ulrich**: I hope it can at least serve as the Timekeeper's backup plan in this Antarctic operation should the worst happen.

**乌尔里希**：我带着它前来实验并进行支援，而你留在拉普拉斯继续研究“人工暴雨”。这是我们和司辰约定好的。\
**Ulrich**: You know the agreement we made with her. I take the "Regulus" record for experimentation and support, and you stay in Laplace to work on the "Artificial Storm."

磁流体将挂在身上的唱片往里掖了掖。\
He adjusts the record to fit snugly and securely under his arm.

同其原主人跨越多场“暴雨”，这张唱片仍边角如新。\
Even after surviving multiple "Storms" with its former owner, the record remains good as new.

**护卫兵**：……老板，我们好像已经驶入了大陆架范围。要是这段长距离通讯信号被敌人捕捉，这场行动就会被宣告失败……\
**Guard**: Boss, we've entered the continental shelf. If Manus Vindictae picks up our long-distance comm signal, this operation will be declared a failure.

斜坐在一旁的护卫兵小声提醒，嘴里还嚼着巧克力口味军粮。\
A guard chewing chocolate-flavored rations mutters out a warning.

远方传来一声震耳的鸣笛声。\
A deafening horn blast echoes in the distance.

护卫兵踱步上了甲板，看向海平面。\
Hearing this, the guard exits her casual slouch and moves onto the deck, scanning the horizon.

**护卫兵**：噢……我们和基金会的舰队算是打上招呼了。

**护卫兵**：噢……我们和基金会的舰队算是打上招呼了。\
**Guard**: Oh, we've finally met the Foundation's fleet.

**乌尔里希**：嗯——？\
**Ulrich**: What?

黑影漫过沸腾的海面。\
A dark shadow cloaks the heaving waters.

刚挂断通讯的磁流体抬起脑袋。\
Ulrich looks up from his communicator.

**乌尔里希**：什么……\
**Ulrich**: What on earth ...

螺旋桨飞速地搅动海面，燃油的味道充斥鼻腔。\
The propellers spin fast against the swelling sea. The distinct aroma of burning diesel hits the air.

**乌尔里希**：这是……？\
**Ulrich**: Is that ...?

站在帆船船头的水手回过头来。\
At the front of the schooner, a sailor turns his face.

**水手**：“迪达号”驱逐舰和“特里格拉夫”战列舰。\
**Sailor**: Ha! "Triglav" the battleship, and "Dida" the destroyer.

**水手**：从堪察加彼得罗巴甫洛夫斯克出发，跨越整个地球，目前已经向着南极洲发起最后的冲刺。\
**Sailor**: Are they deployed from Petropavlovsk-Kamchatsky, ha! Traveled halfway across the world to get here. Looks like they're finally on the last stretch to Antarctica.

**护卫兵**：不是吧……从北边调来的？\
**Guard**: From the north? Surely not.

**水手**：没错，看来刻雷乌斯长官已经和芝诺的索姆将军达成了合作——\
**Sailor**: That's right. Seems that Commander Creius and Admiral Somme have struck a deal.

巡逻鱼雷在百米外炸响，伴随着诡异的兽啼，海面掀起巨大的浪花。\
A torpedo explodes a hundred meters away. A strange, animal-like scream is heard as waves splash over it.

**护卫兵**：抓紧了！正在调整船帆角度！……这，这之前可没人告诉我得突入正面战场啊——\
**Guard**: Hold on! Adjusting the sail angle. Damn it, no one told me we'd be fighting on the front bloody line.

**水手**：那是进行过武装改造的马格努斯巨兽，想不到重塑用这种怪物作为他们的第一道防线。\
**Sailor**: It's one of them armed Magnus beasts that the Manus modified. Didn't expect their first line of defense to be an actual monster.

**水手**：芝诺精锐的远征军，对上重塑在多次穿越“暴雨”中集结的所有力量打造的防线……\
**Sailor**: Zeno's elite expeditionary force versus the army Manus Vindictae has gathered across multiple "Storms" ...

**水手**：这可真会是一场恶战了！\
**Sailor**: This is gonna be a right hell of a fight.

**护卫兵**：……为什么他这么兴奋……快一起来掌舵啊！\
**Guard**: What is he so excited about? Come on, help me at the helm.

随着最后一声巨响沉入海底，惊声嘶叫的马格努斯潜艇迅速摆尾潜入水下。\
After one last loud boom, the shrieking Magnus submarine quickly dives underwater.

很快，铺满浮冰的大海被染成血红色。\
Soon, the icy ocean turns blood red.

一道波纹划开血色的海面，向着舰队疾驰而去。\
A line cuts through the crimson water, moving fast toward the fleet.

**舰长Ⅰ**：135T，准备二次交火。舰桥准备——\
**Captain I**: 135T, prepare to engage. Bridge ready.

士兵们操纵着冰洋上的战舰，通讯里不断传来简洁且有序的回应。\
Warships maneuver over the icy sea. Relays of orders and replies come staccato and clear over the radio.

炮管缓缓调转方向，炮弹的落点被设定在了六点钟方向的海面。\
The guns inch into position, aiming to hit the water at six o'clock.

**舰长Ⅰ**：我不认为他们的液态金属反应堆能抵挡65-76型鱼雷和空中火力覆盖。\
**Captain I**: Let's see if their liquid metal reactor can resist Type 65-76 torpedoes and our aerial firepower.

**舰长Ⅰ**：进攻！\
**Captain I**: Attack!

## 10TH-05 布鲁图斯在呢喃 / Et tu, Brute?

“嗖——”\
*whoosh*

一支铅制的细箭直戳入胆囊中，胆汁四溅，血肉模糊。\
A thin lead arrow hits a gallbladder, spilling bile and blood.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……接近半数……\
**Ms. Grace**: Nearly half ...

年轻的使徒脸色苍白，气若游丝。\
The young Apostle grows pale, her breath faint as a whisper.

**？？？**：什么？\
**???**: What?

**淑女格蕾丝**：……接近半数的马格努斯潜艇已沉没。\
**Ms. Grace**: Nearly half of the Magnus submarines have been sunk.

**？？？**：大声一点。\
**???**: Speak up.

**？？？**：拿掉你那矜贵的做派，“淑女”。我不是那些需要你惺惺作态拉拢的蠢货。\
**???**: Drop your pompous little act, girl. You'll win no favor with me through airs and graces.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……\
**Ms. Grace**: ...

**淑女格蕾丝**：接近半数的马格努斯潜艇已沉没。\
**Ms. Grace**: Nearly half of the Magnus submarines have been sunk.

**？？？**：这才像话！\
**???**: That's more like it.

铅制的箭头重新对准另一个标靶。\
The lead arrowhead finds another target.

**？？？**：终于——迂腐的白家伙终于拿出了一点动真格的反应……谢天谢地。\
**???**: At last, those white-clad fools have levied some retaliation. How kind of them to finally join us.

一箭射出。\
Another arrow is fired.

冻紫的溃肉流出臭烂的脂肪。\
Frostbitten flesh splits open, oozing rancid fat.

**？？？**：——若非如此，所有人都要匍匐在那位“传道者”的脚边，为她的“无所不能”所倾倒了。\
**???**: I am loath to witness any more groveling at the feet of that "Preacher" and her so-called "omnipotence."

年迈的步伐拖着素色布缎走向标靶。\
An elder shuffles forward in plain robes.

**？？？**：“神秘岛屿的优秀除错师”“秘之教诲者沉睡后唯一的领导者”“伟大仪式的最高主持者”……\
**???**: The great "Corrector" of the mysterious island, the "One and Only Leader" in the face of the slumbering Inculcator of Arcanum, the "Supreme Caster of the Great Ritual" …

“噗嗤——”\
*squelch*

禽类头骨中镶嵌的晶状球体被捏碎成泥。\
The orb in the avian skull crumbles under the pressure.

**阿尼姆斯**：只不过是错误的人出现在了对的时机。\
**Animus**: She was nothing but the wrong person at the right time.

**阿尼姆斯**：能听到秘之教诲者的声音？呵！编造出这样的谎言，使得所有人都相信她，臣服她……\
**Animus**: She alone hears the voice of the Inculcator of Arcanum? Ha! What blatant lies! Yet they submit to her all the same, every one.

**阿尼姆斯**：有些人守在后方圣地统筹仪式所需的一切，有些人却全世界“布道”。人心、权力都被她握在手里，出尽风头。\
**Animus**: While she gallivanted around the world, "preaching" on the back of her falsities, who was it who prepared for the ritual, hm? Yet she alone is granted power. She alone holds their hearts in her hands. Ridiculous!

**阿尼姆斯**：物资运输、人员调配，甚至重塑伟大的历史……一个新上任的小姑娘能了解多少？没有我的帮助，她什么也不是。\
**Animus**: What does a little girl know about material transportation or personnel arrangement, let alone the great history of the Manus? She is nothing without me.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……\
**Ms. Grace**: ...

**阿尼姆斯**：噢，我不是在说你。但你最好也夹紧尾巴……\
**Animus**: *sharp exhale* It is not you to whom I refer, girl. But you'd better keep that tail firmly planted between your legs.

**阿尼姆斯**：虽然你带来了重要的仪式材料，但“自由海风号”上的事闹出了太大动静，现在全世界的目光都聚在南半球，这都要拜你所赐。\
**Animus**: Your actions aboard the "Free Breeze" have garnered much attention—attention that could easily have been avoided. Now, the whole world has their sights set on the Southern Hemisphere, and it's all thanks to you. No amount of ritual materials can make up for that.

**阿尼姆斯**：我从最开始就不支持将权力交给你们这些毫无根基之人。自大，冒进，不知收敛。\
**Animus**: This is precisely why I was against giving power to you infantiles in the first place. Arrogant, reckless fools—there's not an ounce of self-control to share among you.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……\
**Ms. Grace**: ...

**淑女格蕾丝**：基金会的军队马上要突破第一道防线了，如果再长驱直入——\
**Ms. Grace**: The Foundation's army will break through our first line of defense soon. If we don't stop them—

**阿尼姆斯**：他们不会一直保持这样的势头。\
**Animus**: Their advance will be halted.

话头被粗暴地打断。\
Words falter mid-sentence.

**阿尼姆斯**：南极不是他们该来的地方，再派多少铁家伙也是一样。现在才举兵进攻，不过是为了证明自己并非全无计划罢了。\
**Animus**: Antarctica is no place for them, no matter how many machines they send. Their war efforts have been naught but the desperate attempt to prove to themselves that they are not utterly without plan. Pathetic, as usual.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……您说的没错，我们无需费心关注注定溃败的蝼蚁。\
**Ms. Grace**: You're right. There's no need to concern ourselves with the insects scurrying beneath our boots.

**淑女格蕾丝**：作为仪式外围应援的我们，眼下必须着眼于让仪式顺利进行……\
**Ms. Grace**: Our role is to support from the outside to ensure the ritual proceeds smoothly. That's all.

**阿尼姆斯**：你那浅薄的眼里一次只能看见一件事吗？你如何能保证我们的内部是滴水不漏的？\
**Animus**: What driver straps the blinders to your face, hmm? Or were you simply born unable to perform more than one task at a time? Tell me, how do you ensure the safety of the interior?

年轻使徒的呼吸变得更轻，她竭尽全力让自己显得更加谦卑。\
The young Apostle allows her breathing to grow fainter, struggling to keep the absolute appearance of humility.

**淑女格蕾丝**：您是指……？\
**Ms. Grace**: I'm not sure what you mean.

**阿尼姆斯**：那位将军的近卫团动向如何？\
**Animus**: The admiral's Sentinel Unit. What is its status?

**淑女格蕾丝**：伊戈尔军？他们已经在海岸多处建起了防线，目前正在警戒可能出现的基金会游兵。\
**Ms. Grace**: Igor's unit? They've set up defenses in multiple locations along the coast. They're on high alert for possible Foundation partisans.

**阿尼姆斯**：可笑的墙头草，如何能够侍奉吾辈伟大的复苏之母？\
**Animus**: The fence-sitters. How could they possibly serve our great Mother of Resurrection?

**阿尼姆斯**：将那些人安插在圣地之上，本身就是一种侮辱和背叛！\
**Animus**: It's an insult that they were ever allowed to set foot on the holy land at all!

**淑女格蕾丝**：但传道者对他们表示出了极高的尊重，何况，他们为仪式带来了最关键的……\
**Ms. Grace**: But the Preacher has treated them with the utmost respect. They did bring the key to the ritual after all.

**阿尼姆斯**：愚钝！\
**Animus**: Utter foolishness!

**阿尼姆斯**：他们甚至不愿意接受神圣的试炼。\
**Animus**: Those heathens are not even willing to undergo the holy trial.

**阿尼姆斯**：与一群未受祝福与引导的庸人为伍，是重塑之手自立于世间以来最大的耻辱。\
**Animus**: Standing among these unblessed, unguided simpletons is the greatest humiliation to befall Manus Vindictae since its inception.

**淑女格蕾丝**：……\
**Ms. Grace**: ...

**阿尼姆斯**：罢了。\
**Animus**: Ugh. Despite this …

**阿尼姆斯**：一切以仪式为重。\
**Animus**: It is of little matter in the face of the ritual.

**阿尼姆斯**：一切——以伟大的复苏之母为重。\
**Animus**: The Great Mother of Resurrection … That is our only goal.

禽类可怜的残骸被扔在了年轻使徒的脚边。\
The pitiful remains of the bird are flung at her feet.

营帐已经扎下，但疲乏仍未消退。\
The tents are pitched, yet exhaustion lingers like frost on a cold morning.

机长从直升飞机里探出半个身子，对着帐篷前的女士摇了摇头。

机长从直升飞机里探出半个身子，对着帐篷前的女士摇了摇头。\
The aircraft captain leans out, shaking his head toward a woman standing before one such tent.

**机长**：已经执行过一次检查程序了，中尉，最大的问题出在脚蹬上。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Lieutenant, we have run the checking program. The problem is with the pedal.

**机长**：由于未知原因，脚蹬控制的偏航角速率未能达到设定的预期。\
**Aircraft Captain**: It's malfunctioning, which is somehow deviating the set yaw rate.

**机长**：这就是刚才飞行过程中出现了强烈颠簸和航向偏转的原因。\
**Aircraft Captain**: That is why we had such severe turbulence and deviation just now.

**机长**：在得到一次充分完整的检修前，“小犬号”是不适宜再起飞了，特别是在南极这么恶劣的环境下。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I suggest we do not fly Canis Minor until we have done a complete overhaul. The weather is just too extreme in Antarctica.

莫莉德尔回头看了一眼已经安置下的士兵，走向了这架载量二十人的运输直升机。\
Moldir takes stock of her soldiers, then makes a confident stride toward the transport helicopter.

**莫莉德尔**：向将军报告我们的情况……虽然距离指定的驻扎地还有些距离，但目前看来只能这样了。\
**Moldir**: Report to the Admiral. We are still some way away from our designated station, but it seems we have no other choice for now.

**莫莉德尔**：所幸这片空地同样有开阔的视野，足够我们执行任务……你完成了一次完美的迫降，辛苦了，丹尼洛夫。\
**Moldir**: At least we landed in a place with enough space and sightlines to perform our task. This is the best we could have done given the situation. Well done, Danilov.

**机长**：这是我应该做的，中尉。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Of course, Lieutenant.

**莫莉德尔**：接下来要做的，只有等待。\
**Moldir**: Now all there is to do is wait.

等待什么？\
Wait for what?

答案呼之欲出。\
The answer is about to be set free.

**莫莉德尔**：全体注意，以下是自伊戈尔将军的指令。\
**Moldir**: Attention! We have an order from Admiral Igor.

**莫莉德尔**：我们需要在这里坚守冰洲的外围防线，以应对基金会的任何进攻。\
**Moldir**: We are the perimeter defense of Antarctica. We must be ready for any possible attack from the Foundation.

**莫莉德尔**：同驻扎在另外一个港口的托勒密步兵班一起，由坐守仪式神殿的将军下达机动调令。\
**Moldir**: The Admiral is stationed in the sanctuary. From there, he will administer orders to both us and Ptolemy's infantry squad at the other port.

莫莉德尔调整了一下领口，她感到口干。\
Moldir adjusts her collar, her mouth dry.

**莫莉德尔**：一旦发现任何单位进入可视范围内的海域，一律视为交火信号。\
**Moldir**: Any unit entering the sea within visual range is to be considered a signal to engage, understood?

**众士兵**：是——！\
**Soldiers**: Yes, ma'am!

士兵们齐声回应。\
The soldiers respond in a disciplined harmony.

她扫视士兵一圈，而后低下头。\
She scans the ranks, then lowers her head.

看着自己浸湿的军靴上迷人的金色落雪，她眨了眨眼。\
Blinking, she finds herself mesmerized by the strange, golden flurry dusting her combat boots.

## 10TH-06 一路平安 / Safe Driving

**十四行诗**：司辰，你确定我们的方向正确吗？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, are you sure this is the right direction?

**诺谛卡**：请相信我的记忆和地图，十四行诗小姐，遗迹就是这个方向。\
**Nautika**: Please trust me and my map. This is the way to the ruins. I promise.

**维尔汀**：为了追上德洛丝医生，我要加速了。请坐稳，各位。\
**Vertin**: We need to catch up with Dr. Dores as soon as possible. Hold on tight, everyone. I'm going to speed up.

**无线电小姐**：请……请您慢、慢一点开吧——！！！\
**Ms. Radio**: Please slow down! Just a lit—AAAH!

蓝色的小花在风中疯狂摇曳，努力地朝避风的方向生长。\
Tiny blue flower shakes wildly in the wind, straining to grow toward the sheltered side.

雪地摩托飞驰在冰原上，驾驶者神色自若。\
The snowmobile races across the frozen plain, its driver's face composed and certain.

乘客却无一不瞪大了眼。\
Yet her passengers' eyes widen.

**诺谛卡**：真不愧是神秘学家……！这台带雪佛兰保险杠的最新型号，我们当初研究了好久，最终只有弗里莱能开——\
**Nautika**: Wow, incredible! You really are an arcanist! We couldn't figure out how this thing worked—the new model with the Chevrolet bumper. Only Friele was able to drive it.

**诺谛卡**：没想到您一上车就掌握了！这就是基金会对神秘学家的培养吗，不仅是神秘术，甚至还教授了人类的科技成果……\
**Nautika**: But you, you knew how to drive it as soon as you touched the handle. Are you trained to use human technology at the Foundation too?

**诺谛卡**：这无疑对于我研究神秘学家的生活提供了最、最好的案例支持！\
**Nautika**: If you are, it would be a huge case support to my study on arcanist lifestyles.

**十四行诗**：事实上，诺谛卡小姐，司辰她……并无驾驶经验……\
**Sonetto**: The truth is, Ms. Amundsen, the Timekeeper has never driven before.

世界在身侧飞速穿行后退，恐慌爬上了后座乘客的脸。\
As the world streaks past in a blur, panic creeps onto the backseat passenger's face.

**诺谛卡**：你——说——什么——？！\
**Nautika**: WHAT DID YOU SAY?

**维尔汀**：不用担心，我通常是安全驾驶的拥护者。\
**Vertin**: Don't worry. I'm generally a proponent of safe driving.

**诺谛卡**：——通、通常？！\
**Nautika**: G-GENERALLY?

**维尔汀**：前面那些雪堆是……？\
**Vertin**: What are those snowdrifts ahead?

**诺谛卡**：是、是喷气冰塔啊啊啊啊啊！！快刹车——\
**Nautika**: Fumarolic ice towers. Pull over!

**十四行诗**：急急旋转停！\
**Sonetto**: Stŭpĕo Swift!

**无线电小姐**：……\
**Ms. Radio**: ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**十四行诗**：呼……还好摩托的损坏并不算严重。诺谛卡小姐，前面还能走吗？\
**Sonetto**: Phew. Thankfully, the vehicle isn't badly damaged. Ms. Amundsen, are there any other obstacles ahead that we should know about?

**诺谛卡**：好奇怪……地图上显示这儿明明是个开阔平原……\
**Nautika**: That's strange. This should be an open plain.

探险家将望远镜从眼前放下，疑惑地嘟囔着。\
Nautika lowers her binoculars, muttering in confusion.

**诺谛卡**：——！\
**Nautika**: ...!

险些被脚边的小冰柱绊倒，探险家快速后退了几步。\
She stumbles backward as her feet slip over an outcropping of ice.

**诺谛卡**：这、这这里……不适合摩托通行，我们最好绕一下路——\
**Nautika**: We should take a detour. This place isn't suitable for snowmobiles.

**诺谛卡**：——呃啊！\
**Nautika**: Ah!

诺谛卡终于被脚边再次喷出的蒸气绊了一跤，坐在了地上。\
Where the ice had failed, a burst of steam succeeds in sending her sprawling back onto the ground.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐！你没事吧？\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen, are you okay?

**诺谛卡**：我……我没事、没——\
**Nautika**: I'm fine. I'm alright.

逞强的话说不下去了，她面色僵硬地仔细吸了吸鼻子。\
Her tough talk dies on her lips. She sniffs the air, her face stiffening.

**诺谛卡**：是我的嗅觉神经失灵了吗，还是说咱们带的干粮腐烂了——？\
**Nautika**: Has my nose gone wrong? Or are we carrying rotten food?

浓烈的味道开始蔓延。\
The pungent odor is not an illusion. It's begun to spread all around them.

**诺谛卡**：你、你们有没有闻到一股……味道？就、就像……夏天里放坏了的麋鹿肉。\
**Nautika**: Do you smell that smell? It smells like, hmm, rotten reindeer meat.

**十四行诗**：蛋白质被微生物消化、分解后散发出来的酸臭。\
**Sonetto**: It's the sour odor of protein being digested and broken down by microbes.

**十四行诗**：这些气味间歇性变得浓郁，又随着时间和吹来的风渐渐消散……\
**Sonetto**: It seems to be coming in waves. First it's pungent, then it gets carried away on the wind.

**十四行诗**：是这些冰柱喷出来的。\
**Sonetto**: It must be coming from the ice towers.

第一助手俯下身，仔细观察起了喷气的冰柱。\
Sonetto crouches, examining the hissing ice formation.

**维尔汀**：说起来，这些冰塔是？\
**Vertin**: What are these towers, exactly?

**诺谛卡**：岩浆流动时，热气穿过狭窄的地壳裂缝冲到地面上，遇到寒冷空气后形成了这种空心冰塔。\
**Nautika**: When there's magma beneath the surface, hot gas escapes through narrow cracks in the crust. When it meets the cold air, it vaporizes and forms hollow towers.

**诺谛卡**：所以一般来说，喷气冰塔只会出现在火山活动区……可这里明明是一片雪原。\
**Nautika**: They're often seen around volcanoes, hmm, but there's no volcano here.

探险家蹲在地上，颤抖着采集起了喷气口边缘结块的物质。\
Crouching on the ground, Nautika's fingers gather crusted deposits from the vent's rim.

**诺谛卡**：呜……好臭……\
**Nautika**: Ugh. It's so stinky.

**诺谛卡**：火山气体中的确存在二氧化硫之类刺鼻的成分，但绝不是这种酸臭味，味道也不该这么重……\
**Nautika**: The sulfur dioxide in lava does have a strong smell, but it's not as sour and smelly as this.

**诺谛卡**：而且……\
**Nautika**: Hmm, besides ...

随着探险家越来越快的分析，豆大的汗珠从她额头坠落，她打了个颤。\
She begins an analysis at breakneck speed. Beads of sweat roll down her forehead as she shudders involuntarily.

**诺谛卡**：我上一次和队员们……并没有遇上这些冰塔。\
**Nautika**: The last time my team and I were here, these towers weren't.

**诺谛卡**：上次来这儿是不足百日前的事，它们、它们不应该形成得这么快。\
**Nautika**: That was less than 100 days ago. They—They shouldn't have formed so quickly.

**诺谛卡**：我从没见过这么密集矮小的冰塔……它们一个个立在这里，和蜂窝巢一样密密麻麻的……\
**Nautika**: And I've never seen towers like these before. They're so ... so short and close together, like a beehive.

**诺谛卡**：它们就像……\
**Nautika**: It's almost like ...

**诺谛卡**：就像大陆的毛孔一样……\
**Nautika**: ... like they're the pores of the continent.

探险家说着不自觉地往第一助手身后靠了靠。\
She unconsciously edges behind Sonetto for protection.

**维尔汀**：这些冰塔的内部是温热的。\
**Vertin**: They're warm on the inside.

**十四行诗**：温热的？\
**Sonetto**: Warm?

第一助手抬起手也准备触摸，自己都没留意指尖已经开始颤抖。\
Sonetto raises a hand to examine the sample, not noticing her own fingertips have begun to tremble.

“轰——”\
*boom*

毫无预兆地，身旁最近的冰塔喷出了数米高的酸臭气流。\
Without warning, the nearest ice tower erupts. A geyser of foul-smelling vapor blasting several meters skyward.

**无线电小姐**：呃——！\
**Ms. Radio**: Ugh!

无线电小姐被吹翻，一头扎进深深的雪地里。\
Ms. Radio is blown over, plunging deep into the snowbank.

**无线电小姐**：□■□△！我精心养护的小植物可没有办法承受这样的撞击……\
**Ms. Radio**: □■□△! Don't hurt my precious flower!

小小的抱怨却被一旁颤抖的惊呼打断。\
Her muttered complaint is cut short by a panicked shriek nearby.

**诺谛卡**：啊、啊……\
**Nautika**: Ah!

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀……十四行诗……你们看、看——\
**Nautika**: Vertin, Sonetto, look ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**十四行诗**：这是……？！\
**Sonetto**: What is that?

**诺谛卡**：这是刚刚从冰塔里被喷出来的……\
指甲？\
**Nautika**: *squeal* A nail. It just sputtered out of the tower.

探险家的声音比刚才提高了一个八度，细软而略带颤抖。她几乎要瘫坐在地上。\
Her voice jumps an octave higher—thin, soft, and wavering, as her legs buckle to the same tune.

**十四行诗**：呜……！\
**Sonetto**: Uh!

**维尔汀**：……至少，我们能确定这附近有人烟。或者说“曾经有”。\
**Vertin**: At least now we can be sure that there are people around here, or there "were."

**维尔汀**：再往前探索看看吧。\
**Vertin**: Let's head further in.

雪浪之上仍有雪浪，陡峭的波状雪脊向远处无限延伸。\
Wave upon wave of snow stretches out beyond them, steep-ridged formations vanishing into the distance.

一深一浅地攀登后，她们站在了雪浪高处。\
After struggling up the shifting slopes, they finally stand atop the snow waves.

**十四行诗**：司辰，你看那边……\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, over there.

血迹斑驳，红色在白色大地上显得尤为醒目。\
Bloodstains bloom across the white expanse, crimson glaring against the snow.

一座大型科考站。\
A massive research station looms ahead.

鲜血被粗暴地涂抹在大门上，昭示着这里曾发生的惨剧。\
Blood has been smeared over its doors in violent streaks—a grotesque testament to the tragedy within.

**维尔汀**：过去看看。\
**Vertin**: Let's take a look.

**诺谛卡**：维、维尔汀……\
**Nautika**: Vertin ...

**维尔汀**：怎么了？\
**Vertin**: Yes?

**诺谛卡**：……我、我就……不去——了吧……\
**Nautika**: I ... I can't go.

拒绝前进的请求最终被自己吞下。\
Her refusal dies half-spoken in her throat.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: *mumbling*

诺谛卡咬紧牙关，惶惶然迈出脚步。\
Nautika clenches her jaw tight against the shivers of both panic and cold and takes a step forward.

想要绕过血迹和倾倒的保温墙板走进黑暗并不容易。\
Picking one's way past bloodstains and toppled insulation panels into the darkness proves difficult.

**十四行诗**：相当大型的站点……厨房、独立卧室、生物实验室，甚至还有独立的日照模拟室。\
**Sonetto**: This is a large station. They have a kitchen, separate bedrooms, a bio laboratory, and a daylight simulation room.

**十四行诗**：但从这一片狼藉来看——这里已经没有人了。\
**Sonetto**: But judging by the mess, it's been abandoned.

**十四行诗**：——？！\
**Sonetto**: ...?!

**维尔汀**：地上这些黏糊糊的东西是……\
**Vertin**: What's this sticky substance on the ground?

**诺谛卡**：是黑藻，这座站点里居然长了这么多……小心些，踩在上面很容易摔倒。\
**Nautika**: It's black algae. There's so much of it here. Watch your step. It could be slippery.

探寻还在继续。\
The search continues.

**十四行诗**：桌椅上留有神秘术的痕迹……\
**Sonetto**: There are arcane fluctuation traces on the desks and chairs.

**十四行诗**：司辰，你看那里——\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, look over there.

顺着手指方向看去，屋内幽邃的尽头，有一丝闪烁的微光。\
Following her pointed finger, deep in the shadowed interior, a faint glimmer pulses.

**维尔汀**：请问有人在吗？\
**Vertin**: Excuse me, is anybody there?

**十四行诗**：您好，我们想问一下路——\
**Sonetto**: Hello, we're here to ask for help.

**诺谛卡**：别、别过去了吧……\
**Nautika**: I-I don't think we should go any further.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗——\
**Vertin**: Sonetto—

同伴的声音突然从隔壁房间响起。\
Her teammate's voice rings out from the adjacent room.

**十四行诗**：怎么了？司……\
**Sonetto**: Yes? Timekeep—

未出口的话落在了地上。\
Unfinished words fall to the ground like wet sand.

已经难以区分是“人类”还是“羔羊”。\
It's impossible to tell whether what is left is a human or a lamb.

帐篷地钉穿过掌心，把他高高钉在了储藏间的墙壁上。\
A tent stake pierces his palm, pinning it high on the storage room wall.

极地寒风从探险家们的脚边穿过，灌进房间，让遗骸的双足踢翻了落灰的罐头。\
The arctic wind slips between the explorers' boots, rushing into the room—the corpse's frozen feet kick out over dust-covered cans.

血在极度的干燥环境中脱水成了碎屑，风一吹过，就像雪一样簌簌飘落下来。\
Dried blood has crumbled into flakes in the hyper-arid air, scattering like snow when the wind stirs.

**十四行诗**：他……已经死去很久了……\
**Sonetto**: He's been dead for quite some time.

**维尔汀**：这个人的额头被刻上了某种怪异的标记。\
**Vertin**: There's an odd mark carved into his forehead.

**十四行诗**：而且他的指甲……全部被剥离了。\
**Sonetto**: Look at his hands. His nails have been pulled off.

沉默在三人中化开。\
Silence falls over the three.

**诺谛卡**：就、就像一种献祭……\
**Nautika**: It's like ... like some kind of sacrifice.

**诺谛卡**：在某些信仰文化中，充满角蛋白的人体结缔组织是某种不洁的存在……哕！\
**Nautika**: Some cultures believe the connective tissues containing keratin are unclean ...

似乎终于无法忍受，她蹲下身子干呕起来。\
Overwhelmed by the horror of the sight, she drops to her knees and retches violently.

**诺谛卡**：别、别闹，小耳朵虫，这只是一具尸体，这样的场景你见过很、很多……不是吗？\
**Nautika**: Stop it, Máhtu. It's just a corpse. It's—It's not the first time you've seen one. It's not the first time.

探险家双手颤抖，她捧着自己的头，自顾自地疯狂甩动起来。\
Her hands are trembling as she clutches at her head.

**维尔汀**：还有一处奇怪的地方。他的伤口边缘有棕色的药粉，地上还有用过的纱布……\
**Vertin**: Something else is off. There's gauze on the floor and brown powder around his wound.

**维尔汀**：有人曾尝试过对他进行急救。\
**Vertin**: Looks like somebody gave him first aid.

**十四行诗**：司辰，你看他脖子上挂着的是什么？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, look. What's that hanging around his neck?

**维尔汀**：……一个听诊器？\
**Vertin**: A stethoscope?

**十四行诗**：听诊器管路上有少许折痕，但整体看起来很新，被主人保养得很好。\
**Sonetto**: Aside from a few creases on the tubing, it looks rather new or at least well-kept.

**十四行诗**：死者难道是一名医生吗？\
**Sonetto**: Do you think he was a doctor?

**维尔汀**：听诊器压着的血迹是完整的，它是之后才被挂上去的。\
**Vertin**: The body's bloodied, but the stethoscope is clean. It was put on afterwards.

**十四行诗**：难道说……除了我们之外，还有其他人也来过这里？\
**Sonetto**: Which means someone came here before us.

分析中断于二人的对视。\
Their analysis reaches a conclusion as their eyes meet.

**十四行诗**：……德洛丝医生。\
**Sonetto**: Dr. Dores.

**维尔汀**：取下来看看吧。\
**Vertin**: Let's take it off and have a look.

在指尖触到听诊器的一瞬间——\
The instant her fingers brush the stethoscope—

染血的防风夹克、羊绒的底衣、干枯发皱的皮肤、萎缩的肌肉，可怖的现实在眼前寸寸崩裂。\
The bloodied windbreaker, wool tops, desiccated skin, atrophied muscles—the horrific truth fractures before their eyes.

**十四行诗**：司辰，小心！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, watch out!

**维尔汀**：——？！\
**Vertin**: ...?!

本能地后退了两步，但现实却在地心引力的牵引下向着众人的方向坍塌——\
She stumbles back instinctively, yet the remains collapse toward them with gravitational inevitability.

**十四行诗**：捂住口鼻！\
**Sonetto**: Cover your mouth and nose.

烟尘散去，储藏室的墙上只剩下两根突兀的帐篷地钉。\
When the dust clears, only two grotesque tent stakes remain embedded in the wall.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

“神秘的神秘万古闪烁，即便死亡亦将拥抱死亡！”\
"Within the great eternal mystery,even death itself shall die—instantly!"

**诺谛卡**：呜……呜呜、呜呜呜——啊啊啊啊啊——！\
**Nautika**: Whuh ... Ahuh ... AAAHHH!

探险家爆发出一阵惊叫，仿佛终于无法按捺恐慌的情绪。\
She screams—a raw burst of terror too long bridled now explodes.

**诺谛卡**：这就是小耳朵虫告诉我的——！我说过不能来，我们不该来的！\
**Nautika**: This is exactly what Máhtu said would happen. I-I told you. I told you we shouldn't have come here.

**诺谛卡**：地母……请保佑我……祖父请保佑我——！\
**Nautika**: Mother Spirit, please, please save me. Oh, Grandpa, save me.

诺谛卡崩溃地咬起了手指。\
Nautika's teeth sink into her own fingers as her frenzy deepens.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐，没事的，放轻松……\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen, it's okay. Just take a breath.

**诺谛卡**：不，不不不……你们不知道这意味着什么！那些躲在白化天里的毒虫……！他们会吃人！会吃掉人的灵魂！\
**Nautika**: No, no, no, no, no. You don't know what this means. Those poisonous monsters, those, those beasts! They hide in the whiteout. They eat people. They eat our souls.

**十四行诗**：司辰，她……\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, she's ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**诺谛卡**：就是这样、就是这样，所有人都会变成这样……最终会只剩下你……只剩下你……\
**Nautika**: That's it. Hah. It's over. Everyone will be eaten, and you—you will be left all alone.

探险家颤抖地蹲下，又一次将自己蜷缩了起来。\
Nautika collapses and curls up on the floor.

**诺谛卡**：除了他们的指甲，他们什么也没留下……什么都留不下……\
**Nautika**: Just you and their nails, alone.

**维尔汀**：指甲？\
**Vertin**: Nails?

突如其来的联想撞进脑海。\
The realization comes as suddenly as a thunderbolt.

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，你的队伍成员也曾遭遇过这样的……暴行吗？\
**Vertin**: Nautika, did something similar happen to your teammates?

已然陷入极大惊恐的探险家似乎根本听不见问话，她抱着头，牙齿打颤。\
Now paralyzed by her growing terror, Nautika seems deaf to all questions.

**十四行诗**：司辰——！小心！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, watch out!

一群等身高的巨物，从不知哪个角落里瞬间蜂拥而出。\
Suddenly, human-sized monstrosities swarm from unseen corners around them.

**维尔汀**：准备战斗，十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: Sonetto, prepare to engage.

**十四行诗**：是——！\
**Sonetto**: Copy that.

恶兽低吼着张开嘴，腐臭的浊气如地热蒸汽般喷薄而出。\
The beasts snarl, breathing in and out with hungry and aggressive pants.

**十四行诗**：Ed è subito sera——！！！\
**Sonetto**: Ed è subito sera!

砰——！！！\
BANG!

尽管《外派任务避难须知》中并未写过要如何在巨犬的围追堵截下逃命——但一支训练有素的队伍似乎是顺利做到了。\
Though the Field Mission Evacuation Instructions never covered how to outrun a pack of monstrous hounds, somehow, the well-trained team manages.

**雪橇犬**：唔汪汪——！汪汪汪汪汪！\
**Sled Dog**: Woof! Woof woof woof!

然而，在雪中奔跑，犬类的速度和耐力明显都要更胜一筹。\
But in deep snow, the beasts' superior speed and stamina render the end of their chase inevitable.

**十四行诗**：我明明已经给它们施展了平静咒，也消除了它们身上重塑的影响——\
**Sonetto**: I removed Manus Vindictae's effect on them. They should've calmed down by now.

几张疯狂的大嘴即将咬上它们正在追捕的衣襟。\
Maws snap wildly, just inches from snagging their fleeing prey.

**诺谛卡**：小、小耳朵虫，地母会保佑我的，对吗？会保佑我……会的……会吗？\
**Nautika**: Máhtu, the Mother Spirit will protect me, right? She'll protect me. Yes, She will, won't She?

**十四行诗**：司辰，摩托车在那儿！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, there's the snowmobile.

保险杠凹陷的雪地摩托忠诚地停在空地上。\
Their snowmobile stands loyally in the clearing.

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱……弗里莱的摩托车来救我了……\
**Nautika**: Friele. Hah. Friele's snowmobile has come to save me.

**十四行诗**：快上摩托车！诺谛卡小姐，把手给我——\
**Sonetto**: Get on. Ms. Amundsen, give me your hand.

**维尔汀**：抓紧，我要点火了。\
**Vertin**: Grab tight. I'm starting the engine.

引擎迅速达到最高转速，冰碴被履带扬起，飞散在空中形成一团薄雾。\
The engine screams to life, throwing a spray of ice shards into the air as its treads churn—a glittering mist rising behind it.

**雪橇犬**：汪汪——！呜汪汪！汪汪汪汪！！\
**Sled Dog**: Woof! Woof woof!!

## 10TH-07 闪耀的白日 / Under Glaring Light

一座同样被遗忘的科考站。\
Another equally forgotten research station.

足够近，仅仅是翻越了几座雪坡；足够远，能让发狂的雪橇犬失去追捕猎物的方向。\
Close enough, just a few slopes away. Yet it proves enough distance to put the crazed dogs off their chase.

门窗漏风，电力储备即将耗尽，优点是没有刺鼻的腐臭与血腥味。\
The windows are drafty, the power dim and dying, but at least the air carries no stench of blood or decay.

进门\
走路\
坐下

**十四行诗**：我检查过所有的房间了，没有发现任何隐藏的敌人。\
**Sonetto**: Every room has been checked. There are no hidden enemies.

**维尔汀**：辛苦你了，十四行诗。我们先在这里安顿一会儿，休整后再出发。\
**Vertin**: Thank you, Sonetto. Let's take a rest before we set off again.

**十四行诗**：司辰……\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper ...

**十四行诗**：从官方地图上来看，刚刚那处建筑是沙克尔顿站。曾是这七十英里范围内规模最大、驻站人员最多的科考站……\
**Sonetto**: According to the official map, the previous station we entered is called Shackleton Station. It's supposed to be the site of the largest scientific research operation in a 70-mile radius.

**十四行诗**：我很难想象在这样一个科考站都遭此毒手后，这片大洲上还有什么人能幸免于难。\
**Sonetto**: If even they fell victim to such a tragedy, it's hard to imagine any of the smaller stations surviving it.

**维尔汀**：有人出于某种目的，袭击了这些科考站。\
**Vertin**: There must be a purpose behind these attacks.

**十四行诗**：从遗体状态来看，队员们被当成了某种祭祀活动的……牺牲品。\
**Sonetto**: Judging from the state of the corpses, the researchers were sacrificed for some kind of ritual.

**十四行诗**：假设这些事都是重塑之手的人做的……\
**Sonetto**: If we assume that Manus Vindictae did this—

**诺谛卡**：不用假设，就是那群“疯雪怪”做的。\
**Nautika**: There is no doubt. This was done by those Snow Monsters.

探险家闷闷的声音从角落里传出，自刚才的遭遇后，她久未发声，现在正沉默地从行囊里掏出瓶瓶罐罐的食物。\
Nautika's muffled voice emerges from the corner. After their last encounter, she had been silent and still as if like a statue, but at last she begins to unpack jars and cans of food from her bag.

**十四行诗**：……那么重塑的行径，应该都指向阿莱夫先生口中的“仪式”。\
**Sonetto**: Then it's highly likely that this was all in service of the same "ritual" Mr. Aleph mentioned.

**无线电小姐**：如此惨绝人寰……他们究竟在筹备一个怎样残忍的仪式？\
**Ms. Radio**: It's so cruel. What kind of ritual would require such a thing?

**十四行诗**：线索太少了，很难推断其全貌。但从他们大肆屠戮南极科考站的行为来看，他们需要人类作为祭品……\
**Sonetto**: We have too little information to piece together the truth. But judging by this massacre, they need human sacrifices.

**维尔汀**：或者说，重塑之手不希望仪式范围内出现“异类”——人类。\
**Vertin**: Or perhaps, they're eliminating any "aliens"—in this case, humans—in the vicinity before they perform the ritual.

**十四行诗**：没错，这足以说明“仪式”对他们的重要性。\
**Sonetto**: In any case, this shows how much this "ritual" means to them.

**维尔汀**：……德洛丝医生。\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores.

**十四行诗**：如果德洛丝医生真的来过的话，我们的方向就没有错。\
**Sonetto**: If Dr. Dores was in fact here, then we're on the right track.

**十四行诗**：从诺谛卡的地图来看，我们离腹地已经很近了。必须赶在德洛丝医生进入重塑地盘前追上她。\
**Sonetto**: According to Ms. Amundsen's map, we're not far at all from the central region. We must catch up with Dr. Dores before she enters Manus Vindictae territory.

**维尔汀**：太阳高度角还很大，天黑前我们还能再追赶一段路。\
**Vertin**: From the looks of the angle of the sun, we still have some time to catch up to her before it gets dark.

人类探险家将食物一个个摆好，发出小声的嘀咕。\
Nautika arranges the food by type and size, muttering under her breath.

**诺谛卡**：亲爱的“地母”，感谢您的食物，感谢您赐予我们的一切……\
**Nautika**: Mother Spirit, thank you for feeding us and for everything you provide.

**诺谛卡**：对了，也得感谢食物的原主人——维尔汀和十四行诗小姐……\
**Nautika**: And, of course, thank you to Ms. Vertin and Ms. Sonetto for providing the food.

静谧的闲暇时刻，咀嚼声不绝于耳。\
Their voices fall quiet for a time, replaced by the soft murmur of chewing and the slurp of canned food.

**十四行诗**：很高兴你的惊恐得到了改善。\
**Sonetto**: I'm glad to see you looking more calm.

**诺谛卡**：……对不起，我以前不是这样的。\
**Nautika**: Sorry. I wasn't always like this.

探险家嗫嚅着，为刚才在科考站中的失态道歉。\
She stammers out an apology that gathers into an explanation.

**诺谛卡**：我以前——\
**Nautika**: I was ...

**诺谛卡**：他们说我以前像只无畏的雪橇犬……\
**Nautika**: They said I was like a fearless sled dog.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**十四行诗**：没关系，我理解。我们都被自身的遭遇塑造。\
**Sonetto**: Don't worry. I understand. We've all gone through things that have scarred us.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

白炽灯小心翼翼地闪烁着。\
The incandescent lights flicker as if nodding in agreement.

**十四行诗**：……和我们刚才在沙克尔顿科考站的遭遇有关吗？\
**Sonetto**: Is it to do with what we saw in Shackleton Station?

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

探险家纠缠在一起的手指被用力错开。\
She untangles her fingers with force.

**诺谛卡**：我知道你们需要信息，可我身上没什么太值得期待的故事……\
**Nautika**: I know you need information, but there isn't much else I can tell you.

**诺谛卡**：精神错乱、“疯雪怪”、物资匮乏……死亡咬着我们不放，弗里莱让我快逃，我就往来的方向一直一直跑……\
**Nautika**: Insanity, Snow Monsters, starvation ... Death just kept on coming. Friele told me to run, so I did. I ran all the way back the way we came.

**诺谛卡**：我跑得很快……但当我回到站点时，留守的所有人不是消失，就是已经……\
**Nautika**: I ran fast, as fast as I could. But when I got to the station, everyone had either left or ... *sigh*

探险家并未继续说下去。\
She stops, unable to continue.

刚才的见闻足以让人补全故事的全貌。\
Words aren't necessary to piece together the rest of her story.

**十四行诗**：对不起……\
**Sonetto**: I'm sorry.

探险家摇摇头，她望着第一助手的眼睛，决定继续说下去。\
Nautika shakes her head. Meeting Sonetto's gaze, she steels herself and tries again.

**诺谛卡**：不知道是磕到了脑袋还是因为过呼吸而缺氧……有些事我已经记不清了。\
**Nautika**: I don't know if it's because of hyperventilation or that I hit my head, but there are some things I can't remember clearly.

**诺谛卡**：但我还是时常能感觉到那种未知的恐惧。我……已经无法像以前那样勇敢了。\
**Nautika**: But that fear I felt—that fear still haunts me. I'm no longer as brave as I used to be.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐……\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen ...

**诺谛卡**：在我的家乡，会驯鹿的人是最勇敢的。我们每年都会举办赛鹿节。\
**Nautika**: Back in my hometown, you're considered brave if you can tame a reindeer. We have a racing festival every year.

**诺谛卡**：赛鹿节上表现最厉害的人会作为“地母”的代言人，敲响颂赞太阳的大鼓，升起全村最高昂的旗帜，宣告迎风招展的胜利。\
**Nautika**: Whoever wins the race serves as the voice of the Mother Spirit. They hear Her voice and beat its rhythm in praise of the sun, and the flag of our village is raised high into the sky to declare their victory.

**诺谛卡**：在同龄人里，我驯犬和驯鹿的技术最好。我一直以为我总有一天会是敲响大鼓的那个人。\
**Nautika**: I was the best dog-and-reindeer trainer of my age. I always thought I would be the one to beat the drum one day.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**诺谛卡**：可是现在，连那些一路陪我到南极的雪橇犬都已经不在了……\
**Nautika**: But now, even my sled dogs are gone. They were so brave to venture all the way to Antarctica with me.

**诺谛卡**：我……\
**Nautika**: I ...

她垂着眼睛，说不下去了。\
Her eyes drop. The words still don't come.

她的十指纠结又松开、纠结又松开。\
Her fingers twist back together, untwist, then twist again.

**诺谛卡**：我不再是原来的自己了。\
**Nautika**: I'm not that girl anymore.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

气氛稍显潮湿，即使是在如此干燥的大陆上。\
The air feels damp, damper than it has any right to be on this cold, dry continent.

第一助手转身，从身后拿出一沓厚厚的资料。\
Sonetto turns and pulls out a thick stack of documents meticulously organized, as always.

**十四行诗**：对了，诺谛卡小姐，我想让你看看这个……\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen, I thought you would like to see this.

**诺谛卡**：《科考日记》……？\
**Nautika**: An expedition diary?

**诺谛卡**：这是……你们从沙克尔顿站带出来的？！\
**Nautika**: Oh! Did you take all these from Shackleton Station?

**维尔汀**：情况紧急，我们只来得及抢出几本。\
**Vertin**: Yes. Due to the urgency of the situation, we were only able to grab a few documents.

**维尔汀**：我们想，如果情况不是如此极端，你一定会是第一个冲上去一睹为快的人。\
**Vertin**: We thought you'd have liked to look through them, had we not encountered those rabid dogs, so we took what we could before we left.

**诺谛卡**：《南极魔精生物圈研究调查》《神秘符文索引词典》……《基于神秘学的极地蔬菜种植指南》！\
**Nautika**: A Survey of the Antarctic Critter Biosphere, An Indexed Dictionary of Arcane Runes ... A Polar Guide to the Arcane Cultivation of Vegetables!

**诺谛卡**：太好了！有了这份资料，我们说不定能掌握在极地环境下种马铃薯的诀窍……\
**Nautika**: Incredible! Fantastic! With this, we may finally master how to grow potatoes in polar regions!

昏暗的灯光下，探险家激动得鼻尖发红。\
Under the dim light, Nautika's face flushes red with emotion.

她低头看了许久，才忽然发现自己已经罔顾同伴多时。\
A long time passes before she realizes she's been lost in her reading.

她珍重地把书页一一收好，然后面色复杂地看着面前的同伴们，上下唇嗫嚅了许久。\
She gathers each precious page, then looks up at her new teammates. There's a conflict burning in her eyes.

**诺谛卡**：……谢谢你们……\
**Nautika**: Thank you. Thank you so much.

最终，她只认真地吐出了最简单的致谢。\
In the end, all she can manage is to repeat her thanks.

**维尔汀**：你喜欢就好。\
**Vertin**: It was worth the risk.

罐头食物的香气氤氲在空气中，旅人们享受着难得安宁的一刻。\
The scent of canned food lingers as each savors both the fullness of their bellies and the rare moment of peace.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，你在看什么？\
**Vertin**: What are you looking at, Sonetto?

第一助手阖上了门，面色凝重。\
Sonetto closes the door, looking very grave.

**十四行诗**：太阳高度角始终没有变过，司辰。\
**Sonetto**: The sun doesn't seem to have moved at all since we last calculated the angle, Timekeeper.

**无线电小姐**：是极昼现象吗？真希望我也能看见这样的景色。\
**Ms. Radio**: Oh, is it the midnight sun? If only I had the eyes to see it.

**十四行诗**：……按常理而言，现在是南极的秋天，并非会出现极昼的季节。\
**Sonetto**: Technically, it's autumn in Antarctica at the moment. Polar day only occurs in the summer months.

**维尔汀**：我们从火地岛出发后，也数次穿越了晨昏。\
**Vertin**: Indeed. We've seen it rise and fall several times since we left from Tierra del Fuego.

**维尔汀**：而就算是极昼期间，太阳高度角也是会随时间变化的……\
**Vertin**: And even if it were the season for polar day, the solar angle would still vary.

随着对现象分析的深入，探险家的呼吸急促了起来。\
Nautika's breathing once again picks up speed as their analysis progresses.

**诺谛卡**：不、不是吧……\
**Nautika**: No. No, it can't be.

**诺谛卡**：反常的、诡异的地理现象，第三天白日出现的极光——\
**Nautika**: All these abnormal phenomena, the sun standing still in the sky, that aurora in the broad daylight—

轰——\
*boom*

**诺谛卡**：呜！！\
**Nautika**: Agh!

**无线电小姐**：什么？什么声音？\
**Ms. Radio**: What? What's that sound?

**无线电小姐**：雪、雪崩——？不，听上去像是混杂了某种魔精的叫声。\
**Ms. Radio**: Are we in an avalanche? No, it sounds like the screaming of critters.

**十四行诗**：司辰，你快来看——！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, take a look at this.

众人冲出科考站小屋。\
They burst out from the station's door.

怪异的飞翼在空中迅猛地鼓动着寒风，对着闯入者惊声嘶叫着。\
Weird creatures flap their wings in the cold wind, hissing desperately at the intruders.

**诺谛卡**：是“疯雪怪”的怪物们……！\
**Nautika**: It's the Snow Monsters. Their flying beasts.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐！退后！\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen, stay back.

伴随着惊声啸叫，奥利图欧径直从空中跌落。\
With a piercing shriek, the Olitiau plummets from the sky.

在它的下方，不偏不倚正是停在科考站外的雪地摩托。\
And as if perfectly aligned, it lands square and heavy on their poor snowmobile.

**诺谛卡**：不、不不不——\
**Nautika**: No, no, no, no, no.

探险家拔腿冲出想要挽留生死线边缘的载具，却被同伴们拦下。\
She dashes out, desperate to save the vehicle teetering on the edge of destruction, only to be held back by her companions.

**十四行诗**：——别过去！\
**Sonetto**: Don't—!

火舌是最先冲出的，接着是尖叫般的耳鸣。\
Flames shoot out first, followed by a screeching roar,

最后，才是一场火光盛大的爆炸。\
rising to its grand finale: a spectacular explosion.

变速器从爆炸中崩出。\
The transmission tears free from the blast.

雪地摩托在白色冰原上四分五裂，火焰熊熊燃烧。\
The snowmobile lies scattered across the white ice field, flames still licking over its spilled fuel tank.

被火焰升起的烟雾熏迷了眼，旅人们只能模糊地见到一团光影，将不曾日落的白昼点得更加明亮。\
Blinded by the smoke rising from the fire, they make out a glowing mass that brightens the endless daylight sky.

**诺谛卡**：不……\
**Nautika**: No ...

**诺谛卡**：这是我们唯一的载具。\
**Nautika**: That was our only means of transportation.

## 10TH-08 世界上最糟糕的旅行 / The Worst Journey in the World

脚步一深一浅，旅人们正艰难地向坡顶攀登。\
They trudge upward through the deep snow.

**诺谛卡**：伟大的……呼……地母啊……\
**Nautika**: Great Mother Spirit ...

**诺谛卡**：只差一点儿了，一定、我一定可以爬上去……\
**Nautika**: I'm almost there. Just-Just a little farther.

雪浪高低起伏，要在这儿站稳脚跟非常困难。\
Unsteady and fresh snowpack makes it nearly impossible to keep a steady footing.

探险者只能走三步后停半晌，稳定身躯后再次踏步向前。\
Each step comes with a wobble as she rebalances herself.

**诺谛卡**：徒步是我最不推荐、最最不推荐的一种出行方式……万恶的疯雪怪……\
**Nautika**: Traveling on foot was never a good choice for an expedition. Evil Snow Monsters!

**诺谛卡**：发狂的雪橇犬、发疯的魔精，呼……\
**Nautika**: First sled dogs, then mad critters. *grunt*

冰镐重重砸进了雪里。\
Her ice ax slams deep into the packed snow.

**诺谛卡**：还有无尽的白天！腹地里不落的太阳！\
**Nautika**: And now endless daylight. Endless glaring sun.

**诺谛卡**：这、这也是那个“仪式”的影响吗？这些疯雪怪，到底在做什么……\
**Nautika**: Is all this because of that ritual? What the heck are those Snow Monsters trying to do?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐，我们还需要多久才能抵达那片遗迹？\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen, how long until we reach the ruins?

**诺谛卡**：说不好……呼……我说不好……\
**Nautika**: I don't know. I-I don't know.

**诺谛卡**：大家小心，有什么东西来了！\
**Nautika**: Careful. Something's coming.

脚底传来隆隆的隐雷般的声响。\
A low, thunderous rumble vibrates the ground beneath their boots.

**十四行诗**：地震？\
**Sonetto**: An earthquake?

**诺谛卡**：不不不——不是地震！压低身体站稳！别滚下坡了！\
**Nautika**: No, no, no, no, no, not an earthquake. Lower your body. Whatever you do, don't lose your footing.

冰下奔涌的黑色物质挤碎了冰层，在不远处的雪脊上喷薄而出。\
The black substance surging beneath the ice shatters the frozen layers, erupting out over a distant ridge.

黑色物质向着雪坡下的远处蔓延，正朝着科考站群的方向令土地寸寸崩裂。\
The creeping darkness spreads downhill, fracturing the earth as it advances toward the cluster of research stations.

**雪橇犬**：汪汪、汪汪汪汪汪——！嗷呜——呜呜呜……嗷呜——\
**Sled Dog**: Woof ...

极地的风远远送来了无助的犬吠，昨日追逐着要撕咬旅者的雪橇犬们发出了嘤嘤的哭声。\
The polar wind carries faint, helpless howls from the same sled dogs that had chased them yesterday.

**诺谛卡**：雪橇犬……它们、它们很聪明，它们不会掉进这些冰裂里……\
**Nautika**: The sled dogs, they're smart. They avoided the cracks very intelligently.

探险家低声喃喃自语，但掩盖不了对远方犬群的担忧。\
Nautika murmurs under her breath, unable to hide her concern.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，你非常擅长驯鹿和驯狗，对吗？\
**Vertin**: Nautika, you're a capable reindeer-and-dog trainer, right?

**诺谛卡**：——？\
**Nautika**: ...?

**诺谛卡**：我、我知道你想做什么——这不是一个好主意，它们昨天还发着疯……\
**Nautika**: Oh, no-no. I-I really don't think that's a good idea. They tried to kill us yesterday.

抵抗的声音越来越小，最后，探险家咽下了其他本能的反驳。\
Her protests die on her lips until, finally, she swallows up her remaining objections.

**诺谛卡**：我也可以试试，这些雪橇犬可能还留有理智……\
**Nautika**: W-Well, maybe I can give it a try. They might still have some sense.

她手脚并用爬上了雪坡，站直后深吸了一口气。\
On hands and knees, she scrambles up the slope.

**诺谛卡**：——我已经很久没有练习过口令了，要是它们不听我的呢？\
**Nautika**: But it's been a while since I last gave any orders. W-What if they don't listen to me?

**维尔汀**：来吧，诺谛卡，“敲下这盏好鼓”。\
**Vertin**: Come on, Nautika. Time to "hit the drum."

探险家睁大了眼，然后重重点了点头。\
Her eyes widen, then she nods.

**诺谛卡**：……我、我知道了。\
**Nautika**: *gulp* You're right.

悠长响亮的哨声从颤抖的双唇中发出，诺谛卡努力挥动着双手。\
A long, clear whistle pierces the air from Nautika's chapped and cold lips as she waves her arms wildly.

远方，疯狂吠叫的雪橇犬慢慢安静了下来。\
In the distance, the frenzied sled dogs take notice and gradually quiet.

**诺谛卡**：来——！\
**Nautika**: Hike!

诺谛卡向后大幅度地挥手。\
She sweeps her arm backward in a grand gesture.

远处传来了混乱的刨雪声，许久未接收过指令的犬队似乎蠢蠢欲动。\
Chaotic snow-scrabbling sounds carry from afar, the long-unruly dog team now stirring to command.

**诺谛卡**：你可以的，诺谛卡，再来一次……\
**Nautika**: You can do this, Nautika. Try again.

123

**诺谛卡**：前进——！\
**Nautika**: Hike!

在无言中等待了片刻后——\
A pause hangs thick in the air.

犬吠声由远及近，松软的雪在路途上卷成了一阵小型海啸。\
The sound of barking dogs gets nearer as approaching paws churn the snow into a rushing tide of powder.

**诺谛卡**：左转——！减速！\
**Nautika**: Haw! Easy!

诺谛卡向下压了压手臂。\
Nautika presses her palms downward.

**诺谛卡**：大家看准时机——！\
**Nautika**: Get ready, everyone!

她双腿打颤，眼中却闪着兴奋的光斑。\
Her legs are shaking, but her eyes glitter with exhilaration.

**十四行诗**：司辰——！我们真的要这么做吗——\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, are we really going to do this?

在犬群即将冲散队伍时，探险家抓住了它们脖子上未被取下的缰绳，翻身骑上了狂奔的雪橇犬。\
The dog team is nearly upon them, still half-wild as they speed forward. Yet in a single swinging motion, Nautika pulls herself up and over the top of the lead sled dog.

无线电小姐再一次差点从帽子里颠出来。\
Ms. Radio rustles, nearly tumbling from her perch.

**无线电小姐**：噢——噢天哪……我们在做什么……\
**Ms. Radio**: Oh, holy mother of—What are we doing?

**十四行诗**：我……我也不知道——！！！\
**Sonetto**: I-I have no idea.

**诺谛卡**：冲呀……冲呀！哈哈——\
**Nautika**: Straight ahead. Straight ahead! Hahaha!

雪橇犬径直冲下雪坡，罔顾薄雾中的前路是否有陷阱。\
The dogs charge downslope without hesitation, ignoring any potential pitfalls that may be hidden in the mist.

**诺谛卡**：噢、噢！对了——！\
**Nautika**: Oh—Oh, right.

**诺谛卡**：多摸摸它们的头和脖子上的毛发，这样很快就能和它们熟悉起来了——！\
**Nautika**: Pet them around the head and neck. That will help you bond with them.

**维尔汀**：有道理。\
**Vertin**: I suppose that makes sense.

手轻轻拂过雪橇犬的头颅，粗质却柔软的毛发陷入指缝。\
Fingers brush over a sled dog's head, coarse yet soft fur slipping between them.

**维尔汀**：希望乌尔里希组长也能遇到像它们一样可靠的伙伴。\
**Vertin**: I hope Ulrich has come across friends as reliable as these.

诺谛卡趴下身子，把脸埋在雪橇犬脖子后的软毛里。\
Nautika presses low, burying her face in the soft fur behind the dog's neck.

**诺谛卡**：……我做到了，我做到了。\
**Nautika**: I did it. I did it.

**诺谛卡**：它们真是我见过最大的雪橇犬……！！\
**Nautika**: These are the biggest sled dogs I've ever seen.

**士兵Ⅰ**：报告中尉，海域内发现可疑船只。\
**Soldier I**: Lieutenant, we have spotted a suspicious unit.

莫莉德尔飞快地拿起对讲机，聆听穿越白化雪雾伪装的传信。\
Moldir grabs the intercom and pulls it close, listening for messages cutting through the whiteout.

**士兵Ⅰ**：离岸正东方向，一艘纵帆船正在接岸。暂时没有其他更多船只进入视野范围。\
**Soldier I**: A schooner has come ashore due east. It appears to be alone.

**莫莉德尔**：一队和二队随我来，三队留守营地。\
**Moldir**: Team One and Two, come with me. Team Three, stay and keep watch.

训练有素、相互信任的士兵们悄声移动，来到最靠近冰架的一处天然掩体后。\
With mutual trust, the disciplined soldiers move in perfect and silent synchronization, slipping behind a natural barrier near the ice shelf.

铁锚落海，那艘纵帆船悠悠然停靠在岸边。\
With an anchor's splash, the schooner drifts up against the icy shore.

铁锚落海，那艘纵帆船悠悠然停靠在岸边。

**莫莉德尔**：目视纵帆船无武装，但不能排除是基金会战力伪装的可能。\
**Moldir**: Target presents as unarmed, but we can't rule anything out yet.

**莫莉德尔**：一队随我行动。\
**Moldir**: Team One, follow me.

**莫莉德尔**：二队至A2掩体后待命，持续警戒海面是否有后续增援。\
**Moldir**: Team Two, stand by at Bunker A2. Keep your eyes on the coast. We don't want to be caught unaware if they send reinforcements.

莫莉德尔双手持枪，带领步兵小队缓步往前进发。\
Her hand held over her firearm, Moldir leads the infantry squad forward in measured strides.

纵帆船的乘客在厚重的白化雪雾中艰难前行，逐步走进埋伏。\
Blinded by the whiteout, the schooner's passengers march themselves obliviously into the waiting ambush.

**？？？**：晕船、白化天……还有以指南针的抖动来看，这里存在磁场紊乱的情况。\
**???**: Sea sickness, whiteout, and judging by the trembling compass pointer, something's messing with the magnetic field here.

**？？？**：……老板，您是全世界最不适合来这里的意识唤醒者。\
**???**: Boss, you're probably the least suitable person in the world to be doing this mission.

**？？？**：该死，我已经能听见二氧化硅开裂的声音了。\
**???**: Shoot. I can already hear my silicon dioxide crackling.

**？？？**：得先找个避风的掩体，我要给玻璃补上一层疏水防冻材料。\
**???**: Find a windproof bunker. I need to reapply the hydrophobic and cold-resistant coatings.

**莫莉德尔**：就是现在！\
**Moldir**: Now!

枪口齐刷刷地对准了意识唤醒者和随行人。\
