Muzzles snap up in unison, all aimed at the Awakened and his guard.

**？？？**：——！\
**???**: ...!

**莫莉德尔**：弗雷希特曼队长，带人登船，确认船舱内是否有其他威胁。\
**Moldir**: Sergeant Frekhtman, take two soldiers with you and search the schooner for any other threats.

在她的手势旨意下，三名士兵持枪走进了弥漫的乳白色雪雾中。\
At her signal, three armed soldiers advance through the swirling snow.

**莫莉德尔**：你被俘了——\
**Moldir**: You are under arrest.

对面前胸挂着明晃晃的工牌。\
An ID badge hangs conspicuously on the chest of the figure before them.

**莫莉德尔**：拉普拉斯的研究员。\
**Moldir**: Laplace researcher.

玻璃缸中的磁流体在一秒内闪烁出了数个不同的形状。\
The ferrofluid inside his head morphs through multiple shapes at blinding speed.

**乌尔里希**：这身军服……你们是芝诺的军人？这一定是一场误会，我受到了圣洛夫基金会的正式派遣——\
**Ulrich**: That uniform ... Are you from Zeno? There must have been a mix-up. We have the official approval of the St. Pavlov Foundation.

沉默半晌的护卫兵打断了磁流体的陈情。\
After a prolonged silence, the guard interrupts his testimony.

**护卫兵**：……老板，记功廊上有他们的遗像。\
如果站在我们面前的不是幽灵的话……\
**Guard**: Boss, I've seen their faces hanging in the Hall of Merit. So, unless they're ghosts ...

**护卫兵**：那么我们就是遇上叛军了。\
**Guard**: We've just stumbled upon the rebels.

莫莉德尔闭了闭眼，像是在回避某个词语。\
Moldir closes her eyes briefly, as if avoiding a particular word.

**莫莉德尔**：你们来这里做什么？\
**Moldir**: What is your purpose here?

乌尔里希在白雾中举起右手，而它的左手始终揣在口袋里。\
Ulrich raises his right hand to the white mist, his left remaining in his pocket.

**乌尔里希**：这与你无关，你只需要知道，我对你们没有威胁。\
**Ulrich**: It's none of your business. All you need to know is that we're not a threat to you.

**护卫兵**：我们单枪匹马来的。\
**Guard**: We came here alone, no backup.

对讲机传出声音。\
A voice comes over the intercom.

**对讲机**：报告中尉，除一名无武装水手外，纵帆船已确认清空。经前哨确认，暂无任何其余船只侵入近海。\
**Intercom**: Lieutenant, the schooner is cleared. Only an unarmed sailor on board. The outpost confirmed that they haven't spotted any other ship.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**乌尔里希**：……该把枪口放下了，我重申一次，我对你们没有威胁。\
**Ulrich**: Lower your gun, Lieutenant. We're not a threat.

**乌尔里希**：我只是想过来听一支曲子。\
**Ulrich**: We're just here to play a tune.

**莫莉德尔**：理由太拙劣了，研究员。\
**Moldir**: A poor excuse, researcher.

**莫莉德尔**：还请回吧，现在不是来南极旅游的最好时节。\
**Moldir**: Please head back to where you came from. Now is not the best time to play sing-song in Antarctica.

**乌尔里希**：我不会离开。\
**Ulrich**: I'm not leaving.

意识唤醒者举起左手，赫然攥着一枚高爆手榴弹。插销已经松落，全靠紧压着握柄才没有即刻爆炸。\
The Awakened raises his left hand, a grenade gripped within it—the pin already loose—the pressure of his fingers on the lever all that stands between the striker and the fuse.

**众士兵**：——！！！\
**Soldiers**: !!!

**莫莉德尔**：全体回避！\
**Moldir**: Fall back!

中尉喝退了下属，独身持枪上前。\
Moldir barks her squad back and advances alone, her firearm held high and steady.

**莫莉德尔**：冷静，先生。你是一名研究员，计算和知识才是你的武装。手榴弹这种危险品还是交给我处理比较好。\
**Moldir**: Calm down, sir. You're a researcher. Perhaps you should stick to the pursuit of knowledge and leave the explosives handling to me.

她的目光却缓缓停留在手榴弹上印着的一小排银字上。\
She locks onto the tiny silver lettering stamped on the grenade.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：RGD5-72-85-128-TTK-006。\
**Moldir**: RGD5-72-85-128-TTK-006.

**莫莉德尔**：我认识这枚手榴弹的原主人。\
**Moldir**: I know the owner of this grenade.

**莫莉德尔**：第一场“暴雨”后，为了更系统地管理军力，芝诺的所有装备均统一刻录了编号，通常以排为单位分发。\
**Moldir**: After the first "Storm," all Zeno equipment was codified under a particular numbering system and distributed among the platoons.

**莫莉德尔**：但这枚手榴弹的原主人非常特殊，她隶属某个带有独立编制的行动小队。\
**Moldir**: But the number on this grenade belongs to someone special. Someone in an independent team.

**莫莉德尔**：她的所有装备，包括她最出名的飞行装备Su-01ве都带有特殊的刻录标识。\
**Moldir**: Someone who has a unique code on all her equipment, including her famous Su-01ве flying device.

**莫莉德尔**：一位斯拉夫人。\
**Moldir**: A Slav.

**莫莉德尔**：……你们和司辰小队有过接洽。\
**Moldir**: So, you've been in contact with Team Timekeeper.

**乌尔里希**：那又如何？\
**Ulrich**: And what if I have?

被重重包围的磁流体可没有好脾气。\
From the swirling pace of his ferrofluid, it's clear he's taken the question badly.

**乌尔里希**：我原本想用来自保的武器却被用来自爆了。\
**Ulrich**: So the weapon that was supposed to protect me is the very thing that gave me away. How ironic!

中尉摆了摆手，示意其他士兵维持回避姿态。自己却放下枪，单手握住了手榴弹。\
With a wave, Moldir signals her squad to hold position while she holsters her gun, then grasps the grenade with one hand.

**乌尔里希**：你要干什么？！这可不是玩具，它的爆炸当量等同于200克的TNT炸弹——\
**Ulrich**: Are you out of your minds? This is a real grenade, you know. Powerful as 200 grams of TNT.

**莫莉德尔**：无新事，复旧形。\
**Moldir**: Что было, то и будет.

插销归位，弹簧回落。一切都被“修复如新”，回到它正确的模样。\
The pin whips back into place. The spring retracts. Everything resets to its factory-new state.

**乌尔里希**：……这是你的神秘术？\
**Ulrich**: Your arcane skill?

中尉没有回答，她反手夺下了不再具有威胁的手榴弹。\
She offers no explanation as she wrenches the now-harmless grenade from Ulrich's grip.

**莫莉德尔**：我最后问一次，你来这里的目的是什么？\
**Moldir**: For the last time, what is your purpose here?

与司辰——维尔汀有关吗？\
Is it about the Timekeeper, about Vertin?

## 10TH-09 愚人与女祭司 / The Fool and the High Priestess

中尉握着通讯器时的神情，比擒获俘虏时要更加紧张。\
Moldir's fingers tense around the intercom.

**莫莉德尔**：是，是。\
**Moldir**: Yes, that's right.

**莫莉德尔**：鉴于直升机的故障，非紧急关头，我们不会使用它进行转移。\
**Moldir**: Given the helicopter malfunction, we would be hard-pressed to make any movements unless absolutely necessary.

**莫莉德尔**：物资和粮食储备充足，我们做好了持久战的准备。\
**Moldir**: We still have plenty of resources. We are prepared for the long haul.

**对讲机**：……\
**Intercom**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

似乎碰上了一个难以回复的问题，持通讯设备的军官沉默了片刻后，朗声作答。\
She hesitates at the difficult question, weighing her answer before speaking.

**莫莉德尔**：……暂无任何基金会的武装势力出现。\
**Moldir**: No Foundation armed forces have yet appeared.

**莫莉德尔**：鉴于此，我怀疑乔治五世海岸不是他们首选的登陆地。\
**Moldir**: I suspect the King George V Coast is not their first landing choice.

**对讲机**：……\
**Intercom**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：维多利亚地吗？那不是正好靠近……？\
**Moldir**: Victoria Land? Isn't that near—

她的疑问被对方打断。\
Her inquiry is cut short.

**莫莉德尔**：——是，是。\
**Moldir**: Yes. Understood.

**莫莉德尔**：我们会严阵以待，不放过任何可疑目标。\
**Moldir**: We are on high alert. No suspect will be spared.

莫莉德尔收起通讯器。\
Moldir puts away the communicator.

平稳流动着的磁流体同它的护卫兵一起被缚，盘坐在驻扎地的角落。\
Ulrich sits restrained along with his guard.

**乌尔里希**：以“是”开头，以“是”结束，但是你省略了最需要报备的信息——我。\
**Ulrich**: All that chatter, yet you didn't report the thing most worthy of reporting. Am I so trustworthy?

**莫莉德尔**：武装已经被我们解除，没有定位器，没有可预见的增援。\
**Moldir**: You're disarmed, with no locator and no backup.

**莫莉德尔**：你们只是一个意外。这样的多余信息，父亲不需要听到。\
**Moldir**: It would be redundant to report you. There's no need to disturb Father with such things.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

**乌尔里希**：多余的、无用的信息，就像恩尼格玛密码机三转子组成的上亿可能性之一，在破译出最后的密码之后，它们就毫无用处了。\
**Ulrich**: Redundant, useless information, like the hundreds of millions of possible combinations of the Enigma machine that are discarded once the code is deciphered.

**乌尔里希**：所以一点谈判的可能性都没有了吗？\
**Ulrich**: Anyway, are you certain there's no room for a deal?

拉普拉斯组长举起被铐牢的双手示意。\
He raises his handcuffed hands.

子弹上膛。\
A bullet is loaded.

一个行为，直接证实了至少这片营地上，话语权的归属在哪里。\
That single action makes it clear who holds authority in this camp.

**莫莉德尔**：提条件不是俘虏该做的事。\
**Moldir**: No deals for captives.

乌尔里希沉默片刻。\
Ulrich pauses, though not entirely too long.

**乌尔里希**：军人的立场无坚不摧……对吗？\
**Ulrich**: A soldier's loyalty should be unwavering, no?

**乌尔里希**：那么，为什么要投靠重塑之手？\
**Ulrich**: Then why did you turn to Manus Vindictae?

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

云翳从山巅倾斜而下，时间在这里同化石一起被冻结。\
The shadows of distant clouds cascade down the mountain, bringing a rush of chill air as if to freeze both time and space.

**莫莉德尔**：就同你此行的目的一样，这个问题是没有答案的。\
**Moldir**: It's "none of your business."

**乌尔里希**：那么是否所有人都同意这一决定？\
**Ulrich**: Touché. Did the other soldiers agree with this decision?

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**乌尔里希**：我了解了，党同伐异的结果。\
**Ulrich**: No need to tell me. Your silence is answer enough.

磁流体不吝在语气中加入了一些讥讽。\
Ulrich laces his tone with sarcasm.

**乌尔里希**：表示出忠心的追随者将无知的人排除在外，得以留下最可靠的选项。但同时，你们的兵力一定出现了折损。\
**Ulrich**: Those who were loyal to you stayed, and those who weren't were exiled. While I'm sure you have a trustworthy team, you must have suffered a significant loss to your manpower.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

……\
...

“无知的人。”\
"Those who weren't."

莫莉德尔操起通讯器。\
Moldir takes out her communicator.

**莫莉德尔**：来听歌，对吧？\
**Moldir**: So, you're here to listen to music, huh?

**莫莉德尔**：父亲会非常喜欢这枚唱片的——鉴于你身上除了各式探险装备外就只剩下它。我猜，这一定与你来此的目的有关。\
**Moldir**: My father would appreciate this record. Given this is the only thing with you besides your expedition gear, it must have something to do with your purpose here.

**莫莉德尔**：看来拉普拉斯科算中心又诞生了新成果，然而这成果的背后，又有多少不计其数的牺牲呢？\
**Moldir**: I assume the LSCC has made another development. But I wonder, how many sacrifices have been made to get to this point?

**莫莉德尔**：这些牺牲换来的是一个圆满的成功课题，还是一个不期的失败推演？我倒是颇为拭目以待。\
**Moldir**: And what will these sacrifices get you this time? The expected results or an unexpected failure? I'm on the edge of my seat.

前芝诺中尉的手指轻轻敲打着通讯器，用好整以暇掩饰着某种怒火。\
She taps the communicator again, masking simmering anger with a distant but focused calm.

磁流体并未如期被激怒，只是在玻璃缸内变换闪烁不定。\
He refuses to take the bait; all he does is flicker.

**乌尔里希**：而你们又能精准地推演出，你们所有行为的后果吗？\
**Ulrich**: Then I assume you're able to accurately predict the consequences of all your actions? So, where do you predict this decision will take you?

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

拨通通讯器的手指停下。\
Her finger freezes mid-dial.

**乌尔里希**：戴上面具成为疯子，大喊大叫着把眼珠子扣出来。\
**Ulrich**: To wearing their mask and losing your sanity? To screaming and gouging your eyes out?

**乌尔里希**：还是说，你的目的就是帮助重塑之手诱发一场又一场“暴雨”，直到你把所有曾经得罪过你的人都丢进“暴雨”里灭口？\
**Ulrich**: Or are you planning to play the loyal Manus dog, helping them bring about one "Storm" after another until every one of your rivals has been washed away?

**护卫兵**：所以得罪她不是我们现在的首要任务——老板！\
**Guard**: Uh, I don't think pissing off the rebels was on the mission brief, boss.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**乌尔里希**：你们走在了亲手推翻过往一切努力的道路上。\
**Ulrich**: Your actions are poised to undo all your past efforts by your own hand.

**乌尔里希**：我对军队纪律不甚了解，但以一个研究员的立场来说，我绝对不会这么做。\
**Ulrich**: I'll admit, I'm no tactician, but as a researcher, I can't see the logic in this choice.

**乌尔里希**：如果我的实验方法被证实是错的，那么我会在尝试所有变量后，改变实验路径，而不是彻底推翻我的课题。\
**Ulrich**: Were my experimental method to be proven wrong, I wouldn't simply give the entire project up. I'd adjust the variables and change my method.

**乌尔里希**：我很喜欢科算中心一位新职员带来的箴言：世界上不存在错误的课题，只有未被找到可复现道路的规律。\
**Ulrich**: As a new Laplace member said, there are no wrong projects, only rules that have not yet been made reproducible.

**乌尔里希**：任何研究员都不会逃避失败，我们被现实短暂击倒后，就会爬起来。\
**Ulrich**: Every researcher will inevitably experience many failures. We just brush ourselves off and get back on our feet.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**乌尔里希**：还是说，听从军令对你来说本身就是一种逃避？可以逃避承担决策的风险。\
**Ulrich**: Or are you hiding behind your military orders to absolve yourself from making decisions?

**乌尔里希**：就像你们现在躲在这片海岸一样。\
**Ulrich**: Is that why you're hiding here on this coast right now?

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**护卫兵**：完了……老板，这下应该是真的得罪她了。\
**Guard**: Well. Guess that ship has sailed.

中尉下意识侧身面向海岸，回避了所有人的视线。\
Moldir turns toward the coast.

她深深呼吸，思绪却莫名飘忽。\
She draws a deep breath, letting her thoughts stabilize in a single direction.

……乔治五世海岸，难攻易守。\
The King George V Coast—a place where defense would be favored.

**莫莉德尔**：情报已证实了战舰从罗斯海海域驶来，从交战情况来看，那边是战事中心……\
**Moldir**: Intelligence has confirmed that the Foundation's fleet is coming from the Ross Sea. Presumably, that's the area of operations.

应该立刻奔赴维多利亚地进行增援。\
They should have rushed reinforcements to Victoria immediately.

**莫莉德尔**：尽管只有一架堪堪可用的运输直升机，但对一支训练有素的部队来说，路途并不远……\
**Moldir**: There's only one transport helicopter. But the journey is traversable for a well-trained team.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

可是……\
But ...

父亲没有下达这样的指示。\
Father never gave that order.

他只是让孩子们留在远离战场的冰架边缘，继续待命。\
He just left his children waiting at the ice shelf's edge, far from the battlefield, still on standby.

**护卫兵**：好吧，任务要以最坏的方式失败了。\
**Guard**: Well, looks like this mission is a great big fail.

**护卫兵**：那……我想申请再吃一块巧克力口味的军粮——你要来一块吗？\
**Guard**: Least we can have one last chocolate MRE before we're toast. Do you want a piece, boss?

**乌尔里希**：……谢谢，“咀嚼”这个动作在执行层面无法做到。\
**Ulrich**: Thank you, but chewing isn't in my repertoire. It doesn't matter how ready-to-eat the meal is.

**莫莉德尔**：——乌尔里希组长。\
**Moldir**: Mr. Ulrich.

中尉从自己的思绪中抽离，目光如炬地回头。\
Moldir snaps out of her thoughts and turns with piercing focus.

**莫莉德尔**：你对重塑之手想要在南极进行的活动了解多少？\
**Moldir**: How much do you know about Manus Vindictae's plans in Antarctica?

话锋一转的询问令组长狐疑起来。\
Her sharp shift in questioning puts Ulrich on edge.

**乌尔里希**：我们似乎并没有达成任何共识，芝诺军备学院的套话技巧未免显得太薄弱了。\
**Ulrich**: No deal made, and you still want some info? Is this how Zeno trains its soldiers?

中尉收回落在俘虏身上的目光。\
She looks away deliberately.

**莫莉德尔**：很薄弱，我向来不精于此——但在把你倒入特拉诺瓦湾前，我必须知道你背后代表着什么样的信息。\
**Moldir**: Honestly, I've never been much of an interrogator. But before I pour you into Terra Nova Bay, I have to know who or what is behind your mission here.

**乌尔里希**：……等、等等？\
**Ulrich**: Wait. What?

磁流体疯狂闪烁，躯壳的电路噼啪作响。\
The ferrofluid flickers, circuits crackling inside.

情况似乎没有转机。\
The situation appears hopeless.

**莫莉德尔**：白手套队长、弗雷希特曼队长。\
**Moldir**: Sergeant White Gloves, Sergeant Frekhtman.

随着中尉的呼唤，两位队长分站在她身侧。\
At Moldir's call, two sergeants flank her on either side.

**莫莉德尔**：把它带回那处科考站的旧建筑，那里是更为合适的审讯地。\
**Moldir**: Take him back to the old building in the station. That will be a more suitable location for interrogation.

前芝诺中尉伸出双指示意，磁流体被两位队长一人架着一只胳膊强行带离。\
She signals with two fingers, and the sergeants seize Ulrich by the arms, dragging him away.

**乌尔里希**：——等等，你们根本不知道自己在做什么！这是一个绝对的错误！\
**Ulrich**: Wait, wait, wait. You don't know what you're doing. You're making a huge mistake.

两位步兵队长无动于衷，只提溜着意识唤醒者向目的地走去。\
There's no response nor reaction.

中尉走在最前方，她军靴上的金色穗条在空中飘荡。\
Moldir leads the way, the golden tassels on her boots fluttering with each step.

**乌尔里希**：哈啊……我就知道，我真的不擅长做演讲，特别是临场状态下。\
**Ulrich**: Hah. Improvised speeches never really were my thing.

**乌尔里希**：谈判破裂了，护卫兵！\
**Ulrich**: Negotiations have failed. Guard!

飞刀快速地划开了缚手的绑带。\
A throwing knife slices through the restraints.

护卫兵脱困的双手立刻搭上了被光学神秘术藏起来的手枪。\
The guard's freed hands immediately find a pistol, concealed by an optical arcane skill.

**护卫兵**：小心脚下。\
**Guard**: Watch your step!

雪灰飞扬而起，枪弹从白雾中穿出。\
Gunfire cuts through the swirling snow.

**莫莉德尔**：……啧，一个棘手的护卫。\
**Moldir**: Tch. She's a tricky one.

俘虏被押解上路，在雪上留下一深一浅的足印。\
The captives trudge onward, leaving uneven footprints in the snow.

在他们的前方，中尉昂首阔步，目不斜视。\
Ahead, Moldir marches with her head high, gaze fixed forward.

**护卫兵**：老板，目前情况较为危急，是否允许我使用……\
**Guard**: Boss, the situation's critical. Do I have your permission to use ...

窃窃私语传进前方带队的中尉耳中。\
The whispers drift up with the wind.

**莫莉德尔**：……看上去你们并不在意自己是否死到临头。\
**Moldir**: So close to death, yet you're still in the mood for chit-chat.

护卫兵弹了一下自己胸前的对讲机。\
The guard flicks the intercom on her chest.

**护卫兵**：战时特权，这个对讲机直连军事部长官。虽然这意味着行动失败，但只要我摁下它，就能直接向长官发送我们的坐标定位……\
**Guard**: This emergency intercom has a direct line to our commander in chief. If I press this button, our mission will fail, but it'll also send our coordinates to him.

**护卫兵**：作为叛军，你比我更清楚你的下场。\
**Guard**: And we both know what'll happen after that.

在前方带队的中尉并未回头。\
Moldir shows no trace of concern. She doesn't even turn back.

**莫莉德尔**：……那么您在等待什么？\
**Moldir**: What are you waiting for then?

**莫莉德尔**：直接拨通，我们早已做好准备。\
**Moldir**: Press it. We're ready.

中尉推开了科考站的门。\
Leading the way, Moldir pushes open the doors to the research station.

微弱的、此起彼伏的呻吟声从门内传出。\
Faint moans echo behind the door.

**莫莉德尔**：白手套队长、弗雷希特曼队长，你们在外面等我。\
**Moldir**: Sergeant White Gloves, Sergeant Frekhtman, please wait outside.

**莫莉德尔**：我想要好好和这两位客人聊聊。\
**Moldir**: I would like to have a private conversation with our guests.

随着陈旧开关被按下的脆响，一盏盏昏暗的灯次第亮起。\
With the click of an aged switch, dim lights flicker on one by one.

**护卫兵**：……？\
**Guard**: ...?

光线一点点驱散黑暗，呻吟的源头也一个个出现在了眼前。\
Light, dim and flickering as it is, dispels the darkness, revealing the sources of moans one by one.

**乌尔里希**：——这是……\
**Ulrich**: This is ...

科考站被改造成了野战医院，每一张床铺上都躺着一个虚弱的病患。\
The research station has been converted into a field hospital. Frail patients lie sprawled out on each cot.

**莫莉德尔**：——这是重塑之手遗留的罪孽。\
**Moldir**: The aftermath of Manus Vindictae's actions.

中尉的脸被白炽灯照亮了一半。\
Moldir's face is half-shrouded under the dim lights.

**莫莉德尔**：他们在南极屠戮了数个科考站，一些人已经遇难，还有一些人被带去了他们的驻地，原因不详。\
**Moldir**: They have slaughtered researchers from stations across Antarctica. Most died immediately, while others were taken to their base. They didn't tell us why.

**莫莉德尔**：而剩下一息尚存的……我们沿路救下后，全部安置在这里了。\
**Moldir**: These are the people we found who were still breathing.

**乌尔里希**：……他们都是人类？\
**Ulrich**: Are they all humans?

愤怒的波动在磁流体的闪烁中清晰可见。\
His indignation is clear enough.

**莫莉德尔**：大多是的——当然其中也有我们的同僚。\
**Moldir**: For the most part. There are some of our kind, too.

中尉走到一张床铺边，轻轻将病患放在被子外的手塞进温暖的被褥里。\
She approaches a cot and gently tucks the patient's hand back under the warm blankets.

**莫莉德尔**：抵达南极后，部分队员在重塑之手驻地外受到了某种影响……有人长久地迷失在了暴雪里，等被我们找到时，已经精神崩溃。\
**Moldir**: When we first arrived in Antarctica, we were hit by a blizzard near Manus Vindictae's base. We lost some of our men in it. By the time we found them, they had all suffered serious mental breakdowns.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲曾向我们承诺一个“保护”……\
**Moldir**: Father promised us a "shelter."

**莫莉德尔**：但安德烈小队全员都已经失去了坚定的意志，他们脱离了我们的队伍，成为了面具之下的狂热追随者。\
**Moldir**: But now, everyone in Andrea's team has donned the mask and become a mad follower of the Manus.

**护卫兵**：……我知道失去战友是什么感受。\
**Guard**: I know how it feels to lose your comrades.

似乎有更多隐情，护卫兵最终选择沉默。\
Some untold story lingers, but the guard chooses silence.

巡查过所有病患的情况后，中尉最终停在一张方桌前。暖色的台灯将她的身影描出一轮金边。\
After inspecting each patient, Moldir halts at a square desk, her silhouette gilded in the lamp's amber glow.

**莫莉德尔**：我向你们摊牌。\
**Moldir**: Alright, I'm putting all my cards on the table.

**莫莉德尔**：面前的现状对你我都不利。\
**Moldir**: The current situation isn't good for either of us.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：想要破局，唯有进行一些互利的信息交换。\
**Moldir**: We need to trade information if we want to stay in the game.

## 10TH-10 荒野的呼唤 / The Call of the Wild

**诺谛卡**：奇怪……\
**Nautika**: That's odd.

诺谛卡低头看着自己的地图，又抬头看向周围的雪坡与山脉。反复几次，试图寻找熟悉的地标。\
Nautika looks down at her map, then up at the surrounding snow slopes and peaks. She repeats this several times, searching for familiar landmarks.

**十四行诗**：我们……迷路了？\
**Sonetto**: Are we lost?

**诺谛卡**：我的队伍曾两次深入到遗址外围，入口应该就在附近没有错……\
**Nautika**: My team reached the outer perimeter of the ruins twice. The entrance should be right around here.

探险家紧张地搓着手指，手套沙沙作响。\
She rubs her gloved hands together, the fabric rustling softly.

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀，对不起……这里的地形和我印象中的完全不一样了……\
**Nautika**: S-Sorry, Vertin. The terrain here is nothing like I remember.

**无线电小姐**：顺便一提，我已经接收不到任何来自基金会的射频信号了。\
**Ms. Radio**: Just so you know, I've lost all radio reception from the Foundation.

**十四行诗**：没有明显地标，指南针失灵，地形与地图无法对应，接收不到信号。\
**Sonetto**: No signal, no landmarks, no working compass, and the terrain doesn't match what's on the map.

**十四行诗**：司辰，我们现在怎么办？\
**Sonetto**: What should we do now, Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

精力充沛的犬队只趴在雪里休息了片刻，便开始追逐起了彼此的尾巴。\
Their energetic sled dogs, after only a brief rest in the snow, start chasing each other's tails.

**诺谛卡**：嘿、嘿！不许抢我的手表，它可不是狗狗能玩的东西，去、去！\
**Nautika**: Hey! Hey! My watch is not for dogs! Give me that! Shoo, shoo!

诺谛卡珍惜地擦了擦古董手表表面的口水，把它收进了包里。\
Nautika wipes the drool off her antique watch before storing it safely in her pack.

群犬像乌洛波洛斯的环一样玩闹了起来，发出了快乐的呜咽。\
The dogs play in an Ouroboros-like circle, happy whimpers filling the air.

**维尔汀**：我有主意了，我想我们并不需要舍近求远……\
**Vertin**: I have an idea. In fact, the answer's right in front of us.

**诺谛卡**：——？\
**Nautika**: ...?

**维尔汀**：嘘——！来，看我。\
**Vertin**: Shh. Watch.

**十四行诗**：德洛丝医生的听诊器？\
**Sonetto**: Dr. Dores's stethoscope?

**十四行诗**：原来如此，我明白了——！\
**Sonetto**: Ah. You're right. It's been staring us right in the face.

**十四行诗**：抛开雪橇犬的工作属性，它们还有犬科动物的本质。\
**Sonetto**: The sled dogs are canines after all. They should have a sensitive sense of smell.

**维尔汀**：是的，让它们熟悉听诊器上残留的气味，说不定能找到她离去的方向……让我们祈祷这能奏效。\
**Vertin**: Yes, if we give them a moment to smell the stethoscope, they may be able to track down the scent left on it. Let's hope it works.

领头犬放过了伙伴湿漉漉的尾巴，低头嗅闻起了听诊器。\
The lead dog releases its companion's soggy tail and lowers its snout to sniff the stethoscope.

**雪橇犬**：汪——！呜汪！\
**Sled Dog**: Woof! Woof woof!

**诺谛卡**：它们有反应了！\
**Nautika**: They—They smelled something!

**维尔汀**：快爬上它们的背。\
**Vertin**: Hop on their backs.

太阳不再落下，腹地的白昼被拉长到了永恒。\
The daylight that shines on this hinterland stretches into eternity.

失去参照物的移动在白色大地上似乎失去了意义，正如无人知道雪橇犬在急停前奔驰了多长时间。\
Movement across the icy wastes seems meaningless without reference points, just as none could say how long the sled dogs run before their sudden halt.

**诺谛卡**：我们成功了！这儿就是我的队伍曾经到过的地方！\
**Nautika**: We made it. This is where my team went before.

她拉起缰绳，犬队随训而停。\
She pulls the harness, and the sled dogs obey in a steady and contented stop.

**耳朵虫**：“引路人的出现转瞬即逝，虔诚者若已在路上，请吹响同路的歌谣。”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "The guide appears, then fades from human sight; If the devoted journey, let their songs unite."

**诺谛卡**：小耳朵虫说得对，地母的指引没有错！和你们一起上路果然是正确的决定。\
**Nautika**: Máhtu was right. The Mother Spirit was right. It was the right decision to join you.

同行者纷纷跳下犬背。\
The companions pat the dogs as they dismount.

**十四行诗**：……我们这是在哪里？山谷里的迷宫？\
**Sonetto**: Where are we? A labyrinth in a valley?

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱相信这里是遗址外围，只要穿过这个山谷，我们就能在隘口后找到真正的遗址——一座神庙，甚至可能是一座城市。\
**Nautika**: Friele believed that these were the only outskirts of the site. She said that if we passed through the valley, we might even find the real ruins of a temple, or a city even.

**诺谛卡**：快看这石壁，上面有人工开凿的痕迹——\
**Nautika**: Look at this stone wall. There are excavation marks on it.

**诺谛卡**：上次队伍到这儿时撞上了反常的白化气候，那些雪雾让我们什么都没看到。\
**Nautika**: We ran into an abnormal whiteout last time. It was too dense. We couldn't make out any details.

探险家奔向最近的石壁，蹲下，摘下手套，用人类温暖的掌心抚摸冰封的岩石。\
She sprints to the nearest rock face, crouches, strips off a glove, and presses her warm palm against the frozen stone.

**十四行诗**：我从来没有见过这种岩石，是某种化石吗？\
**Sonetto**: I've never seen this kind of rock before. Is it some kind of fossil?

**诺谛卡**：是拉斑玄武岩，它们诞生在深海之底的大洋中脊，你瞧这些几何形的气孔和金色的矿物纹。\
**Nautika**: It's tholeiitic basalt. It forms at mid-ocean ridges, down at the bottom of the sea. Look at the geometric pores and the golden mineral veins.

**诺谛卡**：它们出现在陆地上，弗里莱会说这是四亿两千五百万年时间变迁下的奇迹。\
**Nautika**: If Friele were here, she'd call it a miracle. A once-in-a-425-million-year occurrence.

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱，弗里莱……她加入我们的队伍，就是为了在南极洲找到一块这样的石头，哪怕只有掌心大小……\
**Nautika**: Friele ... heh. She would have been so excited to see this, even if it is only the size of my palm. That's why she joined the expedition.

探险家垂下头，悄悄把石头捂热后揣进口袋里。\
Head bowed, she warms the rock before slipping it into her pocket,

就像将其视为某种珍视的生命。\
as if cradling some cherished lifeform.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

一阵轻微的震颤，神秘术的波动消失在飞散的霰雪中。\
After a faint tremor, the arcane fluctuation dissolves into flying snow pellets.

本能地向着那个方向迈出两步，步伐停止。\
Instinct carries her two steps forward before freezing.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**十四行诗**：司辰？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper?

视线被另一侧石壁下凸起的雪堆所吸引。\
Her sight has locked onto an anomalous snow mound at the base of the opposite rock face.

**维尔汀**：不是错觉……\
**Vertin**: Not an illusion.

蹲下身子，拂去上面的积雪。\
Crouching, she brushes away the accumulated powder.

一台便携式古典打字机。\
A portable vintage typewriter.

**十四行诗**：我在档案里见过这台打字机……白朗姆女士和娜娜都曾描述过它。\
**Sonetto**: I read about this typewriter in the file. Ms. White Rum and Nala also mentioned it.

在这个时代，它印出过落水者简短的病历，参与了圣保罗喧闹的夜晚，也见证了乌斯怀亚的小小社会。\
In this era, it typed terse medical records for the drowning girl, recorded São Paulo's raucous nights, and bore witness to Ushuaia's poetry society.

**维尔汀**：没错——德洛丝医生的打字机。\
**Vertin**: That's right. This is Dr. Dores's typewriter.

**十四行诗**：又一件属于她的物品……是否过于巧合了？\
**Sonetto**: Another one of her belongings. Is it too coincidental to be mere chance?

**十四行诗**：咳、咳咳……上面沾了一层什么？鳞粉？\
**Sonetto**: *cough* What's this all over it? Scale powder?

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**十四行诗**：血迹，已经干透了。\
**Sonetto**: Blood. It's dry.

企鹅，海豹，科考站里的遇难者。\
Penguins, seals, or the fallen at the research station.

血迹可能属于任何人，也可能来自德洛丝医生。\
The bloodstains could belong to anyone, including Doctor Dores.

**维尔汀**：不管是有人故意引导还是单纯的巧合，至少这证明了我们的方向是对的。\
**Vertin**: Whether these were left intentionally or not, this proves that we're heading in the right direction.

**十四行诗**：上面的血迹……德洛丝医生可能受伤了，我们得尽快找到她。\
**Sonetto**: So much blood. She may be injured. We need to find her as soon as possible.

所有人都聚了过来，包括躺在雪橇犬身上的无线电小姐。\
Everyone crowds around, including Ms. Radio, who had been lying on one of the dogs.

光秃秃的山体屹立两侧，林立的玄武岩石壁迷宫般镇守在隘口前，迷宫的尽头也被薄雾掩藏着。\
Barren mountains flank them on both sides, a stone labyrinth of basalt standing sentinel at the pass, its end shrouded in mist.

**雪橇犬**：……\
**Sled Dog**: ...

领头犬凑了过来，似乎有什么发现一般地抬起头，警惕地望向某个方向。\
The lead dog approaches, then raises its head, alerted to some unseen threat.

**雪橇犬**：汪——！汪汪！\
**Sled Dog**: Woof! Woof woof!

**无线电小姐**：等等！\
**Ms. Radio**: Wait!

**无线电小姐**：——天啊！你们要带我去哪儿？！\
**Ms. Radio**: Holy—! Where are you taking me?

**诺谛卡**：停下！停下！\
**Nautika**: Stop! Whoa!

探险家把两指贴在下唇，急促地吹了几声犬哨。\
Nautika presses two fingers to her lips and issues sharp whistle commands.

**雪橇犬**：汪——呜！\
**Sled Dog**: Woof! Woof—

飞驰的步伐踩在松软的雪上，扰乱了最忠诚的朋友们的耳朵。\
Their paws churn the soft snow, drowning out the whistle commands meant for the loyal friends.

兴奋的犬队带着可怜的无线电小姐一起冲进了石壁迷宫，消失在了眼前。\
The excited sled dogs charge into the labyrinth, carrying the helpless Ms. Radio with them, and soon disappear from view.

**诺谛卡**：追不上了……这、这可怎么办……\
**Nautika**: They're gone. W-What do we do now?

**维尔汀**：乐观地想，它们只是先我们一步穿越了隘口。我们也出发吧。\
**Vertin**: Think positively. Perhaps they'll just get there before us. Let's go after them.

犬队的跑动似乎也惊扰到了藏匿起来的生命体，雪地表面开始颤抖起来。\
Their movement triggers something hidden, causing the snowfield around them to shake.

**十四行诗**：……？等一下，这里有躲藏起来的魔精！\
**Sonetto**: Wait, there are critters hiding out nearby.

**十四行诗**：果然……司辰，小心！\
**Sonetto**: There they are. Timekeeper, watch out!

## 10TH-11 雪上足迹 / Des pas sur la neige

**诺谛卡**：二位……\
**Nautika**: Umm, guys ...

长久的步行后，探险家终于疲惫地开口。\
Exhausted, Nautika finally breaks the silence of their long trek.

第一助手挥舞玻璃笔，术法在时间的奇迹上刻下一个小小的“Ⅵ”。\
The chief assistant waves her glasfeder, inscribing a tiny "VI" beside them.

在它左边，是前五个序列的数字。\
To its left are the five preceding numerals in solemn sequence.

**维尔汀**：我们注意到了，诺谛卡。这已经是我们第六次路过这面石壁了。\
**Vertin**: Yes, Nautika, we noticed it too. This is the sixth time we've passed this stone wall.

**十四行诗**：恐怕次数要更多，在我们意识到一直在附近转圈前，时间已经走过了十五分钟。\
**Sonetto**: It might even be more than the sixth time. We walked for 15 minutes before we realized we were going in circles.

**十四行诗**：司辰，我们现在必须面对一个事实：我们被困在这处石壁迷宫中了。\
**Sonetto**: I'm afraid we have to face the fact that we're trapped in this labyrinth, Timekeeper.

**诺谛卡**：……就像那些民俗故事里说的一样……\
**Nautika**: Just like in the legends.

**诺谛卡**：“黑森林传说”“无法离开的十字路口”“闹鬼的夕阳循环”……\
**Nautika**: "The Black Forest," "The Demon of the Crossroads," "The Twilight Loop" ...

**十四行诗**：请、请等一等，诺谛卡小姐。\
**Sonetto**: W-Wait, Ms. Amundsen ...

**十四行诗**：……我们要以辩证的思维来观察，不能武断做下有骚灵作乱的判断。\
**Sonetto**: We need to think dialectically. Let's not jump straight to evil spirits.

**十四行诗**：或许是什么人利用了神秘术……\
**Sonetto**: It could be the result of some kind of arcane skill.

**维尔汀**：遗憾的是，我现在没有感知到任何神秘术痕迹。\
**Vertin**: I had the same thought, but I don't sense any arcane fluctuations around here.

**维尔汀**：不过无线电小姐和雪橇犬们不会毫无理由地消失，这里一定存在隐藏的出口或其他奥秘。\
**Vertin**: That said, Ms. Radio and the sled dogs couldn't just vanish into thin air. There must be a hidden exit, or something else at play here.

探险家呼出一口白气，紧张地跺了跺脚，在松软的雪上踩出沙沙的声响。\
Nautika stomps back and forth, soft snow rustling under her feet.

**诺谛卡**：让我来试试吧？\
**Nautika**: Let me give it a try.

**诺谛卡**：我虽然不是神秘学家，但作为极地科考队员，我还有些人类的笨办法……\
**Nautika**: I may not be an arcanist, but we human explorers have our ways.

探险家取下行囊，开始在如山的极地装备中寻找决定性的助力。\
She begins rummaging through a mountain of gear, searching for a vital tool.

机械齿轮尽忠职守地转动着，一如半个世纪前，它也在这片冰冻的土地上转动过一样。\
The mechanical gears turn dutifully, just as they had half a century ago on this same frozen ground.

**诺谛卡**：如何通过时钟与太阳的位置判断方向还是祖父教我的。出发来南极前，我把他的手表也带上了。\
**Nautika**: My grandfather taught me how to tell the directions using a watch and the position of the sun. I have his watch right here. I took it with me.

**诺谛卡**：让我想想他是怎么说的，让时针指向太阳，平分时针与12点的那条线指向南方……\
**Nautika**: Let me see. What was it again? Point the hour hand toward the sun, and bisect the angle between the hour hand and 12 o'clock to find the south.

**诺谛卡**：对了，这里是南半球，所以平分线应该是指向北方！\
**Nautika**: Wait, we're in the Southern Hemisphere, so it actually points north.

**诺谛卡**：幸好还没有进入极夜时期，还有太阳可以参考……\
**Nautika**: Thankfully, we aren't in the polar night yet. We still have the sun in the sky.

然而很快，兴奋的探究落于沉默。\
Her excitement soon falls into silence.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

探险家摇了摇头，像犰狳一般微微蜷缩了起来。\
Nautika shakes her head and curls up, giving the appearance of a startled armadillo.

**诺谛卡**：没有……没有太阳。\
**Nautika**: Th-There's no sun.

北方，南方，西方，东方。天空的每个方向都覆盖着厚厚的云翳。\
North, south, west, east. The sky is smothered under thick clouds in every direction.

雪和雾的漫反射带来了足够的光线，但目之所及处，不见红色恒星。\
Snow and mist scatter enough light to see. The now-red sun lies hidden away.

**维尔汀**：重塑之手的仪式影响了正常的晨昏交替……\
**Vertin**: Manus Vindictae's ritual is affecting the day and night cycle.

**十四行诗**：没关系的，诺谛卡小姐。一定还有其他办法。\
**Sonetto**: Don't worry, Ms. Amundsen. There must be another way.

**十四行诗**：司辰，我提议先尝试撤出这片区域。\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, I suggest we try to exit this area first.

**维尔汀**：我同意，不能继续冒进了。\
**Vertin**: Agreed. We can't afford to risk any more time in here.

**十四行诗**：呼……\
**Sonetto**: *panting*

**诺谛卡**：撤不出去……我们、我们又回来了。\
**Nautika**: We, ah ... We're back at the beginning again.

**十四行诗**：我一直在留意雪橇犬的脚印。虽然我们是跟着脚印走的，但我们似乎只是在绕圈子。\
**Sonetto**: I've been keeping an eye on the sled dogs' footprints. We've been following them all this time, yet we still seem to be going in circles.

**十四行诗**：……它们是怎么带着无线电小姐消失的呢？\
**Sonetto**: How did they disappear along with Ms. Radio?

**诺谛卡**：这、这是什么只有狗狗能走出去的陷阱吗？我、我不想永远被困在这里……\
**Nautika**: Is-Is this a trap? A trap that only lets dogs leave? I-I don't wanna be stuck here forever.

**诺谛卡**：遗址就在隘口后面……真的不能进去看看了吗？\
**Nautika**: The ruins are just behind the pass. They're so, so close. Is it really impossible to get there?

**诺谛卡**：耳朵虫明明告诉我，这次是不一样的……我从未如此接近过……\
**Nautika**: But—but Máhtu told me that it's different this time. This is the closest I've ever been.

探险家声音颤抖，看向远方的眼神却充满了渴望与期待。\
Her voice shakes as she looks into the distance, brimming with expectation.

**耳朵虫**：“祂的光芒普洒大地，而祂的意志流连万千。”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "Across this land the Mother's light is sown. And through all things, Her spirit clearly shown."

**诺谛卡**：我就是为此而来的……\
**Nautika**: This is what I came for.

迷宫尽头传来的犬吠因距离而变得含糊不清。\
Faint barking drifts out from the labyrinth's end, distorted by distance.

不到一英里的距离，在迷宫影响下被拉长得有如天堑。\
It ought to be less than a mile away but seems now to extend into an unimaginably vast space, distorted by the labyrinth's power.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：雪橇犬是闻了打字机上德洛丝医生的气味，才狂奔出去的。\
**Vertin**: The sled dogs followed Dr. Dores's scent from the typewriter.

**十四行诗**：的确如此。\
**Sonetto**: That's right.

**十四行诗**：如果这个迷宫没有扭曲声音的传播，那么它们的声音确实是从尽头传来的——也就是遗址的方向。\
**Sonetto**: And the direction of their barking is consistent. So, unless the labyrinth has been designed to carry sound in a particular direction, they must have made it through to the other side, where the ruins are.

**十四行诗**：这说明德洛丝医生已经成功地穿越了这个地区。\
**Sonetto**: Which means Dr. Dores must've made it through the labyrinth too.

**维尔汀**：没错。\
**Vertin**: Exactly.

**维尔汀**：虽然不能确定她是否受到了其他人的引导，但如果我们假设她一直是孤身一人……\
**Vertin**: Although we can't be sure whether she was guided here, let's assume that she was alone.

**十四行诗**：——！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

**十四行诗**：目盲的她没有被这些石壁困住。\
**Sonetto**: Then, despite the fact that she's blind, somehow she didn't get trapped by these stone walls.

**诺谛卡**：你们要找的那位德洛丝医生，她看不见吗？\
**Nautika**: This Dr. Dores you're looking for—she's blind?

探险家惊讶地深吸一口气，把头从雪里拔了出来。\
Nautika gasps in surprise, lifting her head from the snow.

**维尔汀**：是的，她总是用眼罩或绷带藏着自己的眼睛，始终如此。\
**Vertin**: Yes. She always covers her eyes with a patch or bandage.

一种认真出现在探险家年轻的脸上。\
A look of intense focus settles on Nautika's face.

**诺谛卡**：“巨人人母之骨是必经之路，血染的苦痛使子民永生顿悟。”\
**Nautika**: "Through the Giant Mother's bones the path is laid. In bloody pain, eternal life is made."

**诺谛卡**：“去行无目先知所行之路罢，因现实永远流转于夜之尽头。”\
**Nautika**: "The blind seer walks, and we her path do take. For all will shift in the evernight's wake."

**十四行诗**：这也是地母传说中的箴言吗？\
**Sonetto**: Are those proverbs from the legend of the Mother Spirit?

**诺谛卡**：没错。\
**Nautika**: Yes, they are.

**十四行诗**：在诺谛卡小姐家乡流传的民间神话，地母传说……真的能够指向对现实经验的印证吗？\
**Sonetto**: Could this folk tale from your hometown actually derive from reality?

**诺谛卡**：在我的家乡，也有很多人觉得这句话只是代表了人们对极夜后即将来临的春日的期待，但我总觉得这些传说和颂词有另一层意思。\
**Nautika**: Even in my hometown, many people think this proverb is an expression of the peoples' want for spring after the long polar night. But I've always thought that there is something else behind it.

**诺谛卡**：你看……\
**Nautika**: You see ...

**诺谛卡**：盲眼的德洛丝医生没有被困住，依靠嗅觉的雪橇犬们也穿过了迷宫。\
**Nautika**: The blind Dr. Dores wasn't trapped, and the dogs who followed their noses also made it through the labyrinth.

**诺谛卡**：我们用眼睛丈量距离，用眼睛记录地标，还试图用太阳确定方位……我们和他们的区别，就在于我们一直依赖视力向前走。\
**Nautika**: We looked around this labyrinth, we looked for landmarks and for clues, we even looked for the sun to guide us ... We looked. That's the difference between us and them. We've only been using our eyes.

**十四行诗**：也就是说……\
**Sonetto**: Are you saying that ...

**诺谛卡**：闭上眼，世界将向我们显露它真正的方向。\
**Nautika**: Maybe, if we close our eyes, the true direction will be revealed.

**37**：闭上眼睛，维尔汀。\
**37**: Close your eyes, Vertin.

**37**：肉体的眼睛闭合之时，心灵的眼睛方能睁开。\
**37**: Only when your eyes are closed will your mind open up.

直白的线索，简单的推论，熟悉的理论。\
Clear clues, simple deductions, familiar theories.

**维尔汀**：值得一试，毕竟，我们暂时没有其他办法走出这座“迷宫”。\
**Vertin**: It's worth a try. We don't have any other ideas at the moment.

**维尔汀**：我们相信你。\
**Vertin**: We trust you.

冻得冰凉的手与手紧握着。\
Their ice-cold hands clasp together.

**维尔汀**：那么，准备好在黑暗中行走了吗，二位？\
**Vertin**: Are you ready to walk in darkness, ladies?

闭上眼。\
She closes her eyes.

## 10TH-12 拉普拉斯式希望 / Just Another Laplace Experiment

他只继续在险阻中前进，一面思前想后，\
There was a saviour Rarer than radium, Commoner than water, crueller than truth; Children kept from the sun Assembled at his tongue To hear the golden note turn in a groove, Prisoners of wishes locked their eyes In the jails and studies of his keyless smiles. —Dylan Thomas\
The edge of the world resists change in its own way.

忖度胸中回绕着的种种思念，\
Frozen soil, stagnant time, and roaring winds.

并愿贤良的人们也这样在孤独中静观。\
Yet the battleship's armored prow surges forward, blast waves shattering every obstacle.

——弥尔顿《复乐园》

有一位救世主 比镭更稀有， 比水更寻常，比真理更冰冷； 孩子们瞒过太阳 聚集于其舌尖 倾听于唱片中传出的金色曲调， 希望的囚徒们目不转睛地 盯着这监牢，打量着他脸上那无法猜测的微笑。 ——迪伦·托马斯\
Magnus's scream sinks beneath the sea, staining the thick ice crimson.

世界的尽头在用它的方式抗拒改变。\
冰封的土壤，停滞的时间和咆哮的西风。\
但战舰的重型装甲和爆炸冲击波还是一往无前地撞开了所有阻碍。\
马格努斯的嘶鸣沉入了海底，厚重的浮冰被染成了红色。

**大副**：目标已从雷达上消失，声呐无反应——敌方的马格努斯潜艇已确认被全数歼灭！\
**First Mate**: Radar's out, no sonar contact. Targets eliminated. We got them.

**舰长Ⅰ**：我们取得了一场险胜，但还不能放松警惕。\
**Captain I**: Good work, everyone, but let's not start celebrating yet.

**舰长Ⅰ**：浮冰越来越厚了，我们即将驶入冰区。通知舰桥全员，降低速度回避碰撞。\
**Captain I**: The ice is getting thicker. We are entering an ice zone. Notify all bridge personnel to reduce speed.

**舰长Ⅰ**：机械员，汇报船身受损情况。\
**Captain I**: Engineer, what's the damage report?

**海军士兵Ⅰ**：报告长官，敌方马格努斯潜艇的进攻导致了左侧螺旋桨故障，转向系统仅存有约20%的动力。\
**Triglav Crewman I**: The Magnus hit our portside propeller. We're down to about 20% thrust on the steering, sir.

**海军士兵Ⅱ**：——报告长官！\
**Triglav Crewman II**: Sir!

哨兵推门而入。\
The sentry bursts through the door.

**海军士兵Ⅱ**：冰山——一座冰山正从十二点钟方向朝我们高速移动！\
**Triglav Crewman II**: Visual on an iceberg at 12 o'clock! It's closing in fast!

舰长凑到高倍望远镜前方。\
The captain leans into the high-powered telescope.

**大副**：高速移动的冰山？我说了很多次不要盯着冰山和雪地看！容易出现幻觉。\
**First Mate**: A speeding iceberg? Really? What did I tell you about staring at the snow too long? It messes with your visi—

大副也拿起望远镜，放在自己眼前。\
The first mate takes the telescope next.

**大副**：**的[韦加耶沃脏话]，这根本不是冰山！\
**First Mate**: F**k! That's no iceberg!

**大副**：那是块结了冰的鱼鳍——是个动物！这**的究竟是什么玩意？！\
**First Mate**: It's a fin! A massive one! Something's under the water!

**舰长Ⅰ**：——利维坦巨兽！\
**Captain I**: A Leviathan!

舰长打了个寒颤，果断下达指令。\
A shiver runs down the captain's spine.

**舰长Ⅰ**：特里格拉夫号，全系统发射！\
**Captain I**: Triglav, all systems engage!

武器瞄准系统第一时间启动，但战列舰底部率先受到了重创。\
Weapon targeting systems whir alive, but the bottom of the battleship takes the first brutal hit.

**舰长Ⅰ**：各单位报告受损情况！\
**Captain I**: All units, report your status!

**海军士兵Ⅰ**：主炮塔的弹药库进水！\
**Triglav Crewman I**: Water in main battery magazine!

**海军士兵Ⅰ**：所有水密隔舱都受到了结构性挤压——船长！我们正在沉没！\
**Triglav Crewman I**: All watertight compartments are under pressure. Captain, we're going down!

**舰长Ⅰ**：……我清楚。\
**Captain I**: Understood.

近处的海面上燃起了大火，护卫舰储油仓在爆炸中被点燃。\
Flames erupt across the nearby sea as the frigate's fuel tanks ignite in the blast.

**舰长Ⅰ**：特里格拉夫号战列舰及三艘护卫舰，均进行过神秘术改造。这是我们的骄傲……\
**Captain I**: For all these years, we have fought side by side with Triglav and her three frigates. Not once have these old girls let us down.

**大副**：居然派出了利维坦巨兽这种级别的生物兵器……看来重塑之手是倾尽全力要阻止我们登陆了。\
**First Mate**: The Manus must be desperate to stop our landing—sending a Leviathan after us, of all things.

舰长望向近在咫尺的庞然巨物。它尖声嘶叫着，带着足以吞没汪洋的躁意再度发起冲锋——\
The captain stares out at the colossal creature as it looms closer and closer. Its piercing shriek tears through the air as a prelude to another charge.

**舰长Ⅰ**：很可惜，基金会的战力不会全员被封死在罗斯海。\
**Captain I**: Let them try. The Foundation will not be stopped at the Ross Sea.

舰长按下胸前的通讯器。\
The captain presses the communicator on his chest.

**舰长Ⅰ**：报告长官，特里格拉夫号即将引爆神秘术阵。\
**Captain I**: Triglav to Operations—initiating detonation of the onboard array.

**索姆将军**：……\
**Admiral Somme**: ...

通讯器那头传来一丝杂音，信号中断于南极上空。\
Static hisses briefly before the signal dies over Antarctica.

只消片刻，指令有条不紊地被再次下达。\
Yet within moments, precise and clear orders are reissued.

**索姆将军**：迪达号，回避冰区，进入A2防线。\
**Admiral Somme**: Operations to Dida—steer clear of the ice zone, fall back to defense line A2.

**莫莉德尔**：你们来时穿越了罗斯海的正面战场，应该亲眼见证过海上战况是如何焦灼。\
**Moldir**: You made your way here through the Ross Sea. The front lines must've given you a grim taste of the war.

**莫莉德尔**：为了仪式的顺利进行，重塑之手不惜付出一切代价阻止基金会登陆南极。\
**Moldir**: The Manus won't let the Foundation set foot on Antarctica—not without a fight. The ritual is too important. They will stop at nothing to see it happen.

**莫莉德尔**：为表达诚意，我可以提供重塑之手在南极的布局情报。\
**Moldir**: So here's my offer: reciprocity. As a gesture of good faith, allow me to share some intel on their movements with you first.

**莫莉德尔**：——一切都围绕着他们要举办仪式的地点，腹地中的遗址城。\
**Moldir**: There's a ruin of an ancient city deep in the heart of Antarctica. That is where the ritual will be held.

**乌尔里希**：遗址城？\
**Ulrich**: A ruin? Here?

**莫莉德尔**：日常祭祀、仪式筹备、机要会谈……可以说，那座背靠山体的遗址城就是重塑之手在南极的巢穴。\
**Moldir**: Against that mountain, yes. But it isn't just any ruin. It's Manus Vindictae's stronghold. Rituals, preparations, high-level meetings—that is where they all happen.

**莫莉德尔**：为守住登岸口，启明会、天使兄弟会和前芝诺近卫团等数支队伍，分别被安排驻守在爱德华七世半岛、玛丽·伯德地、塞尔马尼岛以及乔治五世海岸。\
**Moldir**: In order to secure the continent, they have fortified the coastlines, covering every possible landing point. The Order of Enlightenment is stationed at King Edward VII Peninsula, the Apostles Brotherhood controls Marie Byrd Land, and the former Zeno Sentinel Unit has deployed its forces along King George V Coast.

**莫莉德尔**：除了南极环境提供的天然防御，重塑还在近海防线布置了大量经改造的神秘学生物，其中包括了数只马格努斯及一匹利维坦巨兽。\
**Moldir**: The terrain is already a natural fortress, but that wasn't enough for them. They have deployed a number of arcane-modified beasts. Several Magnus and a Leviathan, if my intel is correct.

**护卫兵**：不是吧……利维坦巨兽？听上去足以推平澳大利亚……\
**Guard**: Whoa. No way. A Leviathan? I heard you could sink Australia with one of those things.

中尉转身，侧耳倾听着通讯器中传来的战报。\
Moldir presses the communicator to her ear as battle reports crackle through.

**莫莉德尔**：而基金会的中坚战力，特里格拉夫号——已经和利维坦巨兽同归于尽了。\
**Moldir**: Not anymore. The Triglav just blew it up and sank with it in the explosion. She was one of the Foundation's best battleships.

**莫莉德尔**：正面战场比想象中的要更加激烈。我不建议你们寄希望于基金会大部队能提供更多支援，他们自顾不暇。\
**Moldir**: A heavy price to pay to only reach a stalemate. If I were you, I wouldn't count on support from the Foundation forces. They're already spread thin just holding the front line.

**莫莉德尔**：如果我是你，第一时间需要考虑的就是如何在没有后援的情况下完成任务。\
**Moldir**: You need a plan to complete your mission without their help.

**莫莉德尔**：而当进行过这样的思考后，你就会发现我手上这份能够避开所有重塑之手的地图，是眼下唯一的出路。\
**Moldir**: And if you're as smart as I hope you are, you will see that this map is your best shot at reaching the city without getting caught in their territory.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

**护卫兵**：……老板，最好小心一点，别掉进这个女人的局里。\
**Guard**: It all sounds too convenient, boss. We've got no clue what she's really up to.

然而磁流体的玻璃缸脑袋却始终低垂，只听到电路噼啪作响。\
Ulrich's head remains bowed, only the crackle of circuits breaking his silence.

**莫莉德尔**：你可以不相信我。\
**Moldir**: Fair enough.

**莫莉德尔**：那我们的交集也就到此为止了，我将按照将军的命令执行我的任务。\
**Moldir**: But know that the admiral has ordered the coastline be sealed, I can't let you pass—at least, not without a deal.

**莫莉德尔**：无论你来到南极是为了什么，我对此都只能爱莫能助。\
**Moldir**: Whatever your purpose is, you won't make it further without some assistance.

**乌尔里希**：……好吧。\
**Ulrich**: Fine.

**护卫兵**：老板？\
**Guard**: Seriously?

磁流体抬起头，停留在一个稳定的形状。\
He lifts his fishbowl head, the fluid remaining in a steady flow.

**乌尔里希**：我需要赶到举行仪式的地方，与司辰会合。\
**Ulrich**: I'm meeting with the Timekeeper at the site of the ritual.

**护卫兵**：唉……\
**Guard**: *sigh* Brilliant.

这次轮到护卫兵垂下脑袋，放弃挣扎一般。\
Now it's the guard who lowers her head, as if surrendering to defeat.

**莫莉德尔**：为了什么？\
**Moldir**: What's the Timekeeper doing there?

组长抬起被缚的手。\
Ulrich raises his tied hands.

**乌尔里希**：先放开我们。\
**Ulrich**: I'm not saying another word until you remove these cuffs.

**莫莉德尔**：就凭刚刚那句没来由的信息？\
**Moldir**: You think you're in a position to bargain?

**乌尔里希**：——为了表达诚意，还记得吗？这可不是有诚意的表现。\
**Ulrich**: Bargain? You were the one suggesting reciprocity. Hardly seems reciprocal to keep us locked up, don't you think?

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

钥匙卡进手铐锁眼，锁舌被转开，重获自由的俘虏松了松手腕。\
The key clicks into the handcuff's lock, the bolt turns, and then the now freed captive flexes his wrists.

**乌尔里希**：那张被你收缴的唱片，就是一切的关键。\
**Ulrich**: We really are here because of a song. The record is the key to everything.

**乌尔里希**：第一场“暴雨”前的1995年，作为“星锑空间望远镜”项目的核心动力源，这张唱片与它的神秘学唱片机被搭载在一台卫星上，一起送进了太空轨道。\
**Ulrich**: In 1995, before the world was afflicted with the "Storm," this record—along with its arcane record player—was sent into space aboard the "Regulus Space Telescope," serving as the power source of the satellite.

**乌尔里希**：于轨道上流浪的十二年间，它持续拍摄着照片，并试图将数据传输回地面。\
**Ulrich**: For 12 years, it took pictures and transmitted them back to Earth.

**乌尔里希**：这台卫星最终因零件故障，2007年坠毁于奥尔德堡。除了这张唱片奇迹般地幸存外，其余设备仪器均已损毁。\
**Ulrich**: Then, in 2007, the satellite crashed near Aldeburgh, destroying everything but this record in the process.

**莫莉德尔**：2007年……？\
**Moldir**: 2007?

**莫莉德尔**：你指的是第六次“暴雨”后的1966年？\
**Moldir**: That would have been 1966, right after the sixth "Storm."

**乌尔里希**：是的。司辰小队一位来自该时代的摇滚爱好者回收了唱片，并将它带进了拉普拉斯。\
**Ulrich**: Precisely. A rock music enthusiast from that era found the record and later brought it to Laplace. She is now a member of the Timekeeper squad.

**乌尔里希**：但从照片上的时间戳来看，空间望远镜于2007年4月16日拍下了最后一张照片。\
**Ulrich**: The last image transmitted from the satellite was timestamped April 16, 2007.

**乌尔里希**：在第一场“暴雨”过后，它的时间依旧在向前。\
**Ulrich**: Even after the "Storm" sent everything back, the satellite's timeline kept moving forward.

**莫莉德尔**：——！\
**Moldir**: ...!

**莫莉德尔**：你在暗示——它穿越了“暴雨”，这怎么可能？\
**Moldir**: Are you saying that the satellite crossed the "Storm"? How?

**乌尔里希**：秘密就在这张唱片上。\
**Ulrich**: We believe it's because of this record.

**乌尔里希**：这张“星锑”唱片，是我们目前唯一验证过在“暴雨”中具有免疫性的材料。\
**Ulrich**: It's the only material that has been proven to be immune to the "Storm."

**乌尔里希**：在先前进行的实验中，它在一位研究员身上呈现出了抑制时代病特征的效果，并延缓了我身上的时代病发展进程。\
**Ulrich**: In our previous experiments, it reduced the severity of the Storm Syndrome afflicting one of our researchers and slowed its progression on me.

**莫莉德尔**：什么——？\
**Moldir**: Wait, what?

**乌尔里希**：但目前这一切仅止于理论和小范围封闭实验。针对“星锑”唱片的研究开始后，我们尚未遭遇一场真正的“暴雨”。\
**Ulrich**: But those results were from small-scale, isolated tests. We've never tried it in a real "Storm."

**乌尔里希**：由于“星锑”唱片不具备可复制性，“暴雨研究小组”对它的播放设备进行了一次改造升级。\
**Ulrich**: Since replicas of the record haven't demonstrated the same immunity as the original, we've developed an upgraded amplifier system for it.

**乌尔里希**：通过这台神秘学唱片机播放的“星锑”唱片，现在理论上可以生成辐射半径为二点五英里的免疫性磁场……\
**Ulrich**: Now, when played on our upgraded player, this record can create an immunity zone with a 2.5-mile radius.

**乌尔里希**：尽管“星锑”元素已经被证实会随唱片的播放而被消耗，但在我们的计算中，生成的磁场至少能持续十二分钟。\
**Ulrich**: But the immunity isn't permanent. We found that the element "Regulus" in the record is consumed every minute it plays. At best, we're looking at 12 minutes of protection with this original copy.

**乌尔里希**：计划的核心是……如果最坏的情况发生，重塑之手的仪式带来了一场“暴雨”，这张唱片能为基金会的作战人员带来一丝喘息的机会。\
**Ulrich**: If Manus Vindictae succeeds in triggering another "Storm" with their ritual, this record may be our last line of defense. That's why I've brought it here.

**乌尔里希**：我可以利用这张唱片，最大限度地帮助司辰，减小可能的伤亡。\
**Ulrich**: And that's why I need to get it to the Timekeeper. Should the worst happen, at least we can minimize the damage.

**乌尔里希**：同时我也能对其在真实“暴雨”环境下的效果进行求证，这对我们的研究来说至关重要。\
**Ulrich**: And I'll be able to see how it works during an actual "Storm"—an invaluable boon to our research.

**莫莉德尔**：看来，继开发了平衡伞后，科算中心的“暴雨”研究并没有止步不前。\
**Moldir**: Sounds like Laplace has made remarkable progress since the Equilibrium Umbrella.

**莫莉德尔**：……我很高兴你们再度取得了突破性的进展。\
**Moldir**: I have to say, I'm impressed.

**乌尔里希**：所以现在我能得到一些信息的回报了吗？\
**Ulrich**: So, there it is—all my cards on the table. What have you got for us?

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：真正举行仪式的地点，位于遗址城后孤峰的山体中，那里有一处更为隐秘的神殿。\
**Moldir**: The actual location of the ritual is in a sanctuary hidden in the heart of that mountain behind the city ruins.

**护卫兵**：老板，看上去她的态度并不真诚，你真的上当了。\
**Guard**: Hah, first a city, now a sanctuary? Boss, she's got to be messing with us.

**莫莉德尔**：不，这是实话……城中有一条通向山体内部的甬道，只有受到挑选与认可的人能踏入其中。\
**Moldir**: I am telling the truth. There's a tunnel in the city that leads into the mountain. Only the "chosen" are allowed through.

**莫莉德尔**：——而“敌人”一定会在那里设下重防。\
**Moldir**: And you can bet that the tunnel will be heavily guarded.

中尉侧身，消化着从拉普拉斯研究员处吸收的信息。\
Moldir turns aside, processing the information absorbed from Ulrich.

**莫莉德尔**：你刚才说，唱片机生成的稳定磁场半径为二点五英里，对吗？\
**Moldir**: 2.5 miles of immunity, you said?

**乌尔里希**：没错，这意味着我们至少要掌握遗址城的纵深及甬道的长度，才能计算出播放唱片的最佳坐标。\
**Ulrich**: That's right. I'll need to know the size of the city and the length of the tunnel to figure out the best placement for the record.

**莫莉德尔**：我有一个主意。\
**Moldir**: I have an idea.

**莫莉德尔**：冷凝系统掏空了山体，但它仍保留着自然的骨架——\
**Moldir**: The mountain's interior is hollow. The sanctuary sits right in the heart of it.

**莫莉德尔**：它曾是一座火山，一座可以攀登的死火山。\
**Moldir**: It used to be an active volcano, but it hasn't erupted for centuries.

**莫莉德尔**：而它的相对海拔是11616英尺……也就是不到2.2英里。\
**Moldir**: The elevation of the volcano is 11,616 feet. That's just under 2.2 miles.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

组长和他身旁的护卫兵对视了一眼。\
Ulrich exchanges a glance with the guard beside him.

**护卫兵**：等、等等……老板，你不会在认真考虑她的话吧？\
**Guard**: Boss, it's not exactly easy to tell what you're thinking, you know. Surely you're not taking her seriously, are you?

改造为临时医院的废弃科考站中钻出了三个人。\
Three figures emerge from the abandoned research station, now repurposed as a field hospital.

两位重获自由的俘虏整理好着装，即将启程。\
The two freed captives adjust their clothes, ready to depart.

中尉将地图递到护卫兵的手中。\
Moldir hands the map to the guard.

**莫莉德尔**：在极地攀登火山绝非易事，我在地图上标明了我们已探明的危险地区，至少你们可以挑选出更安全的路线。\
**Moldir**: Scaling the mountain isn't going to be easy. I have marked the dangerous areas on this map. Try to avoid them when planning your route.

护卫兵点点头，收下了地图。\
The guard nods and receives the map.

**莫莉德尔**：我只是提出一个意见，你们不必真的接受。\
**Moldir**: Before you go, let me make one thing clear. This is just my advice. Whether you take it or not is up to you.

**莫莉德尔**：用最小的单位，走最崎岖的道登山——这是一步险棋。\
**Moldir**: If just the two of you go up the mountain, you may keep yourselves out of the enemy's sights, but it will be highly dangerous. There will be no saving you if something goes wrong.

**乌尔里希**：你的提案只是暂时进入了备选，我们当然还有其他的方案。\
**Ulrich**: Of course. We'll weigh our options before we make a move.

**莫莉德尔**：……我明白了。\
**Moldir**: Good. Keep your head on straight, soldier.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

**乌尔里希**：我还是无法理解，你为什么要对我说实话？所谓的信息交换——你想从我这里得到什么？\
**Ulrich**: So, just like that, you're letting us walk out of here? With the record and a map? You call it "reciprocity," but what's in it for you?

寒风中，中尉似乎轻笑了一下。\
It may have just been the wind or a trick of the eye, but for a moment Moldir seems to smile.

**莫莉德尔**：阿尔卡纳死后，重塑之手以不同的名号四处出击，分散着基金会方面的注意力。\
**Moldir**: Arcana's death hasn't weakened Manus Vindictae. In fact, they have kept the Foundation very busy, taking different names and causing chaos around the world.

**莫莉德尔**：这样的策略让他们成功集结了大批信徒，并且在全世界眼皮子底下完成了迁徙，在苦寒之地搭建起举办仪式的舞台。\
**Moldir**: They rallied their followers, journeyed across the globe, and set the stage for their ritual on this barren land, and all right under everybody's noses.

**莫莉德尔**：与如此井井有条的布局相比，你们的计划犹如以卵击石。我不喜欢毫无胜算的进攻。\
**Moldir**: They planned every step, but you—you just barged in here with nothing but a record and an idea. If you were my soldiers, I would have thrown you out of my camp by now.

**莫莉德尔**：但……\
**Moldir**: That said ...

中尉郑重地将先前收缴的唱片物归原主。\
She returns the record to its rightful owner with a solemn gesture.

**莫莉德尔**：我更加不喜欢“暴雨”。\
**Moldir**: I would rather see the "Storm" end than see you fail.

磁流体双手接过失而复得的唱片。\
Ulrich accepts the record in turn.

**乌尔里希**：……\
**Ulrich**: ...

**乌尔里希**：……无论如何，还是谢谢你。\
**Ulrich**: Well then. Thank you for your help.

与对立阵营的代表最后握了握手，磁流体与护卫兵转身踏入雪地。\
After a final handshake, Ulrich turns toward the snowfield with his guard.

走了几步后，组长转身。\
A few steps later, he looks back.

◇ 乌尔里希：你不与我们一起吗？ ◇ 莫莉德尔：我？ ◇ 乌尔里希：不论是以卵击石也好，还是奇迹乍现也罢。 ◇ 乌尔里希：以你的立场来讲，不想来见证一下吗？ ◇ 莫莉德尔：我有军令在身。 磁流体闪烁了几下，不再多言，走入了渐起的粉雪中。 ◇ 莫莉德尔：……\
◇ Ulrich: Why don't you come with us? ◇ Moldir: Me? ◇ Ulrich: Look, we may be rushing in there like a couple of idiots, but if this works, if it really stops whatever scheme the Manus are brewing ... ◇ Ulrich: Don't you wanna see it for yourself? ◇ Moldir: It doesn't matter what I want. I have orders. His ferrofluid flickers a few times before he walks into the gathering powder snow without another word. ◇ Moldir: ...

## 10TH-13 九重城 / The Nine-Layered City

**维尔汀**：收到。非常及时的信息，乌尔里希组长。\
**Vertin**: I see. Thank you, Mr. Ulrich. This is exactly the information we needed.

**维尔汀**：理论上基金会在重塑之手内部的间谍也已抵达南极……\
**Vertin**: If everything's gone to plan, the Foundation's spy should already be in Antarctica.

**维尔汀**：但对方尚未与我们进行过接洽，无从得知关于仪式的更多情报。\
**Vertin**: But they haven't made contact with us yet. It seems we won't be getting any more intel on the ritual from them anytime soon.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：……你确定吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you certain?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：……我明白了。如果你决定这么做的话，之后的行动会非常危险，请务必小心。\
**Vertin**: Alright. If you've thought it through, I won't stand in your way. Just be careful, Mr. Ulrich.

**维尔汀**：乌尔里希组长？\
**Vertin**: Mr. Ulrich?

磁流体的声音归为一道杂音。\
Ulrich's voice dissolves into a static noise.

**维尔汀**：……信号中断了，不知道是哪一方的通讯器出了问题。\
**Vertin**: Signal's gone. I can't tell if it's an issue on his end or ours.

**维尔汀**：但乌尔里希组长传来了重要消息——举行仪式的神殿就藏在遗址城后的火山中。\
**Vertin**: Still, we got what we needed: the ritual will take place in a sanctuary hidden in the volcano at the edge of the city ruins.

众人不约而同看向了遗址城尽头的高山。\
As one, the group turns toward the towering mountain at the edge of the ruins.

**十四行诗**：要抵达那座火山，我们必须徒步穿越整座遗址城。\
**Sonetto**: That means we'll need to cross the city to get there.

**十四行诗**：我提议先与后方进行联络，将我们的发现汇报给基金会，请求增援。\
**Sonetto**: Perhaps it's best to report back to the Foundation and wait for reinforcements before going deeper.

**通讯器**：“哔哔——”\
**Communicator**: Beep-beep ...

**通讯器**：“滋——滋滋——”\
**Communicator**: Buzz ...

**维尔汀**：不行，通讯器彻底无法联通了。\
**Vertin**: I'm afraid comms are down.

**十四行诗**：恐怕这也是重塑之手的影响，就像腹地里反常的白昼一样。\
**Sonetto**: Could be another trick by Manus Vindictae, like the unnatural day-night cycle here.

**十四行诗**：司辰，或许我们应该先退回迷宫外？尝试恢复通讯，发送坐标，等待支援。\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, maybe we should fall back. Get out of here, fix the communicator, and call for support.

**维尔汀**：理应如此。但乌尔里希组长刚才提到，基金会舰队在南极举步维艰。\
**Vertin**: That would be the safest choice, but according to Mr. Ulrich, the Foundation is tied up on the front lines.

**维尔汀**：支援可能不会那么快就能到来，我担心如果等待与支援部队会合后再行动，会耽误太多时间。\
**Vertin**: I doubt they'd be able to come to our aid in time. Besides, with every passing minute, we fall that much further behind Dr. Dores.

**维尔汀**：我想先留在这里进行一些简单调查，搜寻德洛丝医生的下落。\
**Vertin**: I suggest we stay here and search the area. Perhaps we'll find something to point us in the right direction.

第一助手再次环顾了周围的环境。\
Sonetto scans the surroundings.

**十四行诗**：……视野范围内没有敌人的痕迹，我赞成司辰的提议。\
**Sonetto**: Well, there are no immediate signs of danger. It should be safe to look around.

基金会职员的目光游移着，最终落在了人类探险家身上。\
Sonetto's wandering gaze finally settles on their human explorer.

**十四行诗**：我们是否需要先护送诺谛卡小姐到安全的科考站？毕竟之后很可能会和重塑之手发生正面冲突……\
**Sonetto**: But before we proceed, should we escort Ms. Amundsen back to the research station? There's a high probability that we'll come into conflict with the Manus now that we're so close. She'd be safer there.

**诺谛卡**：回、回去？！可我好不容易才到了这里……\
**Nautika**: G-Go back? After all this?

蹲在地上写写画画的探险家猛地抬起头。\
Crouched on the ground sketching, Nautika's head jerks up.

**诺谛卡**：就是为了这座遗址，我才坚持了这么久……\
**Nautika**: These ruins ... They're the only thing that has kept me going.

捏着地图的手指逐渐攥紧，探险家怀着希冀和不甘，小声地发出了反抗。\
Her fingers tighten around the map as a whispered protest slips out, filled with both hope and defiance.

**诺谛卡**：我……我不想现在就回去。\
**Nautika**: No. I can't turn back now. I can't.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，我会和诺谛卡在外围进行探索。我向你保证，我们不会深入到城中。\
**Vertin**: It's okay, Sonetto. Nautika can come with me. We'll just look around the city's perimeter. You have my word.

**十四行诗**：……好，请一定注意安全。\
**Sonetto**: Alright. Please be careful.

点点头，迈开步子。\
She nods and strides forward.

积雪被风和时间压成了厚重结实的毯子，踏足其上，犹如踩进了一条迎宾的通道。\
The snow, compacted by wind and time into a thick blanket, forms a welcoming path underfoot.

探险家兴奋地吸了一口气，随即像雪地卡邦克鲁那样跳进了积雪里，遗址城白色的地面仿佛都因此震颤了一瞬。\
Nautika takes a breath, then leaps as gingerly as a hare. The white ground of the ruins seems to radiate from her impact.

**诺谛卡**：所以、所以我可以在这里进行考古了，对吗？\
**Nautika**: Ah. Then I can take some samples, right? Maybe even dig a little?

探险家的眼里闪动着激动而坚决的光。\
A determined gleam flickers in Nautika's eyes.

**十四行诗**：是的，诺谛卡小姐。但不能放松警惕，敌人可能藏在看不见的角落。\
**Sonetto**: Yes, but please keep an eye out for anything suspicious while you work. The Manus might be closer than we think.

**十四行诗**：请稍等片刻，让我为你再施一层温暖咒吧。\
**Sonetto**: Oh, and before you go, let me enhance the warming incantation on you.

第一助手轻轻踩上积雪。\
Sonetto steps lightly onto the snow.

**众人**：啊——！\
**All**: Urghhh!

**无线电小姐**：陷阱？！\
**Ms. Radio**: What in—Did we fall into a trap?

**无线电小姐**：各位？你们还好吧？\
**Ms. Radio**: Is everyone alright?

**诺谛卡**：这可真是……我的胳膊……\
**Nautika**: My arm ...

**十四行诗**：司辰，你没受伤吧？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper! Are you injured?

**维尔汀**：我没事。\
**Vertin**: I'm fine. Don't worry.

**诺谛卡**：塌陷的路面结了冰，又盖上了雪……呜，这是自然的陷阱……\
**Nautika**: The ground was probably already caved in. We must've stepped on the thin layer of ice left behind. Ugh, this happened back home once.

踩塌积雪陷阱的众人落在了一片柔软的半流体上。\
The group crashes through the snow trap, landing on a soft, semi-fluid surface.

**十四行诗**：我们这是掉到遗址的下一层了……理所应当的，这里也没有通讯信号。\
**Sonetto**: Looks like we've fallen into some underground part of the city ruins. No signal here, either.

**十四行诗**：我得赶紧找路回到入口，不能再耽误联系基金会的时间了。\
**Sonetto**: We need to get back to the surface and contact the Foundation as soon as possible.

**十四行诗**：——！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

试图从地上爬起的基金会职员脚下一滑，险些又一次栽倒在地。\
She tries to stand but slips, barely keeping her face from slamming into the ice.

**十四行诗**：这些东西是……\
**Sonetto**: This is ...

**诺谛卡**：——黑藻！\
**Nautika**: Black algae!

**诺谛卡**：还记得我说过的吗？踩在上面很容易摔倒，得避开它们走。\
**Nautika**: Careful! It's slippery, remember? You need to walk around it.

**维尔汀**：之前我就想问了，“黑藻”到底是？\
**Vertin**: I've been meaning to ask: what is black algae, exactly?

**诺谛卡**：最先发现这种黑藻的是奥兹，我们队伍里的神秘学生物学家。\
**Nautika**: Aase, my team's arcanobiologist, was the first to notice it.

**诺谛卡**：她认为这是一种由古老菌种和未知生物纤维构成的类藻生物，并验证了它的无毒性。\
**Nautika**: It looks like algae, but it's actually a hybrid of an ancient fungus and I think some kind of fibrous plant. Luckily for me, she found that they were edible.

**诺谛卡**：站点的储备食物耗尽后，我就是靠着黑藻才支撑了下来。\
**Nautika**: This is what I ate after I ran out of food at the station.

探险家走上了几级台阶，向遗迹深处眺望。\
Nautika climbs a few steps and peers deeper into the ruins.

**诺谛卡**：不过我没想到，黑藻居然在遗址里长得这么茂盛……它们看起来是从火山脚下长出来的。\
**Nautika**: But, there's so much of it here. Look at the pattern. It looks like they've grown all the way from the foot of the volcano.

探险家拍着手上的灰，跳下了台阶。\
She dusts off her hands and hops down from the steps.

**诺谛卡**：它们长得又快又猛，一夜就能长到几十米，能冲破冰层我一点儿也不意外。\
**Nautika**: This algae grows very fast and very violently. I saw one grow by a few dozen meters overnight. It's no wonder they can crack open ice and make those "earthquakes" happen.

**十四行诗**：它也许是一种未被世人发现的神秘学材料，围绕它的生物分类一定能展开一场别开生面的辩论。\
**Sonetto**: Hmm. Perhaps it's a new type of arcane material. I imagine there'd be quite a debate over its classification.

**维尔汀**：我明白了，我们会注意脚下的。\
**Vertin**: Alright. Let's just watch where we step.

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，你能判断我们当前的位置吗？\
**Vertin**: Nautika, do you have any idea where we are?

探险家点点头，从口袋里掏出一张皱皱的防水合成纸。\
Nautika produces a familiar crumpled sheet of waterproof synthetic paper from her pocket.

**诺谛卡**：当然了！刚才在你和那个后援伙伴通讯时，我就根据你们的对话补充了我的南极神秘学地图。\
**Nautika**: Oh, I think I do. I listened in on your conversation over the comm and filled in a few gaps on my map based on what your colleague said.

**诺谛卡**：即将举行仪式的神殿藏在遗址城的另一头，那座死火山的内部。\
**Nautika**: Let's see. The ritual sanctuary is here, at the far end of the city, inside the dormant volcano.

**十四行诗**：这样的地方，不难想象山脚会有重重把守。\
**Sonetto**: Manus Vindictae will surely have that area heavily guarded.

**诺谛卡**：神殿大门外的空地是一个环形广场，听上去是他们举行各种日常祭祀活动的场所。\
**Nautika**: And outside the sanctuary entrance there's this, a kind of circular clearing, probably one of their daily ritual sites.

**诺谛卡**：而这里就是我们目前所在的地方，最外围的遗址城。\
**Nautika**: And this is where we are, at the outskirts of the ruins.

**诺谛卡**：如此恢弘的遗迹，就像神话中的迷宫一样——\
**Nautika**: Just look at it—this ancient city—from here, all the way up to the foot of the volcano. It's, hah, it's incredible.

**诺谛卡**：不知道这城里藏着多少珍贵的考古资料呢……\
**Nautika**: Just imagine all the secrets and answers hidden away within these walls.

**维尔汀**：如果这里真的是重塑之手的巢穴，我们一定能发现什么关于仪式的线索。\
**Vertin**: If we're going to find out anything about Manus Vindictae's ritual, the answers will be in this city.

**维尔汀**：我们先一起行动，寻找一条回去的路吧。\
**Vertin**: Stay close, everyone. Let's head back to the exit of the labyrinth first.

在话说出口前，激动的探险家已经开始了自己的冒险。\
Before the words are even spoken, Nautika has already begun to bound forward.

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀，维尔汀——\
**Nautika**: Vertin, Vertin!

**诺谛卡**：快过来看！\
**Nautika**: Come look at this!

在探险家的召唤下，众人走进了最近的房间。\
Heeding the call, the other two file into the nearest room.

探险家第一个伸手抚摸这些姑且能被称为家具的用品。\
Nautika is the first to reach out and touch what might be called furniture.

**诺谛卡**：一张普通的橄榄岩床铺，一对简单的片麻岩桌椅……这里似乎承担着起居功能。\
**Nautika**: A peridotite stone bed, a gneiss stone table and chairs ... Someone used to live here.

**诺谛卡**：但也太简陋了吧……那些戴面具的“疯雪怪”就住在这种地方？\
**Nautika**: It's so stark, even for life in Antarctica. Do you think this is where those masked Snow Monsters live?

**维尔汀**：房间主人的喜好，倒是非常明显。\
**Vertin**: I can't say for sure, but the owner wasn't exactly subtle about their interests.

小型祭坛之上，摆着蒸馏瓶、水浴器以及盛有各种汤剂的红绿试管，台面上还铺撒着数种黑红金属粉末。\
On the small altar sit retorts, water baths, and test tubes filled with red and green potions, while dark metallic powders are scattered across the surface.

**维尔汀**：一个炼金术士的房间。\
**Vertin**: This is an alchemist's chamber.

第一助手仔细观察后，从各种炼金材料之下小心地抽出一本手稿。\
After careful examination, Sonetto delicately extracts a manuscript from beneath the alchemical materials.

**十四行诗**：该手稿由伟大的帕拉塞尔苏斯撰写，他的诗歌与谜语带来生命之水，是不老泉的起源。\
**Sonetto**: "This manuscript was written by the great Paracelsus, whose river of verses quenches our thirst for an endless life and whispers the secret of the Fountain of Youth."

**十四行诗**：由……“卡文迪许”抄录。字迹模糊了，只能看出姓氏。\
**Sonetto**: "Transcribed by ... Cavendish." I can only make out the surname.

**维尔汀**：不老泉？手稿里还有什么其他有价值的信息吗？\
**Vertin**: The Fountain of Youth? What else does it say?

**十四行诗**：除了题记外，都是一些诗词和插画。\
**Sonetto**: There are just a few verses and illustrations.

**维尔汀**：帕拉塞尔苏斯……好耳熟，我一定听说过这个名字。\
**Vertin**: Paracelsus ... Why does that name ring a bell?

**十四行诗**：第一防线学校，第六学年下半学期的第一堂炼金术史课上，教员介绍了帕拉塞尔苏斯的生平。\
**Sonetto**: Sixth grade, second semester, History of Alchemy, week 1 ... "The life of Paracelsus."

**十四行诗**：他是古代炼金术与医学的先驱，传说中他留下了“起死回生汤剂”的配方……\
**Sonetto**: He was a pioneer in ancient alchemy and medicine. Legend has it that he invented a potion that could revive the dead.

起 死 回 生\
REVIVE THE DEAD

心底一声警钟敲响。\
A warning alarm sounds deep in her mind.

**维尔汀**：起死回生……\
**Vertin**: Revive the dead ...

**维尔汀**：我们在蓝手帕旅馆中找到的术阵，被基金会研究员指向了某种复活术式。而现在又有了重塑之手内部有人正沉迷于调制“起死回生汤剂”的证据。\
**Vertin**: There was an array in Tuesday's Motel, which the Foundation confirmed to be part of a resurrection ritual. And here in Manus Vindictae's city, there's a manuscript about a revival potion.

**维尔汀**：重塑之手正在筹备的仪式说不定真的和“复活”有关。\
**Vertin**: Perhaps this is what their ritual is for. To bring back the dead.

**维尔汀**：而值得他们如此大费周章的人……\
**Vertin**: And the only person they'd go to such lengths to bring back is—

答案显而易见。\
The answer is clear.

阿尔卡纳……\
Arcana.

**十四行诗**：但……德洛丝医生为什么又与这一切有关联？\
**Sonetto**: But what's Dr. Dores's part in all this?

**维尔汀**：我们还不得而知。\
**Vertin**: That's still unclear.

**维尔汀**：但如果她真的是仪式中重要的一环……等基金会增援赶到，一切恐怕就来不及了。\
**Vertin**: But if Manus Vindictae needs her to complete their ritual, we're on borrowed time. I'm afraid waiting for reinforcements is no longer an option.

**维尔汀**：最坏的情况下，我们要做好穿越遗址城的准备，十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: We have to go through the city. Now, Sonetto.

**十四行诗**：……是，事态变得更加严峻了，我们必须万分小心。\
**Sonetto**: Agreed. The situation may be more urgent than we thought. We can't afford to linger any longer.

第一助手叹了口气，侧身转向正与建筑外墙较劲的探险家。\
Sonetto sighs and turns toward Nautika, who's busy grappling with the building's exterior.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐，计划有变，我们即将直接踏入重塑之手的大本营。\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen, there's been a change of plan. We're entering the city.

**十四行诗**：我们会尽力保护你的安全，但谁也无法预料接下来会遇到什么事……\
**Sonetto**: We'll do everything we can to keep you safe, but there's no guarantee we'll—

**十四行诗**：——诺谛卡？\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen?

一旁久未参与讨论的探险家，正用手慢慢感受着建筑物风化的岩石外壁，逐步走向另一个方向。\
Nautika had kept quiet during their discussions and continues to run her hand along the weathered stone walls without reply.

**诺谛卡**：没有错，弗里莱的想法没有错……我们家乡的神话在极南之境真的得到了验证。\
**Nautika**: You were right, Friele. The tales are true. The Mother Spirit is here at the southernmost edge of the world.

**诺谛卡**：传说中地母最终的落脚点就是这里……\
**Nautika**: This is Her resting place.

探险家轻轻将自己的脸贴在石壁上，体温将覆在其上的薄薄白雪融化。\
She presses her face against the stone, body warmth melting the thin snowdrift clinging to it.

“属于那最初时代的挽歌，在最后一个世纪唱响……”\
"The first age ends, the tolling bells are rung. Before the last, a mournful dirge is sung."

“地母的福祉，无论在何地，将带我辈前往栖身的尽头。”\
"Alas! Where will our bones be laid to rest? O Mother, let us lie upon your breast."

声音落在地上，探险家激动异常地抬起头。\
The sound causes her ears to spring up and her head follows shortly after.

**诺谛卡**：维、维尔汀！这里……这里就是我要找的地方！\
**Nautika**: Ah, Vertin. Here, this place. Oh. This is the place I've been searching for.

**维尔汀**：……？\
**Vertin**: ...?

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**诺谛卡**：你们看，在这些建筑表层的下面……\
**Nautika**: Look, here, beneath the surface of this rock.

她用冰镐敲了敲墙面，灰白的岩石碎屑剥落，露出了一种几乎透明的乳色晶体。\
She taps the wall with her ice ax, causing pale fragments to flake off and reveal a translucent, milky crystal beneath.

**诺谛卡**：这种类似隐晶质石英的岩石密度极高，是从未在其他大陆发现过的种类，它们属于一片未被调查出来的“空白时代”……！\
**Nautika**: Feel it. It looks like chalcedony, right? But it's much heavier. This rock is totally unique to Antarctica. It's never been seen anywhere else. We call it Rock of the Blank Era.

**诺谛卡**：这与我和弗里莱的研究不谋而合！\
**Nautika**: This is the exact same rock Friele and I studied!

**诺谛卡**：三年前，我们对祖父当年从南极带回来的岩石样本进行了新的检测。\
**Nautika**: Three years ago, we ran a carbon dating test on the rock samples my grandfather brought back from Antarctica.

**诺谛卡**：根据样本中放射性同位素衰变产物的含量，我们认定远古时代存在一段非常特殊的时期。\
**Nautika**: When we ran the test on this rock, we found something strange. It was pointing to an era that didn't exist in any geological record.

**诺谛卡**：除了这种特殊的晶体外，我们找不到任何关于那个时期存在的证据……\
**Nautika**: None of the other samples matched that strange era. We looked for other evidence, but we found nothing—no fossils, no minerals, no records.

**诺谛卡**：但……当科学的语言走到尽头的时候，我们从神话的碎片中找到了灵感。\
**Nautika**: But then, when we couldn't think any longer, our folk tale suddenly came to mind, and it all started to make sense.

**诺谛卡**：地母的神话指引我们来到了南极，我又通过她的旨意找到了遗址，再次找到了这种晶体！\
**Nautika**: Our book, Tales of the Mother Spirit, led me here, to the end of the Earth. It guided me to these ruins, to this very rock.

**十四行诗**：听起来确实是一种值得研究的矿物，但它与神话之间是否真的存在联系……\
**Sonetto**: I see what you're saying, and I'm sure there's more to discover through this rock, but isn't it a little too soon to link it to your tale?

**诺谛卡**：一定是这样的！没有错！\
**Nautika**: I'm sure of it. This is the place.

**诺谛卡**：我的小耳朵虫就是这么告诉我的，“地母栖身的尽头”……毫无疑问，就是这里！\
**Nautika**: It's just like Máhtu said. This is where the Mother Spirit rests. There is no doubt.

**诺谛卡**：只要采集到更多的样本带回实验室，我就一定能找到空白时代和“地母”间的联系——她一定是历史背后的答案！\
**Nautika**: If I can bring more samples back to the lab, we might be able to figure out the connection between the Mother Spirit and the Blank Era. We can finally find out what it was like.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

探险家沉迷于自己的思绪中无可自拔，她摸着墙一路走出了房间，企图找到墙体最脆弱的部分，凿下一块完整的晶体。\
Lost in thought, Nautika continues to trace out the wall of the room, searching for its weakest point to extract an intact crystal.

**无线电小姐**：……我也可以说说我的感受吗？\
**Ms. Radio**: Sorry to interrupt, but may I point something out?

**无线电小姐**：……阿嚏——!\
**Ms. Radio**: *sneeze*

**无线电小姐**：这里突然变得好冷，我、我的电阻性质都快变化了……\
**Ms. Radio**: It's getting very cold in here. I can feel my resistance starting to drop.

**诺谛卡**：——维尔汀！\
**Nautika**: Vertin!

随着探险家的低声惊呼，众人纷纷走出房间。\
A soft exclamation from Nautika draws the others out.

**诺谛卡**：怪、怪……\
**Nautika**: Mo-mon-monster ...

**祇役**：呜……

一具白色的诡异肉身站在诺谛卡身前。\
A pallid, grotesque figure stands before Nautika.

没有五官，周身的皮肤如同被翻转后重新贴在血肉上。\
Its face is blank, its skin appearing to have been peeled and reattached inside-out.

它抽搐着，如同地苔在寒风中抽搐着，并用它不存在的双眼注视着外来者。\
It twitches as if watching the intruders from nonexistent eyes.

**祇役**：呜……\
**"Servant"**: *wailing*

**维尔汀**：先别动，小心刺激到它……\
**Vertin**: Don't provoke it. There's a chance it might just leave us be.

**祇役**：呜……\
**"Servant"**: *wailing*

不远处传来低低的犬吠，被意外留在原地的巨犬们似乎开始了又一阵嬉戏，雪地在追逐中簌簌作响。\
Distant playful barks echo back through the walls, drawing a stark contrast to the scene.

**祇役**：呜……\
**"Servant"**: *wailing*

呜咽着的人形怪物突然狂奔着冲了上来。\
With a whimper, the humanoid creatures lurch toward the group.

**维尔汀**：咳、咳咳……\
**Vertin**: *coughing*

敌人的攻击打碎了风化的地面，几人正狼狈地从下一层的废墟中爬出来。\
The enemy's strike shatters the weathered ground, sending them scrambling up from the rubble below.

**十四行诗**：司辰，你们没事吧！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, are you alright?

**维尔汀**：我没事，十四行诗。诺谛卡呢，你怎么样？\
**Vertin**: Alive and well, and you? Where's Nautika?

被呼唤名字的人并没有应声。\
They call out her name, but it goes unanswered.

**十四行诗**：糟糕，她没有和我们一起掉下来。\
**Sonetto**: She didn't fall through with us. She's still up there, alone.

**维尔汀**：别担心，没有其他脚步声……她应该是找地方躲起来了。\
**Vertin**: I don't hear any movement above us. Perhaps she's found a place to hide.

**维尔汀**：无线电小姐，尝试联系诺谛卡身上的通讯器。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Radio, could you get her on the comm?

**无线电小姐**：……我、我在努力。\
**Ms. Radio**: I ... I'm trying.

一只轻盈的蛾子擦耳而过。\
A delicate moth brushes past her ear.

**？？？**：她……也是你们的同伴吗？\
**???**: Is that girl with you?

**维尔汀**：——？\
**Vertin**: ...?

无数只轻盈的、洁白的蛾子在明媚的极圈阳光下，自同一个方向飞来。\
Countless pale and weightless moths stream forward from a fixed direction, reflecting in the bright polar light.

**？？？**：终于找到你们了。\
**???**: You're a tricky one to track, Timekeeper.

**？？？**：我很高兴，你们终于来了。\
**???**: I'm ever so glad you've made it this far into the continent.

**？？？**：基金会的人，任何人，来到这里……都非常好……\
**???**: I'll admit, I'd be more than happy to welcome anyone from the Foundation here.

她缓缓走近，脚步中流露出一丝蹒跚。\
She approaches, her steps betraying a faint unsteadiness.

**淑女格蕾丝**：与我心里的小念头不谋而合的是，来的人果然是你。\
**Ms. Grace**: But, oh, what a pleasure it is that you, of all people, would be the one to show up.

**维尔汀**：……格蕾丝？\
**Vertin**: Grace? Is that you?

面前的“老朋友”轻喘了一口气，似乎刚经历过一番消磨体力的奔走。\
Her "old friend" seems to be recovering her breath from some kind of exertion.

**维尔汀**：不对，你到底是谁？是牧场的凯拉，还是“自由海风号”上的格蕾丝……\
**Vertin**: No. Who are you really? Kayla from the ranch? Captain Grace of the "Free Breeze"?

**维尔汀**：抑或是说……\
**Vertin**: Or ...

**淑女格蕾丝**：抑或是说，我谁也不是……\
**Ms. Grace**: Or just a familiar stranger.

**淑女格蕾丝**：你会询问一枚蛾子的名字与身份吗？若非点起烛火，你甚至都不会注意到阴影里的它。\
**Ms. Grace**: Who would ask a common moth its name? Who would even notice it if it weren't drawn to the flames?

**淑女格蕾丝**：无名之人千千万，千千万——居于这具躯壳之内。\
**Ms. Grace**: So many lives have been lived through me—so many names taken.

**淑女格蕾丝**：我可以是塞西莉，可以是凯拉，可以是格蕾丝……我只是一个“无名者”。\
**Ms. Grace**: Cecilie, Kayla, Grace ... I've been them all, yet never quite been any of them.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：那么我换个说法，我想问的是——你为什么会出现在这里？\
**Vertin**: So which one are you now? What's your goal here?

第一助手已经举起术杖，竖在胸前严阵以待。\
Sonetto already has her glasfeder raised, ready to fly into attack or defense as needed.

**“无名者”**：别紧张。\
**Ms. Stranger**: No need to get worked up.

“无名者”向前伸出手。\
Ms. Stranger reaches out a hand.

**“无名者”**：德洛丝医生，又或者说，兀尔德女士……\
**Ms. Stranger**: About Dr. Dores, or rather, Ms. Urd ...

**“无名者”**：有关她下落的最后一块拼图，在我这里。\
**Ms. Stranger**: I have the final piece of the puzzle that will lead you to her.

## 10TH-14 我亲爱的 / My Dear Siblings

在通讯器上敲下一串代码后，莫莉德尔将通讯器放回口袋里。\
Moldir taps a code into the communicator before putting it back in her pocket.

**白手套队长**：莫莉德尔中尉。\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Lieutenant.

凛风中，黑发中尉将遮挡视线的卷发捋至耳后，应声回头。\
Against the howling wind, Moldir tucks her curls behind her ears and turns toward the voice.

**莫莉德尔**：怎么了？白手套队长。\
**Moldir**: What is it, Sergeant?

**白手套队长**：我们现在在做什么？\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: With all due respect, what are we doing here?

她的下属问出了一个简单而尖锐的问题。\
Her subordinate poses a simple but tough question.

她的军队驻扎于此，在她的授意下围在火炉旁取暖歇息，但个个整装待发，只等她的一声令下。\
Her troops are relaxed, warming themselves around their fires. Yet each one would be ready the moment she gives the word.

**莫莉德尔**：……我们在等待。\
**Moldir**: We're on standby.

她暂时无法回答这样的问题，于是垂下了眼。\
It's a question Moldir can't answer, so she turns away.

坚定是可以扮演的。\
She'll have to feign determination for now.

**白手套队长**：在等待什么？\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Standby for what?

**莫莉德尔**：等待基金会游兵散将的登陆，一举擒获他们，守卫好这处海岸。\
**Moldir**: To capture any Foundation soldiers that make it to the shore.

**白手套队长**：虽然还有一名水兵处于俘虏之下，但最关键的人……\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Then what about the ones we already captured? Why are we only holding the run-of-the-mill seaman? The other two could have been useful, but we just ...

队长适时停止，他瞟向了医疗站的方向——乌尔里希和他的护卫刚刚离开。\
The sergeant stops, his eyes flicking toward the clinic, where Ulrich and his guard just departed.

**莫莉德尔**：意识唤醒者研究员，乳臭未干的护卫兵。在这片大地上，这样的队伍没有反抗的力量，也就没有扣押的价值。\
**Moldir**: Those two? Hardly. What can an Awakened researcher and a rookie guard do in Antarctica? Holding them would be a waste of resources.

中尉侧身看向远处，用身体语言表示出不愿再在这个话题上停留。\
She directs her stare out into the white distance.

**莫莉德尔**：丹尼洛夫机长在哪里，让他到直升机处找我。\
**Moldir**: Where's Danilov? Tell him to meet me at the helicopter.

中尉离去，留下一串深深的脚印。\
The order comes quick, as do her steps out and away.

丹尼洛夫机长刚喝下一口肉罐汤，白手套队长从背后拍了拍他的肩膀。\
Captain Danilov takes a long and deep sip of stew, letting the warmth linger on his tongue, making it all the worse when he is suddenly tapped on the shoulder.

**机长**：嘿——别老是从背后接近别人！\
**Aircraft Captain**: Ah! Stop sneaking up on me like that!

**白手套队长**：哈哈，你还是像小时候一样，经不起一点吓唬。\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Haha, gotcha! Some things never change, huh? Still as jumpy as you were when you were a kid.

**机长**：别闹了，我早就不是跟在你们这些大人身后晨练的小孩了。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Come on. Cut it out. I'm a captain now, you know. Not some kid.

机长放下肉罐头，站起身。\
He sets down the can reluctantly and rises to his feet.

**机长**：中尉找我？\
**Aircraft Captain**: What do you want? Did the lieutenant send you?

**白手套队长**：让你去直升机那儿见她。\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Yep. She wants you over at Canis Minor.

擦身而过时，丹尼洛夫机长听到了一句低声抱怨。\
As they pass each other, Captain Danilov catches a muttered complaint.

**白手套队长**：你倒好，收到了第一条命令。不知道其他人什么时候能等到除了“等待”外的其他指令呢？\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Lucky you, getting to stretch your legs while the rest of us have to sit here idling away the hours.

**机长**：……日子艰难。\
**Aircraft Captain**: *sigh* Guess that's how it is these days. Everything still seems foggy.

走出去

他往外走出了两步，白手套队长始终亦步亦趋地跟着。\
He takes two steps outward, and the sergeant matches him stride for stride.

**白手套队长**：我曾以为在巴西那段日子是最艰难的，如今看来，那个时候还是想得太简单了。\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Tell me about it. I thought Brazil was tough, but this? This is worse.

**白手套队长**：真正难的是做出选择后，面对自我的勇气。\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Sometimes, it takes more courage to stick to a choice than to make one. I think someone might be struggling with that.

**机长**：我相信中尉和将军。\
**Aircraft Captain**: You should know better than to doubt our leadership, White Gloves.

白手套队长闻言停下脚步。\
The sergeant stops.

**白手套队长**：问题在于，如果你最相信的两个人——如果中尉和将军之间已经产生了分歧呢？\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Sure, but what if they start doubting each other? What if the admiral's steering us one way and the lieutenant another?

**白手套队长**：中尉放走那两个人的时候，你也看见了——\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: You saw how the lieutenant let that Foundation researcher go. Didn't that bother you?

**机长**：……\
**Aircraft Captain**: ...

话音落下，丹尼洛夫机长在原地驻足片刻，看见雪花落在了他的军靴上。\
Silence lingers as the captain finds himself watching snowflakes settle on his boots.

而后，他再次踏雪向前。\
At last, he forces himself forward.

**机长**：我相信他们。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I trust them both. No matter what.

机长合上了维修手册，思考着如何用外行人也能听懂的方式，向中尉解释直升机的故障所在。\
The captain closes his maintenance manual, finding himself in search of the least technical way to explain the helicopter's malfunction.

**机长**：一般而言，偏航角速率出现偏差的原因要从脚蹬去找。\
**Aircraft Captain**: A yaw rate issue might just be a pedal problem, you see.

**机长**：要么是脚蹬结构元件出现松动，导致尾桨总距未能如期改变；要么是脚蹬控制的尾桨受撞击后，角度发生了偏移。\
**Aircraft Captain**: In this case, either the rudder pedal has loosened, which is affecting the responsiveness of the tail rotor, or the tail blades were damaged by the impact.

**莫莉德尔**：了解了，我来试试看。\
**Moldir**: I see. Let me take a look.

中尉点点头，钻进了驾驶舱。\
She nods and climbs into the cockpit.

她从手边的工具包中抽出一枚小巧的神秘学道具。\
From her tool set, she draws out a small, arcane item.

**莫莉德尔**：无新事，复旧形。\
**Moldir**: Что было, то и будет.

一串晶莹的金色粉末轻轻从镊子尖灌入被卸下的旋钮。\
A stream of glimmering powder flows from her tweezers into the detached knob.

中尉额头渗出一层汗。\
Beads of sweat form and then evaporate into the cold air.

**莫莉德尔**：……并没有想象中那么简单。\
**Moldir**: This is more complicated than I thought.

神秘术并未如期生效，中尉摇了摇头，收起了工具。\
As the arcane skill fails to activate, she shakes her head and puts away the tool.

收起浮窗

**机长**：飞行器的控制和运行原理很复杂，一时半会儿搞不明白很正常。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I would be surprised if you managed to fix it in one go. Aircraft can be tricky.

**机长**：我在军备学院时，光《飞行器机械原理》这门课就花了两年时间学习呢。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Took me two full years back at the Academy to pass "Theories of Flight Mechanics," and even longer to really get the hang of it.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

中尉看了丹尼洛夫机长一会儿，最后久违地露出一个微笑。\
She studies Captain Danilov for a moment before offering a rare smile.

**莫莉德尔**：而因为你不合格的成绩单，我三次被你的老师叫到了学院办公室。\
**Moldir**: *chuckle* I remember. Your teacher called me in three times because of the "extreme frustration and concern about your grades."

**机长**：哈、哈哈……谢天谢地，他们不敢直接向“父亲”汇报。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Haha ... I'm just glad they didn't call Father. That would've been the end of me.

**机长**：我很少见你使用神秘术，中尉。\
**Aircraft Captain**: You know, I don't see you using your arcane skill much these days.

**莫莉德尔**：是的，它是很无用的天赋……\
**Moldir**: Well, there's not much use for it, really.

**莫莉德尔**：在救死扶伤或维护公义这些事上，它与抗生素和弹药相比，无用至极且不值一提。\
**Moldir**: Bullets and medicine are a thousand times more useful on the battlefield.

似乎从语气中听到了某种非刻意流露的情绪，机长忖度了一下。\
Detecting the rare and likely unintentional emotion in her tone, the captain hesitates.

**机长**：……我很抱歉，我需要回避一下吗？\
**Aircraft Captain**: Oh, I didn't mean it like that, sorry. Do you want some space?

**莫莉德尔**：不用，你呆在这里就好。\
**Moldir**: No, it's fine. You're fine.

**莫莉德尔**：我希望可以早点修好直升机，你能够再整体检查一下吗？\
**Moldir**: We just need to get this helicopter fixed as soon as possible. Can you run another check?

**莫莉德尔**：我的神秘术钻进操纵系统后就碰到了死胡同，或许问题并不出在刚才提出的那两种可能性上。\
**Moldir**: There was a blockage in the system that stopped my arcane energy from flowing through. Maybe the issue isn't as simple as just the pedal or blade.

**机长**：我再试试。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Got it. I'll take another look.

中尉几不可闻地叹了口气。\
The lieutenant exhales softly.

**莫莉德尔**：它碰到了死胡同。\
**Moldir**: That blockage. I just couldn't push past it.

**莫莉德尔**：它走在了正确的电路上吗？\
**Moldir**: Did I follow the wrong circuit?

**莫莉德尔**：……是我做得不对吗？\
**Moldir**: Or did I just do the whole thing wrong?

机长在一小阵沉默后，换了一个姿势。\
A silence lingers after her words, forcing the captain to shift position.

**机长**：不，中尉。你的神秘术帮我们的伤员修好了冻坏的耳骨支架、开裂的石膏和被风吹裂的帐篷布。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I wouldn't overthink it if I were you, and stop underestimating your arcane skill. It's saved us more times than I can count—frozen prosthetics, broken casts, ripped tents.

**机长**：而从小到大，你每次都能帮我们把枪修理得崭新如初。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Hell, you've been fixing our guns since we were kids.

**机长**：这没有什么不对的。\
**Aircraft Captain**: There's nothing wrong with your power. We all appreciate it a lot more than you think.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

机长将自己庞大的身躯塞进狭小的座位下，举着手电仔细检查每一根线路。\
He wedges his bulk beneath the cramped seat, flashlight in hand, inspecting each wire and following it with his fingers.

**机长**：中尉收到过那张收养申请表吗？\
**Aircraft Captain**: Did you get the adoption form when you were little too, Lieutenant?

**莫莉德尔**：……你是说？\
**Moldir**: Hm? You mean the ...

**机长**：我的父母死于1999年，我至今不知道为什么。\
