**Aircraft Captain**: Yeah. Mine came after my parents died in 1999. Even now, I still don't know what happened that day.

机长像说笑话一般，口吻轻松。\
His tone turns light, as if he's telling a joke.

**机长**：与阵亡通知书一同寄到我手上的，还有一张伊戈尔将军的收养申请表。\
**Aircraft Captain**: When they brought me the death notice, they handed me an adoption form along with it. It was from Admiral Igor.

**机长**：一开始，我是抵触的——我不可能管另一位陌生人叫父亲。\
**Aircraft Captain**: At first, I hated the idea. I didn't want anyone to take my father's place.

**莫莉德尔**：但你最终还是签了名。\
**Moldir**: But you signed it; otherwise, you wouldn't be here.

**机长**：是的，因为我想知道我父母付出生命追随的人是什么样子，他们为之奋斗一生的组织又是什么样子。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I did. Because I needed to know what my parents gave their lives for, and the man they fought beside.

与我一样。\
"We are alike."

中尉并未将自己的心声说出，她只是低头检查着自己的修理工具。\
Moldir keeps that thought unspoken, turning her eyes down to her repair tools.

**机长**：而时至今日，我仍为这支队伍感到自豪。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I've never regretted it. I'm proud of where I am, proud of everyone in this army.

**机长**：不是因为它代表了芝诺最王牌的战斗力——当然，如今已经沦为万人可鄙的过街鼠。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Not because we're the best soldiers Zeno's ever had. I mean, I'm sure they definitely don't think that now.

**机长**：我感到自豪，是因为……\
**Aircraft Captain**: No, I'm proud because we're more than just an army.

机长整个脑袋都探进了座位下面，他的声音仿佛从远处传来。\
The captain's head disappears entirely beneath the seat, his voice coming through muffled and distant.

**机长**：我们不仅是战友，更是“家人”。\
**Aircraft Captain**: We're a family.

**机长**：在将军和旧部长官们的照顾下，我们这些“暴雨孤儿”共同训练、生活、长大。没有一支队伍比我们更有默契，更信任彼此。\
**Aircraft Captain**: We "Storm" orphans grew up together, trained together, fought side by side. We trust each other like we trust ourselves, hell, maybe even more so.

机长终于把身体从内舱里抽出，他满脸油污，视线对上中尉的眼睛。\
He extracts himself from the cockpit, grease smeared across his face.

在后者闪动的目光中，丹尼洛夫压低了声音。\
Under her flickering gaze, Danilov drops his voice.

**机长**：当然，当然，有些大事儿父亲不会告诉所有人。事关所有人的未来，知道计划核心的人越少就越保险。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I know Father hasn't told us everything. But maybe that's for the best. The less everyone knows about his plan, the better.

**机长**：但只要您与将军一声令下，我们就会无条件服从——哪怕是开飞机冲进基金会总部，哪怕是在雪地里等到春天。\
**Aircraft Captain**: But no matter what, I will follow you and the admiral to the very end, whether it's flying a fighter into the Foundation headquarters or waiting here until the spring.

**机长**：我相信将军的计划能带我们跨越时间。\
**Aircraft Captain**: I believe in him. I believe that he can take us home.

**机长**：我也相信你，“姐姐”。\
**Aircraft Captain**: And I believe in you, sister.

**莫莉德尔**：……！\
**Moldir**: ...!

机长深深地敬了一个礼，鼻尖的机油滑稽地反射着光线。\
He salutes solemnly—proudly, but the smears of engine oil on his nose take all the seriousness from the moment.

莫莉德尔中尉久违地感受到一阵喉间的酸胀。\
A long-unfamiliar tightness rises in Moldir's throat.

**莫莉德尔**：感谢你的信任，丹尼洛夫机长。\
**Moldir**: Thank you, Captain Danilov.

**莫莉德尔**：我们目前的任务是……继续等待。\
**Moldir**: Our current mission is to wait here.

莫莉德尔眨了眨眼，深呼吸后吐出一口白雾。\
She blinks, breathes deep, and then exhales a misty stream into the air.

**莫莉德尔**：这是军令。\
**Moldir**: Those are our orders. Let's be sure we see them through.

## 10TH-15 疯人之口 / In the Mouth of Madness

第一助手跨步上前，笔杖直指重塑使徒的胸膛。\
Sonetto steps forward, her glasfeder aimed squarely at the Manus Apostle's chest.

**十四行诗**：重塑之手的使徒，淑女格蕾丝——\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Grace, you're a Manus Apostle.

**十四行诗**：你已经在“自由海风号”上犯下累累恶行……如今你又在策划什么阴谋？\
**Sonetto**: Don't think we've forgotten what you did aboard the "Free Breeze." What exactly are you scheming now?

“无名者”侧脸，用余光感受着笔杖尖端蓄势待发的神秘术能量。\
Ms. Stranger tilts her head, sensing the arcane energy gathering at the glasfeder's tip out of the corner of her eye.

突然，她咳嗽了一声，但很快将余下的肌肉运动咽了回去。\
A cough escapes her and is quickly suppressed, her whole body twitching to contain it.

**“无名者”**：……同你们一样，我也怀念我们曾在“自由海风号”上相遇的时光。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Ah, the "Free Breeze." My lovely little cruise ship. Like you, I often find myself missing those serene days on the water.

**“无名者”**：一段难忘的回忆，一个值得被误解的形象，令我给你们留下了难以洗刷的深刻印象。\
**Ms. Stranger**: But it seems a few unpleasant memories and misinterpreted actions have deeply wounded your trust in me.

“无名者”靠得更近，让笔杖尖端抵在自己的皮肤上。\
She leans closer until the glasfeder point presses against her skin.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

往前走一步，立于第一助手身侧，轻轻按下她几近颤抖的手。\
The Timekeeper steps forward and stands beside Sonetto, allowing her to lower her shaking outstretched hand.

**十四行诗**：司辰……！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：放心，十四行诗。我只是想问她几个问题。\
**Vertin**: It's fine, Sonetto. I have a few questions I'd like to ask.

风将“无名者”脖颈上的飘带吹起，晶莹的粉末瞬间融进了雪里。\
Wind lifts the ribbon around Ms. Stranger's neck as glistening powder dissolves into the snow.

**维尔汀**：在奔赴遗址城的路上，我们非常凑巧地找到了一些属于德洛丝医生的东西——一个听诊器、一台打字机。\
**Vertin**: On our way here, we discovered a couple of items that I believe belong to Dr. Dores—a stethoscope and a typewriter.

**维尔汀**：它们被看似随意地扔在了前往这里的必经之路上——就像引路的信物。\
**Vertin**: It seems they were intentionally left behind, like a series of signposts pointing us here.

**维尔汀**：你对我们发现的这些信物，有什么想法吗？\
**Vertin**: You wouldn't happen to know anything about these items, would you?

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

**维尔汀**：又或者，我可以问得更直接一点，打字机上的鳞粉。\
**Vertin**: How about the powder we found on the typewriter?

**维尔汀**：这种比雪细的粉末在阳光下会有异样的反光，粘在手上难以擦拭，还有些苦味。\
**Vertin**: It's finer than snow and reflects the sunlight differently. It sticks to the skin and is bitter on the tongue.

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

**维尔汀**：这些线索，与你有关吗？\
**Vertin**: Any idea how it got there? And how the typewriter ended up lying in the snowfields?

**维尔汀**：是你为了指引基金会相关人员，而故意留下的吗？\
**Vertin**: Did you leave it there? Were you giving directions to the Foundation's investigators?

**十四行诗**：鳞粉？鳞翅目昆虫双翅上的微小颗粒，具有防水性和迷惑敌人的功能。鳞翅目昆虫，蝴蝶，飞蛾……\
**Sonetto**: Come to think of it, that powder looked like the scales from a lepidoptera wing—a butterfly, or a moth.

**十四行诗**：——！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

**十四行诗**：“飞蛾”？你就是基金会安插在重塑之手的间谍——\
**Sonetto**: Moth. It's you, isn't it? You're the Foundation's spy!

飞蛾落在了“无名者”的指尖，又在举手投足间向着光的方向展翅。\
A moth alights on Ms. Stranger's fingertip, then flutters off with a barely perceptible twitch of her finger.

**“无名者”**：如果你们需要更多的证明……我可以列举进行“趋光性研究”所需的每个步骤。\
**Ms. Stranger**: I could provide you with a detailed account of the Foundation's phototaxis experiments if you need further proof of my identity.

**“无名者”**：不过，我们的时间很紧迫。\
**Ms. Stranger**: But we're running out of time.

在基金会职员惊讶的目光中，“无名者”侧过脸，朝向重峦叠嶂般错落着的遗址建筑。\
Their astonished stares hold on Ms. Stranger as she turns her face toward the ruins beyond.

**“无名者”**：我会带你们到火山神殿处，德洛丝医生——兀尔德女士已经抵达了那里。\
**Ms. Stranger**: I'll lead you to the sanctuary. Dr. Dores—Ms. Urd—is already inside.

**“无名者”**：同时，我的蛾子已传回了消息——\
**Ms. Stranger**: Oh, and my moths have just brought some new information.

**“无名者”**：你们的人类同伴，似乎也是冲着那个方向逃窜而去了。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Your human friend has also gone in that direction.

说着，她转身背对着基金会职员，缓缓向前走去。\
With that, she turns her back to them and advances without fear.

一声疲惫而释然的叹息落在雪地里。\
A weary yet relieved sigh sinks into the snow.

**“无名者”**：通向神殿的门不会永远开启，要加快脚步了，司辰。\
**Ms. Stranger**: The gate to the sanctuary won't stay open forever, Timekeeper. Shall we?

**诺谛卡**：完了，完蛋了……一切都完蛋了……\
**Nautika**: No, no. This-This can't be real.

**诺谛卡**：我会死在这里，呜呜——没有你们我一定会死在这里！\
**Nautika**: This is how it ends, isn't it? I can't ... I can't do this. I can't do this alone!

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀、十四行诗、无线电小姐——！\
**Nautika**: Vertin? Sonetto? Ms. Radio?

孤立无援地走在危机四伏的迷宫里，并不是探险家想象中的科考场景。\
Trudging alone through a perilous labyrinth had never been Nautika's idea of an ideal scientific expedition.

**诺谛卡**：第一种死法：在冰天雪地里手捧着一堆尚未被研究的全新考古样本然后被活活冻死。\
**Nautika**: Possible cause of death one: freezing. Frozen solid with a bunch of unstudied samples clutched in my hands.

**诺谛卡**：第二种死法：被那些白色黏糊糊的怪物抓住活生生撕开吃掉。\
**Nautika**: Possible cause of death two: getting torn apart. Cold, sticky monster fingers sinking into my skin and ripping me to pieces.

停顿

**诺谛卡**：第三种死法：……直接自杀……！\
**Nautika**: Possible cause of death three: killing myself before one or two can happen to me.

反相\
心灵破碎

走一步\
An empty room.

一间空屋。\
Another empty room.

经过\
又一间空屋。

“阿德利企鹅”步子细碎地朝一间又一间巢穴里探头，企图找到失散的伙伴。\
Like a waddling penguin moves from nest to nest, Nautika swivels her head around in constant search for her lost companions.

经过

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

出乎意料的，这是一个有人的房间。只是那房间中静坐的人既没有鲜亮的发色，也没有带着神秘学箱子。\
A break in her rhythm finally comes—this room holds life. Yet the occupant possesses neither brilliant copper hair nor an arcane suitcase.

**诺谛卡**：——！\
**Nautika**: ...!

探险家迅速抱头蹲下，将自己缩成一团受惊的犰狳。\
She drops into a crouch, tucking her legs in close to her chest, turning instantaneously from penguin to armadillo—in appearance, anyways.

**诺谛卡**：没有……没有追出来？\
**Nautika**: Who ... Who was that?

鼓起了全身的勇气，她抬头把目光投向了那个人。\
She summons every ounce of courage in her, forcing her head and vision up to the figure.

出人

**诺谛卡**：——弗里莱？！\
**Nautika**: F-Friele?

记忆中的派克大衣被风吹褪了色，黯淡的颜色与主人灰败的气质如出一辙。\
The once-bright parka in her memory has faded with the wind, its dull hue mirrors the owner's new ashen demeanor.

诺谛卡猛地站了起来，踉跄着朝着房间中的人奔去。\
Nautika uncurls, half-stumbling as she rises to her feet.

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱——\
**Nautika**: Friele!

**诺谛卡**：我……我还以为你已经……\
**Nautika**: Oh, I thought ... I thought you were gone.

眼泪夺眶而出，探险家不管不顾地抱住了幸存者消瘦的臂膀。\
Tears burst forth as Nautika clutches her friend's gaunt arms.

幸存者涣散的双目缓慢聚焦，她张嘴吐出两口浊气，视线才最终落在了小探险家身上。\
The survivor's glazed eyes roll into focus. Two labored breaths escape, each exhaling without drawing anything back.

**诺谛卡**：太好了……你没事……我们、我们都没事——！\
**Nautika**: Oh, thank you, thank you, Mother Spirit. Thank you for keeping us both in one piece.

**诺谛卡**：我得先想办法带你出去，天哪……你怎么瘦成了这个样子？\
**Nautika**: We'll find a way out of here. We'll look after each other. Goodness, Friele, you're a sack of bones.

**诺谛卡**：对了……我遇到了几位神秘学家，我们结伴才找到了这儿。她们会用很厉害的神秘术，甚至能打得那些“疯雪怪”嗷嗷叫——我们得赶紧找到她们。\
**Nautika**: I met two arcanists. They'll help us. I would have never even gotten here if it weren't for them. You should've seen how they chased off those Snow Monsters. You can trust them. Come, come, Friele. We have to find them.

**诺谛卡**：她们一定能保护我们，带我们离开这里……\
**Nautika**: They'll protect us. They'll get us home.

**弗里莱**：……\
**Friele**: ...

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱，你怎么一直不说话？\
**Nautika**: Friele? Why aren't you saying anything?

消人\
出图

弗里莱只是看着她，等她又进行了一次急促的呼吸后才眨了眨眼，指向了自己的嘴巴。\
Friele holds her gaze on Nautika, letting out another ragged breath as she points to her own mouth.

**诺谛卡**：——不能说话了吗？\
**Nautika**: Can't you speak?

**诺谛卡**：没事，没事的！这里太冷了，害得你舌头都冻僵了。\
走，等我们回了家就好了。\
**Nautika**: Hm, it must be the cold. Yes, once we get back, you'll feel better, I promise.

探险家努力地想把人从石板床上拔起，可对方却像长在了床上似的巍然不动。\
Nautika strains to pull her up from the stone bed, but it feels as if she is rooted to it.

在探险家气喘吁吁地放开她后，她才用脚在积雪上画出了一个个单词。\
Panting and spent of her strength, she releases and spies the motion of her friend's foot as it cuts words into the snow.

"No."

“不”\
"Can't."

“不能离开”

**诺谛卡**：为、为什么？\
**Nautika**: No? Why?

**诺谛卡**：我已经找到了“地母栖身的尽头”，采集到了“空白时期”的样本——我完成了队伍原本在南极计划的一切科考！\
**Nautika**: Friele, Friele, listen. I found it. The resting place of the Mother Spirit. And the Rock of the Blank Era. Remember? I found lots of it. I found everything we came for.

弗里莱抬头看着自己昔日里多加爱护的年轻伙伴，突兀地露出了一个虔诚的笑容。\
Friele holds her eyes on her once-cherished friend, shifting into a devout smile.

她擦去了雪上的痕迹，写下一行文字。\
She wipes away the words, writing something new.

**诺谛卡**：“我即将”……\
**Nautika**: "Mother Spirit ..."

诺谛卡倒吸了一口气。\
Nautika gasps.

渐入

**诺谛卡**：“我即将面见地母”……\
**Nautika**: "... will see me soon."

**弗里莱**：……\
**Friele**: ...

昔日的队友微笑着点头，手里紧紧攥着挂在脖子上的吊坠。\
Friele nods with a smile, fingers clenched on the pendant around her neck.

**诺谛卡**：我不懂你的意思……\
**Nautika**: I ... I don't understand.

**诺谛卡**：你要面见“地母”？\
**Nautika**: You're going to meet the Mother Spirit?

对方认真地点头，神情如此笃定。\
Friele nods; her conviction seems absolute.

**诺谛卡**：“地母”……\
**Nautika**: But ...

探险家感觉自己的后背冒出一阵冷汗。\
Cold sweat runs down her spine.

**诺谛卡**：你的意思是——她真的存在？她就在这里，在这片遗址里？\
**Nautika**: You mean She has a mortal form? She's a living creature, like us? And She's here, in this ruin?

点头。\
Friele nods.

**诺谛卡**：可、可是这怎么可能呢……\
**Nautika**: But ... But how?

诺谛卡原地打转，她感觉血液流向四肢，即将把自己的身体扯裂。\
Nautika's blood surges into her limbs with sudden intensity.

弗里莱急切地想要反驳她，可嘴里只发出了风箱鼓动般的气音。她只能再度抚平一片积雪，用鞋尖表达自我。\
Friele tries to object but only produces wheezing breaths. With visible frustration, she smooths a fresh patch of snow.

“敬拜”\
"Homage."

“接近”\
"Approach."

“给你好消息”\
"A great gift."

**诺谛卡**：……这与《地母故事集》中的第九个故事有关吗？\
**Nautika**: Is this what the ninth story in the Tales of the Mother Spirit is about?

**诺谛卡**：“孩子终于见到了地母，他们在时空的子宫中相拥。”\
**Nautika**: "Mother and child, their heartbeats both align, in joyful union, through the womb of time."

弗里莱点头，用肢体动作表达着欣慰的赞同。\
She nods, her relief obvious through gesture alone.

**诺谛卡**：……不对，不对。假设《地母故事集》中描述的一切都是真的，那么在北极圈极昼来临前，“地母”应该在沉睡。\
**Nautika**: No. No, it can't be. The tales say that the Mother Spirit should be asleep. She shouldn't wake up until after the Arctic polar day.

年轻的探险家甩了甩脑袋。\
Nautika grips her head tightly, as if preventing it from flying off.

**诺谛卡**：如果“地母”此时正在沉睡，那、那能给你好消息的人又是谁？弗里莱，我搞不明白……\
**Nautika**: So, she's asleep, then who are you going to see? Friele, I really don't understand.

**弗里莱**：……\
**Friele**: ...

弗里莱只是微笑了一下。\
Friele merely smiles.

大脑因过载和寒冷而缺氧，诺谛卡软软地坐到了地上。\
Hypoxia sets in, whether from this information overload or the bleak coldness, and Nautika crumples once again.

**诺谛卡**：……真的不跟我回去吗？\
**Nautika**: You really won't come back with me?

**诺谛卡**：回去的路会很顺利的。我学着你的样子画了地图，在路上设置了小型补给站，我还驯服了一支犬队，它们有使不完的力气……\
**Nautika**: But if, if you come with me now, we'll be home soon. I-I drew a map, like you always did. There's food cached in the depots on the way. I even managed to train new sled dogs—

探险家的话并未说完，她的嘴被弗里莱猛地捂住。\
Friele slaps a hand over her mouth.

**弗里莱**：嘶——\
**Friele**: *hiss*

弗里莱横起一脚踢起地上的厚雪，把诺谛卡按在了地上。\
With a swift kick, Friele sends a wave of snow bursting upward, then shoves Nautika flat against the ground.

**诺谛卡**：——？！\
**Nautika**: ...?!

诺谛卡本能般趴下，扬起的雪落在她身上，将她掩盖了起来。\
Nautika presses down deeper as the snow blankets her.

踩雪的脚步声越来越近，谨慎、坚决、有条不紊。\
Footsteps crunch closer, deliberate, unwavering, methodical.

最终，脚步停在房间门口。\
They halt at the room's entrance.

**追随者**：“仪式”正在等你，“祂”也正在等待着你。\
**Follower**: The ritual is ready. THEY are waiting.

身边传来起身的声音，然后弗里莱的脚步声离开了自己。\
Nautika hears Friele get up and walk away.

脚步越来越远，但却突然停了片刻。\
The sounds pause for a moment.

**追随者**：时间不容耽搁。\
**Follower**: Time to go.

脚步声再次响起，这次没有任何停留，逐渐远去，直至世界再度归于寂静。\
The footsteps resume without hesitation, fading until silence reclaims the room.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

探险家从雪堆中探出头，轻轻抖落身上的雪。\
Nautika emerges from the snowdrift.

她踮着脚快步蹿到门边，想要捕捉那两人离开的身影。\
On tiptoes, she darts to the doorway, desperate to catch a glimpse of her friend.

但世界上，只有雪地上留下的一块吊坠仍有颜色。\
But beyond the door, there is only one spot of color—a pendant lying in the snow.

她鼻尖顶着一簇软雪，低头注视着吊坠上的刻印。\
Shaking off snowflakes still clutching to her nose, she stares at the engraving.

**耳朵虫**：“跟上去，跟上去，信仰的子民们……”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "Onward, child, follow the word of mouth."

**耳朵虫**：“跟上去，答案就在远方……”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "To the Earth's edge, the land farthest south."

**诺谛卡**：“地母古迹的光芒，引导我辈臣服于自然的律法。”\
**Nautika**: "The Mother Spirit's light, with ancient glow, guides us to the great current—nature's flow."

探险家大汗淋漓，咽了一口口水。\
Sweat drips down her temples as she swallows hard.

**诺谛卡**：……弗里莱，等等我。\
**Nautika**: Wait for me, Friele.

她抬起腿，踩在雪中的足迹上。\
She lifts her foot, placing it precisely over the footprints in the snow.

## 10TH-16 破碎的乐土 / The Broken Land of Bliss

**十四行诗**：“无名者”小姐，我们走到哪儿了？还有诺谛卡小姐，身为人类的她如果被重塑之手抓住……\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Stranger, where are we now? Ms. Amundsen is a human. If she's been caught by Manus Vindictae ...

**“无名者”**：嘘……小声些。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Shh, keep it down.

**“无名者”**：这是进入火山神殿的唯一通道，是最保险，也是最危险的路。\
**Ms. Stranger**: We're in the tunnel to the sanctuary. It's the easiest path to follow, but also the most dangerous.

**十四行诗**：这里是……一片黑湖吗？\
**Sonetto**: Is that a lake?

场景图-环形广场-差分1-塞满教徒

长久的沉默后，似乎没有人敢开口定论，但所有人都已心知肚明。\
A prolonged silence hangs after the question. The answer obvious, yet the words petrify on their tongues.

**维尔汀**：不，不是黑色的湖水……\
**Vertin**: No. That isn't water.

风吹拂着黑色的麻布披挂，盖在众人头上的兜帽却纹丝不动，只有边角似涟漪一般颤抖。\
The wind tugs at black hemp cloaks, but the hoods remain unnervingly still.

**十四行诗**：信徒……\
**Sonetto**: It's the believers ...

环形广场被信徒淹没，“湖面”随他们高低跪坐的姿势起起伏伏。\
The circular plaza is flooded with believers, the "lake" rippling with their kneeling forms.

**众教徒**：启明的星，闪烁不见他们的双眼\
**Believers**: Their eyes see not one light of the Bright Star.

**阿尼姆斯**：殉难使祂进一步重归圣座，至此，即便是苦难和死亡都再不能使祂黯淡。\
**Animus**: Down THEY fell in martyrdom, but from death's murky waters, THEY rise once more.

女性长者正站在环形废墟上，她脚踩寒冷的大地，进行着炽热的演讲。\
An older woman stands atop the ringed ruins, delivering fiery words upon the frozen earth.

**阿尼姆斯**：伟大的复苏之母啊，祂的治愈之力存于祂的民中。唯祂能洞悉世间万物，除祂之外，别无主宰。\
**Animus**: Children of the resurrected Mother—lowly bearers of THEIR mantle—let your bodies and souls be the means of THEIR return. It is through THEIR eyes alone that we may see the truth of this world, for there is no Inculcator but THEM.

身着黑衣的信徒们无不低头肃穆地念诵着颂歌。\
Black-clad believers chant hymns that undulate with each wave of rhythmic bows.

**阿尼姆斯**：呼唤吧，祈求吧，复苏之母已经降下启示，超越之门即将打开——此为何等的荣耀啊！\
**Animus**: Call THEIR name! Beseech THEIR light! With the Mother's will manifested, the gate of ascension will swing open! Oh. What glory! Oh. What exaltation!

高亢激昂的声音从广场中心传来。\
A fervent voice erupts from the center.

**“无名者”**：通向神殿的大门就在环形广场后方。\
**Ms. Stranger**: The gate to the sanctuary is at the far end of the plaza.

她执扇指向“黑湖”的对岸。\
Her fan points across the "lake."

**十四行诗**：可这么多重塑信徒……只凭我们几人是无法过去的。\
**Sonetto**: But how do we get past all these Manus followers?

**“无名者”**：别急，十四行诗小姐。\
**Ms. Stranger**: If you look closely, Ms. Sonetto ...

**“无名者”**：看看他们的模样吧。\
**Ms. Stranger**: You'll see what they've become.

黑袍信徒或跪坐，或匍匐，无一例外都低垂着头颅，机械一般念诵着颂歌。\
The believers kneel or prostrate, every head held low, their recitations seeming more and more mechanical.

**维尔汀**：他们的状态很奇怪，就像……没有意识一样。\
**Vertin**: Strange. It's almost like they're in a state of unconsciousness.

**“无名者”**：最保险，也是最危险的路。\
**Ms. Stranger**: "It's the easiest path to follow, but also the most dangerous."

**“无名者”**：每当环形广场举行祭祀活动，使徒阿尼姆斯就会利用面具控制所有信徒，以防节外生枝。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Whenever a sacrificial ceremony is held in the plaza, Animus has all the believers put on masks to ensure she has full control over them.

**“无名者”**：处于这样的控制下，他们心无旁骛，只会关注祭祀一事。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Right now, there is only one thing on their minds—the ceremony.

**“无名者”**：只要我们足够谨慎，就能在祭祀时从他们的眼皮子底下走过，找准时机进入神殿……而除了阿尼姆斯，甚至没有人会注意到我们。\
**Ms. Stranger**: If we're careful and choose our route wisely, we can slip by them unnoticed. No one will see us except for Animus.

**维尔汀**：这是一场什么样的祭祀？\
**Vertin**: What's the purpose of this sacrifice?

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

**“无名者”**：……一场为打开神殿之门而举行的祭祀。\
**Ms. Stranger**: To open the gate.

**十四行诗**：仅仅是为了打开门？\
**Sonetto**: They're taking a life just to open a gate?

“无名者”没有接话，只是全神贯注地盯着那主持仪式的老者。\
Ms. Stranger keeps her focus locked on the elder conducting the ritual.

**“无名者”**：……我们必须要把握住这唯一的最佳时机，才能穿过神殿之门。\
**Ms. Stranger**: We must take this opportunity to slip through to the sanctuary.

**维尔汀**：最佳时机？\
**Vertin**: What exactly do you mean by that?

广场远处传来的念白打断了低声窃语的讨论。\
Another rising wave from that distant voice muffles their whispered discussions.

**阿尼姆斯**：秘之启示者啊，请接受我等的奉献——\
**Animus**: Great Revealer of Arcanum, we humbly present this offering.

女性长者的声音结束，“祭品”走上广场。\
As the elder's voice fades, the "offering" steps onto the plaza.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

即便饱经风霜，其着装仍昭示出了她曾经的身份。\
Though well-worn, her attire betrays her former status.

**十四行诗**：祭品是人类——？！\
**Sonetto**: The offering is human?!

**维尔汀**：不……不仅仅是人类……\
**Vertin**: No. Not just any human.

**维尔汀**：她是一名科考队员。\
**Vertin**: That's one of Nautika's expedition team members.

**十四行诗**：司辰！你看——诺谛卡小姐在他们附近！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, look over there. It's Ms. Amundsen.

黑袍信徒涟漪般一圈圈填满了广场，而在广场对侧的大门边——诺谛卡正站在那里。\
The believers fill the plaza in concentric rings; while across the gates, Nautika stands motionless.

她出神地盯着那名“祭品”，目不转睛。\
She is transfixed on the "offering" with unblinking eyes.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡小姐怎么会在那儿？她的表情看上去……不太对劲。\
**Sonetto**: What's she doing there? Something about her doesn't look right.

**“无名者”**：她离使徒阿尼姆斯太近了，控制信徒的神秘术恐怕也会对她产生影响。\
**Ms. Stranger**: She's too close to Animus. At that distance, the arcane skill controlling the believers could affect her too.

**维尔汀**：——我们要想办法把她救出来。\
**Vertin**: We need to get her out of there.

**“无名者”**：嘘——不是现在！阿尼姆斯会发现我们。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Stay down. Not yet. Animus could spot us at any moment.

**“无名者”**：仪式马上就要开始了。\
**Ms. Stranger**: The ceremony is about to begin.

**阿尼姆斯**：祈祷吧！赞美吧！血与肉的孩子们，与我一同见证吧！我们即将领受祂降下的洗礼——\
**Animus**: Praise THEM! Worship THEM! Children of flesh, bear witness, for we shall bask in THEIR radiant blessing!

**阿尼姆斯**：“门”将代行祂的意志，祭物的血肉将铸就返归旧日荣耀的通途。\
**Animus**: An offering taken, a gate opened! Through bone and blood let the gate fling open, and the path to ancient glory be revealed!

**阿尼姆斯**：你当感恩，未受启迪的愚昧者啊。你竟被允许向复苏之母的奉献，这是何等慈悲，何等垂怜！\
**Animus**: Be thankful, you unenlightened little beast, that the Mother is willing to take your pitiful life as THEIR gift. What great mercy THEY show!

使徒话语中可怖的光景昭然若揭，科考队员却仍然保持着某种诡异的微笑。\
The horrific vision in Animus's words is laid bare, yet Friele maintains her eerie smile.

她信步走向神殿之门，沿途向着跪拜的信徒不停颌首，仿佛正走在一条光明的大道上。\
She walks toward the gate, nodding respectfully to the kneeling believers along the way.

很快，她停在了门前。\
Then she halts just before the entrance.

科考队员的嘴缓缓嚅动，似乎在无声地念诵着什么。\
Her lips mouth inaudible words.

**诺谛卡**：“巨人人母之骨是必经之路，血染的苦痛使子民永生顿悟。”\
**Nautika**: "Through the Giant Mother's bones the path is laid. In bloody pain, eternal life is made."

**诺谛卡**：地母的歌谣……\
**Nautika**: It's just like in Tales of the Mother Spirit.

弗里莱的目光慢慢移动，最终她侧目看到了自己曾经的同伴。\
Friele drifts her eyes rolling over the scene until they seize on the sight of her former companion.

二人的目光在这一瞬间重叠。\
Their eyes lock.

弗里莱干裂的嘴唇上下相接，无声中送来几个熟悉的词。\
Cracked lips part, soundlessly forming words.

“敬拜”、“接近”。\
"Homage." "Approach."

**诺谛卡**：——！\
**Nautika**: ...!

“给你好消息”。\
"A great gift."

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱，你真的要面见“地母”了……\
**Nautika**: You really are going to see Her.

**耳朵虫**：“地母古迹的光芒，引导我辈臣服于自然的律法。”\
**Ear Worm Máhtu**: "The Mother Spirit's light, with ancient glow, guides us to the great current—nature's flow."

**诺谛卡**：《地母故事集》里的第九个故事——\
**Nautika**: The ninth story in Tales of the Mother Spirit.

**诺谛卡**：你即将通过地母身体之门，走向她的灵魂深处，成为她的孩子……\
**Nautika**: "It happened in that season on that day—The children found their Mother at the gate."

**诺谛卡**：你将向她献以至高的礼……你会体会她、了解她、包容她、爱她……\
**Nautika**: "With offerings the finest of their art, they paid Her homage with a faithful heart."

**诺谛卡**：最后，慈爱的她将“给你好消息”……\
**Nautika**: "And in return, their reverence repaid. By Her great gift, Her children were remade."

**诺谛卡**：……改变一切的“好消息”。\
**Nautika**: "By Her great gift, Her children were remade."

门内伸出的无数双手，前仆后继地抓住了弗里莱。\
Countless hands reach from inside the gate, swarming over Friele in waves.

她的四肢荡涤出地脉一般的枝条，现实在她的身体上寸寸解离。\
They coil around her like vines and gnarling roots, reality fracturing across her body inch by inch.

**诺谛卡**：没错，没有错……\
**Nautika**: Right, that's right.

**诺谛卡**：这——就是故事里最“美妙”的情节。\
**Nautika**: This is the climax of the story.

**诺谛卡**：孩子最终走进了地母，了解了地母的悲哀和痛苦，与地母成为了此生唯一的朋友。\
**Nautika**: When the children come close to the Mother Spirit, share Her pain and Her sorrow, and become one with Her.

体内的鲜血沸腾，探险家的喘息几乎要跳出喉咙成为难以自控的尖叫。\
Her breath hitches, a scream claws up her throat, blood boiling in her veins.

**诺谛卡**：孩子——得到了“地母”的指引！\
**Nautika**: The Mother Spirit will come! She'll come to guide us!

“门中之手”缩了回去。

**诺谛卡**：太好了，弗里莱……你做到了！\
**Nautika**: She'll come to guide you, Friele!

消人\
特效-白屏强光

突然，门内爆发出震耳欲聋的悲鸣。\
Suddenly, a deafening wail explodes from within.

**弗里莱**：啊啊啊啊——！\
**Friele**: AAAHHHHH!

仿佛目视了亘古的恐怖一般，尖锐的声音自灼热的胸膛冲出。\
Friele crosses the threshold, and a shriek tears out from her searing chest.

**诺谛卡**：……？\
**Nautika**: ...?

**诺谛卡**：……弗里莱？\
**Nautika**: Friele?

**弗里莱**：啊啊啊啊啊啊啊啊啊——！！！\
**Friele**: AAAAAAHHHHHHH!

尖叫声回荡在纯白的大地上，连地幔中的岩浆都因此停滞凝固。\
The scream echoes across the expanse, its force so profound even the lava seems to halt mid-flow.

场景图-环形广场-差分1-塞满教徒（焦点B）

无措的探险家推了推身边匍匐的信徒，呼吸急促地提问——\
Nautika latches her hands onto a prostrate worshipper, gasping out questions—

**诺谛卡**：你进去过吗？你知道她怎么了吗？\
**Nautika**: What's happening to her? Have you been through there? Why is she screaming?

信徒用沉默表达了虔诚。\
Her questions are met with a devotional void.

一分钟，两分钟，人潮沉默着。\
One minute. Two. The crowd does not speak, does not murmur. Silence rules.

**诺谛卡**：“地母”……\
**Nautika**: Mother Spirit ...

在尖声嘶唳的耳鸣中，世界进入真空。\
That shriek still rings in her ears, muffling all sound as if it were vacuum-sealed.

瞬移\
The believers are unresponsive. Unspeaking.

移动镜头

但每一个身披黑衣的信徒，都不曾为此所动。\
Unbreathing.

他们如死尸一般没有呼吸。

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱……\
**Nautika**: Friele ...

门内不再传出尖叫声了。\
The shriek fades into a dull tinnitus.

使徒持弓点地，寂静就此被打破。\
Animus taps her longbow on the ground, shattering the silence.

**阿尼姆斯**：只是截断舌头便被允许接近伟大之门，真是个幸运的“人类”。\
**Animus**: You humans should be grateful, flawed and pathetic as you are, yet nonetheless granted access to the gate at the mere cost of your tongues.

**阿尼姆斯**：净化未能真正洗清她的罪，审判未能拯救她的灵魂，而伟大的复苏之母仍然宽容地接纳了这份卑微的祭物——\
**Animus**: Deeper is her sin than our cleansing could purge, greater her crimes than our judgment could mete. Yet, in THEIR boundless benevolence, the great Mother of Resurrection has seen fit to accept her.

**阿尼姆斯**：愿引导之人光复肉身，施以神迹，重返世界于本能的秩序。\
**Animus**: May the Guiding One return to us and restore this world to the ancient order.

**众教徒**：愿引导之人光复肉身，施以神迹，重返世界于本能的秩序。\
**Believers**: May the Guiding One return to us and restore this world to the ancient order.

长者疯狂地摇响铃铛，而在她的喜悦中，所有静立的教众也低着头爆发出一片齐声的呼叫。\
Animus shakes her bell, and at the cue, the entire congregation erupts in synchronized cries, heads bowed.

**诺谛卡**：等一下……净化和审判？\
**Nautika**: Cleansing ... judgment? What are they talking about?

为首的女性长者摇铃起舞。\
Animus sways with her bell, the spectacle becoming a wild dance.

祷颂重新开始。\
And the chant resumes.

**众教徒**：启明的星，闪烁不见他们的双眼\
**Believers**: Their eyes see not one light of the Bright Star.

**众教徒**：古旧的迹，便满布羞耻的荫蔽\
**Believers**: Men's past ways are shaded by their shame.

女性长者赤脚在中心绕圈，沉浸在自己略显老态的舞姿中。\
Barefoot, Animus circles the center, fully lost in her movements.

**诺谛卡**：仪式、仪式结束了对吗？\
**Nautika**: I-Is that it? Is that the whole ritual?

探险家左右环顾，小声呼喊询问身旁的教徒。\
She darts her eyes around, searching for some purchase in her whispered questions.

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱去哪里了？门里面究竟是什么地方，还有那些手——\
**Nautika**: W-Where's Friele? What's behind the gate? And those hands ... What were they?

**诺谛卡**：她真的见到“地母”了吗？\
**Nautika**: Is she really with the Mother Spirit now?

众教徒却始终空洞地看向前方，没有回应。\
But their hollow eyes only stare ahead.

**众教徒**：明镜不映诗歌，盲目高呼礼赞\
**Believers**: Paeans are but admiration's mirror half.

**诺谛卡**：那、那个……到底发生什么了？\
**Nautika**: Uh, what just happened?

整齐的祷颂中，出现了一丝不和谐的杂音。\
A dissonant note cuts through the chant.

人类微不足道的声音在天地间回响起来。\
A small voice reverberates between earth and sky, the sound almost pitiful against the enormous volume of the scene.

**阿尼姆斯**：……\
**Animus**: ...

女性长者停下舞蹈，用余光俯视着这位探险家。\
Yet Animus pauses her dance; atop the raised center, she spies down at Nautika from the corner of her eye.

**阿尼姆斯**：——鬼鬼祟祟的耗子，它卑贱的脏爪子竟然踏足了如此神圣的地土！\
**Animus**: Ah, a conniving little rat dares to taint the purity of our sacred land with her profane, filthy paws!

诺谛卡深呼吸了一口气，连肺泡都在颤抖。\
Nautika draws a shuddering breath, the crisp air shivering her inside and out.

**诺谛卡**：我的同伴——弗里莱，她为什么没有从门里出来？\
**Nautika**: My friend—Friele, where is she? Why hasn't she come back through the gate?

**阿尼姆斯**：哈啊，那个卑下的祭物。\
**Animus**: Why, it seems the lowly little beast has a friend to share in her misery.

厌恶和不耐烦挂在她的嘴角。\
Disgust and impatience twist her lips.

**阿尼姆斯**：赞美复苏之母的宽大与包容，祂收下了这份不洁的血肉和那点可怜的灵智。\
**Animus**: She has been taken by the Mother of Resurrection—not that there was much flesh and wit to take.

**诺谛卡**：血肉与灵智……？\
**Nautika**: Flesh and wit?

特效-强光\
A blinding light hits Nautika's face, and her eyes narrow by instinct.

一束强光照射到脸上，探险家下意识眯起眼睛。\
The gate cracks open.

那扇大门打开了一道缝隙。

而后，缝隙越来越大，最终完全敞开。\
They watch as the crack widens into a gap, then a doorway, and finally, the gate swings open.

**阿尼姆斯**：赞颂吧，血与肉的孩子们！\
**Animus**: Praise THEM! Worship THEM, children of flesh!

**阿尼姆斯**：通往神殿的大门已经打开，复苏之母认可了我们的虔诚，我们将被允许观礼最终的仪式！\
**Animus**: The sanctuary gate has opened! The Mother is pleased with our offering, and we have been welcomed into THEIR hall to bear witness to the final ritual!

**阿尼姆斯**：只是献出肉身便能如此靠近祂，那些开门的钥匙应当对祂的仁慈接纳感激涕零。\
**Animus**: Yes, bear witness to all THEIR infinite kindness—THEIR unmatched benevolence! THEY have taken so little, yet THEY grant us so great an honor.

**阿尼姆斯**：伟大的复苏之母、引导之人……感谢您的一切付出和挂念、您的恻隐与仁慈。\
**Animus**: Great Mother of Resurrection, O Guiding One. We fall to our knees before your boundless love.

像是无法再忍受诺谛卡存在于此，阿尼姆斯不耐烦地挥动手掌，驱赶着想象中的苍蝇。\
As if Nautika's presence had become intolerable, Animus waves her hand with the kind of lazy energy usually reserved for swatting flies.

**阿尼姆斯**：别再让肮脏的人类继续玷污圣地，快把她处理掉……复苏之母需要更多血肉，别浪费。\
**Animus**: How much longer do you intend to allow this human to sully THEIR holy land, hm? Feed her to the gate. She must be removed.

没有再看诺谛卡一眼，她径自迈向神殿大门的方向。\
Without another glance, she surges toward the gate.

在她身后，两名沉默的门徒迅速将诺谛卡架住。\
Behind her, two silent disciples seize Nautika.

**诺谛卡**：放、放开我！\
**Nautika**: No, let me go!

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡！糟糕，她被挟持住了……！\
**Sonetto**: They're taking her!

**“无名者”**：……不行，现在还不是最佳时机。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Don't. Now is not the time to act.

**“无名者”**：贸然行动只会让阿尼姆斯解开对信徒的控制，届时我们将更难穿越广场……\
**Ms. Stranger**: If Animus spots us, she might lift her control over the believers. Then we'll find ourselves in some serious danger.

人类探险家像小型禽类动物一样被提起，摔在地上。\
Nautika is lifted up like a fledgling bird, then slammed onto the ground.

**诺谛卡**：——呃！！\
**Nautika**: Ugh!

头晕目眩，耳鸣中，诺谛卡抬起眼，望向不远处的“门”。\
Still halfway in a daze, she looks up toward the gate.

**诺谛卡**：这……这才是整个祭祀的意义吗？只是为了能够打开神殿的门……吗？\
**Nautika**: All this ... It was all just to open the gate?

**诺谛卡**：不、不应该是这样的……对吧？嗯？对吧，小耳朵虫。\
**Nautika**: But this feels wrong, horribly, horribly wrong. This isn't how it's supposed to be. Is it, Máhtu?

**诺谛卡**：弗里莱说她是去面见地母的，她刚才一定是见到地母了，对吧？\
**Nautika**: But, Friele did say that she was going to see the Mother Spirit, so she must be with Her now, right?

**诺谛卡**：不会错的……地母就栖息在那道门之后！\
**Nautika**: Then the Mother Spirit must be there. She must be behind that gate!

仿佛听见笨拙的魔精学语一般，使徒停下了脚步，回身对探险家露出一个莫名的微笑。\
Animus stops—turns back with an inscrutable smile.

**阿尼姆斯**：地母？\
**Animus**: Hah, Mother Spirit?

**阿尼姆斯**：那是什么？\
**Animus**: What nonsense are you sputtering?

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

被摔在地上的探险家摇摇晃晃地站起来。\
Nautika staggers to her feet.

**诺谛卡**：万、万物的潮汐、流动的地衣与岩石、那些滑翔的鹧鸪与游隼，她是统管一切自然的神话！\
**Nautika**: She is the tides! The flowing light! She is the rocks and the soaring partridges and the swooping peregrines! She is the energy behind all things!

**诺谛卡**：她的指引会给孩子们带来“好消息”……足以改变一生的唯一一个“好消息”！\
**Nautika**: She will give Her children a great gift! A gift that will change their lives forever!

**诺谛卡**：从我北境尽头的家乡，到极南之境的此地，正是她指引着我一路探究而来。\
**Nautika**: I have traveled all the way from the northernmost edge of the world to this place, following Her guidance!

**诺谛卡**：而我在这里找到了真相的碎片，找到了残存的，能够验证神话的可能性——！\
**Nautika**: And I have found proof—proof that the legends were true, proof that She is here!

**阿尼姆斯**：噢……我懂了。\
**Animus**: Ah, I see.

长者缓缓走回，长弓在地上敲了一敲。\
Animus strides toward her, longbow tapping once again over the ground.

**阿尼姆斯**：地母……哈哈……哈哈哈哈！\
**Animus**: Mother Spirit ... Ahahahaha!

**阿尼姆斯**：所以，这便是你们所见所想的穷极。真是可悲……何其愚昧！\
**Animus**: That's how you imagine the supreme being of this world, is it? A deity no greater than a charlatan shaman? And what flattery to claim yourself personally guided by a goddess.

**阿尼姆斯**：但我也能理解……未受眷顾的凡俗肉眼，如何能得见至高的真容呢？\
**Animus**: Yet, still, I cannot help but feel a twang of pity. What hope can there be for a kind born with minds too narrow to comprehend true greatness?

使徒露出微笑，眼中升起玩味的恶意。\
Playful malice kindles in her eyes.

**阿尼姆斯**：愚昧不堪造就的人类啊，看在你即将成为祭物的份上，我愿意赐予你一点点真相。\
**Animus**: An inescapable predicament, indeed. Before you are thrown to the gate, allow me to share with you a fragment of truth, so you may die knowing what you've served.

年老的使徒张开双臂，闭上双眼，如主持仪式那般虔诚颂赞。\
Arms spread wide, Animus shuts her eyes with sick devotion.

**阿尼姆斯**：从来就没有什么地母，伟大的复苏之母早在古老之前便存在于此。\
**Animus**: There is no "Mother Spirit." The great Mother of Resurrection has cast THEIR eye upon the Earth from time immemorial.

**阿尼姆斯**：南极——从来都只是重塑之手的“所居之地”，而从来也只有阿尔卡纳女士是唯一的秘学圣母。\
**Animus**: Antarctica has ever been the sanctuary of Manus Vindictae. Here, we serve Arcana, the only and eternal Mother of Arcanum.

当她再次睁开眼睛，恶意的潮水便迫不及待地捂住诺谛卡的口鼻。\
Her lids slip open again, and a flood of venomous glee surges out.

**阿尼姆斯**：这样的真相可不是谁都有资格知道的……比如刚才那个卑下的祭物。\
**Animus**: Few are fortunate enough to learn this truth. What was that pitiful thing's name again?

**阿尼姆斯**：她的名字是……弗里莱吗？无所谓了。她自以为和我等抱有同样高贵的信仰，自愿投入门中，奉献血肉，妄图窥见神明。\
**Animus**: "Fraley"? ... No matter. Your little friend came to me, boldly claiming to share our noble faith, and pleaded to be thrown to the gate so that she may meet her goddess.

**阿尼姆斯**：而我，勉为其难地接受了。\
**Animus**: And though I was inclined to turn down such a blindly foolish request, I agreed.

**诺谛卡**：……？！\
**Nautika**: ...?!

**阿尼姆斯**：她被消化的时候，一定很愤怒，很失望……难怪叫得如此凄厉。\
**Animus**: She must have been ever so disappointed when the flesh dissolved from her bones and her body melted into naught but a lump of flesh behind the gate—all that screaming and crying.

**阿尼姆斯**：谁让你们人类就是这样的东西——以理性自我标榜，目空一切。却只要一点小小的神秘术影响，就会晕头转向。\
**Animus**: Ah, humans. So full of your precious "reason" and "logic," yet turned at even the most basic arcane trick. How foolishly simple you are.

**诺谛卡**：……！！！\
**Nautika**: ...!!!

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

如愿在诺谛卡脸上看到了足够的震惊和痛苦，阿尼姆斯放声大笑。\
Animus laughs. The shock and agony on Nautika's face is expected—anticipated.

**阿尼姆斯**：哈哈哈哈哈哈！对，就是这样，只有这样痛苦又迷茫的表情才最适合人类。\
**Animus**: Ahahahahaha! Yes, that's the look—confusion, disbelief. It suits your kind perfectly.

**阿尼姆斯**：可怜、愚蠢的——人类。\
**Animus**: What a miserable, blind existence.

**阿尼姆斯**：凭着那可怜的、被局限的感官和从未被神秘亲吻启迪的思想，便妄图窥探世界的真相。\
**Animus**: Scurrying about in the dark, unseeing, unperceiving, your limited, darkened minds blind to the spark of enlightenment.

**阿尼姆斯**：明明只是被弃的可鄙造物，从一开始就不具备追随伟大的复苏之母的资格！\
**Animus**: A creation forsaken from its inception. You could never wield true knowledge!

**阿尼姆斯**：你们却胆敢宣称，要解开所有未知的谜题——\
**Animus**: Yet still, you have brazenly infested every corner of this Earth, claiming that you would uncover all its mysteries.

**阿尼姆斯**：如此无知！如此傲慢！\
**Animus**: Such ignorance! Such arrogance!

愤怒和厌恶堆积得太多也太久，如同南极的积雪。诺谛卡正面遭遇着这场恶意的雪崩。\
Rage and revulsion accumulate too much and too long, like a vast bank of snow waiting to fall into an avalanche.

**阿尼姆斯**：你们从未目睹真正的神迹，又要如何支撑自己的想象呢？\
**Animus**: How could you possibly grasp its secrets? How could you catch so much as a glimpse of the greater existence in the barren tenebrosity of your minds?!

像是为了证明她的话，那道巨大的、扭曲的门开始蠕动，做出如呕吐般的姿态。\
The enormous, twisted gate pulses as if to match her statement, a movement somewhere between convulsing and retching.

咕……\
Gulp ...

咕嘟……\
Glug ...

似乎有什么，正在被消化殆尽。\
Something is being digested.

溶解\
赤藻

**诺谛卡**：……？\
**Nautika**: ...?

最终，从门下方延伸出一条条血红的藻类植物，如血管一样盘踞在白色大地上。\
From beneath the gate, strands of crimson slime creep out toward her.

**诺谛卡**：赤藻……？\
**Nautika**: Is that red algae?

赤藻多\
The algae surges below and beyond her, bleeding over the white rock. With every inch it advances, its color decays.

鲜红的赤藻从她的身边冲过，血一样的汁液渗进了白色岩层中，色泽随着它的前进而逐步黯淡。\
Scarlet.

鲜红色。\
Maroon.

棕红色。\
Brown.

棕黑色。\
Black.

黑色。

**诺谛卡**：——！\
**Nautika**: ...!

血红色的、黑色的藻类盘根错节地铺满了遗址城，甚至向着整座冰川延展。\
Red and black algae sprawl across the ruins in tangled knots, their tendrils creeping toward the glacier beyond.

它们构成了这片土地的血管与经脉。\
Blackened arteries pumping and pulsing over the land.

**诺谛卡**：黑藻……\
**Nautika**: There's black algae here, too.

**诺谛卡**：不……不可能……\
**Nautika**: No ... I ... No, no, no way.

**诺谛卡**：我没有吃……我没有……呕……\
**Nautika**: I ate them. I was eating ... No. *vomit*

呢喃般的自我催眠并未起效，探险家抱着自己的肚子跪在地上，喉咙止不住地抽搐着喷出秽物。\
Her murmured mantras fail her. Kneeling, she clutches her stomach as her throat convulses and a stream of vomit pours out.

**阿尼姆斯**：噢……无知的羔羊，满意你得到的“好消息”吗？\
**Animus**: Are you satisfied? Has this "great gift" satiated your curiosity?

使徒踩在了柔软、粘稠的黑藻上。那熟悉的、咀嚼一般的声音几乎要咬碎诺谛卡的大脑。\
Animus steps onto the soft, viscous algae. That familiar, chewing sound grates against Nautika's mind.

**阿尼姆斯**：还不明白吗？\
**Animus**: Has realization finally dawned in your darkened mind?

**阿尼姆斯**：你的同伴，不会再从门里走出来了。\
**Animus**: Your friend is gone. She will never return from the gate.

## 10TH-17 弥涅尔瓦的侍女 / The Owl of Minerva

**阿尼姆斯**：你的同伴，不会再从门里走出来了。\
**Animus**: Your friend is gone. She will never return from the gate.

使徒沉浸在人类破碎的理智中，愉悦地眯上了眼睛。\
Her eyes crinkle with pleasure, drinking deep from tears running over Nautika's face.

在神秘术的控制下，黑袍信徒们仍维持着静止。\
Still held under the arcane skill, the believers remain frozen in place.

**“无名者”**：——司辰，“最佳时机”就是现在！\
**Ms. Stranger**: Timekeeper, now!

场景图-环形广场\
Three figures burst in from the edge of the plaza.

三个人飞速从广场侧翼冲出。

**“无名者”**：Slæstu í djúpan dvala.\
**Ms. Stranger**: Slæstu í djúpan dvala.

特效\
Ms. Stranger charges through the believers, her fan-spell dazing the gate-guarding Apostle just long enough to reach back for the other two.

“无名者”率先从信徒群中冲出，扇面飞出的咒语让门前使徒产生了片刻失神，她趁机回头向落后的二人伸出手。

**“无名者”**：趁现在穿过神殿之门，司辰！\
**Ms. Stranger**: Go! Through the gate, Timekeeper!

**维尔汀**：不能放着诺谛卡不管，十四行诗！\
**Vertin**: We can't just leave Nautika here! Sonetto!

**十四行诗**：Ed è subito sera——！\
**Sonetto**: Ed è subito sera!

特效\
An incantation is cast from Sonetto's glasfeder, and Nautika's bonds begin to unwind.

随着咒语从笔杖中射出，束缚着诺谛卡的桎梏徐徐松开。

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

探险家终于抬起了头，失焦的目光却无论如何都没法在同伴身上停留。\
She lifts her head, but her glazed eyes don't fix on her rescuers.

**“无名者”**：“门”只在接受祭品时会短暂开启——咳咳。\
**Ms. Stranger**: The gate only stays open for a brief time after an offering.

**“无名者”**：时间必须卡得刚刚好！\
**Ms. Stranger**: You have to pass through it before it closes again.

重塑之手的神秘术没能困住使徒太久，阿尼姆斯在几息之间回过了神。\
The Manus's arcane skill falters too soon as Animus shakes off its effects in a blink.

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，我们先走！\
**Vertin**: Come, Nautika!

恍惚的人类探险家被闯入者牵向神圣的大门，目光聚焦之处，领头人颈间蓝色的飘带被风吹起。\
Half-conscious, Nautika is tugged toward the sacred gate, her wavering vision briefly pausing over a blue neck-ribbon as it flutters in the distance.

**阿尼姆斯**：呵！我就知道……！\
**Animus**: Hmph! Why am I not surprised?

她冷笑了一声。\
She sneers.

**阿尼姆斯**：她必定教会我生，或教我死。\
**Animus**: Sie mußte mich leben lehren oder sterben lehren.

**重塑·信徒**：ㄞ——！！\
**Manus Believer**: *roar*

**十四行诗**：——？！\
**Sonetto**: ...?!

原本雕塑般静立门两侧的信徒突然动了起来，巨锤横在了门前，挡住了即将冲进门内的步伐。\
The still disciples flanking the door snap into motion, their massive hammers barring the threshold.

**阿尼姆斯**：卑贱而天真的灰鼠呵……\
**Animus**: How hopelessly naive. How delusionally optimistic.

情况似乎遭遇了滑铁卢，陷入了进退两难之地。\
Their rescue teeters on the brink.

使徒一边擦拭着长弓，一边缓缓踱步走来。\
Animus approaches slowly, wiping her longbow.

**阿尼姆斯**：我很好奇，你们那愚昧的脑袋里有没有考虑过哪怕一秒？\
**Animus**: Has the thought not crossed your ignorant little minds for even a moment?

**阿尼姆斯**：护卫圣所，筹谋仪式，被复苏之母托付以至高使命的我——真的会放任蝇营狗苟之辈在眼皮下乱跑吗？\
**Animus**: Would I, under the supreme guidance of the Mother of Resurrection, simply allow you poisonous little pests to scurry about these sacred grounds right beneath my nose?

**阿尼姆斯**：从始至终，你们都是透明的——无所不在的眼睛早已捕捉到了你们的一举一动！\
**Animus**: Ha! Since the moment you stepped foot on this holy land, every one of you has been under my watch. Nothing escapes my gaze. Not here.

她振臂一呼，更多信徒纷纷从恍惚中苏醒，一拥而上包围了众人，更有信徒在她的示意下钳住了闯入者的双手。\
With a raised arm, she raises more believers up from their trance. They swarm in to encircle the group, some seizing the intruders' wrists at her signal.

隔着黑袍信徒组成的人墙，阿尼姆斯斜视着“无名者”。\
From behind the dark wall of believers, Animus holds a hard stare on the face of Ms. Stranger.

**阿尼姆斯**：“淑女格蕾丝”，我一直想问你一个问题……\
**Animus**: And you, Ms. Grace. Indulge my curiosity.

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

长者越走越近，最终她停在了闯入者面前，长弓点在“无名者”脚边。\
Animus closes in, halting just before the intruder, letting her longbow's tip rest by Ms. Stranger's feet.

**阿尼姆斯**：你脖子上绑着一条迷人的缢索，它提醒着你自己的如履薄冰……\
**Animus**: That noose about your neck—is it simply a choice of fashion, or a reminder of the precariousness of your situation?

**阿尼姆斯**：尤其是刮风的时候，它勒得更紧，更令人喘不上气，一定很难受吧。\
**Animus**: Life must be ever so suffocating, knowing that the smallest breeze could tighten its grip at any moment.

**阿尼姆斯**：如今，你终于能松松这条缢索了，对吗？\
**Animus**: You must be longing to loosen it.

**“无名者”**：您真是会开玩笑……\
**Ms. Stranger**: You're making sport of me again.

“无名者”抬手撩了撩碎发，一只蛾子随之从她的耳侧无声无息地飞出，向光的方向振动双翅。\
She tucks her hair behind an ear, a moth slipping out from her collar as it twirls toward the light.

**“无名者”**：——咳！\
**Ms. Stranger**: *choke*

蛾子被长者两指拈住，碾成了细碎的闪光粉末。\
Animus snaps it from the air, crushing it into glimmering dust between two fingers.

**阿尼姆斯**：蛾子，神秘的辉光之下，人们很难注意到一只微不足道的蛾子……\
**Animus**: Moths. Creatures easily overlooked when eyes are turned to matters of greater import.

**阿尼姆斯**：你是何时加入我们的？\
**Animus**: Tell me—how long have you been with us?

**阿尼姆斯**：又是如何设计爬上光荣的“使徒”之位的？\
**Animus**: What made you worthy to ascend so quickly to the glorious heights of "Apostle"? Hm?

在信徒巨大鼓槌的掩护下，长者绕着“无名者”徐徐踱步。\
A throbbing drumbeat provides cover as she circles Ms. Stranger with measured steps.

**阿尼姆斯**：筹备得如此严密的计划，却正好在你成为“使徒”后频频受阻……我虔诚的眼睛，不会错判任何一名不诚者。\
**Animus**: We have painstakingly cleared the path to THEIR final ritual, yet ever since you reared your head, greater and greater complications have continued to arise. Do not take me for a fool, girl. I know treachery when I see it.

**阿尼姆斯**：你的运气不错。靠着筹备仪式的功劳，顶上了因炼金术事故而离开圣地的勿忘我，得以观礼这场伟大的仪式……\
**Animus**: You were lucky, taking Mr. Forget Me Not's place after his expulsion over his alchemical failure.

**阿尼姆斯**：但你也油尽灯枯了吧？\
**Animus**: But fortune can be fickle, don't you think?

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

**阿尼姆斯**：引导之人的试炼一劳永逸，如祂的存在本身一般永远高悬于我们的灵魂之上……面具的余音随时准备着蚕食不诚者的大脑。\
**Animus**: You need no reminder that the trial of the Guiding One is not to be tampered with. Those who sow discord will be silenced forever.

**阿尼姆斯**：为了维持神智而竭尽全力，丑相百出……可不见半点“淑女”之相，格蕾丝。\
**Animus**: You've fallen. Your ladylike visage cracked. I can only imagine how strenuous the fight against THEIR will must be in the face of your waning willpower.

“无名者”抬手抚过自己的发髻，动作间落下更多细碎的鳞粉。\
Ms. Stranger runs a hand through her hair, releasing a shower of scale powders.

**阿尼姆斯**：只可惜，你燃尽自己换来的这些情报只是微枝末节，基金会的虫豸根本无法与阿尔卡纳女士忠诚的孩子们抗衡。\
**Animus**: You are courageous, I suppose. Ambitious, even. But my! Do you lack wit? For you have found yourself in service to the wrong master. The Foundation is already crumbling at our feet. The information you risked your life to provide has been of little import.

**阿尼姆斯**：你们的兵力被困海上，登陆遥遥无期，而你等来的唯一帮手只有几个可怜的小女孩……噢，其中甚至还有人类。\
**Animus**: At this very moment, the Foundation's fleet is stranded off the Antarctic coast, and the only reinforcements you've received are some arcanist children and a human.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

在长者来回走动的身影之间，两位基金会的闯入者紧张地互相交换着眼神。\
As Animus paces away, the two intruders from the Foundation exchange nervous glances.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

最终，她们的眼神一起来到“无名者”的身上。而后者，在众目睽睽中垂下眼皮。\
Both pairs of eyes settle on Ms. Stranger, who lowers her eyes to the crowd.

**“无名者”**：您说笑了，阿尼姆斯大人。\
**Ms. Stranger**: As I said, you must be jesting, Lady Apostle.

**“无名者”**：我的病根是在“自由海风号”上落下的，您也知道，基金会的司辰……可是一条爪牙锋利的鹰犬。\
**Ms. Stranger**: I fell ill at sea while serving the Guiding One aboard the "Free Breeze." The Timekeeper isn't an enemy to be taken lightly, as I'm sure you're aware.

**维尔汀**：——！？\
**Vertin**: ...?!

**“无名者”**：大名鼎鼎的司辰，乘坐我们留给乌斯怀亚的船只，并被我留下的线索一路指引来到圣所……\
**Ms. Stranger**: She took the ship we left in Ushuaia and followed the trail I carefully placed for her, all the way here.

**“无名者”**：我将她带到了您的面前。\
**Ms. Stranger**: I have brought her to you.

**“无名者”**：这是我一开始就做出的选择，是我带给您与引导之人的礼物。\
**Ms. Stranger**: She is my tribute to you and the Guiding One—a toll I pay for the path I've chosen.

她轻轻拍了拍面前信徒的手臂。\
She pats the believer before her on the arm.

**重塑·信徒**：ㄡ……？\
**Manus Believer**: *roar of confusion*

信徒举着武器的手臂被慢慢按下。\
The weapon-bearing arms lower.

饰蛾的女士信步向前，在阿尼姆斯身旁停下。\
She steps forward, pausing beside Animus.

她跪下身，低头，亲吻长者枯萎的手背。\
Then she kneels, pressing lips to Animus's withered hand.

**“无名者”**：您看，要怎么处理她们？\
**Ms. Stranger**: What would you have me do with them?

**无线电小姐**：你——你从最开始就在骗我们？！\
**Ms. Radio**: You've been lying to us this entire time?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**阿尼姆斯**：……呵。\
**Animus**: Heh.

长者的目光停留在“无名者”年轻的脸上，审视着她的效忠。\
Animus lingers on Ms. Stranger's youthful face, weighing the truth of her allegiance.

**阿尼姆斯**：想要证明你的虔诚，你要做的还远不止这些。\
**Animus**: What did I say about airs and graces? It'll take more than the kiss on the hand and a few hostages to prove your loyalty, girl.

长者绕到饰蛾的女士身后，递出长弓，引着她的手搭上弓弦。\
She offers up her longbow, guiding Ms. Stranger's hand to the string.

**阿尼姆斯**：何不现在就立一个头功，你知道的——伟大的女士会乐意见到如此的故事桥段。\
**Animus**: Go on, end them. The Great Mother will be quite pleased to see THEIR enemies dealt with.

二人一同面朝着几位闯入者。\
Now they face the intruders together.

**阿尼姆斯**：瞄准眼珠，那是我最喜欢的部位。\
**Animus**: Perhaps you'd like to start by piercing their eyes. I personally find it particularly potent in sowing fear.

饰蛾的女士架起铅制细箭，准心指向面前人铅灰色的眼睛。\
Ms. Stranger raises the arrow's tip, holding it level at a pair of cloud-gray eyes.

**十四行诗**：司辰——！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper!

第一助手试图脱困，却被两位信徒架着动弹不得，持笔杖的手几乎要被反向折断。\
Sonetto struggles against the disciples' control; her hand—still grasping her glasfeder—is nearly bent backward.

人类探险家虽然未被挟持，但她只是垂着头喃喃自语，目光呆滞，似乎早已深陷谵妄中无法自拔。\
Though now unrestrained, Nautika mutters vacantly, lost in delirium.

消瘦苍白的双手搭起了箭。\
Pale, slender fingers draw the bowstring taut.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

沉默地抬起头，铅灰色的眼眸迎上了箭尖的寒光。\
Gray eyes face down the arrow's gleam.

**“无名者”**：司辰，注意风向。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Follow the wind, Timekeeper.

飞蛾潮

一瞬间，广场突然刮起雪暴，飞舞的、折射着光斑的白遮蔽了所有人的视线。\
A forceful burst of snow erupts as a squall that covers the plaza; its dazzling whiteness blinding every open eye.

**重塑·门徒Ⅰ**：ㄕㄣㄇㄚ\
<什么？——>\
**Manus Disciple I**: What?

**重塑·门徒Ⅱ**：ㄗㄣㄇㄜㄏㄨㄟㄕ\
<怎么回事？>\
**Manus Disciple II**: What's going on?

**重塑·门徒Ⅰ**：ㄕㄒㄩㄝㄅㄠㄇㄚ\
<是雪暴吗？>\
**Manus Disciple I**: A snowstorm?

**阿尼姆斯**：门徒，别让她们跑了！\
**Animus**: Don't let them get away!

**重塑·信徒**：ㄠㄠ——？\
**Manus Believer**: *roar of confusion*

**重塑·信徒**：ㄞ——！！\
**Manus Believer**: *roar*

迷人眼目、遮天蔽日的蛾群笼罩了广场，落在每一副面具上。\
A swirling tide of moths comes next, thick enough to blot out the sun, wings settling over every mask.

在飞蛾的怀抱中，“无名者”看向基金会的“同僚”，露出一丝欣慰的微笑。\
Ms. Stranger turns to her Foundation colleagues, her lips curling into a faint, relieved smile.

**“无名者”**：“最佳时机”……司辰。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Now is the time to act.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，就是现在！\
**Vertin**: Sonetto, now!

瞬间反应过来的第一助手趁着信徒的一时不察，挣脱了桎梏。笔杖射出的咒语击退了同伴身边的敌人。\
Sonetto pulls herself free, then casts an incantation from her glasfeder, repelling the enemies surrounding her companions.

**阿尼姆斯**：——该死！看住她们！你们这帮蠢货！！！\
**Animus**: Stop them, you fools!

长者的嘶叫在蛾群中翻飞。\
Animus's cries are suffocated in the moth-filled air.

无数对翅膀扇动着，反射着腹地的不落日光，将世界染成纯白。\
Countless wings beating in an audible flutter, reflecting the hinterland's eternal sunlight, washing the world in blinding white.

**重塑·门徒Ⅰ**：ㄨㄛㄨㄛㄎㄢㄅㄨㄐㄧㄢㄌㄜ\
<我、我看不见了！>\
**Manus Disciple I**: I can't see!

**重塑·门徒Ⅱ**：ㄨㄛㄧㄝㄎㄢㄅㄨㄐㄧㄢㄌㄜ ㄊㄚㄇㄣㄗㄞㄋㄚㄌㄧ\
<我也看不见了，她们在哪里？！>\
**Manus Disciple II**: Where did they go?

一时间，神殿门前的广场陷入了疯狂无序的吼叫中。\
The plaza becomes drowned in a cacophony of screams.

**重塑·信徒**：ㄞ——！ㄞㄞ——！！！\
**Manus Believer**: *roar*

**阿尼姆斯**：那副残躯还能施展如此大型的神秘术？你究竟还留了什么基金会的后手——!\
**Animus**: How could you pull such a thing from that feeble body of yours? Just how far are you willing to go in service of the Foundation?

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

“无名者”并未应答，她一点一点地、慢慢地倒在了地上。\
Ms. Stranger doesn't respond. She collapses slowly onto the ground.

飞蛾一一落在她静止的身体上，很快将她裹成了一个无法自如行动的茧。\
Moths descend one by one upon her motionless body, encasing her, piece-by-piece, in an immobile cocoon.

而长者暴怒的余光中，忽然掠过三个身影。\
Out of the corner of the furious elder's eye, she sees three figures flash toward her.

强光之下，手挽手的女孩们已然快要跃进黑暗的门洞——\
The girls stand hand in hand under the glaring light, already leaping toward the dark gate.

**维尔汀**：三、二、一，一起跳进去！\
**Vertin**: On the count of three!

**维尔汀**：三！\
**Vertin**: Three ...

**维尔汀**：二！\
**Vertin**: Two ...

**阿尼姆斯**：——你们是不可能通过的！\
**Animus**: You cannot pass. I will not allow it!

受击\
A lead arrow pierces into Nautika's flesh.

铅箭穿透了血肉。

**诺谛卡**：——呃！\
**Nautika**: Ugh!

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡？！\
**Sonetto**: Nautika!

鲜血溢出厚实的裤脚，探险家踉跄着扑倒在了神殿之门前。\
Blood soaks through the leg of her trousers as Nautika falls before the gate.

**阿尼姆斯**：呵……\
**Animus**: Heh ...

重塑使徒的术法击落了大片飞蛾，越来越多的信徒聚集了过来。\
The Manus Apostle's incantation strikes down whole sheets of moths as more and more believers swarm forward.

**阿尼姆斯**：留下司辰，处理掉其他人。\
**Animus**: I need only the Timekeeper. Dispose of the rest.

**重塑·信徒**：ㄞ——！ㄞㄞ——！！！\
**Manus Believer**: *roar*

**阿尼姆斯**：棘手的虫豸，打不死的灰老鼠，亵渎的不诚者……\
**Animus**: Sickening little pests, blasphemous filth.

**阿尼姆斯**：呵，还有那狂妄自大、自以为是的“传道者”……\
**Animus**: And that ever self-important "Preacher."

阿尼姆斯眯起眼睛看着顽强抵抗的众人，脸上突然露出玩味的笑容。\
Animus narrows her eyes at their stubborn resistance, then flashes a smirk.

**阿尼姆斯**：走吧！血与肉的孩子们，无须再与愚者纠缠，祂可等不了这么久。\
**Animus**: Come, children of flesh! We need not entertain these fools any longer. The Mother awaits.

特效\
Her longbow taps the ground as arcane light floods the plaza in eerie blue.

长弓点地，神秘术的光芒将广场照成了一片蓝。\
At her command, the Manus believers advance like a long-awaited avalanche—layer upon layer closing in, yet none spare a glance for the intruders.

随着长者的号令，重塑信徒们像流动的山一般层层靠近、收拢，却无人再对几名闯入者投来关注。\
The crowd presses around Animus, who stares back at the intruders with undisguised contempt.

众信徒簇拥着阿尼姆斯，后者用蔑视的眼神看着闯入者们。\
Then, she sets a foot into the sanctuary gate.

然后，她一脚跨入了神殿之门内。

**阿尼姆斯**：永别了，蝼蚁。\
**Animus**: Let this meeting be our last, heathens.

爆炸\
The blinding light fades and the plaza is empty—the rushing tide of black is gone. Each and every believer has followed the Apostle through the gate.

停顿

强光过后，广场上已无人烟——信徒们追随使徒而去，前往了“门”的对侧。

**十四行诗**：神殿之门……关闭了？\
**Sonetto**: The gate ... It's closed?

“无名者”长长呼出一口气。\
Ms. Stranger exhales a long breath.

**“无名者”**：我们错过了“最佳时机”。\
**Ms. Stranger**: We missed the window.

所有人望向广场前一片冷清的狼藉。\
All eyes turn toward the deserted plaza, now strewn with the chilling aftermath.

**十四行诗**：这也就是说……\
**Sonetto**: And it'll only open again ...

**维尔汀**：……只有又一次活人的献祭，才能让门再次打开。\
**Vertin**: When we make another offering.

## 10TH-18 致云雀 / To a Skylark

长黑屏

停顿

长黑屏

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**无线电小姐**：司辰，你……你在说什么？\
**Ms. Radio**: What-What are you suggesting, Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**“无名者”**：……咳——呼、呼——\
**Ms. Stranger**: *panting weakly*

**“无名者”**：……司辰说的没错，这是进入神殿的唯一……方式……\
**Ms. Stranger**: She's right. It's the only way to open the gate.

**“无名者”**：既然如此……咳咳……\
**Ms. Stranger**: We have no choice. Listen.

**“无名者”**：我去吧。\
**Ms. Stranger**: You have to offer me to the gate.

**十四行诗**：“无名者”小姐！\
**Sonetto**: What? No, Ms. Stranger! We—

**“无名者”**：你们必须往前走，找到兀尔德女士，阻止仪式——咳……\
**Ms. Stranger**: You have to get through. You have to find Ms. Urd and stop the ritual. *cough*

**“无名者”**：而我的任务就是……把你们送进神殿，完成我的使命……\
**Ms. Stranger**: My mission is to get you into the sanctuary by any means necessary.

**维尔汀**：不可能。\
**Vertin**: No, I won't allow it.

**维尔汀**：我们不会为了进门牺牲任何一个人。\
**Vertin**: No more sacrifices.

**“无名者”**：……\
**Ms. Stranger**: ...

**“无名者”**：……肺鱼。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Have you heard of the lungfish?

**维尔汀**：什么？\
**Vertin**: What?

**“无名者”**：一种栖息在非洲淡水中的鱼，它的鳃萎缩到几乎失去了意义，却奇迹般演化出了肺。\
**Ms. Stranger**: It's an amphibious fish found in Africa. Its gills are so shrunken that it developed a second respiratory system—lungs.

**“无名者”**：生活在水中，却靠肺呼吸。\
**Ms. Stranger**: It's an obligate air-breather, despite being a fish.

**“无名者”**：于是，它不属于陆地，可它赖以栖息的水也会杀死它。\
**Ms. Stranger**: It's not a land-dwelling creature, but if it's kept from the air for too long, it'll drown in its own watery habitat.

**维尔汀**：赖以栖息的水……\
**Vertin**: A creature that doesn't belong to land or water ...

**“无名者”**：刚才的蛾潮，损毁了全部的蛾子……我已经失去了回到陆地上的价值。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Exactly. The Foundation is no home to me, and I just used the last of my moths to create that storm. I'm useless to them. If I go back there, I'd drown, just like the lungfish.

**“无名者”**：唯有完成使命，才不至于白白溺毙于水中，这才是使我具有成为“我”意义的结局。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Let me open the gate. Spare me from drowning like the lungfish. Let me fulfill my role.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：不，“无名者”小姐。厅堂很宽广，屋檐下一定有你的一席之地。\
**Vertin**: It's a big world, Ms. Stranger. There will always be a place for you.

**维尔汀**：而我们一定还能找到其他开门的方法，或者找到其他的路。\
**Vertin**: We'll find another way to enter the sanctuary.

**维尔汀**：无线电小姐，麻烦你尝试一下能否联系上乌尔里希组长，他们那儿或许能有新的发现。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Radio, could you get Mr. Ulrich on the line? Perhaps he has another lead.

**十四行诗**：……？\
**Sonetto**: ...?

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡？你还好吗？\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen? How are you feeling?

**十四行诗**：你还能走吗？对了，我这里还有些独角鲸牙糖，能抑制恐慌……\
**Sonetto**: Are you able to get up? Here, take these narwhal ivory candies. They might help calm your nerves.

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡！你要去哪里？诺谛卡？\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Amundsen? Where are you going? Nautika?

下降

**弗里莱**：这是一块龙涎香，罗夫伯伯。\
**Friele**: It's ambergris, Uncle Rolf!

**诺谛卡**：动作轻一些，弗里莱！龙涎香里还包裹着什么——！\
**Nautika**: Be careful, Friele! Gently! Look, there's something trapped inside.

随着精密切刀一点点将龙涎香的外壳割开，一老一小两双眼睛凑近一块小小的石头。\
A scalpel slides delicately over the ambergris, revealing a small stone that draws in the faces of an old man and a child.

在照明灯下，那新鲜的乳色石块散发着流动的光彩。\
Beneath the glow of the work light, the newly exposed milky pink stone shimmers with liquid radiance.

**祖父**：光泽、颜色、结构同我们之前分析过的所有岩层都不一样……无与伦比。\
**Grandfather**: The reflection, the color ... What an interesting structure. This isn't like any rock sample we've studied before. How extraordinary.

**祖父**：不是由岩浆结晶演化而来，也没有任何由生物沉积形成的特征……\
**Grandfather**: It's not crystallized magma, nor any sediment I'm familiar with.

**祖父**：诺谛卡……这是“地母”给我的“好消息”。\
**Grandfather**: I believe this is a gift from Her, Nautika.

**祖父**：这是神迹。\
**Grandfather**: The great gift of the Mother Spirit.

小孩胖乎乎的手轻轻握起吊坠。\
The girl's fingers close around the pendant.

**诺谛卡**：这是神迹，弗里莱。\
**Nautika**: Grandpa said that it's a gift from the Mother Spirit, Friele.

**诺谛卡**：一定有什么秘密藏在南极，藏在这枚石头里。\
**Nautika**: I bet Antarctica is filled with all kinds of secrets about this little stone.

雪原1

**众科考队员**：“富足的收成是人类的福音，盲童亦要被指引迷津。”\
**Expedition Team Members**: "The harvest's bounty mankind's blessing be. We children, blind, from mazes must be free."

**诺谛卡**：祖父没有找到的岩层，我会去找。\
**Nautika**: I'll find the stratum Grandpa never found.

雪原2

**队友Ⅰ**：已经进入冰区了！拿上望远镜，探险家们！\
**Team Member I**: Entering the ice zone. Grab your telescopes, explorers.

**诺谛卡**：祖父没有发现的时代，我会去发现。\
**Nautika**: I'll explore the eras Grandpa never explored.

雪原3

**队友Ⅰ**：六分仪的测算准确无误，只要我们一直沿着这个方向进发……\
**Team Member I**: The sextant was right. As long as we stick to this direction ...

**诺谛卡**：祖父没有解开的南极谜团，我会去揭露——\
**Nautika**: I'll reveal the secrets Grandpa never revealed.

**队友Ⅳ**：给，这是我最爱的奈普顿巧克力，它能让你多暖一阵子。\
**Team Member IV**: Here. It's a Neptune bar—my favorite. It'll keep you warm a little longer.

进独白黑屏

关闭浮窗道具

回黑屏

**无线电小姐**：诺谛卡小姐？诺谛卡小姐！\
**Ms. Radio**: Ms. Amundsen? Ms. Amundsen!

**无线电小姐**：怎么办，她好像没有办法自主脱离谵妄……\
**Ms. Radio**: What do we do? She's not responding. It's like she's in some kind of trance.

**十四行诗**：抑制恐慌的独角鲸牙糖已经给她嚼完了……司辰，我想尝试对她施展一次平静咒。\
**Sonetto**: I already gave her all of our candies. Maybe a calming spell will snap her out of it.

**诺谛卡**：呜……大家都在……\
**Nautika**: *soft groan* What ... What's everybody doing here?

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，你醒了？\
**Vertin**: Nautika! Thank goodness.

**维尔汀**：你刚刚似乎陷入了谵妄，我们叫了你很久，你都没有反应。\
**Vertin**: You were caught in a trance. You weren't responding at all.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

**诺谛卡**：我们现在是什么情况……？\
**Nautika**: What's happened?

**十四行诗**：神殿之门关闭了，如果想要开启……我们可能无法满足条件。\
**Sonetto**: The gate's closed. We're trying to figure out how to get past it without ... resorting to that.

**维尔汀**：没错，我们正在尝试联系乌尔里希组长，准备制定下一步的行动计划。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Radio is currently trying to reach Mr. Ulrich so we can come up with a plan of action.

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

从眼神能看出，探险家的思维正逐步清明。\
Nautika's vision sharpens as clarity returns to her.

她望向紧闭的神殿之门，思索了一会儿。\
Her sight finds focus on the closed gate as thoughts trickle back to her mind.

**诺谛卡**：每座火山的山体里都存在一种特殊的结构：熔岩管。它是熔岩曾经冲出的通路，有时会像网一样遍布山体内。\
**Nautika**: Lava tubes. Every volcano has them. They're pathways made by flowing lava that lead to the heart of the volcano.

**诺谛卡**：穿过熔岩管，或许就能绕过那扇门。\
**Nautika**: If we find one, we might be able to get to the sanctuary through it.

**“无名者”**：可能性……微乎其微……\
**Ms. Stranger**: Not very likely.

已然无法支撑自己的“无名者”，斜斜地倚靠在门边。\
No longer able to support herself, Ms. Stranger slumps against the face of the gate.

**“无名者”**：重塑将整个火山都据为己有……阿尼姆斯亲自带人踩遍了每一条通路。\
**Ms. Stranger**: The entire volcano is under Manus Vindictae's control, and Animus has eyes on every possible route. Trust me. There's no way of getting in without her noticing.

**“无名者”**：连……咳咳……连雪地松鼠都找不到可乘之机。\
**Ms. Stranger**: Not even *cough* a squirrel could slip past her.

“无名者”摇了摇扇子，目光再次聚焦在门上。\
With a flick of her fan, she lets her vision rest on the gate once more.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：走吧，我们绕着火山上行，说不定能找到被重塑遗漏的熔岩管，也能试试在高处能否联系上乌尔里希组长。\
**Vertin**: Let's get moving up the mountain. We may still find a lava tube that they overlooked, or at least we'll have a better signal to get in contact with Mr. Ulrich.

第一助手点点头，上前搀扶起虚弱的“无名者”。\
Sonetto nods and steps forward, lifting the weakened woman to her feet.

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，我们出发吧。\
**Vertin**: Nautika, time to go.

探险家点点头，将吊坠挂在了自己的脖子上。\
Nautika gives a nod and fastens the pendant around her neck.

背在身后的背包被沉沉地砸在地上，而后探险家从里面掏出一顶安全帽和一副护目镜。\
With a heavy thud, her backpack drops to the ground. After a short and purposeful rummaging, she produces a safety helmet and a pair of goggles.

地质锤和钢钎也被她拿在手中。\
A geological hammer and steel-pointed chisel now weigh in her grip too.

**诺谛卡**：走吧。\
**Nautika**: Alright. Let's do this.

她抬起眼睛，向前踏出一步，两步，三步。\
She lifts her eyes and takes a step forward, then another, and another.

其他人也依次跟上，向着广场外的方向走去。\
The others follow, heading out of the plaza.

突然，她站定了身子，最后回望一眼一路走来的同伴。\
Then she stops, casting one last look at her companions.

她举起手，晃了晃手中的勘探锤。\
Nautika raises her hand. Her hammer shakes with pride.

而后，她吻上了挂在自己脖上的吊坠。\
Then, she kisses the pendant around her neck.

切跑1放大\
Just as abruptly, she turns back. Her snow boots grind into the snow, carving a deep footprint in the opposite direction.

突然，脚步调转，雪地靴辗在积雪上，踏出一个深深的一百八十度拐弯的脚印。

切跑1

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀、十四行诗、无线电小姐！再见——！！！\
**Nautika**: Vertin, Sonetto, Ms. Radio! Goodbye!

切跑2\
She dashes away.

她飞速地往回头的方向冲去。\
Straight toward the sanctuary gate.

——向着神殿大门的方向。\
Her sprinting strides grow faster and faster,

切跑3\
as she discovers a soaring power in her, one ready to erupt into action.

飞跑的步子越来越快、越来越快。

她脚踩在松软的雪地上，发现自己似乎有某种飞翔的能力，在一瞬间从身体内部凶猛地爆发出来。

**无线电小姐**：诺谛卡小姐！你要去哪里？！\
**Ms. Radio**: Ms. Amundsen! Where are you going?

身后的同伴都在飞速地追赶自己。\
Her friends swivel, moving to catch her.

然而，她们的脚程丝毫赶不上一个探险家的决心。\
Yet no one could hope to outrun this determined explorer.

**诺谛卡**：对不起！我骗了你们！熔岩管不一定通向火山的内部——\
**Nautika**: I'm sorry. I lied. The lava tubes don't always lead to the heart of the volcano.

**诺谛卡**：但是你们总有机会进去，你们一定能进去——！\
**Nautika**: But you'll find a way in. You will, because you must.

**诺谛卡**：而我，我也要用自己的方式去找到我的“好消息”——！\
**Nautika**: And I, also, must find my own path, in my own way.

切跑4\
She's one step from the gate.

她的脚已然踩在距离神殿大门一步之遥的地方。

**维尔汀**：——诺谛卡！！！！\
**Vertin**: NAUTIKA!

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀、十四行诗，我的好朋友们。\
**Nautika**: My friends, my teammates.

**诺谛卡**：我要稍微离开一会儿。\
**Nautika**: I'm going away.

**诺谛卡**：请不要耽误时间——继续往前走吧。\
**Nautika**: But you keep moving, okay? Don't wait for me.

渐白

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡——！不要！\
**Sonetto**: No! Nautika! Come back!

胸前的吊坠随动作前荡，凌空划出一个坚决的弧度。\
The pendant swings forward with her movement, cutting a decisive arc through the air.

人类一跃而起，向前眺望。\
She leaps up, fixing her eyes ahead.

渐白

**诺谛卡**：这块龙涎香里裹着的到底是什么，爷爷？\
**Nautika**: What's inside this ambergris, Grandpa?

**诺谛卡**：是一块未经研究的样本，是神迹，还是什么都不是？\
**Nautika**: A new area for research? A message from the Mother Spirit? Or just an ordinary mix of minerals?

**诺谛卡**：与这片冰川底下的大地相比，人类的年龄太小、能看到的东西太少。\
**Nautika**: The mountains and plains beneath the snow and ice ... They're so very large and old. We're just so tiny and young compared to them, you know?

**诺谛卡**：在这个探知的过程中，我们或许终其一生都无法理解自然界中所有的秘密。\
**Nautika**: I think some secrets will always stay that way—secrets. No matter how much we explore.

人类垂下眼。\
Nautika lowers her eyes.

在凝固的光芒中微笑。\
She smiles in the frozen light.

**诺谛卡**：但是，只要我足够近——\
**Nautika**: But still, if I get closer, look harder ...

**诺谛卡**：只要我足够近，我就能看到足够多。\
**Nautika**: Maybe I'll see just a little bit more.

她重新抬起眼。\
She lifts her eyes again.

那全然的、深邃的寂静，在其面前鼓动着。\
A deep and utter silence pulses in the air before her.

消白

渐入

**诺谛卡**：祖父，原来……\
**Nautika**: Grandpa, I see it now.

渐入

**诺谛卡**：原来那发光的未知本身——\
**Nautika**: It was the unknown that I was chasing, not answers.

**诺谛卡**：竟会令我如此着迷啊……\
**Nautika**: It was the beautiful, glorious unknown.

停顿

**诺谛卡**：……！！！\
**Nautika**: ...!!!

**诺谛卡**：……\
**Nautika**: ...

一瞬间。\
One heartbeat.

世界万物一新。\
The world stands renewed.

变浅\
None among them even manages to catch the hem of her garment as it lifts in the wind.

众人甚至未能抓住她被风扬起的衣角。

**维尔汀**：——不要！\
**Vertin**: Don't!

变浅\
Silence returns, as if sound itself has drained away into a hidden funnel.

静得像一切都被抽干。\
No wind. The lava lies still. The sun holds its place in the polar sky.

没有风，岩浆静止，甚至如极昼和极夜一般漫长的缄默都没有。

渐白

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

门。\
The gate.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

开了。\
Opens.

## 10TH-19 旧路新程 / Same Road, Different Destinations

起步\
And he still on was led, but with such thoughts Accompanied of things past and to come Lodged in his breast as well might recommend Such solitude before choicest society. —John Milton, Paradise Regained The way he came, not having marked return, Was difficult, by human steps untrod;\
In a place as silent as a tomb, even the slightest motion can feel like a crashing wave.

他所行之路，不曾留下记号，

难以折返，也不见他人踪迹；

他拾路前行，但脑中思绪萦绕，

回忆往事，思考未来，

胸中积满种种念头，并劝导人们，

需在此种孤寂中静心思考。

——弥尔顿《复乐园》

他拾路前行，但脑中思绪萦绕， 回忆往事，思考未来， 胸中积满种种念头，并劝导人们， 需在此种孤寂中静心思考。 ——弥尔顿《复乐园》 他所行之路，不曾留下记号， 难以折返，也不见他人踪迹；

静如墓地的巢穴内，仅是一点细微的震动就足以掀起巨大的波澜。

**？？？**：……“门”又一次打开了。\
**???**: The gate has opened once again.

**伊戈尔将军**：也是时候兑现你们的承诺了，传道者。\
**Admiral Igor**: Then it's time you made good on your word, Preacher.

传道者将目光从远处收回。她摩挲着胸前的圣像，缓缓转过身。\
The Preacher withdraws her gaze from the distance. Fingers hang over the idol at her chest as she turns.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：使徒阿尼姆斯已经做好了主持仪式的准备。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The stage is set. Apostle Animus is ready to preside over the ritual.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：雾气也才刚刚涌起，将军。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: But the mist has only just begun to rise, Admiral.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：基金会的舰队还在试图登岸，这种时候，您不该在这里。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The Foundation's fleet is still threatening our coastline. I'd expected you to be busying yourself with wartime affairs.

**伊戈尔将军**：……\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

将军站在阴影中，目光如炬。\
The admiral stands in the shadow, his eyes blazing.

**伊戈尔将军**：你知道我在这里的理由。\
**Admiral Igor**: I am exactly where I must be. You know the reason.

**伊戈尔将军**：自赤道至极点，我的士兵随我风雨兼程。他们的等待与牺牲应该止于此地。\
**Admiral Igor**: My men have fought from the tropics to the tundra in service of our pact. They have endured enough. It ends today.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：那该是您预料之中的牺牲。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: That is a cost you should have anticipated when you entered the pact.

**伊戈尔将军**：预料之中并不等同于理所当然。\
**Admiral Igor**: Anticipation is not the same as endurance.

阴影中的将军岿然不动。\
He remains still.

**伊戈尔将军**：仪式的最后一环也已经凑齐，我们如约践行了祂所传达的一切期望。\
**Admiral Igor**: Now the final piece has fallen into place, and we have done all THEY asked of us.

**伊戈尔将军**：在最后的时刻到来前——我需要祂为我们降下“奇迹”。\
**Admiral Igor**: It's time that you fulfilled your promise—the "boon" for my army.

传道者看着将军，似是审视着他的贡献。片刻后，她点了点头。\
The Preacher studies him, as if weighing his contribution. After a moment, she nods.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：好。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Very well.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：如我们之前所谈，这是我们的承诺。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: As we agreed—

**传道者·苏菲亚**：这就是您所期待的“奇迹”。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: —An army for a "boon."

**伊戈尔将军**：……\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

**伊戈尔将军**：焰光闪烁。\
**Admiral Igor**: Flamo Flicker.

触到盒子外壁的瞬间，神秘学能量的火光倏地撞入了虚无。神秘术没能在盒子上留下丝毫痕迹。\
The moment her fingers touch the box's surface, arcane energy vanishes into void, leaving not a single mark behind.

**伊戈尔将军**：……\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

**伊戈尔将军**：……如果……\
**Admiral Igor**: If only we had claimed it sooner ...

**伊戈尔将军**：如果1999年我们能拿到它……\
**Admiral Igor**: If only we had held it in our hands in 1999 ...

传道者摇了摇头，伸手按在了盒子上。\
The Preacher shakes her head, then presses her hand against the box.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：将军，潘多拉之盒还没到打开的时候。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The fruit is not yet ripened, Admiral. To pluck it too soon is to bring ruin.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：这的确是一份奇迹，但也仅此而已。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: The "boon" will grant precisely what you asked, but not without a price. Take heed of my words: some doors are better left unopened.

传道者看向将军胸前闪烁着银色寒光的军徽。跨越数场“暴雨”，它依旧锃亮如新。\
She shifts her vision up to the admiral's chest, where his silver insignia glints under the cold sun. Awarded for surviving multiple "Storms," it remains polished, like new.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：您应该已经决心摒弃过往的荣耀，踏上这条新的道路。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: I trust you laid down your past when you chose to stand with us.

**伊戈尔将军**：……我已经做出了选择，传道者。\
**Admiral Igor**: My path is set, Preacher.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：那么，希望您能坚定地走在正确的道路上，将军。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Then do not stray, Admiral.

将军别开传道者的手，将“奇迹”收入怀中。他没有丝毫留恋，转身离开了冰冷的巢穴。\
The admiral brushes her hand aside, tucking the "boon" into his coat. He leaves the frozen den without so much as a backward glance.

通讯器如约响起。\
The communicator crackles to life.

**莫莉德尔**：将军。\
**Moldir**: Admiral.

**伊戈尔将军**：“交易”已经完成了。\
**Admiral Igor**: The pact is concluded.

**莫莉德尔**：收到。接下来的命令是？\
**Moldir**: Understood. What are your orders?

**伊戈尔将军**：计划可以进入下一阶段了。\
**Admiral Igor**: Proceed to the next stage.

**莫莉德尔**：……我明白了。\
**Moldir**: Yes, sir.

听筒对面，呼吸均匀。\
The one on the other end of the line breathes evenly.

**莫莉德尔**：执行下一阶段计划前，我希望先完成一件个人事务。\
**Moldir**: But may I first request permission to attend to a personal matter?

**伊戈尔将军**：个人事务？\
**Admiral Igor**: A personal matter?

将军轻笑了一下。\
He lets out a soft chuckle.

**伊戈尔将军**：当然，这是你的权利。\
**Admiral Igor**: *chuckle* Permission granted. Do as you see fit.

**莫莉德尔**：是，父亲。\
**Moldir**: Thank you, Father.

通讯切断。\
The call ends.

将军低头摩挲着自己的手掌，上面的每一个茧他都认识。\
The admiral looks down, rubbing his calloused palm—every bump and scab familiar.

正如他熟悉自己的每一个“孩子”。\
As familiar as each of his children.

结束通讯。中尉深吸一口气，让冰凉的空气灌入肺部，迫使身体的每一寸都苏醒过来。\
Moldir takes a deep breath, the icy air forcing every fiber of her body awake.

**莫莉德尔**：白手套队长，我们的等待结束了。\
**Moldir**: Standby is lifted. We are clear to proceed. Sergeant White Gloves?

**白手套队长**：中尉，您的意思是……\
**Sergeant White Gloves**: Lieutenant! Did you just ...

队长看着自己的上级，从她的眼眸中看到了与其父亲相似的坚毅神采。\
The sergeant watches his superior. The gleam in her eyes holds the same unyielding resolve that once belonged to her father.

**莫莉德尔**：通知队伍，清理之前探查出的重塑之手眼线，做好从据点撤离的准备。\
**Moldir**: You heard me. Eliminate the Manus spies. Prepare for immediate evacuation.

**莫莉德尔**：通讯员，按照之前的准备屏蔽重塑之手所有的监听信号，和托勒密那边取得联络。\
**Moldir**: Comms, block all intercepting Manus signals and get Ptolemy on the line.

**莫莉德尔**：对了，还有——丹尼洛夫机长呢？\
**Moldir**: Where is Captain Danilov?

**机长**：中尉，我正要向您汇报好消息。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Here, Lieutenant. And I have good news.

**机长**：您的神秘术发挥了作用。各处都检查完毕，直升机可以顺利启动了。\
**Aircraft Captain**: Your arcane skill did the trick. The helicopter is now fully operational.

**莫莉德尔**：很好。\
**Moldir**: Very good, Captain.

迎着机长标准的军礼，中尉踏雪步伐坚定地向着直升机走去。\
Returning the captain's salute, Moldir marches through the snow toward the helicopter.

**莫莉德尔**：既然已经选择了脚下的道路，此刻唯有前进。\
**Moldir**: This is the path we have chosen. There will be no straying from it.

**莫莉德尔**：“以卵击石还是奇迹乍现”……我们将亲身验证最终的答案。\
**Moldir**: Time to find out whether we're the "idiots" or the ones to leave victorious.

漆黑的熔岩壁彰显着它古老的可怖。\
The black lava wall looms, its ancient terror undisguised.

静如墓地的通道内，哪怕落针的声音都显得格外刺耳，闯入者只得将声音放得更轻。\
The tunnel is as quiet as a tomb; even a dropping pin would send waves of echoes between the walls. The unwanted visitors lower their voices.

**十四行诗**：司辰，“无名者”小姐和无线电小姐都已经进入箱中休息了。\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, Ms. Stranger and Ms. Radio have settled down in the suitcase.

**维尔汀**：辛苦你了，十四行诗。前面的路只会越来越危险，箱子里更安全。\
**Vertin**: Thank you, Sonetto. It's the safest place for them to stay now that we're getting deeper into the volcano.

关上卡扣，提起箱子。\
She snaps the clasps shut and picks up the suitcase.

尽量不去回望身后可怖的神殿大门，而是向前看去。\
She forces herself forward, away from the terrifying gate at her back.

**维尔汀**：穿过这条甬道后，恐怕就是仪式举行的地方了。\
**Vertin**: The sanctuary is just ahead. Manus Vindictae should be holding the ritual there.

**维尔汀**：如果发生最坏的情况，就按照我们之前商量好的对策执行。\
**Vertin**: Should the worst happen, you know what to do.

**十四行诗**：……好的。\
**Sonetto**: Yes, Timekeeper.

**十四行诗**：对了，司辰……我想将它交给您。\
**Sonetto**: Oh, and, I'd like you to have this.

皱巴巴的手绘地图，红色的笔迹深深地刻印其上。除却许久之前的记录，又多了不少新的印记。\
The crumpled hand-drawn map bears deep red markings, old records now interlaced with fresh annotations.

它曾被人类探险家的汗渍和泪水打湿，最终来到了期许之地。\
This map, soaked with Nautika's sweat and tears, has at last found the promised land.

——以不被期望的方式。\
But in a way no one had ever hoped.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

沉默着接过地图，将难言的情感化作向前的脚步。\
She takes the map without a word, her unspoken feelings driving her every step.

令人窒息的沉默之中，零星的脚步声显得格外刺耳。\
The oppressive silence makes every scattered brush of boot on stone unbearably loud.

脚步声越来越快、越来越快，直至为石子所绊，几欲跌倒。\
Someone's pace quickens until a loose stone trips her.

**十四行诗**：唔——！\
**Sonetto**: Urgh!

**维尔汀**：小心，十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: Careful, Sonetto. Are you alright?

**维尔汀**：……你在发抖吗？\
**Vertin**: Are you ... shaking?

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**十四行诗**：……我没事，司辰。只是这里有点冷。\
**Sonetto**: Don't mind me, Timekeeper. It must be the cold air.

第一助手站直了身体，但手臂仍有些不自然地弯曲着。\
She straightens her body, though her arm remains stiff and held at an unnatural angle.

**十四行诗**：冷到连温暖咒都无法生效。我不由得在想……\
**Sonetto**: Even the warming incantation is failing.

她停顿了一会儿，声音颤抖起来。\
She pauses. A wavering hint of pain creeps into her voice.

**十四行诗**：……诺谛卡走入门内的时候，是否也感受到了一样的寒冷呢？\
**Sonetto**: Is this how Ms. Amundsen felt when she passed through the gate?

**维尔汀**：十四行诗……\
**Vertin**: Sonetto ...

**十四行诗**：司辰，我觉得诺谛卡很勇敢……要是我也能像她一样勇敢就好了。\
**Sonetto**: She was so brave. Braver than I could ever be. I wish I had the same courage to pursue what I want.

**十四行诗**：不、对不起……我不该在这时候说这个的。\
**Sonetto**: Sorry, Timekeeper. This isn't the time.

**十四行诗**：忘了它吧。我明白，我们还有任务在身。\
**Sonetto**: Let's move on. There's still much to be done.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

第一助手深吸一口气，抑制住自己颤抖的声音。\
With a deep breath, Sonetto suppresses the shaking in her words.

**十四行诗**：“我们该把精力放在最高使命上……”\
**Sonetto**: "We must turn our eyes to the supreme mission alone."

她喃喃念着，再度向前迈步。\
Muttering to herself, she takes another step forward.

**十四行诗**：我们走吧，司辰。一定要阻止重塑之手的仪式才行。\
**Sonetto**: The ritual must be stopped. Shall we go, Timekeeper?

**维尔汀**：……嗯。\
**Vertin**: Yes.

急促脚步声再次响起。\
The sound of hurried footsteps rises again.

然而这一次，它很快得到了来自甬道另一端的回应。\
This time, it's met with an echo from the far end of the tunnel.

脚步声\
Footsteps come to a sudden stop, the ring of metallic ornaments lingering in the air.

赤足的脚步先停了下来，金属饰物与衣料的摩擦声回荡了约1.414秒后，才消弭于空气中。

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia the Preacher**: ...

**十四行诗**：……苏菲亚小姐！\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Sophia!

甬道内的空气近乎凝滞，传道者的影子却在岩壁上不断跳跃。\
The air hangs stagnant in the dark space, yet the Preacher's shadow dances wildly over the stone walls.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: Sonetto.

第一助手交换来一个眼神，她点了点头，笔杖尖端凝聚起神秘术的能量。\
Sonetto exchanges a glance with her, then nods, arcane energy coalescing at the tip of her glasfeder.

传道者握紧了手中的圣像，染上漆色的光辉瞬间席卷而来。\
The Preacher tightens her grip on the idol, and radiance surges forth from it.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：Διορθωθεί το σφάλμα!\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Διορθωθεί το σφάλμα!

震屏

**维尔汀**：就是现在！\
**Vertin**: Now, Sonetto.

“砰——！！”

**传道者·苏菲亚**：咳咳、咳……这是……\
**Sophia the Preacher**: *coughing* What's ...

粉紫色的烟雾弥漫开来。烟尘散去的时候，传道者眼前只剩下了一顶帽子。\
A haze of pink and purple smoke billows out. When the dust settles, only a hat remains.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，我们快走！\
**Vertin**: Run!

第一助手应声而动，从通道深处却再度涌出了一股浓厚的雾气，将她隔离在外。\
Sonetto springs into action, but another wave of dense mist rolls out from the tunnel, cutting her off.

**十四行诗**：这不是迷障泡泡球的味道……\
**Sonetto**: This mist ... It's not from the Misty Bubble Ball.

这场雾无味、轻薄，却又沉重得无处不在。正如那笼罩湖面，孤独地试图推动纺车的雾一般。\
Odorless, thin, yet oppressive and omnipresent, like the fog over the lake trying to turn the Spinning Wheel.

**维尔汀**：别过来——！\
**Vertin**: Stay where you are!

隔着朦胧的雾，第一助手的身影猛地停了下来。\
Through the mist, Sonetto jerks to an abrupt halt.

**维尔汀**：这场雾和箱中湖泊的雾气很像……还记得吗，你曾差点晕倒在雾气中。\
**Vertin**: It looks just like the mist that hangs over the lake in the suitcase. You collapsed in it once, remember?

**十四行诗**：……！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

**传道者·苏菲亚**：别想离开！\
**Sophia the Preacher**: You cannot escape!

漆黑的粘液再度追逐试图离去者的脚步而来。\
The black mucus surges forward again, chasing after those attempting to flee.

**十四行诗**：Regna sereno intenso ed infinito!\
**Sonetto**: Regna sereno intenso ed infinito!

粘液被神秘术挡下。第一助手拦在传道者身前，握紧了玻璃笔杖。\
The arcane skill intercepts the creeping black. Sonetto steps in front of the Preacher, her glasfeder gripped tight.

**十四行诗**：……看来我只能走到这里了。\
**Sonetto**: It seems this is the farthest I go.

**十四行诗**：司辰，请您继续前进。我留在这里掩护您。\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, go on without me. I'll hold her off.

最后一次交换了眼神，脚步毅然地踩进了渐浓的雾中。\
A final glance is exchanged before she disappears into the thickening mist.

**十四行诗**：我不会让你阻拦司辰的道路，苏菲亚小姐。\
**Sonetto**: If you want to stop the Timekeeper, Ms. Sophia, you'll have to get past me first.

**十四行诗**：你曾说过，下次见面时我们就是敌人了。\
**Sonetto**: You once said that you'd draw steel the next we meet. Well, now's your chance.

**十四行诗**：所以，你的对手是在这里的我。\
**Sonetto**: Make your move.

消人\
The glow of arcane skills collides and flickers out in midair, over and over.

攻击

神秘术的光辉在空中反复碰撞又消逝。

**十四行诗**：苏菲亚小姐……\
**Sonetto**: Ms. Sophia ...

**十四行诗**：我至今仍不明白，你为什么要站到重塑之手那一方。\
**Sonetto**: To this day, I struggle to understand why you chose to stand against us.

**十四行诗**：究竟是怎样的“使命”，能让你离开曾经的家园，与过往的同伴为敌？\
**Sonetto**: Why did you turn your back on everything? On everyone you loved and who loved you?

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……你变了。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: You've changed.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：在那座岛上你更少说话，更多聆听。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Grown too fond of your own voice and paid too little attention to what's happening around you.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：这就是你想做的事吗？\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Are you sure this is where you want to be?

**十四行诗**：你想说什么？\
**Sonetto**: What do you mean?

传道者漠然的目光投向甬道的尽头。\
The Preacher fixes her gaze on the tunnel's far end.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：司辰已经离开你的监护范围了。这样好吗？\
**Sophia the Preacher**: As we speak, the Timekeeper is leaving your watch. Would the Foundation agree to this course of action?

**传道者·苏菲亚**：比起在这里阻拦我，牢牢看紧她才是你的首要任务吧？\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Shouldn't you be keeping your eyes on her, rather than wasting your words on me?

**十四行诗**：……司辰的使命是阻止仪式的举行。\
**Sonetto**: I trust the Timekeeper will fulfill her duty.

**十四行诗**：而我要做的，是为她扫清前路的尘埃。\
**Sonetto**: As for me—I will clear the dust off the path.

消人\
Every attacking gleam is caught and devoured by the viscous liquid surrounding the Preacher. Yet Sonetto keeps scribbling with her glasfeder in midair.

攻击

攻击的光辉每每发出都被传道者周身的粘稠液体捕获、吞没。即便如此，十四行诗仍源源不断地在空中书写着神秘术式。

**十四行诗**：我也想问你同样的问题，苏菲亚小姐。\
**Sonetto**: I have the same question for you, Ms. Sophia.

**十四行诗**：这就是你想做的事吗？\
**Sonetto**: Is this where you want to be?

**十四行诗**：我在那座岛屿上见过你战斗时的姿态，你那时使用的神秘术和现在截然不同。\
**Sonetto**: I saw how you fought on the island. Your arcane skills aren't at all like the ones you used back then.

**十四行诗**：你的神秘术中不再有过往的信念了。\
**Sonetto**: You've changed, too. Something new has taken root and choked your old faith out from you.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia the Preacher**: ...

攻击\
A single streak of light finally breaks through, severing crimson strands at the Preacher's temple.

一道神秘术式化作的辉光终于穿越粘液的围捕，切断了几缕传道者鬓边的红发。

**十四行诗**：你会在这里阻拦，是代表着我们已经接近仪式的核心了吗？\
**Sonetto**: We must be close to the ritual site for you to show up.

**十四行诗**：德洛丝医生……也在那里吗？\
**Sonetto**: Which means Dr. Dores is close by, doesn't it?

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia the Preacher**: ...

迎着那沉默、坚定、绝不退让的眼神，苏菲亚向前一步，涌起的漆黑粘液再度化为了一道密不透风的屏障。\
Sophia steps forward to meet those silent, resolute, unyielding eyes, as the surging black mucus solidifies into an impenetrable wall again.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：德洛丝女士凭借她的意志到达了这里。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Ms. Dores came to us led by nothing but her own purpose.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：那么你呢，十四行诗？\
**Sophia the Preacher**: But what of you, Sonetto?

传道者抬起手，身前的圣像随着她的动作微微摇晃。\
The Preacher raises a hand; the little idol sways gently against her chest.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：你又是为什么而前行？\
**Sophia the Preacher**: What's your purpose in all this?

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

她只是再度握住玻璃笔。像过往无数次一样，在空中写下术式。\
Her grip tightens around her glasfeder. Just as she has done countless times before, she raises it into the air.

反击

## 10TH-20 人间的线 / The Weaving of Our Pasts

**维尔汀**：呼……呼……\
**Vertin**: *panting*

雾气渐起。\
The mist begins to rise.

**维尔汀**：没错……我曾经见过这种雾，在箱中的湖泊周围……\
**Vertin**: Yes, I've definitely seen it before. This is the same mist from the lake in my suitcase.

渐白

越是深入神殿，雾气便越是浓重，直至连所在何处都难以分辨。\
The deeper she ventures into the sanctuary, the thicker the mist grows, until each step feels meaningless and indistinct.

**维尔汀**：……我走到了哪儿？\
**Vertin**: Which way did I come from?

在无尽绵延的白色之中，一条金色的丝线飘忽着落到了身旁。\
Amidst the endlessness, a single golden thread drifts down.

**维尔汀**：是纺车的线……\
**Vertin**: A thread ...

**维尔汀**：但为什么……我无法捉住它？\
**Vertin**: I can't seem to grasp it. It's like a wisp of smoke.

**？？？**：……♪\
**???**: … ♪

**维尔汀**：是谁？\
**Vertin**: Who's there?

向着声音的来处望去。朦胧雾气的尽头，隐约能看见正缓缓转动的金色圈环。\
Investigating the source of the sound. At the far edge of the hazy mist, the faint outline of a rotating golden ring emerges.

熟悉的景致。一如千百年前，一如数十年前，一如昨日。\
A familiar sight. Just as it was millennia ago. Just as it was decades past. Just as it appeared yesterday.

**维尔汀**：我应该在哪里见过这一幕……但……\
**Vertin**: A spinner at the Wheel. I've seen this before, but where?

什么都想不起来。\
Yet nothing comes to mind.

轻柔的歌声牵着丝线引导去路，追寻的答案就在前方。\
A soft song tugs at the thread, guiding the way forward—the answers lie just ahead.

来吧。向前走，更近一步。\
Come. Move forward. Step closer.

直至触及雾气深处的记忆。\
Until the memories deep within the mist are within reach.

**维尔汀**：……我忘记了什么？\
**Vertin**: What have I forgotten?

渐白\
纯白

**维尔汀**：我遗忘的东西……去了哪里？\
**Vertin**: Where do things go when we forget them?

**？？？**：你忘记了这个吗？\
**???**: Are you looking for this?

停顿

一顶帽子。一顶靛色之上，系着温柔碧青色丝带的帽子。\
A hat. A deep indigo hat tied with a soft teal ribbon.

**维尔汀**：噢，是的……这是我的帽子。\
