**Vertin**: Oh, yes, my hat. Thank you.

**维尔汀**：谢谢您，女士。我没注意到它丢了。\
**Vertin**: I didn't even realize it was gone.

**维尔汀**：它对我来说很重要。您在哪里找到了它？\
**Vertin**: It's ever so important to me. Where did you find it?

**？？？**：在你来时的路上。\
**???**: Along the path you took.

她向远处指去。夏季光线猛烈，模糊了第一防线学校的光景。\
She points into the distance. The fierce summer light blurs her view of the SPDM.

**维尔汀**：我明白了，一定是约瑟夫恶作剧把它藏起来了。多亏您将它还给了我。\
**Vertin**: Must've been another one of Joseph's pranks. Thank you for bringing it back to me.

**维尔汀**：您是学校新来的职员吗？我似乎没有在学校见过您。\
**Vertin**: Are you a new staff member in the school? I don't believe I've seen you before.

**维尔汀**：但您给人的感觉又很熟悉……\
**Vertin**: Though, strangely, I feel as though we've met before, a long time ago.

**？？？**：呵呵……\
**???**: Heh-heh ...

柔和的风掠过，藏起了轻笑的尾音。\
A breeze sweeps by, carrying the trailing notes of a laugh.

**？？？**：我们会再见的。\
**???**: We will see more of one another in the time to come.

风轻轻吹拂过头发，然后远去了。\
The wind rustles through her hair, then nothing.

低下头，手中空空如也。\
She looks down at her empty hands.

**维尔汀**：……那是什么时候的回忆？\
**Vertin**: When did that happen?

金色的线催促着向前的脚步，线另一端的歌声还在继续。\
The golden thread urges her onward, while the song at the other end lingers.

**？？？**：“出发吧，启程吧”\
**???**: Sail, sail free,

**？？？**：“我最亲爱的”\
**???**: my heart and light.

**维尔汀**：“告别港湾”\
**Vertin**: Wave your home a last goodbye.

不知不觉，纺车转过了一格。\
Unnoticed, the Wheel spins out a length of thread.

**维尔汀**：“撑船远航”\
**Vertin**: Wave your home a last goodbye.

**学生Ⅲ**：你在唱什么，维尔汀？\
**Student III**: What's that song you're singing, Vertin?

**维尔汀**：我在梦里听到的歌。\
**Vertin**: It's a song I heard in a dream.

**学生Ⅲ**：我也会梦见爸爸妈妈给我唱歌、对我说话，但醒来之后就忘记他们说了什么了……\
**Student III**: I dream about songs too—about my mom and dad singing them to me. They sing and say all kinds of stuff, but when I wake up, I can't seem to remember any of it.

**学生Ⅲ**：真羡慕你还能记得。你做了怎样的梦？\
**Student III**: It's nice that you remember, though. What was your dream about?

**维尔汀**：我不知道……实际上，我从来没做过梦。\
**Vertin**: I'm not sure. I don't think I really dream at all.

**维尔汀**：不过偶尔，我会在夜晚感觉有谁坐在我的床边，抚摸我的脸庞，唱着这首歌。\
**Vertin**: But sometimes, just before I fall asleep, I feel someone sit beside me. She strokes my hair and sings this song.

**维尔汀**：但每当我醒来的时候，床边总是空无一人。\
**Vertin**: But when I wake up, there's nobody there.

**学生Ⅲ**：这应该不是梦吧。是不是教员来看你了？\
**Student III**: That doesn't seem like a dream to me. Maybe one of the instructors comes to check on you at night?

**维尔汀**：我想应该不是。虽然没有看清过脸，但那个人总给我一种很熟悉的感觉。\
**Vertin**: I don't think so. Even though I don't remember her face, I know she isn't one of the instructors because I feel like I know her.

**学生Ⅲ**：在夜晚带来歌声的人……听起来就像书里的童话故事一样。\
**Student III**: It sounds like a fairy tale. A lady singing by your bed at night.

**学生Ⅲ**：还有什么线索吗，维尔汀？\
**Student III**: Do you remember anything else?

**维尔汀**：嗯……\
**Vertin**: Hmm ...

**维尔汀**：……我想不起来了。我甚至没办法确定她是否存在。\
**Vertin**: Not really. I'm not even sure if she's real.

**维尔汀**：但我好像能隐约想起被她注视着的感觉。和现在很像，被阳光照耀着，暖洋洋的……\
**Vertin**: But when she looks at me, it feels warm, like being in the sun, like we are now.

转过身，伸出手，像是要够到太阳。\
She turns, reaching out as if to grasp the sun.

视野的边缘，霎那间捕捉到了那熟悉的身影。\
At the edge of her vision, she catches a glimpse of that familiar silhouette.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**学生Ⅲ**：……维尔汀？\
**Student III**: Vertin?

定睛望去，树林边缘只剩飘落的树叶被风牵动远去。\
But when she looks, there are only fallen leaves drifting away from the forest's edge.

**？？？**：“所以睡吧，孩子，愿你永远信念坚定、真诚善良”\
**???**: So sleep my baby, grow bright, grow firm.

纺车又转动了一格。歌声停了。\
The Wheel completes another rotation. And the song falls silent.

**？？？**：……维尔汀？\
**???**: That voice ... Vertin?

**？？？**：维尔汀……\
**???**: Vertin ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

又是这个梦……不，是梦吗？\
The same dream again. No, is it even a dream?

今天似乎略有不同。那熟悉而温暖的歌声没有响起，取而代之的是冰冷的沉默。\
It feels different today. The familiar warmth of song is absent, replaced by a chilled silence.

**？？？**：……\
**???**: ...

微凉的手指抚过眉毛、鼻子、脸颊、嘴唇，像是在细致地勾画轮廓。\
Cool fingertips trace across brows, nose, cheeks, lips, mapping every contour.

最终，那只手轻轻地覆盖在了眼睛之上。\
At last, that hand comes to rest over her eyes.

**？？？**：我的孩子……\
**???**: My child ...

**？？？**：去行你应行之路，去求索究竟何为命运。\
**???**: Tread the path you must tread, turn the page you must turn,

**？？？**：去见证最终的答案吧。\
**???**: and seek the answer you must seek.

额头落下一吻，冰凉的液体随之而下，如同雨滴。\
A kiss falls on her forehead, cold liquid trailing after it like rain.

这是最后的告别。\
This is the final farewell.

覆盖在眼睛上的手松开，床边的人起身离去，甚至没留下一句再见。\
The hand lifts from her eyes. The figure at her bedside rises and leaves without even a word.

——不行！不能让她就这样离开！\
No! She can't leave like this!

快从温暖而引人沉溺的睡梦中苏醒，去面对那冷硬的现实，尝试抓住那缕飘散的风。\
Wake up. Shake off this warm, alluring slumber. Rise up to meet reality, harsh, but true. Try to catch that scattering wisp of wind.

快醒醒！\
Wake up!

**维尔汀**：不……\
**Vertin**: No ...

**维尔汀**：停下——\
**Vertin**: Stay with me—

渐白\
白屏

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

记忆中的场景溶进了一片空白。\
The scene in her memory dissolves.

而与那追寻的身影重叠的，是一张关切的脸。\
And overlapping with that figure she's been chasing is a face filled with concern.

**？？？**：你还好吗，孩子？\
**???**: Are you alright, child?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：……德洛丝女士？\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores?

**维尔汀**：不，不对……\
**Vertin**: No. That isn't right.

**维尔汀**：玛尔塔、别斯米尔、兀尔德……我该如何称呼您？\
**Vertin**: Who are you? Marta, Bessmert, Urd?

**德洛丝医生**：……我是德洛丝医生，而“兀尔德”的确是我的笔名。\
**Doctor Dores**: I'm Dr. Dores. My pen name is indeed "Urd."

**德洛丝医生**：我用它写一些文章，但并没有告诉其他人……你是如何得知的？\
**Doctor Dores**: I might have published a few stories under that name, but I've never spoken of it to anyone. How did you come to know it was me?

**维尔汀**：我……我沿着您走过的足迹，找了您很久。\
**Vertin**: I ... I've been looking for you for a long time. I've followed your trail across the world.

**德洛丝医生**：这样啊……辛苦你了，孩子。\
**Doctor Dores**: Ah. I can only imagine how hard such a journey must have been for you, dear child.

盲眼者的手落在头上，勾起了温暖而令人怀念的感觉。\
Dores's hand rests upon her head, stirring a warmth thick with nostalgia.

**德洛丝医生**：但很遗憾，至于你提及的其他名字，应该并不是我。\
**Doctor Dores**: But I'm afraid the other names you mentioned don't belong to me.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**德洛丝医生**：我记得你的名字，维尔汀。我和你在圣保罗有一面之缘。\
**Doctor Dores**: You're Vertin, aren't you? I believe we met briefly in São Paulo.

**德洛丝医生**：你是怎么来到这里的？\
**Doctor Dores**: But tell me, how did you come to be here?

**维尔汀**：我是……我是来找您的，还有阻止重塑之手的仪式……\
**Vertin**: I'm ... I'm here for you, and to stop Manus Vindictae's ritual.

**德洛丝医生**：“重塑之手”……？抱歉，我好像不太明白你所说的……\
**Doctor Dores**: Manus Vindictae? Forgive me, child. I'm afraid I'm not sure what you mean.

**维尔汀**：……请容许我重新说明情况。\
**Vertin**: *steadying breath* Allow me to explain.

**维尔汀**：我是来自圣洛夫基金会的神秘学家。这里即将发生一场极其危险的仪式。\
**Vertin**: I'm an arcanist of the St. Pavlov Foundation. We have intel that a dangerously powerful ritual is soon to be performed here.

**维尔汀**：为了您的安全考虑，请您与我一同回到基金会，接受庇护。\
**Vertin**: In the interest of your own safety, I must ask you to come with me to the Foundation headquarters.

**德洛丝医生**：原来是这样。我明白了。\
**Doctor Dores**: I see.

**德洛丝医生**：我会和你走的，但请稍等我一会儿。\
**Doctor Dores**: I will go with you, but not just yet.

**德洛丝医生**：纺车轮才转动了一点，我想尝试纺织出这些线。\
**Doctor Dores**: There is something I must finish—these threads I'm spinning.

**维尔汀**：……这些线？\
**Vertin**: Threads?

**德洛丝医生**：或许说“线”有些不准确，毕竟只有我能“看到”它。其他人都感知不到它的存在。\
**Doctor Dores**: Yes. Others don't seem to see them, but I do.

**德洛丝医生**：说来奇怪，虽然不明白它是什么，但我却知道该如何纺织它……抱歉，是不是有些难以理解？\
**Doctor Dores**: It's strange. I don't know what they are, but I know how to spin them. Does that sound ridiculous to you?

**维尔汀**：不……我也能看见这些线。\
**Vertin**: Not at all. In fact, I can see them too.

**维尔汀**：这里很危险。或许您可以先和我走，之后我们可以试着一起纺织这些线。\
**Vertin**: But perhaps we should do it together, later, when the danger has subsided.

盲眼者缓慢而坚定地摇了摇头。\
Slowly, firmly, Dores shakes her head.

**德洛丝医生**：我不知道还有没有“下次”。所以，我必须在这里完成。\
**Doctor Dores**: There may not be a "later." I must finish this now.

**维尔汀**：……为什么？\
**Vertin**: Why?

**维尔汀**：这比您的生命还重要吗？\
**Vertin**: Is this worth more than your life?

**德洛丝医生**：是的。\
**Doctor Dores**: I believe it is.

**德洛丝医生**：正如必然纠缠的因果，必须存在的永恒律法。\
**Doctor Dores**: These threads must be spun so the all-ruling law may be woven.

**德洛丝医生**：这是我唯一的选择，是我应尽的使命。它引导我到达了这里。\
**Doctor Dores**: That is my purpose—my calling. That is why I was led here.

**德洛丝医生**：你也是因此而走到这里的，不是吗？\
**Doctor Dores**: That's why you're here too, is it not? To answer your calling?

**维尔汀**：“因此”……？您的意思是……\
**Vertin**: My calling? You mean—

**德洛丝医生**：虽然无法看见，但我能感知到。\
**Doctor Dores**: My child. I may be blind of sight, but my senses are clear.

**德洛丝医生**：你也在行你应行之路。你在求索究竟何为命运。\
**Doctor Dores**: This is a path you must tread, a page you must turn.

**德洛丝医生**：你想要见证最终的答案。\
**Doctor Dores**: This is the answer you must seek.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

熟悉的话语，一如往昔。\
The words sound familiar.

盲眼者不再言语，回过身去，再度将手放上纺轮。\
No more is said. Dores turns away, hands returning to the spindle.

霎那间，她的身影与过往的记忆重叠。\
And in that instant, her figure merges with memories of the past.

**维尔汀**：不……\
**Vertin**: No ...

直觉发出呼喊，然而纺车却已经不可阻止地转动起来。\
She hears herself cry out in desperation. But the Spinning Wheel has already begun to turn.

**维尔汀**：不，停下——\
**Vertin**: No, stay with me—

白色背景。尽头是兀尔德的背影，背影被白光淹没，前景是维尔汀伸出的手。

**维尔汀**：——妈妈！\
**Vertin**: Mum!

视频

**维尔汀**：这是……？！\
**Vertin**: This is ...?

**德洛丝医生**：维尔汀！\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin?

水漫了上来。\
The water rises.

水，更多的水漫了上来。\
More and more water rises.

**德洛丝医生**：怎么会……？！\
**Doctor Dores**: How can this be?

**德洛丝医生**：不……“答案”不该如此……\
**Doctor Dores**: No. This can't be my calling.

**众教徒**：千百万潮水，皆遵循潮汐奔流\
**Believers**: Tides run in blind by their ever-be routine,

**众教徒**：以亵渎不洁的姿态，玷污天幕\
**Believers**: Staining that Heaven with obscene calamity.

**众教徒**：破除枷锁者，主宰一切的复苏之母\
**Believers**: The breaker of death's shackles shall rule us all,

**众教徒**：于今降下，至高福祉\
**Believers**: From this day forth, and evermore.

**众教徒&阿尼姆斯**：来日的恩典即将显现，吾等信徒将于今日蒙福\
**Believers & Animus**: The blessing of the coming age is near. And, humbly, we kneel to receive such grace.

**众教徒&阿尼姆斯**：愿您至高无上之躯，再度降下——\
**Believers & Animus**: O Glorious One, walk the Earth again—

**众教徒&阿尼姆斯**：以无穷大能，重塑应许之地！\
**Believers & Animus**: Shape this land with your mighty, vengeful hands!

**阿尼姆斯**：呵呵……兀尔德女士，感谢你为我们启动了仪式。\
**Animus**: Heh. Ms. Urd. We owe you our thanks for starting the ritual.

**阿尼姆斯**：终于，我们终于可以重新迎回祂——\
**Animus**: At last, we are no longer lost.

**阿尼姆斯**：——吾等的引导之人！\
**Animus**: For the Guiding One is risen!

## 10TH-21 朝圣于来时路 / The Way I Came

伴随着教徒的吟诵声，漆黑的肉团如心脏般不断跳动着，涌动的墨色液体淌入井中那些没有质量，亦没有湿度的雨。\
A lump of dark flesh pulsates like a heart, its flowing black fluid spilling into the well, mixed with rain with neither weight nor wetness.

**维尔汀**：那是……阿尔卡纳？！\
**Vertin**: That lump of flesh is Arcana?

闪回

闪回2

**德洛丝医生**：我纺织的线连向了井底……为什么？这些线的使命不该流向那里……\
**Doctor Dores**: The threads ... They were drawn away somewhere deep below me. This—this isn't right.

盲眼者试图扶住飞转的纺轮，指尖却被擦出一道金色的伤痕。\
She reaches to steady the spindle, only for golden wounds to bloom across her fingertips.

**德洛丝医生**：纺车也无法停下……\
**Doctor Dores**: And the Wheel ... I can't seem to stop it.

**德洛丝医生**：维尔汀，快走——\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin, you must leave.

**阿尼姆斯**：天真。\
**Animus**: Spare me the theatrics.

攻击\
Animus swings her longbow. Black, viscous liquid twists into bonds that pin them both in place.

使徒挥动权杖，漆黑的黏腻液体化作绳索将二人牢牢束缚在原地。

**阿尼姆斯**：仪式已经开启，复苏之母即将降临，休想亵渎这神圣的时刻！\
**Animus**: The ritual has begun. The Mother will return! Such a moment is not to be disturbed!

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

使徒缓缓走近。吟诵声中，她自水中拾起一块白骨。\
Step by step, Animus approaches. Through the chanting, she plucks a white bone from the water.

**阿尼姆斯**：看看这些骨殖，如此苍白冷峻……堪称典雅、神圣。\
**Animus**: These bones are relics of a sacred age—primal, elegant, powerful, just like the era to which they belong.

**阿尼姆斯**：这是不属于被窃夺之世的造物，唯有被抹去的空白时代才能孕育。\
**Animus**: They are but a fraction of the creatures from a time erased from history, from the Blank Era.

**阿尼姆斯**：而现在，我们终于等到奇迹之卵显现，复苏之母将这已逝的时代带回给了我们——\
**Animus**: The moment is nigh. From the embryo, the Great Mother shall rise once more to restore what was lost!

**阿尼姆斯**：祂已重临！与生俱来的枷锁于今破去，过往的荣光再度照耀！\
**Animus**: And break the shackles that were forced upon us eons ago!

**德洛丝医生**：空白时代？带回已逝的时代？……不，时代应该要向前走的。\
**Doctor Dores**: A Blank Era? Restore what was lost? No. Time should move forwards, not backwards!

**阿尼姆斯**：呵，尚处于愚昧中的人啊，看在你为我们开启仪式的份上，我将原谅你的冒犯。\
**Animus**: It seems your blindness is not just of the eyes, but of the mind. Still, I shall forgive your blasphemies. You were the one to start the ritual, after all.

**阿尼姆斯**：即便你对此一无所知，但你的贡献会被铭记。在新世界里，或许还会被授予圣名。\
**Animus**: In fact, your contribution should be commemorated with a title. "The Unseeing Saint," perhaps? It is rather fitting, don't you think?

**德洛丝医生**：不、不……\
**Doctor Dores**: No, I ...

**德洛丝医生**：不对，不能让纺车再转下去……\
**Doctor Dores**: I must stop the Spinning Wheel.

盲眼的女士浑身颤抖着又一次伸出手，试图停下那转动不息的纺车。\
Dores's hand shakes with pain as she reaches out once more, desperate to stop the turning.

**德洛丝医生**：——快停下！\
**Doctor Dores**: Please! Stop!

**阿尼姆斯**：做梦！\
**Animus**: Not while I still draw breath!

使徒的长弓猛地敲击地面，整座神殿微微颤动起来。丝线在刹那间绕上兀尔德的身体，向盲眼者汲取着最后的力量。\
Animus's longbow strikes the ground with a resounding crash, sending a quake through the entire sanctuary. Responding to her command, threads coil out and around Dores's body, pulling taut around her weakened frame.

**德洛丝医生**：唔……！\
**Doctor Dores**: Ugh!

仪式的光辉更甚，而盲眼者的脸色越发惨白。金光散去，她晕倒在了翻涌的雾气中。\
The ritual's glow intensifies, while her face grows paler still. As the golden light fades, she collapses into the swirling mist.

**阿尼姆斯**：呼……呵呵，我还以为又会像1999年那般……\
**Animus**: *sigh of relief* Heh ... For a moment, I thought you might've succeeded as you did in 1999.

**阿尼姆斯**：可惜，你已经不再有过往的力量了。\
**Animus**: But it seems your prime has passed.

**阿尼姆斯**：仁慈的复苏之母已经携来伟大的奇迹！任何人都休想阻止你们可悲命运的降临！\
**Animus**: The Mother of Resurrection will soon grace us with THEIR presence. Your fate is inevitable.

使徒挥动权杖，墨色的粘液包裹住盲眼者的身体，将她与纺车一同沉入黑暗。\
With a swing of the longbow, Animus encases Dores in black mucus, dragging both her and the Spinning Wheel down into darkness.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士！\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores!

**阿尼姆斯**：别着急，维尔汀。很快，无论是你还是兀尔德，都会与伟大的复苏之母融为一体。\
**Animus**: Oh, there's no need for haste, girl. The Mother shall welcome you both into THEIR embrace.

**阿尼姆斯**：谦卑地领受这无上的荣誉吧。\
**Animus**: It is a great honor to become one with THEM. You ought to be grateful.

使徒回身看向周围的教众，他们泣血泣歌，任水上涌，淹过他们的身体。\
Animus turns to her weeping believers, still chanting hymns as the rising liquid engulfs them.

——缓缓流动着的水，没有水的重量，也没有水的湿度。\
A liquid devoid of weight or wetness.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

受击\
Behind them, an arcane item about to activate is violently struck down.

身后正欲启动的神秘学道具被猛地击落。

**阿尼姆斯**：收起那些小伎俩，它只会徒增你的可笑。\
**Animus**: Well, that was amusing. But that's quite enough folly for one day.

**阿尼姆斯**：呵，无论是你，还是那个撞开门的卑下小虫子——都是一样愚蠢。\
**Animus**: You think too highly of yourself, just like that bullheaded fool who threw herself to the gate.

**阿尼姆斯**：不过她已经意识到了自己的无知，最终奉献了自身血肉和灵魂，重归复苏之母。\
**Animus**: But she realized her error, paid the price in her blood, and thus has been forgiven.

**阿尼姆斯**：如果你愿如她一般领受这份恩典，便奉献吧！仁慈的复苏之母也会吸纳你所有的悲苦，赐予你享受不尽的来日恩典。\
**Animus**: If it is redemption you seek, then you must first make an offering of yourselves. The Mother, in THEIR great mercy, shall alleviate you of your suffering.

**维尔汀**：你错了。诺谛卡进入门中的原因绝非如此——她有自己的信念。\
**Vertin**: Nonsense. Nautika didn't enter the gate to gain forgiveness. She died for her beliefs.

**阿尼姆斯**：呵……那你就自己去向她索要答案吧。\
**Animus**: My, how ignorant of me. Do send her my apologies. After all, you'll be seeing her very soon.

束缚的绳索猛地收紧。\
The ropes tighten in a sharp heave.

**阿尼姆斯**：领受这份荣光吧。你的血肉将归于复苏之母，铺就祂降临之路！\
**Animus**: Surrender unto THEM your flesh and blood, and pave the path to the Mother's return!

变暗\
Through her obscured vision, the viscous hands from beyond the gate surge through the endless tube, grasping out over the mountain's heart with terrifying speed.

几近被完全覆盖的视野中，粘稠的“门中之手”顺着冗长的甬道卷入山体内，急速靠近。

Suffocation strikes instantly.

The distant howl of wind escapes the sanctuary's gaping maw.

Vision tinged with red.

空间间歇性地鼓动，不时向着黑暗的尽头喷发一阵阵令人作呕的恶臭。\

往昔的一幕幕如在眼前。\

紧握住诺谛卡的手。尽管身处地狱，这双纤细的手却依旧充满力量。\
She clutches Nautika's hands. Even in hell, those slender fingers remain strong.

身体逐渐溶解，视野逐渐变黑，如同这个世界在否定这份意志。\
Her body is dissolving, her vision darkening, as if the world itself were rejecting her.

但彼此的双手依旧在末日紧紧相握。\
Yet even in annihilation, their hands stay locked together.

**诺谛卡**：也可以用血肉铸就新的身体。\
**Nautika**: And I will grow another.

**诺谛卡**：——因为我也不会放弃寻找“答案”，寻找我的“好消息”。\

世界的新生由风而起。\

黑色粘液自她的体内伸展，化为骨骼，而洁白的布料构成了羽翼。\
Black mucus extends out from her body, forming bones, while white fabric weaves itself into wings.

鼓声似从远方隐隐响起，她的翅膀是最高昂的旗帜，宣告迎风招展的胜利。\
A drum seems to beat from afar. She stretches her wings wide, catching the wind beneath them.

**诺谛卡**：很像……\
**Nautika**: I ...

**诺谛卡**：这和我梦中“地母”的样子很像！\
**Nautika**: Oh, I look just like the Mother Spirit when She came to me in the dream.

她骄傲地抬着下巴，踏碎神殿的巨石，跳跃间带起一阵阵风。\
Chin lifted in pride, she shatters the boulders that line the sanctuary. She leaps, and the wind follows.

下一刻，她踏风而动，摆脱无数双手的束缚，冲向天际。\
Then, she rides that wind upward, breaking free from the countless grasping hands.

**诺谛卡**：太好了，这样一来，我就可以带你们回家了！\

**Nautika**: ...!

快黑\

快亮\
Deep within the sanctuary, tremors pulse outward.

巨兽挥动着新生的羽翼躲开飞来的碎石，看向危险来源的方向。

收翅膀

神殿深处正传来阵阵颤动。

**Nautika**: Wh-What is that?

**维尔汀**：……阿尔卡纳……\
**Vertin**: Arcana.

鼓动的不定形黑色肉团伸出无数双手，紧紧融在了石壁上，整座神殿瞬间如活过来了一般吐息着。\
Throbbing black flesh stretches over countless hands, fusing snugly with the stone walls. The entire sanctuary breathes like a living thing.

**维尔汀**：如果“门”是嘴，那么我们先前或许就是被困在了胃袋中……\
**Vertin**: If the gate is the mouth, and inside it is the stomach ...

风自神殿内穿过，撞在黑色肉团上，发出呢喃一般的呼唤声。\
The wind courses through and around, carrying soft whispers with it. Until, all at once, it dives into the flesh.

**维尔汀**：是的……整座遗迹就像有生命一般活着。\
**Vertin**: Then, it seems the ruins themselves are alive.

**维尔汀**：而阿尔卡纳……她……也许就是其中的“心脏”。\
**Vertin**: And Arcana is its very heart.

**维尔汀**：恐怕很快……她就会完全复活。\
**Vertin**: I fear it's only a matter of time before she's fully resurrected.

## 10TH-22 以我纯净的血 / By Their Untainted Blood

攻击\
Words fall alongside the arcane skill's radiance. Sonetto and the Preacher's pupils each reflect the other's form.

话语随着神秘术的光辉一同落下，基金会职员与传道者的瞳孔中清晰地映照出彼此的身影。

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……这就是你的答案吗。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: It seems you've already made up your mind.

**十四行诗**：是的。无论未来如何，我都不会为此刻的选择而后悔。\
**Sonetto**: I have. My duty is clear, and I'll honor it no matter what.

短暂的沉默后，火山深处的神殿忽然传来了剧烈的震动。\
After a brief silence, another violent tremor rocks the sanctuary.

**十四行诗**：司辰……？\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper!

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……看来已经结束了。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: So, this is how it ends.

**十四行诗**：结束？你的意思是……\
**Sonetto**: Ends? What are you talking about?

传道者没有回答，她放下手中的圣像，向基金会职员走去。\
The Preacher doesn't respond. Setting down the idol, she walks toward her.

十四行诗绷紧神经，但传道者只是与她擦肩而过。\
Sonetto tenses, but the Preacher merely brushes past.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：希望你能记住今天的答案。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Remember your words today, Ms. Sonetto.

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

看着传道者的身影远去，十四行诗正欲向前，忽然看见角落里的闪光。\
The Preacher leaves. Sonetto steps forward, then freezes at a glint from the shadows.

**十四行诗**：这是……\
**Sonetto**: This is ...

**阿尼姆斯**：哼……没想到你们两个居然还活着，简直比阴沟里的老鼠还要难缠。\
**Animus**: Hmph. You've proven yourselves to be quite resistant to death. I should've known you'd have yet another shared quality with a cockroach.

**阿尼姆斯**：既然你们胆敢拒绝复苏之母仁慈的宽恕，那便领受殛灭的命运吧。\
**Animus**: No matter. You have blasphemed in the face of the Great Mother. There is naught for you but damnation now.

岩石被撞破

**诺谛卡**：小心！\
**Nautika**: Vertin, watch out!

加速\
Nautika swings her tail, scattering Animus's intense arcane energy.

庞大的兽形笨拙地扫动长尾，打散了使徒尖锐的神秘术能量。

**诺谛卡**：维、维尔汀，我们该怎么做？\
**Nautika**: Wh-What do we do now?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

黑色的肉团鼓动着，已然膨胀到了极点。\
The flesh pulsates again, swelling more, now swollen to its limit.

**维尔汀**：现在还不是回家的时候，诺谛卡。\
**Vertin**: Sorry, Nautika. I'm afraid we'll have to postpone your plans to head home.

**维尔汀**：趁阿尔卡纳还没有完全复活，我们需要破坏这场仪式。\
**Vertin**: We have to stop the ritual before Arcana is fully revived.

**诺谛卡**：阿尔卡纳就是“疯雪怪”要复活的那个家伙吗？\
**Nautika**: Arcana? Is that what those Snow Monsters were trying to do? Bring someone back from the dead?

“疯雪怪”手下的幸存者跺了跺脚，做好了反击——或者说，“复仇”的准备。\
Nautika stamps her talons into the ground, bracing for a counterattack, or more accurately, vengeance.

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，一点钟方向。\
**Vertin**: Nautika, at one o'clock!

**诺谛卡**：好、好的！\
**Nautika**: Oh. Okay!

消人\
She swings her bone-whip toward the flesh, but before impact, a rising surge of black mucus walls off each side.

毒液

巨兽挥舞绳骨袭向鼓动的肉团，然而还未等接近，骤然涌起的漆黑粘液便将二人拦了下来。

**诺谛卡**：呜……！\
**Nautika**: Ugh!

**维尔汀**：从上面，诺谛卡，从天上发起进攻。\
**Vertin**: Strike from above!

**阿尼姆斯**：天真的虫豸！\
**Animus**: Hmph! Child's play.

蛛丝\
The black liquid weaves a filament-thin net, straining to trap the soaring prey. Still fumbling with her unfamiliar flesh, Nautika loses balance.

铺天盖地的黑色液体织成一张细密的网，试图捕捉空中的飞鸟。新生的巨兽缺乏对血肉的控制，很快就失去了平衡。

**诺谛卡**：我的尾巴……！不行，要掉下去了——\
**Nautika**: Ah! My tail! I-I can't fly!

**十四行诗**：在此异邦之土，唯有月亮是我们的故人。\
**Sonetto**: I know the moon, and this is an alien city.

护盾\
A transparent shield forms in the air, blocking off the sizzling liquid.

空中书写的术式化作一道透明的光幕，挡下了灼烧的液体。

**维尔汀**：十四行诗！\
**Vertin**: Sonetto!

**十四行诗**：司辰，看到您没事就好。还有……\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper! You're alright! And ...

**十四行诗**：诺、诺谛卡小姐……？\
**Sonetto**: Is that Ms. Amundsen?

**阿尼姆斯**：又一只可恶的老鼠！该死，你是如何穿越雾气的……\
**Animus**: Another one? Filthy little wretch. How did you slip past the mist?

不速之客手中的瓶子给了她答案。\
She trails off upon seeing the little bottle clutched in Sonetto's hand.

**阿尼姆斯**：……是那个装模作样的“传道者”。\
**Animus**: Ragh! That damnable "Preacher"!

**阿尼姆斯**：无能，浅薄！愚蠢的狂妄之辈，她怎敢犯下如此疏失？\
**Animus**: How utterly feckless must one be to be bested by a child?

**阿尼姆斯**：果然，一开始就不该将如此重要的职责交在那个自命不凡的小姑娘手上。\
**Animus**: That worthless, shameless, thankless imbecile! She was always unworthy of her role!

**诺谛卡**：十四行诗，抓住我！\
**Nautika**: Sonetto, take my hand.

飞鸟带着烈风呼啸而过。巨大而坚硬的尾巴击退攻击的同时，十四行诗抓住机会一跃而起，够到了诺谛卡的足爪。\
She dives, splitting the air into a shriek. As her massive, hard tail knocks aside attacks, Sonetto seizes her chance, jumping up to grab Nautika's talons.

**维尔汀**：上来！\
**Vertin**: Get up here.

**十四行诗**：唔——！\
**Sonetto**: Urgh!

双手紧紧相握，曾经分开的伙伴们终于在空中再度会合。\
The once separated companions now meet again in midair, hands clasped tight.

**诺谛卡**：太好了，这下大家都在这里了，我们一定能中断这场仪式！\
**Nautika**: Haha! The team's back together again. And we can stop them together.

**阿尼姆斯**：……难缠的老鼠，卑下的虫豸……\
**Animus**: You have well and truly reached the boundaries of my patience.

**阿尼姆斯**：愚昧的无信者，竟妄想改写由伟大的复苏之母写定的命途……\
**Animus**: To think that you believe you can alter the path designated by the great Mother of Resurrection! Hah!

即便被来者逼退，使徒却高举权杖，发出一阵瘆人的笑声。\
Though forced back, Animus raises her longbow and lets out an ominous laugh.

**阿尼姆斯**：无妨，至高之时已至！\
**Animus**: Utter futility! The final reckoning has come!

**阿尼姆斯**：待到真正面见复苏之母的那一刻，你们的恐惧和哀嚎，都将成为最悦耳的圣诗。\
**Animus**: And when you lay your eyes upon THEM, I shall delight in the melody of your screams!

阿尼姆斯带头向着那汩汩跳动的肉团双膝跪地，而环绕在神殿内沿的全体教众亦匍匐了下来。\
Animus is the first to kneel before the throbbing, swollen flesh. At her lead, every believer drops to the ground.

周围的粘液涌起，为仪式铸就了牢不可破的屏障。\
The mucus surges around them, forming a protective barrier for the ritual.

**诺谛卡**：这个动作——等等！难道说，他们要献祭自己？！\
**Nautika**: What are they—Wait! Are they offering themselves as the final sacrifice?

教徒们手挽着手，唇贴着地。亦如婴儿紧贴着他们的母亲。

**众教徒**：来日的恩典即将显现，吾等信徒将于今日蒙福\
**Believers**: The blessing of the coming age is near. And, humbly, we kneel to receive such grace.

血液从教徒的黑袍下缓缓溢出，流向蠕动的黑色肉团。

**众教徒**：愿您至高无上之躯，再度降下——\
**Believers**: O Glorious One, walk the Earth again—

死亡不断蔓延，吟诵声渐渐沙哑、低微，却不曾停止。

那些黑袍所覆盖着的身躯干瘪下去，直至衣袍被水流带走，底下空无一物。\
The robes shrivel until only empty fabric remains, carried away by the formless liquid.

流动的鲜红血液渐渐被染黑，化作肉块的血管，随其鼓动一同涌起。\
The once-red blood darkens, becoming veins, pulsing with the rhythmic throbbing of the black heart at their center.

**维尔汀**：好强的神秘术波动……糟了。\
**Vertin**: These fluctuations are powerful. This is bad.

**阿尼姆斯**：至圣的时刻已经来临！\
**Animus**: At last, the moment has come!

**阿尼姆斯**：受苦者的肉身已于此复苏，为我们降下光明，辨识谬误。\
**Animus**: The Sufferer is returned! For through flesh and blood a vessel is forged, and so SHE walks among us once more!

**阿尼姆斯**：祂将引领我们，重塑往日的荣光，踏向应许的天园！\
**Animus**: SHE shall right the wrongs of this world and lead us to our former glory!

**阿尼姆斯**：这场洪水将洗涤一切丑陋和虚假，它将引领我们归于一切的开端！\
**Animus**: SHE shall restore the promised land! Let the great "Flood" wash away all falsehood!

**阿尼姆斯**：我们将重回真正由神秘学家主宰的“空白时代”——\
**Animus**: Let the ages begin anew! Return us to the Blank Era, where arcanists reign as masters of all!

**阿尼姆斯**：那才是最初的乐园，是本应属于我们的“理想国”！\
**Animus**: Return us to paradise! Restore the true utopia!

**阿尔卡纳**：……

## 10TH-23 有一位救世主 / And Then Came the Savior

**阿尼姆斯**：啊啊……竟能有幸亲眼目睹……何其荣幸，何其光耀！至高无上的神秘学圣母啊——\
**Animus**: Aah. What an honor it is to bear witness to Her return with my own eyes! Great Mother of Arcanum—

**阿尼姆斯**：您卑微的信众渴望您的引导！请显示您的大能，席卷一切，重塑一切，带我们回归最初的乐园！\
**Animus**: Guide us! Protect us, in your infinite might! Let the "Flood" come! Let all be reshaped! Bring forth the primordial garden!

**维尔汀**：阿尔卡纳……\
**Vertin**: Arcana ...

**阿尔卡纳**：……\
**Arcana**: ...

复活的神祇抬起无尽之手中的一肢，在空中轻点。\
The resurrected deity lifts one of her endless hands and taps the air.

井中涌出的液体骤然激荡，将没过的一切事物吞噬殆尽。\
Liquid erupts from the well, swallowing everything it touches.

**诺谛卡**：那是……\
**Nautika**: Look.

**十四行诗**：小心避开那些液体！那不是普通的水！\
**Sonetto**: Stay away from that liquid! It's no ordinary water.

**维尔汀**：井中涌出的那些水……你们在制造“暴雨”？！\
**Vertin**: It's spilling out from that well. Are you attempting another "Storm"?

**阿尼姆斯**：“暴雨”？呵呵……哈哈哈哈！\
**Animus**: "Storm"? AHAHAHAHA!

**阿尼姆斯**：可悲的羔羊，你对祂的伟大一无所知。\
**Animus**: Oh, to be so blissfully ignorant of Her true power.

**阿尼姆斯**：这并非那徒有表象的“暴雨”。\
**Animus**: This is no mere "Storm."

**阿尼姆斯**：复苏之母、秘之教诲者将带给我们的——\
**Animus**: This is a gift from the Inculcator of Arcanum.

**阿尼姆斯**：——是一场真正的、将一切带往过去的“洪水”！\
**Animus**: A great "Flood" that will return this world to primal chaos!

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**军舰士兵Ⅰ**：舰长！报、报告舰长！水……有水在升上来——！\
**Crewman I**: Captain! Sir! We're sinking.

**军舰士兵Ⅰ**：甚至已经没过甲板……升到脚边了……\
**Crewman I**: The water is rising fast. It's flooding over the deck.

**舰长Ⅱ**：只是船舱进水，不用惊慌，通知损管排查漏水源头！\
**Captain II**: Stay calm! Find the breach and seal it immediately.

**军舰士兵Ⅰ**：不，那不是海水，而是……\
**Crewman I**: But, it's not seawater, sir.

**军舰士兵Ⅱ**：报告舰长！\
**Crewman II**: Captain! Report on the enemy's status!

**舰长Ⅱ**：又发生什么事了？！\
**Captain II**: What is it?

**军舰士兵Ⅱ**：是重塑之手！他们突然停止了攻击，好像在吟唱什么咒语……\
**Crewman II**: Manus Vindictae have halted their attack! They're chanting on the deck.

**舰长Ⅱ**：咒语？\
**Captain II**: Chanting?

吟诵声隐约从冰封的海岸上传来。\
Faint chanting echoes from the frozen coast.

**众教徒**：千百万潮水，皆遵循潮汐奔流\
**Believers**: Tides run in blind by their ever-be routine,

**众教徒**：以亵渎不洁的姿态，玷污天幕\
**Believers**: Staining that Heaven with obscene calamity.

**众教徒**：破除枷锁者，主宰一切的复苏之母\
**Believers**: The breaker of death's shackles shall rule us all,

**众教徒**：于今降下，至高福祉\
**Believers**: From this day forth, and evermore.

船舱内

**舰长Ⅱ**：各单位保持冷静！\
**Captain II**: All units, stay at your posts! Wait for my order!

舰长小心翼翼地走近从内舱突然涌出的洪水边缘。\
The captain steps toward the flood pouring from the inner cabin.

**军舰士兵Ⅰ**：舰长！这些水有问题——\
**Crewman I**: Captain, something isn't right with this water.

舰长的鞋子已经没进水中。\
His boots are already submerged.

**舰长Ⅱ**：……什么？\
**Captain II**: What the hell?

**舰长Ⅱ**：我的脚……消失了？\
**Captain II**: My feet ... I can't ... They're gone!

浸入水中的部分迅速溶解、消逝，化为万千洪水中的一滴。身体沿着接触面被整齐地切断，没有流血，也没有痛感，仿佛本就不存在。\
Everything below the waterline dissolves, vanishing into the flood without a trace. His body is severed cleanly—no blood, no pain, as if it was never there.

眼前的一片汪洋并未倒映出任何画面，而是呈现着十年前、百年前、千万年前的废墟景象。\
The water reflects no present image, only ruins from ten years, a hundred years, millions of years ago.

万千水鸟疯狂地齐聚、扎堆、俯冲入水，就像火化般被洪水烧熔，消失在漫天遍地的水中。\
Numberless waterbirds gather in flocks, dive, and melt into the "Flood" like flames joining a fire, turning from the many into one.

**军舰士兵Ⅱ**：……呜啊啊啊啊啊！！！\
**Crewman II**: Arghhhhhhh!

第一声惊叫爆发，来自一位弱小的士兵，他抱头鼠窜，企图跑向高处躲避。\
The first scream erupts from a young soldier. He clutches his head and scrambles for higher ground.

然而在他还未发出第二声呼救时，却已经完全被洪水吞没了。\
But before his second cry for help can escape, the flood swallows him whole.

**众教徒**：来日的恩典即将显现，吾等信徒将于今日蒙福\
**Believers**: The blessing of the coming age is near. And, humbly, we kneel to receive such grace.

**众教徒**：愿您至高无上之躯，再度降下——\
**Believers**: O Glorious One, walk the Earth again—

**众教徒**：以无穷大能，重塑应许之地！\
**Believers**: Shape this land with your mighty, vengeful hands!

**军舰士兵Ⅰ**：——舰长！！\
**Crewman I**: Captain!

**舰长Ⅱ**：这不是正常的洪水，而是刻雷乌斯长官所说过的……\
**Captain II**: This flood ... Creius warned me about this.

**舰长Ⅱ**：快联系索姆将军！全员将平衡伞打起来！\
**Captain II**: Equilibrium Umbrellas open, everyone! Get Admiral Somme on the line!

一只只伞柄被飞快举起，伞罩中闪烁出强有力的光芒。\
Umbrella handles are lifted, the canopies blazing with light.

**舰长Ⅱ**：平衡伞能够抵挡“暴雨”，那么也一定可以抵挡……\
**Captain II**: This is just another "Storm." The umbrella's will—

然而话音未落之际，洪水已然将人连同平衡伞一起吞噬。\
Yet before the words are spoken, the flood devours them whole, and soon after, the Equilibrium Umbrellas too.

一顶顶伞以及一个个举着伞的人瞬间融化在水中。\
One by one, umbrellas and their bearers dissolve into the water.

士兵的呼救声与重塑海兽的咆哮声不绝于耳，而下一瞬，一切声音都化为空寂。\
The soldiers' screams and the Manus seabeasts' roars clash. Then silence. Absolute silence.

**伊戈尔将军**：……99年的一切又一次重演了。\
**Admiral Igor**: It is happening again. Just like in 1999.

将军眺望着远方舰队的沉没。\
The admiral watches the distant fleet sink beneath the waves.

**伊戈尔将军**：对于下达指令的人来说，他们不过是沙盘上的数字，棋盘里的棋子。\
**Admiral Igor**: To a commander, troops are just numbers on the sand table, pieces on a chessboard.

**伊戈尔将军**：相对即将发生的灾难，他们的力量微乎其微。然而他们不曾知晓这点，而知晓这点的人并不在乎他们的生命。\
**Admiral Igor**: But in the face of a calamity, what can a foot soldier do? Many men and women have been marched to their deaths, cannon fodder for the cause—a "necessary sacrifice" ...

**伊戈尔将军**：那些曾被不断投入的生命和热情，最终也只是归于一片空白。\
**Admiral Igor**: And their loyalty and passion turned to dust in an instant.

海平面飞速上升，远方的陆缘冰已经不见踪影。整个世界只剩下一片洁白如新的洪水，像透明的纱布，将所有杂质抹去。\
The sea climbs faster now, the coastal ice shelves already gone. Only a pristine flood remains, like a veil of translucent gauze wiping away all impurities.

**托勒密**：父亲，我们已经和姐姐的队伍完成会合了。\
**Ptolemy**: Father, Moldir's men have arrived.

**伊戈尔将军**：人数清点完毕了吗？\
**Admiral Igor**: Good. Has the team been mustered?

**托勒密**：包括受到重塑之手影响的病患在内都确认完毕了，与名单一致，只差丹尼洛夫机长和……\
**Ptolemy**: Yes, including the wounded from the Manus Vindictae attack. Everyone's here except Captain Danilov ...

**托勒密**：姐姐，她不在这里。\
**Ptolemy**: ... and Moldir. She wasn't with the team when they arrived.

**伊戈尔将军**：我明白了。\
**Admiral Igor**: I see.

**伊戈尔将军**：准备动身吧。\
**Admiral Igor**: Prepare to move. We are breaking camp.

**托勒密**：我们要去哪里？\
**Ptolemy**: Yes, sir. Where to?

**伊戈尔将军**：去一片能自洪水中庇护我们的奇迹之地。\
**Admiral Igor**: Somewhere safe. Somewhere the "Flood" cannot reach us.

将军从怀中掏出那个黑色的盒子。它浮于半空，在将军手上缓缓旋转起来，隐约向外辐射着一圈圈金光。\
From his coat, the admiral draws the black box. It rotates in slow motion over his palm, emitting faint golden light.

**托勒密**：这就是我们和重塑之手交易的成果吗？\
**Ptolemy**: Is that what we got from the Manus deal?

老将军点了点头。\
He nods.

**伊戈尔将军**：不再有无谓的牺牲，我们将踏上的是一条全新的道路。\
**Admiral Igor**: It is. From this day on, we are taking a different path. One without fruitless sacrifice.

**托勒密**：可姐姐她……\
**Ptolemy**: But Moldir is still ...

**伊戈尔将军**：她亦有自己选择的道路。\
**Admiral Igor**: She is walking her own path.

将军将目光投向遥远的雪山之巅，像是看着自己的来时路。\
Igor looks out toward the distant snowy peaks, seeing instead the long road that brought him to this moment.

**伊戈尔将军**：我相信她。\
**Admiral Igor**: I have faith in her decision.

**乌尔里希**：躁动的魔精、异常的海水情况、突然发生的雪崩……\
**Ulrich**: Restless critters, rising sea level, abnormal avalanches ...

**乌尔里希**：——该死，一定是重塑之手的仪式已经开始了！我们得尽快想出对策……\
**Ulrich**: It's the Manus ritual. It's already begun. We need to do something before it's too late!

**护卫兵**：老板！现在不是说这些的时候！！\
**Guard**: You've got to be kidding me. Boss, this isn't exactly the time for chit-chat!

**嚼嚼松果**：雪崩要来了！路线更改——各位！跟好我！\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Avalanche incomin'! All units, change course! Follow me, now!

护卫兵一把扛起还在试图分析现状的研究员，加足马力飞快地向上冲去。\
The guard hoists up the still-analyzing researcher and charges uphill at full speed.

震动

**嚼嚼松果**：糟糕，雪浪要冲下来了！\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Heads up! Snow's comin' down! Anchor yourselves!

**护卫兵**：呃——！\
**Guard**: Ergh!

护卫兵在积雪剧烈的坍塌中试图稳住身体，但雪崩的震动还是轻易击垮了渺小的两人。\
In the collapsing snowfield, the guard struggles to steady herself, but the sheer force of the avalanche overwhelms them both.

雪崩\
A massive snow chunk slams into them, sending Ulrich's tank spinning into the void.

雪崩2

一团巨大的雪块袭来，将承载磁流体的玻璃缸击飞了出去。

**乌尔里希**：该死！\
**Ulrich**: Ah! For Flux's—

**护卫兵**：——老板，你的头！！\
**Guard**: BOSS!

玻璃缸运动的抛物线止于一双稳稳的手。\
The glass tank's arc ends in a pair of steady hands.

**莫莉德尔**：……呼，还好赶上了。\
**Moldir**: Phew. We made it just in time.

骤风中，黑色的头发从帽檐下飘飞出来。\
In the howling wind, black hair escapes from under her hat.

**莫莉德尔**：丹尼洛夫机长，降低高度，放下挂梯，接应他们。\
**Moldir**: It's them, Captain Danilov. Lower the altitude and release the ladder.

拉镜头

下拉

**莫莉德尔**：各位，快跳过来！\
**Moldir**: Over here, all of you!

剧烈的风声中，她的声音却显得清晰而有力。\
Yet despite the roaring gale, her voice rings out clear and strong.

**嚼嚼松果**：莫莉德尔中尉！\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Lieutenant Moldir!

**莫莉德尔**：抱歉，我们来迟了。\
**Moldir**: My apologies. We should've come sooner.

机舱\
The guard shoves Ulrich's body into the cabin. With help from Moldir, the two groups finally merge.

护卫兵连忙将意识唤醒者的身体推进机舱，在前芝诺近卫团副官的帮助下，两边的队伍终于会合。\
Miraculously, aside from some surface damage to Ulrich's glass container, no arcanists or penguins are harmed.

所幸除了组长的玻璃装置些微破损外，并无任何神秘学家和企鹅的伤亡。

**嚼嚼松果**：多亏您及时赶到，莫莉德尔中尉！\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Hooey, Lieutenant! You got here just in the nick o' time.

**莫莉德尔**：客套话就不必再说了。\
**Moldir**: That's quite enough.

快切

**莫莉德尔**：水位在上升——它绝非自然的海水，其毁灭性更甚于“暴雨”。\
**Moldir**: The sea level is rising, but not with any ordinary water. This is something far worse than we have ever seen. Something even more destructive than the "Storm."

**莫莉德尔**：这场“洪水”正将所有东西冲刷殆尽。\
**Moldir**: At this rate, it will soon wipe this era from the face of the Earth.

**乌尔里希**：重塑之手的仪式已经开始了，我们必须采取行动。\
**Ulrich**: I figured as much. An event of this scale and severity could only be the result of the Manus ritual. We must act now.

研究员将头重新固定回身体，取出了“非对称核素R”采样装置。烈风并未阻碍磁流体一如既往地在缸内快速流动。\
Ulrich reattaches his head, then pulls out the apparatus for "asymmetrical nuclide R." The ferrofluid churns in his tank, unfazed by the shifting gale.

采样装置几乎在眨眼间就盛满了金色流体。\
The apparatus fills with golden liquid in the blink of an eye.

**乌尔里希**：目前空气中急剧上涨的非对称核素R浓度、以及与“暴雨”相似的一系列现象或许可以导向一个结论——\
**Ulrich**: This "Flood" looks different from the "Storm," yes, but the sudden surge in the level of asymmetrical nuclide R in the air suggests they come from the same source.

**乌尔里希**：“洪水”与“暴雨”存在着一定关联，或者进一步猜想，“洪水”是另一种形态的“暴雨”。\
**Ulrich**: Or, to take a leap, they are one and the same. The "Flood" is the "Storm."

**莫莉德尔**：那么，你们之前所说的“星锑”唱片或许可以发挥作用？\
**Moldir**: So, the "Regulus" record might still work?

**乌尔里希**：你理解得很快，中尉。\
**Ulrich**: You're a quick learner, Lieutenant.

**乌尔里希**：既然唱片可以延缓时代病的发展，或许也可以延缓仪式的进程。\
**Ulrich**: If the record can slow the progression of the Storm Syndrome, then it stands to reason that it might do the same for the ritual.

**乌尔里希**：我们现在必须尽快播放唱片，生成稳定性磁场。\
**Ulrich**: Time is against us. We need to place the record and generate the immunity zone as soon as possible.

**乌尔里希**：为了让它的辐射范围能够覆盖到山中的仪式现场，我们需要抓紧时间赶往山顶！\
**Ulrich**: Which means we need to reach the mountaintop. It's the only location where we can be sure the ritual site will fall within its radius.

**莫莉德尔**：丹尼洛夫机长！\
**Moldir**: Captain Danilov!

**机长**：收到！请各位坐稳！\
**Aircraft Captain**: I heard him, ma'am! Hold tight, everyone!

默契让军人之间略去了多余的指令交换，“小犬号”在螺旋桨轰鸣中倾斜着爬升。\
No orders are needed between seasoned soldiers. The Canis Minor tilts upward, propellers screaming.

**莫莉德尔**：以目前海平面上升的速度来看，我们能来得及吗？\
**Moldir**: The sea level is rising fast. Do you think we still stand a chance once we get there?

**乌尔里希**：不止有我们在试图阻止重塑之手的仪式，司辰她们也同样在努力着。\
**Ulrich**: I can't say for certain, but I have faith. I'm sure the Timekeeper is doing everything she can to hold off the ritual for us.

喧嚣的风声中，磁流体的声音异常清晰坚定。\
Despite the chaotic wind, Ulrich's voice holds steady.

**乌尔里希**：莫莉德尔中尉，从过往无数次的科研，无数次的成功与失败中，我学会最为关键的一点就是——\
**Ulrich**: If there's one thing I've learned from all my years of research, Lieutenant,

**乌尔里希**：相信我们的协作者，然后，全力以赴。\
**Ulrich**: it's that you give it your all and trust your collaborators to do the same.

**维尔汀**：……水面在迅速上升。再这样下去，洪水会将一切全部吞噬。\
**Vertin**: The water's rising quickly. At this rate, we'll all be underwater in a matter of minutes.

**维尔汀**：我们必须破坏仪式，阻止洪水的上涨。\
**Vertin**: We must disrupt the ritual before the "Flood" drowns us all.

仪式、雾气、洪水——一切都缠绕在那具诡异的庞大身躯之上。\
Rituals, mist, the "Flood"—all twist around the grotesque colossus.

**维尔汀**：攻击阿尔卡纳，或许能找到破绽！\
**Vertin**: Attack Arcana. Maybe we can find a weakness!

**诺谛卡**：好、好的！\
**Nautika**: G-Got it!

攻击\
A lead arrow splits the thick air, embedding itself beside Nautika's twitching talons.

铅箭破开浓稠的空气，钉在诺谛卡蠢蠢欲动的足爪边。

**阿尼姆斯**：呵呵，痴心妄想。\
**Animus**: Hah! What a farce.

**阿尼姆斯**：世界重溯是必然的结果，仅凭你们这些虫豸也想阻止？\
**Animus**: A few squirming little insects think they can defy fate's design!

**阿尼姆斯**：所谓的现在，还有现在正发生的一切——都只是虚假根系上长出的罪恶果实，本就不该存在。\
**Animus**: This world you so desperately cling to is naught but the poisonous fruits of a corrupted tree—rotten to the very core.

**阿尼姆斯**：你们将见证洪水没过一切。所有罪孽都将消失，世界会回到最初始的、它本该有的样子！\
**Animus**: Watch as it falls to pieces. Watch as the "Flood" washes away all the impurities of this world and returns us to what should have been!

**阿尔卡纳**：……\
**Arcana**: ...

“阿尔卡纳”巨大的躯体动了动，从那模糊不清的面庞上似乎能看到熟悉的笑容。\
"Arcana" shifts, her blurred face showing a familiar smile.

**阿尼姆斯**：啊，啊！至高的圣母！我已聆听，我已明悟，我将践行您的教诲！\
**Animus**: The Mother has awakened! O Great Lady, I kneel before You. Enlighten us with Your divine knowledge!

**阿尼姆斯**：请降下您仁慈的威能——将她们永远留在这里！\
**Animus**: Grant us Your benevolent might! Bring down Your mighty hand of vengeance!

**十四行诗**：诺谛卡，小心那些黑色粘液的攻击！\
**Sonetto**: Nautika, watch out for the black mucus!

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀，十四行诗，抓紧我！\
**Nautika**: Hold on, team!

加速\
Nautika spreads her wings, charging headfirst into a storm of black arrows.

飞鸟伸展翅膀，迎着粘液化作的无数箭矢猛地飞去。

毒液

**十四行诗**：——！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

毒液\
At the last possible moment, Nautika folds her wings and slips into the narrow gap between the flood and piercing arrows.

在即将与雨幕般的箭矢相撞之时，诺谛卡收起双翼，从洪水和箭雨的夹缝中穿行而过。

**诺谛卡**：呜、呼……大家没事吧？\
**Nautika**: Ugh! Is everyone okay?

**十四行诗**：你的身体被灼伤了！诺谛卡，我帮你治疗一下！\
**Sonetto**: You're burned! Let me take care of that.

**诺谛卡**：我、我还好，没关系，你们抱紧我就好！\
**Nautika**: I'm fine, really, I am! Just hold onto me!

**维尔汀**：但我们不能一直以你的受伤为代价躲避进攻。\
**Vertin**: You're injured, Nautika. We can't dodge these attacks forever.

**诺谛卡**：……我知道了。\
**Nautika**: You're right.

**诺谛卡**：告诉我要怎么做吧，维尔汀！\
**Nautika**: Then, tell me, Vertin. Tell me what to do.

**诺谛卡**：我还无法熟练运用这份新的力量，但我相信，你能想出更好的办法！\
**Nautika**: I'm still not used to this body. I need your guidance.

**十四行诗**：请您指挥我们进行作战吧，司辰。\
**Sonetto**: Just give the word, Timekeeper.

**维尔汀**：嗯，助我一臂之力吧。\
**Vertin**: We'll make it through this, together.

羽翼再次向天空伸展，而伙伴也坚守在地面。

**阿尼姆斯**：卑下的虫豸，挣扎是徒劳的！\
**Animus**: All this writhing and squirming—it is utterly in vain!

**阿尼姆斯**：“洪水”带来的空白见证者们将聆听吾辈的呼唤。\
**Animus**: The "Flood" shall summon the creatures of the Blank Era.

笑声毛骨悚然。\
Her words dig deep into the bone.

**阿尼姆斯**：无论是你们，还是神殿之上试图搞小动作的那些蝼蚁，都将成为旧日复苏的奠基石！\
**Animus**: And your elimination, along with those pitiful beings sneaking atop the sanctuary, shall serve as its foundation!

**十四行诗**：司辰，恐怕乌尔里希组长他们会有危险！\
**Sonetto**: They ... Timekeeper, Mr. Ulrich might be in danger!

**维尔汀**：冷静下来，十四行诗。\
**Vertin**: Don't act in haste, Sonetto.

**维尔汀**：请你尽可能攻击阿尼姆斯。如果能阻止她施展神秘术，或许能对乌尔里希组长那边有所帮助。\
**Vertin**: We'll do what we can from down here. Keep Animus engaged. Draw her attention away from Mr. Ulrich.

**维尔汀**：还有……如果可能的话，尽可能留意德洛丝女士的踪迹。\
**Vertin**: And if possible, keep an eye out for Dr. Dores.

**十四行诗**：我明白了，司辰。\
**Sonetto**: Understood.

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀，洪水越涨越高了，再这样下去，我们就没有空间飞行了……！\
**Nautika**: Vertin! The water just keeps getting higher. I'm running out of space to fly in.

**维尔汀**：嗯，我们必须远离洪水，创造作战空间。\
**Vertin**: You're right. We need to make more space.

**维尔汀**：诺谛卡，你有办法破坏神殿吗？\
**Vertin**: Can you break through these walls?

**诺谛卡**：破、破坏神殿？\
**Nautika**: B-Break the walls?

**维尔汀**：没错，你刚才飞行时踏碎了侧壁的岩石，就像那样。\
**Vertin**: Yes, just like you did earlier when you kicked those rocks.

向前望去，诡异神祇的庞大身躯正通过无数黑色的血管与整个神殿紧密相连。\
Ahead looms the grotesque deity, her form tethered to the sanctuary by endless pulsing black veins.

**维尔汀**：神殿在为阿尔卡纳供给力量。\
**Vertin**: The entire sanctuary is feeding power to Arcana.

**维尔汀**：如果能冲破神殿，既能削弱阿尔卡纳，创造飞行空间，又能利用落石进行攻击。\
**Vertin**: If we can break these walls, we may be able to slow down her recovery. We can also use the falling debris to attack the believers below, and create more space for us to stay above the "Flood."

**诺谛卡**：呼、呼……我明白了，交给我吧！\
**Nautika**: Okay. I'll give it my all.

**莫莉德尔**：这里就是神殿的正上方了，乌尔里希组长！\
**Moldir**: We've reached the target area. The sanctuary is directly below us.

**乌尔里希**：海平面上升的速度很快，我们的时间不多了。\
**Ulrich**: This will be a race against the clock.

未等直升机停稳，中尉便率先跃下，接应着意识唤醒者走出了机舱。\
Before the helicopter can even stabilize, Moldir leaps out, guiding Ulrich from the cabin.

**乌尔里希**：事不宜迟，立刻开始设置唱片机，生成稳定性磁场……\
**Ulrich**: Now's the time. Give me a hand with the record player while I generate the magnetic field.

鼓捣

不行

**乌尔里希**：该死！这里的地磁情况在不停变动，唱片机无法校准至理想调校状态！\
**Ulrich**: Damn it! The field is totally unstable. I can't accurately calibrate the record player under these conditions.

**乌尔里希**：这与我之前的两千三百次实验的情况都不一样，大气中非对称核素R的浓度超乎想象！\
**Ulrich**: The asymmetrical nuclide R in the air is far denser than anything we've ever had in the lab.

**乌尔里希**：变量太多，在这种情况下，我甚至无法确定“星锑”能否如我们所期望的那般奏效……\
**Ulrich**: There are too many variables. There's no way to be sure that "Regulus" will function as expected.

磁流体混乱地将自己分散成无数小点，而后又猛烈聚拢。\
The ferrofluid fractures into scattered dots, then coalesces.

**乌尔里希**：总之先检测环境中非对称核素R的浓度，对应调整实验数值；接下来改进信号处理算法，设置防护设施；要是能推导地磁场变化规律……\
**Ulrich**: Calm down, Ulrich. First, get the latest asymmetrical nuclide R reading and make the necessary adjustments. Then we'll deal with the signal interference. If I can find the pattern of the geomagnetic change—

鼓捣

不行

**乌尔里希**：**的[拉普拉斯脏话]——这个装置冻坏了，有人能搭把手——\
**Ulrich**: For Flux's sake! The device is frozen. Somebody help me out here.

自脚下的又一次震动险些将磁流体震倒。与此同时，头顶传来了奥利图欧的啸叫。\
Another quake in ice and earth all but topples Ulrich. Above, Olitiau's screech pierces the air.

**莫莉德尔**：小心，乌尔里希组长。\
**Moldir**: Be careful, Ulrich.

中尉眼疾手快地扶住了研究员。\
Moldir steadies Ulrich just in time.

**莫莉德尔**：只是被冻坏了的话，这个环境监测装置交由我修理。嚼嚼松果，排除那些干扰实验的魔物！\
**Moldir**: Leave the monitoring device to me. I can fix it. Buddy, keep those creatures off of us.

**嚼嚼松果**：中尉，那似乎不是普通的奥利图欧，那中间的是……\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Ain't gotta tell me twice. But, Lieutenant, that thing don't look like no Olitiau I ever seen.

白骨构成的庞大生物遮蔽天空，领着疯狂的奥利图欧向山巅的众人袭来。\
A great boney creature spreads its wings and dives toward them, followed by a swarm of Olitiaus, eager to feast.

**嚼嚼松果**：哇！好一块硬骨头！\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Heavens to Betsy! Now this'll be a tough nut to crack.

**莫莉德尔**：……各位，做好战斗准备，保护组长完成实验！\
**Moldir**: Prepare to engage. Hold them off while Ulrich works on the record. There is no room for error.

**嚼嚼松果**：这些该死的丑鸟越来越多了……！\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Goshdarnit! These birds 're meaner 'n a two-headed snake and twice as tenacious!

**企鹅**：嘎啊——\
**Penguins**: Uragh!

**护卫兵**：精神错乱的程度也在加深！……哇啊！机长！别咬我的五倍压缩巧克力口味军粮！\
**Guard**: Captain Danilov's spiraling. I can't hold on much longer. Come on, Captain, let go! That's my chocolate MRE!

**莫莉德尔**：乌尔里希组长，你还需要多久！\
**Moldir**: Ulrich. Hurry it up.

**乌尔里希**：……神秘学材料设置完毕，方位确认，环境数据确认。\
**Ulrich**: Materials, check. Location, check. Environmental factors, check.

鼓捣

不行

**乌尔里希**：——第二十一次实验失败！该死，磁场方位和预设值不符，唱片无法发挥作用！\
**Ulrich**: Flux! It's just not working. I must've got the magnetic poles wrong again.

**乌尔里希**：最后一次尝试……\
**Ulrich**: Experiment number 22. Last chance.

**护卫兵**：老板，我们必须得走了！——我快拉不住丹尼洛夫机长了！\
**Guard**: Oh, but, just forget it, boss. We have to go before Danilov crashes us all to the ground.

松鼠中士、企鹅列兵一一被莫莉德尔甩进了机舱里。最后，她也一脚踩在了舱门的边缘上。\
Moldir hurls the squirrel and penguins all into the cabin in a heap before making the jump herself.

**莫莉德尔**：乌尔里希组长，拉住我的手！\
**Moldir**: Give me your hand, Ulrich. That's an order.

**乌尔里希**：预设值调整，参数确认，最后一次——！\
**Ulrich**: Program set. Parameters confirmed. Initiating.

中尉提起磁流体的领子飞离山巅的前一刻，磁流体终于将指针第二十二次放在了唱片之上。\
With a yank on Ulrich's collar, Moldir hauls him skyward, just as he presses the needle onto the record for the twenty-second time.

**乌尔里希**：地磁场的强烈波动停止了……\
**Ulrich**: The magnetic field—it's stabilizing. It worked.

**乌尔里希**：……成功了！\
**Ulrich**: We did it!

拉远镜头

**莫莉德尔**：看——海平面不再上升了！\
**Moldir**: Look. The water's stopped rising.

**十四行诗**：听见了吗，司辰？是星锑常听的摇滚乐！\
**Sonetto**: Do you hear that? It's Regulus's song.

**十四行诗**：洪水平静下来了，看来是乌尔里希组长他们减缓了仪式的进程！\
**Sonetto**: And look, the "Flood" has stopped. Mr. Ulrich made it.

**维尔汀**：趁不受洪水干扰的时候，诺谛卡！\
**Vertin**: Nautika, this is our chance.

伴随着摇滚的节奏，飞鸟踏碎了神殿的最后一根支柱。\
With the pounding beat of the song, the last pillar crumbles under Nautika's strike.

**诺谛卡**：我、我做到了！\
**Nautika**: I-I did it.

**维尔汀**：干得漂亮，诺谛卡。\
**Vertin**: Well done, Nautika.

**维尔汀**：神殿开始坍塌了，小心躲避！\
**Vertin**: But stay sharp. The sanctuary's coming apart. Watch out for falling debris.

飞鸟穿过隆隆的坠石。一阵剧烈的震动后，过往的祭坛已成废墟。\
Nautika weaves through crashing boulders. With a final quake, the altar collapses into ruin.

落石将一切活物掩埋，最底层的巨石下露出信徒们的黑袍一角。\
Rubble buries all life below, only the edges of the believers' black robes still visible beneath the crush of stone.

**阿尼姆斯**：呃……\
**Animus**: Urgh ...

**阿尼姆斯**：亵渎……之人……！\
**Animus**: Blasphemous little ...

又一块石板落下，喷出一口血与气后，她再也无法发出声音。\
Another stone falls. A gasp, a spurt of blood, then silence.

**诺谛卡**：……这里应该安全了……\
**Nautika**: We should be safe here.

诺谛卡小心翼翼地在没有洪水的狭窄空间内伸展翅膀，将二人安置在不受洪水与落石侵袭的安全地带。\
Nautika extends her wings, careful of the narrow space, sheltering the pair from both the "Flood" and falling rocks.

**十四行诗**：所有的一切……都掩埋在了废墟和洪水之下。\
**Sonetto**: Everything's been buried beneath the "Flood."

**十四行诗**：但阿尔卡纳……\
**Sonetto**: And yet Arcana ...

崩塌\
The body dissolves, reshaping into a familiar human silhouette.

可怖的神祇身体逐渐溶解，化作了熟悉的人形。\
She stands on the surface of the "Flood" on her toes, watching the sanctuary collapse.

祂脚尖轻点于洪水之上，抬头仰望不断震动着、坍塌中的神殿。

**阿尔卡纳**：这篇终章，确实缺了一首动听的挽歌。\
**Arcana**: A dirge to mark the end of this world. How fitting.

**阿尔卡纳**：嘘……\
**Arcana**: Shh ...

于是碎裂的神殿静了下来，所有声音都被泯灭，唯余祂的话语在空中回响。\
Only her voice remains, echoing through the void.

**阿尔卡纳**：当歌谣的尾音落下，洪水将再度翻涌。\
**Arcana**: When the final note falls, the "Flood" shall rise once more.

**阿尔卡纳**：旧时代将被寻回，新秩序将要诞生。\
**Arcana**: An ancient era shall be reclaimed, and a new order forged.

阿尔卡纳站在水中，对众人露出一个微笑。\
Arcana stands in the water, smiling all the same.

**阿尔卡纳**：你的世界正迎来终结，“众人跟随的救世主”。可惜，你还不能停下。\
**Arcana**: The end is nigh. But do take solace in thine achievement, my little savior, that this world should draw its final breath on a tune and not a scream. But alas, this is no true end for you.

**阿尔卡纳**：再会，维尔汀……\
**Arcana**: We shall meet again, Vertin.

**阿尔卡纳**：在“我们的世界”。\
**Arcana**: In a world that is rightfully ours.

身影消失在上涌的水中。\
Then she disappears into the rising tide.

## 10TH-24 对岸 / The Other Bank of the River

**诺谛卡**：她……消失了？！\
**Nautika**: She's gone? Just like that?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

随着阿尔卡纳的消失，神殿再度开始震颤。不断坠落的巨石预告着一切有生之物的陨落。\
As Arcana vanishes, the sanctuary rocks once again. Yet more boulders fall, their tumbling cacophony heralding death.

**维尔汀**：“我的世界正在迎来终结”……\
**Vertin**: "The end is nigh" ...

**十四行诗**：司辰，虽然进程减缓了，但仪式并未崩溃——洪水还在缓慢地上涨。\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper, we may have slowed down the "Flood," but the water is still rising.

**十四行诗**：恐怕……我们的时间不多了。\
**Sonetto**: There are very few options left for us now.

**诺谛卡**：维尔汀，十四行诗，神殿好像快要完全坍塌了，我们还是快离开吧……\
**Nautika**: This place could collapse any minute. W-We should go. We should go right now.

**维尔汀**：你先走吧，诺谛卡。去找最近的基金会部队，他们提前设置了大型传送术阵，至少能将你带回最近的免疫区。\
**Vertin**: You're right. Go find the Foundation troops. They'll get you to safety.

**诺谛卡**：你、你不走吗，维尔汀？\
**Nautika**: Wh-What about you?

**维尔汀**：不能让这个世界如重塑之手所愿变为空白。\
**Vertin**: I cannot allow Manus Vindictae to wipe this world clean.

**维尔汀**：距离神殿完全坍塌还有一段时间，我还想再尝试一下。\
**Vertin**: The sanctuary should hold a little longer. I have to try again to stop this "Flood."

**维尔汀**：乌尔里希组长好不容易为我们争取了这段宝贵的时间，还不能在这里放弃。\
**Vertin**: Mr. Ulrich risked his life to buy us this time. We mustn't squander it.

第一助手微微点了点头，陷入了思虑。\
Sonetto nods, still lost in thought.

**十四行诗**：可无论是破坏神殿，还是击溃仪式的主持者……我们之前阻止仪式的尝试都没能奏效。\
**Sonetto**: But, neither attacking Animus nor destroying the sanctuary stopped the ritual.

**十四行诗**：您还有什么想法吗？\
**Sonetto**: What else can we do?

**维尔汀**：仪式既然还在继续，那么其核心就并未被阿尔卡纳带走，它还在这里的某处运转着。\
**Vertin**: Even though Arcana is gone, the ritual is still ongoing. She must have left the source of its power here in the sanctuary.

**维尔汀**：以之前德洛丝女士与仪式的关联性来推测，她也很可能会在那里。\
**Vertin**: They needed Dr. Dores to start the ritual. Perhaps the power source is tied to her somehow.

**维尔汀**：……我要再去看一眼祭坛中央。\
**Vertin**: I need to check the altar again.

**诺谛卡**：但、但这里已经被水淹没了，而这些水又不能碰……我带你飞——\
**Nautika**: But ... But it's under the "Flood." You can't touch the water, or you'll disappear. Let me take you. I can fly you over the top, and you can take a look from there, ugh!

“地母”的巨兽抬起前爪，可翅膀却因为先前战斗中受的伤而难以伸展。\
Nautika raises her forepaws, but her wings fail to spread. Blackened, bruised, and wounded.

**维尔汀**：没关系，诺谛卡，我能过去。\
**Vertin**: I'll be fine, Nautika. The water can't harm me.

**维尔汀**：这里的洪水是“暴雨”的“水”与冰川融水的结合，兼具二者的特性。\
**Vertin**: The "Flood" is a mix of glacier water and "Storm" water, which doesn't affect me.

**维尔汀**：但我不会受到“暴雨”的影响，所以它对我来说——只是普通的水而已。\
**Vertin**: So, to me, it's just ordinary water.

**维尔汀**：看。\
**Vertin**: Look.

**十四行诗**：——！\
**Sonetto**: ...!

水流从指尖划过，浸入水中的手完好无损，时间并未留下痕迹。\
Water slips through her fingertips, and the hand submerged in it remains unscathed—time has left no trace.

**维尔汀**：不痛，只是有点凉，也没有其他异常。看来我的猜想是对的，那么，或许我的计划也值得一试。\
**Vertin**: See? I'm fine. It's a little chilly, but nothing more.

**维尔汀**：十四行诗，诺谛卡，请帮我照看好箱子，去安全的地方等我。\
**Vertin**: Sonetto, please take my suitcase and go with Nautika. I'll catch up to you later.

回身，尝试寻找一个合适的地方入水。小腿浸入冰冷的水的刹那，身体不由自主地颤抖起来。\
She turns around, searching for a suitable spot to enter the water. The icy water sending shivers up her thigh all the way to her neck.

**十四行诗**：司辰！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper.

身后的第一助手抱紧箱子，似乎想要说些什么。\
Behind her, Sonetto clutches the suitcase, holding off her desire to speak.

**维尔汀**：这里很危险。你不走吗，十四行诗？\
**Vertin**: Sonetto, it's dangerous here.

**十四行诗**：……我是您的副手。追随您至任何险境是我的责任与义务。\
**Sonetto**: I'm your assistant. It's my duty to stay by your side, no matter how great the danger.

**十四行诗**：我会等您回来的，司辰。\
**Sonetto**: I'm staying. I'll wait here for your return, Timekeeper.

跃入水中，远古生物的骨骼与建筑碎块从身侧划过。\
Leaping in, ancient bones and debris glide past.

对于要如何前进，心中早已有了答案。\
The path forward is already decided.

**维尔汀**：如果我没记错的话，在德洛丝女士转动纺车后，仪式就启动了。\
**Vertin**: If I remember correctly, the ritual began right after Dr. Dores spun the Wheel.

回忆

**德洛丝医生**：我纺织的线连向了井底……为什么？这些线的使命不该流向那里……\
**Doctor Dores**: The threads ... They were drawn away somewhere deep below me. This—this isn't right.

**德洛丝医生**：……纺车也无法停下了……\
**Doctor Dores**: And the Wheel ... I can't seem to stop it.

**德洛丝医生**：维尔汀，快走——\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin, you must leave.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士通过转动纺车开启了仪式，后续纺车也在不断转动，维持着仪式的继续。\
**Vertin**: The ritual began when Dr. Dores turned the Spinning Wheel, and once it started, it kept turning as if it were sustaining the ritual.

**维尔汀**：那么无论要阻止仪式，还是找到德洛丝女士，那架纺车都是关键。\
**Vertin**: So the Wheel must be the key to all this. That's what I should be looking for.

闭眼\
Just like before, with eyes closed, instinct takes over.

像之前一样，闭上眼，遵循自身的感觉。\
Upon reopening them, the golden thread flickers into view once more.

睁眼

睁眼时，再一次，飘忽的金线落在了眼前。

**维尔汀**：“线”……\
**Vertin**: A thread?

**维尔汀**：是德洛丝女士在指引我吗？\
**Vertin**: Is Dr. Dores guiding me?

**维尔汀**：跟随金线深入……\
**Vertin**: It's leading me deeper.

然而金线牵引的路似乎漫无尽头。\
Yet it stretches without end.

**维尔汀**：唔……！\
**Vertin**: Ugh!

一阵激烈的水流干扰了视线。再度睁开眼时，引路的线又不知去了哪里。\
A strong current pulls a dense thicket of obscuring debris into her path; the guiding thread vanishes from just beyond her grasp.

**维尔汀**：水流越来越快了，按照歌曲时间来推算，星锑的摇滚乐也要接近尾声了……\
**Vertin**: The current is growing stronger. Regulus's song must be coming to an end.

**维尔汀**：需要尽快找到纺车……可纺车的线去了哪里？\
**Vertin**: Time's running out. I need to find the Wheel as soon as—Huh? Where did the thread go?

**？？？**：……♪\
**???**: … ♪

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

令人怀念的哼唱声从上方传来。攀附着岩石将头探出水面，正寻觅的面容映入眼帘。\
A familiar hum drifts from above. Clinging to the rocks, she lifts her head, and there stands the one she sought.

水花

**德洛丝医生**：……！\
**Doctor Dores**: ...!

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士！\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores!

**德洛丝医生**：维尔汀，你真的来了……！我的感觉没有错，我知道你会找到这里。\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin. You came. My instincts were correct. I knew you'd find your way here.

歌声的主人欣喜地扶住身侧的纺车支撑起身体。它正以极其缓慢的速度转动着。

**德洛丝医生**：这架纺车纺织出的线与井底相连，带来了这场洪水。\
**Doctor Dores**: The threads are no longer under my control. It's as if they're flowing down into some sort of well. I believe it is the source of the "Flood," too.

**德洛丝医生**：所以我想，如果要阻止这场仪式，就必须想办法让纺车停下才行。\
**Doctor Dores**: If we're to have any hope of stopping this, I think we'll have to halt the Spinning Wheel first.

**维尔汀**：这和我的推断一致。请您稍等，德洛丝女士——\
**Vertin**: Agreed. Stay where you are, Dr. Dores. I'll—

做出进一步的判断前，率先注意到的是盲眼者裙下的异样。\
A singular fixed detail catches her eye.

双足突兀地消失了，好似从未存在过一般。她只得倚靠着纺车才能站起来。\
Dores's feet are gone, as though they never existed in the first place. She now maintains her balance by gripping the sides of the Spinning Wheel.

**维尔汀**：您的脚……怎么了？\
**Vertin**: What happened to your feet?

**德洛丝医生**：……应该是先前昏迷时，我接触到了这些洪水。\
**Doctor Dores**: Ah. They were gone when I woke up. They must've touched the water when I was unconscious.

**德洛丝医生**：抱歉，我想将纺车带给你，可一旦触碰到这片水，我的身体就会消融。\
**Doctor Dores**: My apologies. I would bring the Spinning Wheel to you, but my body will dissolve in the water.

**维尔汀**：……没关系，我这就过来找您！\
**Vertin**: No problem. I'll come to you.

**德洛丝医生**：小心！这片水域非常湍急，我几次尝试离开都失败了。\
**Doctor Dores**: Be careful. The current is strong here. I tried several times to escape, but the conditions are too unpredictable.

**德洛丝医生**：因为这里——\
**Doctor Dores**: I think it's because this is ...

下方传来的一阵尖利呼啸声打断了盲眼者的话语，洪水中开始涌起阵阵激烈的浪涛。\
A shriek cuts her off. The "Flood" churns below them.

白色的浪带旋转着，渐渐汇作一个深不见底的漩涡。\
White waves spiral, coalescing into a fathomless vortex.

**维尔汀**：这是……“暴雨眼”！\
**Vertin**: Eye of the "Storm."

**德洛丝医生**：纺车又要再度开始转动了，维尔汀！\
**Doctor Dores**: Careful, Vertin. The Spinning Wheel is resuming its pace.

盲眼者捧起纺车，绳轮伴随着水流正微微颤动着。\
Dores cradles the Wheel. Its rotations seem to match the trembles of the current's pulse.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士，等我过来……呜！\
**Vertin**: Stay right there, Dr. Dores. I'm com—Urgh!

松开侧壁的岩石尝试前进，但身体瞬间就被激烈的波涛带走，只能在慌乱中再度抓住另一块石头稳住身形。\
She lets go of the rock wall and tries to move forward, but the raging waves grab her and sweep her away. Despite a moment of panic, she manages to steady herself on another rock.

好像有某种尖锐的物体划破了手心。所幸洪水寒冷刺骨，疼痛才显得没那么强烈。\
A sharp slice coats her palm in red. Fortunately, the water's icy chill numbs the pain.

**维尔汀**：咳、咳咳……\
**Vertin**: *coughing*

手心渗出的鲜血很快随水而逝，而身处的漩涡却还在不断扩大。\
Her blood dissolves quickly in the water. Next to them, the whirlpool is growing ever larger.

**维尔汀**：呼、呼……\
**Vertin**: *panting*

**维尔汀**：……没关系，我可以再试一次……\
**Vertin**: It's alright. Just try again.

第二次尝试、第三次、第四次……每一次尝试，都以再度被浪涛拍回边缘的岩石而告终。\
Another attempt. Then three. Four ... Each time, the waves slam her back against the rock.

而水流却越发湍急。\
And the current grows fiercer.

**德洛丝医生**：维尔汀……！\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin!

似乎是下定了决心，盲眼者撕下裙子的布条，将不停转动的纺车捆在了自己的身上。\
Resolute, she tears her dress's hem, lashing the Spinning Wheel to her body.

**德洛丝医生**：等着我，维尔汀，我会将纺车带给你！\
**Doctor Dores**: Wait there. I'm bringing the Wheel to you.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士？！\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores, no!

盲眼者扶住岸边的岩石，用颤抖的双臂支撑自己挪入了湍急的水流中。冰冷只是让她打了个寒战，却没有阻挡她深入的步伐。\
Propped against the rocks, Dores drags herself into the torrent. The cold wracks her with shivers, but she moves undeterred.

**德洛丝医生**：唔……！\
**Doctor Dores**: Ugh!

很快，她被洪水淹没的半个身子都已经消失，只余上半身抓着岸边的岩石，艰难地前行着。\
Soon, half-submerged, only her arms cling to the shore as the flood devours her lower half.

水流不断拍击着她纤细的身体，而她带着纺车在浪带间艰难地浮沉。\
The raging pool batters her slender frame, yet she and the Spinning Wheel keep bobbing up amid the waves.

**德洛丝医生**：这个位置，应该可以了……\
**Doctor Dores**: Just a little closer.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士，停下！您不能再——\
**Vertin**: That's far enough. Just stop right there, please. Don't—

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：韧绳缠绕。\
**Vertin**: Lazo Lock!

神秘术难得如期生效，将脚踝与岩石绑定，让自己不至于被洪水带走。\
An unusually successful arcane skill anchors her to the rock, defying the pull of the rushing water.

竭力倾斜身体，将手臂伸到最远，但那仅有数米的短暂距离似乎永远无法跨越。\
She leans, stretches—yet those final meters feel insurmountable.

纺车的颤抖越来越剧烈。\
The Wheel shudders ever more violently now.

耳边只有激烈的水声和漩涡的呼啸。\
The roar of water fills her ears.

**德洛丝医生**：——维尔汀。\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin.

**德洛丝医生**：不用担心，维尔汀。\
**Doctor Dores**: Don't worry about me.

盲眼者的声音跨越浪涛的嘶吼传来，却显得平静而温柔。\
Dores's voice cuts through the roaring waves—calm, gentle.

**德洛丝医生**：我很高兴能再次见到你。\
**Doctor Dores**: I'm glad to have seen you again, child.

**德洛丝医生**：一路顺风。\
**Doctor Dores**: I wish you my very best on the journey ahead.

**维尔汀**：——！\
**Vertin**: ...!

盲眼者松开了用以支撑身体的岩石，激烈的水流将她带了过来。\
Dores releases the rock. The current seizes her, pulling her forward.

金色的纺车在水面上浮沉着，盲眼者浸入水中的部分正不断消散。\
The Spinning Wheel bobs on the surface while what's left of her dissolves piece by piece.

动画

**维尔汀**：我拿到纺车了！\
**Vertin**: Okay. I got the Wheel.

**维尔汀**：握住我的手，德洛丝女士！\
**Vertin**: Now take my hand, please.

兀尔德笑容特写，嘴型“再见”

**德洛丝医生**：再见。\
**Doctor Dores**: Goodbye.

维尔汀想要抱住兀尔德，却只抱住了纺车

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士！！！\
**Vertin**: DR. DORES!

声嘶力竭的呼喊被浪涛覆盖。\
And the Spinning Wheel stills, and the furious waters grow quiet.

盲眼者化为了一阵风，消散在无边的水中。\
One raindrop rises from the "Flood."

帧动画复用部分结束，屏幕渐暗，黑屏。\
Then two, three ...

随着纺车停止转动，汹涌的波涛，也渐渐平息了。\
The "Flood" recedes.

先是一滴雨，离开水面升向半空。\
And the "Storm" begins.

然后是两滴、三滴……

洪水褪去。

而后，“暴雨”将临。

下雨持续

## 10TH-25 启示录变相 / Apocalypsis cum figuris

**莫莉德尔**：这是……\
**Moldir**: This is ...

中尉走下直升机，看着水滴从水面浮起。\
Moldir steps down from the helicopter, watching drops float upward.

**嚼嚼松果**：从地上往天上下的雨？这倒是新鲜！这种事在佛罗里达都不常见——\
**Buddy Fairchild**: Butter my backside and call me a biscuit! Rain pullin' itself right off the ground and risin' up into the sky! I ain't never seen nuttin' like it!

莫莉德尔伸手抓住嚼嚼松果中士的外衣，阻止了他冲进雨中。\
Moldir yanks Sergeant Buddy Fairchild back by his coat before he can dash into the rain.

**莫莉德尔**：小心，别碰到那些雨滴。\
**Moldir**: Careful, Sergeant. Stay clear of those raindrops.

她看向了海平面，汹涌的洪水不再上涨，却以别样的姿态向空中回归。\
She scans the horizon. The flood no longer pours out across the land; instead, it ascends back into the sky.

**莫莉德尔**：……海平面正在下降。\
**Moldir**: The sea level is dropping.

**莫莉德尔**：真不可思议，如此鲁莽的尝试竟然成功了。\
**Moldir**: I can hardly believe it. The plan actually worked.

**莫莉德尔**：看来这一次你赌对了。“奇迹”发生了，乌尔里希组长。\
**Moldir**: I guess you're less of a fool than I thought, Mr. Ulrich.

**乌尔里希**：与其感叹奇迹，不如说是维尔汀她们所做的努力。\
**Ulrich**: I was only one part of the plan.

**乌尔里希**：不知道维尔汀那边经历了什么。你该感谢她，如果还有机会的话。\
**Ulrich**: I wonder how Vertin's doing down there. She's the one you should be thanking.

**莫莉德尔**：当然。\
**Moldir**: I'll make sure I do.

**莫莉德尔**：……雨很快就会下大了。\
**Moldir**: The "Storm" is growing heavy.

**莫莉德尔**：不知圣保罗是否有能遮雨的地方。\
**Moldir**: I wonder have my people in São Paulo found shelter?

开伞

**护卫兵**：还好临行前多申请了几把平衡伞……老板，我给你撑伞！\
**Guard**: I knew I wasn't mad for bringing a few extra Equilibrium Umbrellas. Boss, get under here!

研究员点了点头，看向了远处坍塌的山体。\
Ulrich nods and looks at the collapsed mountain.

一切痕迹都被“暴雨”冲刷，而磁流体在缸中静默地流淌。\
Every trace has been erased by the "Storm." The ferrofluid flows through his tank without any trace of emotion.

独白黑

**乌尔里希**：重塑之手的仪式崩溃了，所创造的洪水化作了一场“暴雨”……\
**Ulrich**: The ritual has been disrupted, and the "Flood" is turning into a "Storm."

**乌尔里希**：难道……\
**Ulrich**: Then, does that mean ...

思想电流

**乌尔里希**：我们所经历的所有“暴雨”，都来源于过去一场失败的“洪水”？\
**Ulrich**: All the "Storms" were the result of a failed "Flood"?

远处的舰船上，平衡伞一把接一把地打起。\
On distant ships, Equilibrium Umbrellas snap open one by one.

索姆将军远眺南极。\
Admiral Somme looks out over Antarctica.

**索姆将军**：如同99年一般，倾覆世界的仪式又一次被阻止了。\
**Admiral Somme**: The ritual has been halted, just as it was in 1999.

**索姆将军**：然后，又一场“暴雨”落下了。\
**Admiral Somme**: And now comes another "Storm." History has a way of repeating itself, it seems.

将军身后，另一双军靴踏出。\
Behind him, crisp boots step forward.

**刻雷乌斯**：不知这一次我们又会重返何时……亦或是去往未来。\
**Creius**: Where will it take us this time? Back to the past? Or into the future?

**索姆将军**：这已经是最好的结果。\
**Admiral Somme**: Perhaps this is the best outcome we could have hoped for.

**索姆将军**：这场战役的后果本会更加惨烈。\
**Admiral Somme**: We might have suffered many more casualties.

**刻雷乌斯**：是的。\
**Creius**: Agreed, sir.

**刻雷乌斯**：基金会的那位“司辰”，看来她确实有过人之处。\
**Creius**: The Timekeeper has certainly exceeded her reputation—quite remarkable indeed.

**索姆将军**：无论如何，这场战役已然落幕了。\
**Admiral Somme**: Regardless, the battle is over.

**刻雷乌斯**：我们只有短暂的休整之机。\
**Creius**: But our respite will be brief.

**刻雷乌斯**：……这场“暴雨”，很快就会结束。\
**Creius**: After all, the "Storm" won't last for long.

“暴雨”洗刷的世界里，枪炮军火从四起的硝烟中逐一挺立而起。\
In the "Storm," firearms and artillery rise one after another.

**维尔汀**：唔……\
**Vertin**: Urhm ...

**十四行诗**：司辰！\
**Sonetto**: Timekeeper!

**维尔汀**：十四行诗、诺谛卡……？\
**Vertin**: Sonetto? Nautika?

**诺谛卡**：你终于醒了，维尔汀！我们找了好久才找到你，我、我真的很担心……\
**Nautika**: You're awake! We were searching and searching, and we couldn't find you anywhere, and we were so worried and ... and ...

**十四行诗**：洪水退去之后，我们在坍塌的神殿内找到了您。所幸您从外表看没什么大碍。\
**Sonetto**: We found you in the sanctuary ruins after the "Flood" subsided. I don't see any issues with your physical condition, but ...

**十四行诗**：您感觉怎么样，有什么不适吗？\
**Sonetto**: How are you feeling? Any discomfort?

**维尔汀**：纺车……\
**Vertin**: The Spinning Wheel ...

**十四行诗**：……\
**Sonetto**: ...

**十四行诗**：我们找到您的时候，您的怀中正紧抱着一架残缺的纺车。\
**Sonetto**: The only piece of it we found was the one that you were holding in your hand when we found you.

**十四行诗**：那架纺车和箱中的纺车很像，我猜想它很重要，就将它放回箱中保管了。\
**Sonetto**: It looks almost identical to the one we have in the suitcase. I assumed it was important, so I put it in the suitcase for safekeeping.

**十四行诗**：那是最安全的地方，您不用担心。\
**Sonetto**: Probably best to keep it in there for now.

**维尔汀**：我好像听见了……雨声……\
**Vertin**: Wait. Is that rain I hear?

**十四行诗**：是“暴雨”。洪水化作“暴雨”落下了。\
**Sonetto**: Yes. It's the "Storm." The "Flood" transformed into it.

**十四行诗**：但这里……神殿里是安全的。\
**Sonetto**: But don't worry. We're safe within the sanctuary walls.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

支撑起身体，向外望去。\
Pushing upright, she looks out.

渐白\
The "Storm" purges all things.

雨幕冲刷着世间的一切。\
Yet at the edge of vision, a familiar silhouette appears like a haze within the rising rain.

但在那尽头，依稀映照出一个期盼的身影。

**维尔汀**：那是——\
**Vertin**: That's ...

**维尔汀**：——德洛丝女士？\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores?

脚步不由自主地迈出，向远方追逐而去。\
Her feet move on their own, chasing the distant image.

**维尔汀**：德洛丝女士，请等等！\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores, wait!

**维尔汀**：我、我还有问题想问您——\
**Vertin**: I-I still have things I need to ask you!

那个身影停了下来。这一次，她回过头来。\
The figure stops. This time, she turns.

**德洛丝医生**：维尔汀。\
**Doctor Dores**: Vertin.

“暴雨”正在冲刷她的面容。\
The "Storm" blurs her face.

**德洛丝医生**：我们在不同的命途之上追逐着各自的答案。\
**Doctor Dores**: We all walk our own paths, seeking our own answers.

**德洛丝医生**：但在未来，我们一定会再见的。\
**Doctor Dores**: But our paths will surely cross again.

渐白\
The rain dissolves the figure, carrying it away—impossible to tell whether anything truly stood there or if it was just a waking dream.

雨幕将那个身影溶解、带走，无法分清那里曾有某人真实存在，亦或是一场幻梦。\
Except for the song, familiar and bright drifting down from beyond the sky.

唯有歌声从遥远的天边响起。\
Sail, sail free, my heart and light.

长白\
Wave your home a last goodbye.

视频\
Go and seek the Golden Fleece.

出发吧，启程吧，我最亲爱的\
In the land of endless peace.

告别港湾，撑船远航\
Sail, sail free, my heart and light.

金羊毛在道路的尽头等待\
Find your home beneath your feet.

那里无人衰老、硕果遍开\
Winter, spring, the years they turn.

去吧，去吧，我最亲爱的\
Let your heart grow brave and strong.

我们的故乡正在脚下

冬去春来，夏去秋来

愿你永远脚步轻盈、无畏、勇敢
